Ukwengeza kulokhu , imibandela iyenziwa ukwakha amakomiti amawadi , njengezinhlangano ezelulekayo , lawa maqembu ahlanganisa abamele umasipala kanye nomphakathi ukuba badlulise izidingo zomphakathi kanye neziphakamiso ziye kumkhandlu . Indlela esebenza ngakubili yewadi kanye nokumela ngokulingana kusho ukuthi imiphakathi ikhethe ngqo abayimele abanesibopho kubo ukuba badlulise futhi babike ukukhathazeka kwabo . Chaza izindlela ezahlukene zokubhekana nengxabano . Ukongela umhlalaphansi negebe lobungozi benzuzo kumele kuvalwe ngezinguquko kubandakanya neminikelo okumele ifakwe , kubhekelelwe kakhulu ekuxhaseni leyo minikelo kulabo abahola kancane noma abasebenza izikhathi ezithile . Imithombo yangaphakathi : eyenziwa ngumasipala qobo lwakhe , isib. izintela zikamasipala nemisebenzi enjengokuqashiswa kwezakhiwo kanye nezinkokhelo namanani komsebenzisi . Ukuhlelwa kokulandelana kwezigigaba zomphakathi , ukuhlaziywa kwezimo zezikhathi zonyaka nezesikhathi eside kwenza kube lula ukuba umphakathi uhlonze ukuthi kuyini okuletha intuthuko kuwenze ukwazi ukuhlonza uhlaziye impumelelo noma ukungabi nagalelo kwezinhlobo zokungenelela emizamweni yokuqhubezela intuthuko yomphakathi . Umdwebo kaVenn , ukuhlaziywa kwezindlela zokuziphilisa , imisebenzi yokwenza amabalazwe nokunqamula izindawo zibe yiziqephu kukhipha isithombe sesimo samanje somphakathi , kuqhakambise izimo zendawo , kusize ekuhlaziyeni izindlela zokuziphilisa nezidingo zomphakathi . Ukuqaphela inqubekelaphambili yephrojekthi kusemqoka ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ihlala isesimeni esifanele nokuthi ubungozi noma izinguquko ezintsha ziyaqashelwa bese ziyalandelelwa ekusetshenzisweni kwazo kamuva . Amathimba amaphrojekthi asebenzisa izinkomba ukuze aqaphele inqubekelaphambili . Izinkomba zingokuhlosiwe okukhombisa ukuthi ngabe izinjongo zifeziwe yini . Amalogifreyimu kwesinye isikhathi abiza izinkomba ' ngezinkomba eziqinisekiswe ngokungachemi ' . Izinkomba kudingeka ziqondane , zenele , zicace , zilinganiseke , zibe nokonga futhi zitholakale . Ama-CDW abantu bomphakathi abayizinsinzakusebenza abasebenza nomphakathi lapho bekhethwe khona futhi ababika kuwo ngomsebenzi wabo . Baxhaswe yiminyango kahulumeni eyinhlobonhlobo , ikakhulukazi owohulumeni basekhaya . Umjikelezo Wokulethwa kwemisebenzi ukhonjisiwe kuthebula ekhasini lama-28 . Likhombisa amazinga omjikelezo kanye nemisebenzi yamazinga ahlukahlukene kahulumeni . Izinga lokunikezela kwemisebenzi yilapho kwenzeka khona ukusebenza kanye nokugcinwa , okungukunikezelwa kwemisebenzi ngokwempela . Ukuvikela izindawo zemvelo ngazo zonke izindlela , ukushiyela izizukulwane ezizayo okungenani isipho esiyinani elilinganayo . I-MFMA , ka-2003 idinga ukuthi isabelomali sikamasipala sihambisane ne-IDP . Ukuxhumanisa isabelomali sikamasipala ne-IDP kuqinisekisa ukuthi amakhansela azibophezela kumiphakathi yawo kanye nokuthi izidingo zalabo abamelwe yiwo kuyabhekwana nazo ukuze lezo zidingo zibe ngezangempela . Okuphambili ohlwini lokubalulekile okuhlonzwe ku-IDP kumele kuboshelelwe kuzindleko zekhephithali kusabelomali sikamasipala . Umthethosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika unikeza uhlaka olulingene okulona yonke imiyalo nemithetho okufanele yenziwe . Unikeza amalungelo , ukukhululeka , amandla nokuvikeleka kwabo bonke abantu ezweni . Ubeka izimbulunga ezintathu zikahulumeni zezwe-Uhulumeni kuzwelonke , esifundazweni nowendawo . Umthethosisekelo ubophezela uhulumeni wendawo ukuba uthathe indima egunyeni lokuthuthukisa ngokunikeza imisebenzi ethile yokuthuthukisa kuhulumeni wendawo . Ukulawulwa kwezinguquko jikelele : Ukubheka umthelela kanye nezinguquko ezihlanganisiwe emaphuzwini asemqoka nokuthi yini okumele yenziwe ngazo . Ukwenza umbono kwenza umphakathi ukwazi ukukhuluma ngezifiso zawo zezentuthuko . Kuyindlela enamandla ikakhulukazi uma , njengoba kuvela emsebenzini olandelayo , kususelwa ekubuyekezweni kwempahla nezidingo . Lokhu kukhuthaza umphakathi ukuba wenze umbono ofanele nonokufezeka kanye nezinyathelo zokufinyelela embonweni . Muningi umsebenzi okumele wenziwe ukugcizelela imisebenzi izakhamuzi ezinayo entuthukweni yazo nasekusebenzisaneni nabanye emphakathini ukusombulula izinkinga nezinselelo . Isiqubulo esithi , " hlala ubukele , uhulumeni uzosebenza " kumele siphikiswe - asisilo iqiniso futhi-ke asihambisani nendlela yaseNingizimu Afrika yokubusa . Yini imiphumela yohlelo mayelana nokuthuthukiswa kwezinsiza zabasebenzi kanye nokwakhiwa kwamandla abesifazane ? Abesilisa bona ? Kungabe isimo sabesifazane kanye nezinga labo lithuthukisiwe njengomphumela wohlelo ? Ukhetho oluvamile , olukhululekile , olufanele kanye nolukholekayo oluphethwe isiphathimandla sokhetho esingachemile sinikeza izakhamizi ithuba lokwenza ukhetho . UMSEBENZI 2 Iqembu lixoxa ngezingxenye ezibalulekile zohlelo lwesigceme zihlonze namazinga azokwakha uhlelo . Acela inselele abuye acele nocwaningo uma ezwa ukuthi kunokumoshwa kwezimali zikamasipala . Ababambe iqhaza bayehlukana babe ngamaqembu amancane babhekane nezinto ezintathu zezentuthuko eziqhakanjiswe emsebenzini owandulela lona . Ababambe iqhaza bazejwayeza leso naleso sinyathelo sokwakha uhlelo lwesigceme wadi bedlala izindawo abaqokelwe zona . Abagqugquzeli bagqugquzela inqubo , amaqembu abhala imininingwane yawo kwifliphushadi lelo nalelo qembu licelwa ukuba lenze isethulo emhlanganweni wezingxoxo . Hola ingxoxo ngalo msebenzi uxoxe ngezimpendulo zababambe iqhaza kanye nokuthi bangazisebenzisa yini iziphakamiso zabo ohlwini lokuhlola bese ubonisa ezinye izindlela ezingasetshenziswa ukufeza ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi . Izinkomba zomphumela zilinganisa ' lokho okuqhamuke kwiprojekthi ' . Izinkomba kumele zinqunywe yimiphakathi ethintekayo . Izinkomba ziba nengqondo kuphela uma zihambisana nabantu abathintekayo . Inani labantu elivela kumaqembu okuqondiswe kuwo mayelana nokuqashwa ngokulingana aqashwe kumazinga ezokulawula aphezulu amathathu ngokuhambisana nohlelo lokuqashwa ngokulingana olwamukelwe ngumasipala . Aqinisekisa ukuthi amalungu omphakathi ayaqonda mayelana nesabelomali kafuphi kanye nemicikilisho okuqondene nesigceme . Imihlahlandlela ayiwona imthetho , kodwa iwuhlaka olungasiza omasipala ukwakha Amakomiti Amawadi . Omasipala bendawo bahlukile futhi badinga ukuba nekhono lokwazi ukuthola izinxazululo zezinkinga abahlangabezana nazo emphakathini wabo . Omasipala kufanele babhale inqubomgomo yamakomodi yamawadi izokwazi ukuvunyelwa Umkhandlu Kumasipala . Kungabe Ikomidi Lesigceme linazo izindlela zokugqugquzela ngamandla ukubandakanywa kwabesifazane kwiKomidi Lesigceme kanye nasemaqhingeni ukwandisa ukumeleleka kwabo emazingeni okuthathwa kwezinqumo ? Yiziphi lezo zindlela ? Uhlelo LukaZwelonke Lwezentuthuko luhlose ukulwa nobuphofu nokunciphisa ukungalingani ngonyaka wezi-2030 . INingizimu Afrika ingazifeza lezi zinhloso ngokubheka amandla abantu bayo , ukukhulisa umnotho wabantu bonke , ukwakha ukukwazi ukusebenza , ukukhulisa amandla ombuso , nokuthuthukisa ubuholi nokubambisana emphakathini wonke . Ukusetshenziswa ngempumelelo kwaloku hlelo kudinga ubuholi obuqinile obuvela kuhulumeni , amabhizinisi , abasebenzi nomphakathi . Ukuhlaziywa kwababambe iqhaza kumele kude kubhekiswa kukho ngaso sonke isikhathi sokwenzeka kwephrojekthi . Kufanele kubhekwe ngokuhlanganyela nokuhlaziywa kwenkinga , kunokuthi kubhekwe njengento ezimele nje . Ukuhlaziywa kwesabiwomali sobulili kusiza ohulumeni ukuba banqume ngokuthi izinqubomgomo kumele zilungiswe kanjani , nanokuthi yikuphi lapho izinsiza okumele zabelwe khona . Ukuhlaziywa kwesabiwomali sobulili kunikeza abesifazane inkomba yokuzibophezela kukahulumeni ukwethula izidingo ezithile zabesifazane kanye namalungelo okunakekelwa kwezempilo , ezemfundo kanye nokuthola umsebenzi . Imihlangano yezinyanga ezimbili yokulandela uhlelo ibalulekile ekomidini emva kokwenziwa kohlelo njengendlela yokuhlanganisa abantu yokwethula uhlelo nokwenza abantu babone ukuthi inqubekelaphambili yohlelo isemahlombe abo abantu . Ahlomisa okwenziwa ngumphakathi kanye nokwesabela komphakathi , ukuze kuqinisekiswe impendulo eya kumkhandlu . Ukudlondlobala kokukhula komnotho ngaphezu kwamaphesenti ayisi-5 ngonyaka kuyodinga ukuthi osomabhizinisi nabasebenzi baqinisekise umbono owodwa abavumelana ngawo . Izwe alikakaqali ukubhekana namaphuzu omphakathi anomthelela enkohlakalweni . Umlando waseNingizimu Afrika wosizo oluvela kuhulumeni uphinde usithibeze amazinga amahle okuziphatha . Okwenzeka emazweni ngamazwe kukhombisa ukuthi ngesifiso sezombusazwe nokusetshenziswa kwamasu afanele ngokusimeme , inkohlakalo ingancishiswa kakhulu kubuyiselwe nokuthemba komphakathi . Ukubona abantu abafanele isehlakalo esithile . Isibonelo uma ngabe kuludaba oluphathelene nezempilo , abasebenzi bezempilo , iziguli , abeluleki bokunakekela emakhaya , abeluleki bomphakathi njll . kungaba ngabantu okuzodingeka ukuthi bazibandakanye . Ukumeleleka kwamaqembu amele izimfuno - Yiziphi izinhlelo ezikhona zokwenza ngithole uvo lwamaqembu amele izimfuno ? Kungabe ngiyadinga ukuhlela imihlangano njalo neqembu ngalinye elimele izimfuno ? Qinisekisa ukuthi uzinike isikhathi sokwazisa iKomidi Lesigceme kulelo nalelo qembu elimele izimfuno futhi wawanikeza imininingwane yokuxhumana . Umgqugquzeli uhola futhi aphathe indlela yokugqugquzela . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kungenzeka abizwe ukuba agqugquzele umhlangano ukuze athole uvo lomphakathi oluqondene noHlelo Lwentuthuko Oludidiyele noma ekwakhiweni koHlelo Lokuhlola Ukusebenza . Imiphakathi yakhiwe ngabantu bemilando engefani , abathanda izinto ezingefani , kanye namasiko , izinkolo , izizwe namaholo angefani . Ukulinganisa kanye nokwamukela lezi zinto ezingefani kuyinselelo enkulu . Izinto ezifana nezinsiza eziyingcosana , ukutholakala nokulawulwa kwezinsiza kwengeza kwengeza izinselelo . Abagqugquzeli bohlelo lwe-CBP kumele baqikelele ukuthi kuba khona ukumeleleka ngesikhathi sokuhlela , futhi kumele bahlinzeke ngethuba lokuzwakalisa izinto ezifunwayo ngokwehlukana kwazo , bese kuxoxwa kuvunyelwane ngazo . Iqhaza labo emine isimo esiqinisekisa ukuzibandakanya ngokuphelelayo kwamaqembu enqubeni yokuhlela . Yimiphi imithetho kanye nezinhlelo zokuthathwa kwezinqumo : Kungabe isuka phezulu iya phansi ? Kungabe iyabandakanya ? Kungabe akhona amathuba abantu abasebenza ngaphandle , abasebenza emahhovisi kanye nabanye abangebona abaphathi ukuba baqhamuke nokusha ; ukuba babe negalelo kwizinqumo zeKomidi lesiGceme ? Ukubamba iqhaza okusiza izinkampani zangaphandle ukufeza izinhloso zezinhlelo zabo , ikakhulukazi ngezindleko eziphansi . Abantu bangabamba iqhaza ngokwenza amaqembu ukuhlangabezana nezinhloso ezibekwe ngaphambili , eziphathelene nohlelo . Ukubamba iqhaza okunjalo kuvamise ukuba khona emva kokuba izinkampani zangaphandle sezithathe izinqumo ezisemqoka . Umkhandlu oqokiwe yiwo inkundla yokugcina ekuthathweni kwezinqumo kuma-IDP . Igalelo ledemokhrasi lapho kubanjwa iqhaza khona luwukwazisa , ukuxoxisana kanye nokuphawula mayelana nalezo zinqumo , ngesikhathi senqubo yokuhlela / sokuthathwa kwezinqumo . Funda nababambe iqhaza amanothi esifundo emakhasini ama-75-76 . Ababambe iqhaza kumele benze uhlelo lomhlangano wekomidi lesigceme nolomhlangano womphakathi . Umkhandlu ukhangise ithenda yokudiliva ukudla ngamaphasela emphakathini . Ithenda inikwe usonkontileka wangaphandle , kodwa abaningi babona ukuthi bebekhona emphakathini abebengawenza lo msebenzi . Usonkontileka usebenzisa abantu bangaphandle abangayazi indawo futhi ngesinye isikhathi amaphasela okudla awafiki kulabo abhekiswe kubo . Kunokungaxhumani kahle phakathi kukasonkontileka , iKomidi Lesigceme nomphakathi . Vele sekunezinkinga ezibonakalayo futhi umphakathi ubona ukuthi amaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele enze okuthile ngale nkinga . Ngonyaka wezi-2030 , abantu abahlala eNingizimu Afrika kufanele baziwe bephephile futhi bengenakho ukwesaba ubelelesi . Abesifazane , izingane namaqembu ahlaseleka kalula kumele bazizwe bevikelekile . Kufanele bayethembe inqubo yokusebenza komthetho ukubopha nokushushisa ngempumelelo izelelesi ezilwa nokuphepha kwabantu nomphakathi . Uphiko Lwezemisebenzi Yamaphoyisa AseNingizimu Afrika namaphoyisa edolobha kumele kube yizikhungo ezisebenza kahle ezinabasebenzi abanamakhono , abakwazi ukuzilawula , abaziphethe kahle abawuhloniphayo umsebenzi wabo futhi abasiza umphakathi . AmaKomidi Ezigceme abalulekile ekuqinisekiseni ukubamba komphakathi iqhaza ekusebenzeni kukamasipala . Lokhu kufaka phakathi ukuhlola ukusebenza kukamasipala nokuba novo kwi-PMS . Kunomgomo womthetho kumasipala wokumbandakanya amakomidi endawo , ngokusebenzisa amaKomidi Ezigceme ukwenza ama-KPI nemiklamo yokusebenza nokuqinisekisa ukumbandakanywa komphakathi ekuhloleni nasekubuyekezeni izinkomba . Kungenzeka kube nezimfuno ezishayisanayo kuzigceme ezihlukene kumasipala futhi lezi zimfuno kufanele zibhekisiswe uma kwenziwa i-PMS . IKomidi Lesigceme ngayinye kumasipala lingakujabulela ukuthi izimfuno zalo ziyakhathalelwa . Isibonelo , isigceme esinezimboni eziyimbijana nezinga lokungaqashwa eliphezulu ingafuna ukuba kwenziwe isimo lapho kugqugquzelwa khona izimboni . Esinye isigceme singaba nesikhumulo sezindiza futhi isikhalazo sayo kube ngumsindo nokungcola komoya . I-PMS kungafuneka izame ukufaka zonke izimfuno ngokubheka ukuthi yikuphi okungenzeka kulowo masipala . Uhulumeni wendawo kufanele aqinisekisa ukuthi kukhona ulawulo lwangempela ukuze kuvikeleke imali engenayo , impahla , nemali kamasipala edalwa ukumosha , ukulahleka noma ukutshontshwa . Kusemqoka ukuthola izidingo zomphakathi ngaphambi kokwenza iphrojekthi noma ukuqala umsebenzi wentuthuko endaweni . Umfanekiso osekhasini elilandelayo ukhombisa amanye amaphuzu asemqoka okumele abhekelelwe . Kungabe uhlelo lwaphendula kanjani kwizidingo ezingungqaphambili zamaqembu athile ahlosiwe phakathi kwemiphakathi yabesifazane kanye neyabesilisa ethintekayo ? Umlaleli - ukugqugquzela kudinga amakhono okulalela , bheka iSahluko 2 ukuthola ulwazi olwanele ngamakhono okulalela . Indlela evamile yokwethula imiphumela yenkinga kanye nezimbangela zayo ukusebenzisa isihlahla sezinkinga . Injongo yalo mfanekiso ukukhombisa amaphuzu ababambe iqhaza abafisa ukubhekana nawo nokusiza ukwenza iqoqo lezinjongo zezinqumo zephrojekthi . Inqubomgomo kahulumeni yokuthenga impahla nemisebenzi isithibeza indlela yokulwa nenkohlakalo ; indlela kahulumeni yokuthenga impahla nemisebenzi isigxile kakhulu kubasebenzi basemahhovisi . Ukugcizelela ekuhlonipheni ngokubeka uphawu ebhokisini kwenza indlela ibize kakhulu , isinde , ingasebenzi kahle futhi ilinge abasebenzi ukuthi benze inkohlakalo . Sihlongoza ukungabheki kakhulu amathenda amakhulu nawesikhathi eside , ukwenza ukuthi kungabi semthethweni kubasebenzi bakahulumeni ukwenza izinhlobo ezithile zamabhizinisi nokwenza ukuthi abantu ngabanye bazithole benecala ngokulahlekelwa emacaleni enkohlakalo aqinisekisiwe . Ukufika kwabavela kwamanye amazwe kulindeleke ukuthi kwengeze ngephesenti eliphakathi kweli-0.1 kuya kweli-0.2 ngonyaka ezingeni lokukhula kwesibalo sabantu esikhathini sonyaka wezi-2030 . Nokungabi nesikhathi - Amalungu omphakathi kwesinye isikhathi kumele achithe isikhathi nemizamo azame ukuziphilisa futhi awatholakali nganoma yisiphi isikhathi ukungenela imihlangano . Lokhu kwenzeka kakhulu kwabesifazane kanye namalungu omphakathi angasebenzi . I-PMS ne-IDP kuyasebenzisana kumasipala njengoba lokhu kukala ukuthi umasipala ukwenza kanjani okuhlelwe kwi-IDP , njengoba i-IDP ingumnyombo wokulethelwa izinsizakalo nokuthuthukiswa komphakathi . I-PMS kufanele ihambisane nesimo sikamasipala . Kufanele incike kwizinsizakusebenza nokusemqoka , izinjongo , izinkomba nemiklamo ekwi-IDP . UNgqongqoshe Kahulumeni Wesifundazwe Nohulumeni Basekhaya ubeke ama-KPI amaningi aphoqelekile . Omasipala kufanele bawafake kanye namanye ama-KPI abonakala efanelekile kuma-PMS abo . Uhlelo oluyimpumelelo oluzinze emphakathi ludinga ukubandakanywa kwabo bonke abathintekayo ohlelweni lokuhlela , njengezakhamuzi , amakhansela , izikhulu zikamasipala , amalungu ezinhlaka zomphakathi njengamakomidi ezigceme nezinhlangano ezigqugquzela ukusebenza komphakathi sisekelo , abalethi bezidingo , abelaphi bendabuko , amaqembu anake okwenzeka endaweni kanye nosomabhizinisi bendawo . Lowo nalowo othintekayo ubamba iqhaza ohlelweni lwe-CBP . Ukwengeza esifisweni somphakathi kwezombusazwe , inkohlakalo kumele kuliwe nayo ngezindlela ezintathu : ukukhipha inyumbazane , ukuvimbela nokufundisa . Ukukhipha inyumbazane kwenza ukuthi abantu baqonde ukuthi bangabanjwa bajeziswe . Ukuvimbela kumayelana nezinhlelo ( imininingwane , ukucwaninga , njalonjalo ) , okwenza kube nzima ukubamba iqhaza ezenzweni zenkohlakalo . Imikhakha ehlukene yenkohlakalo yomphakathi kudingeka kubhekanwe nayo ngokugxila kokungamagugu , ngokusebenzisa ezemfundo . Ubuthakathaka bezinhlaka eziningana kumele kunqotshwe uma i-Afrika izokwazi ukuguqula ukukhula ngokushesha nokudingeka kakhulu kwezimpahla ekukhuleni kwamathuba emisebenzi namazinga okuphila . Okusemqoka , ukuxhumana okungekuhle kwezinto zokuthutha nezinhlaka zezingqalasizinda , kanjalo nezingqinamba zokutheliswa nokungatheliswa kwempahla , okukhuphula izindleko zokwenza ibhizinisi bese kukhubaza kokubili utshalomali nokuhweba kwangaphakathi . Izikhungo zomthetho ezingasebenzi kahle , futhi kwesinye isikhathi , ukungabinawo kahle amandla okubusa , kukhuphula izinga lobungozi bokutshalwa kwemali . Isithombe siyathuthuka kancane , kodwa izinselelo zilokhu zikhona , kubandakanya nenhlangano yezokuthuthukiswa kwamazwe aseningizimu ne-Afrika , i-Southern African Development Community ( i-SADC ) , ebhekene nezinkinga ezimayelana nengqalasizinda , izingqinamba zokuhweba namandla okubusa . Ngesikhathi iNingizimu Afrika ikuthola kunzima ukuncintisana ekukhiqizeni ngamakhono aphansi ngenxa yohlaka lwezindleko eziphezulu , amazwe amaningi ezwenikazi angancintisana njengoba izindleko zokukhiqiza zikhula eMpumalanga ne-Asia . Izindlela eziyimpumelelo kufanele zihlole ukuthi ukwehluka kungamukelwa futhi kuthathwe njengento ebaluleke kanjani ukuze wonke amalungu omphakathi abandakanywe ngendlela esiza umasipala afeze izinhloso zakhe ekuqinisekiseni ukulethwa kwezidingo okuyimpumelelo ngokubamba iqhaza komphakathi . Kodwa-ke , ukukhuthaza nokwamukela ukwahlukahlukana kungokuzibekela indima , noma ukufunda ukuthatha njengento ebalulekile ukwahluka kwabantu kodwa kudinga ukwakha ukwamukela nokukhuthaza ukubekezelelana kanye nenhlonipho . Funda isifundo sokubonakalayo kwiSahluko 5 , 5.6 ebese nikhombisa eqenjini lenu ukuthi ningabhekana kanjani nesigaba ngasinye . Ababambe iqhaza babheka umdwebo osekhasini 15 obheke isigaba ngasinye senqubo yokuxhumana . Amakomidi Esigceme kufanele enziwe ngamalungu akhethiwe angeqile kwayi-10 amele izimfuno ezahlukahlukene emphakathini . Umkhandlu ngamunye wenza imigomo yokukhetha amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme . Kodwa-ke , amalungu ayakhethwa , ngisho noma kuthiwa ngebhalothi emhlanganweni womphakathi , noma ngokuphakamisa isandla noma ngokuvumelana , kufanele kuvunyelwane nabo bonke ababambe iqhaza futhi imibiko ecacile yenqubo kufanele itholwe yiwo wonke umuntu uma beyidinga . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kufanele abe ngabavoti ababhalisiwe futhi kufanele abe ngabazimisele , abathembekile nabahlonishwa ngumphakathi neqembu elithile alimele . Abagqugquzeli bezigceme - abangathathwa emalungeni aqokiweyo ekomidi lesigceme noma kube ngamalungu ahlonishwayo omphakathi njengamavolontiya abaholi bezenkolo nabaholi abayizibonelo emphakathini , noma kube ngabantu abanolwazi emphakathini njengabantu asebethathe umhlalaphansi , othisha , umholi wabesifazane , njll . Kuzo zonke lezi zinhlobo zabantu kumele kube ngabantu abanomdlandla nabanentshisekelo yokusiza ekwenzeni nasekusebenzeni kwezinhlelo zomphakathi . Emsebenzini olandelayo lokho izinhlobo zabantu ngokwenhlalo ezifisa ukuba kwenzeke kwengezwa ekuhlaziyeni okubizwa nge-SWOT kuzo zonke izinhlobo zabantu ngokwenhlalo , ukwakha isithombe ngokubanzi ngomphakathi . Lokhu kusiza ekuqhakambiseni okusemqoka okufiswayo . Kudingeka isikhathi esingakanani ukuqeda izinhlelo kanye nemikhankaso ezigcemeni zawo ? Imfundo ephakeme . Ukusebenza kwezikhungo ezikhona kusuka ezingeni lomhlaba kuye ezingeni elilingene nje . Ukuthuthuka okuqhubekayo kwezinga kuyadingeka njengoba inqubo yokusebenza ikhula ngesivinini esikahle nje . Inselelo enkulu ukuthi izinga eliphansi lemfundo yasesikoleni kukhulisa izindleko zokukhiqiza abaneziqu zemfundo ephakeme , futhi liphansi izinga labafundi abamnyama abathola iziqu zasemayunivesithi . Izilinganiso zokubamba iqhaza nokuthweswa kweziqu , okunokukhetha iziqu zaseyunivesithi zeminyaka emine , kuhlanganiswa nezifundo zokulungiselela ukungena eyunivesithi noxhaso olwengeziwe lwaseyunivesithi lokusiza abafundi abamnyama ababencishwe amathuba , kungase kube nemiphumela emihle . IKomidi Lesigceme lidinga ukuba nohlelo lonyaka olubeka ngokucacile ukuthi yimiphi imisebenzi yalo ebalulekile nokuthi lilindele ukufezani . Lokhu kuyosiza iKomidi Lesigceme ukubona ukuthi ngabe likufezile yini lokho elathi lizokufeza . Kuyophinda kusize iKomidi Lesigceme ukuthi libike kumasipala , njengoba lingabika inyanga ngayinye ngokuqhathanisa nohlelo lwalo lokusebenza . Uma usebenzisa izinto zokwethula inkulumo njenge-overhead , ishadi , kusebenzise lokhu ukuzilungiselela ngaphambi kwesikhathi . Ukuhlela - Ikomiti Lewadi lisebenzisana nekhansela yewadi ukutomula izidingo bese baqiniseka ukuthi lezo zidingo ziyafakwa kwibhajethi kanye nemisebenzi ehlongoziwe . Ikomiti Lewadi kudingeka ukuba libe ngohlelo wenyaka obonisa ngokucacile ukuthi yini izidingo futhi kufanele zifezwe kanjani . Loku kuzosiza Ikomiti Lewadi ukuhlola ukuthi liphumelele yini ukufeza izinjongo zabo . Izosiza futhi Ikomiti Lewadi uma litshela umasipala , ngoba lingabatshela njalo ngenyanga libheke uhlu labo lokusebenza . Umbono omuhle wokuthi Ikomiti Lewadi lihlelele umhlangano obalulekile ngakuphazima kweso ukuhlela uhlelo lokusebenza lonyaka . Amalungu ekomiti lewadi kufanele benze uhlelo lwabo licace futhi likwazi ukufezeka . Lolu hlelo luyithuluzi elinqumayo ukuthi umphakathi ufisa ukubhekaphi , ekwenzeni iziphakamiso ohlelweni lwe-IDP , ekulandeleni inqubekelaphambili ekusetshenzisweni kohlelo , futhi lungafakelwa ulwazi olusha njalo ngonyaka ngesikhathi izinhlelo ziqhubekela phambili , kuvela nezinto ezintsha ezisemqoka . Ngesikhathi kwenziwa uhlelo , kungaphuculwa nobunikazi ngokunaka ukuthi yiziphi yiziphi izindlela okuqukethwe okungaziswa ngazo amaqembu omphakathi ngokubanzi , okuhlanganisa amaqoqa ezilimi zendawo , izingqwembe nedrama . Lokhu kumele kuxoxwe ngakho emhlanganweni womphakathi wokuphothula . Kusemqoka ukuqikelela ukuthi izinto ezisemqoka ezinjengombono nezinhloso kuhunyushelwa olimini lwabantu endaweni . Ukuguqula umnotho kuphinde kusho ukuguqula izindlela zobunikazi nokulawula . Kuze kube manje , imizamo yokudlulisela ubunikazi bempahla yokukhiqiza ayikakabi nemiphumela edingekayo , kanti izinhlelo zokwabelana kwabaqashwa ngobunikazi bamasheya zibamba iqhaza elingabalulekanga . Indlela eqinile nokuhlosiwe okucacile kuyadingeka . Izinsizakusebenza zenqubomgomo ukukhuthaza umkhakha ozimele ukuthi uguqule izindlela zobunikazi kubandakanya amakhadi okuzithandela okubheka izinga lokwenziwa komsebenzi , imithetho yokuthenga impahla nemisebenzi , ukuhlelwa kwezincwadi zemvume ( okufana nezokuxhumana ngocingo nezimayini ) nezimali zezentuthuko . Amakhono esikhungo abalulekile empumelelweni yale ndlela , okubandakanya izinguquko ukubhekana nobudlelwane obubangwayo phakathi kwezinhlangano zomdabu nezigunyazwa ngumthethosisekelo . Kungabe uhlu lokubheka ukulinganisa ( kanye nokuhlola ) lihlanganisa izidingo zokuhlukaniswa kobulili ezicacile kanye nolwazi lokuhlukaniswa kobulili ? Ukunciphisa izindleko zokuphila emakhaya ahola kancane nabantu abasebenzayo . Ukungalingani nobuphofu kungabhekanwa nakho ngokukhuphula imiholo ngokukhula kwemikhiqizo nokwehlisa izindleko zokuphila . Ukuzibophezela ezingeni elikahle lokuphila kuyoqinisekisa ukuthi wonke amakhaya ayobamba iqhaza ngokuzwakalayo emnothweni . Izindleko zokudla , ezokuthutha nezezindlu kumele zincishiswe ngesikhathi kukhushulwa izinga lemfundo nokunakekelwa kwezempilo kwamahhala noma okubiza kancane . Ikomiti Lewadi lingaqamba ikomiti elincane elilodwa noma amabili bese lifake izinhlangano zomphakathi kulawo makomiti amancane . Bonke abahlanganyeli bewadi kufanele bagqugquzelwe ukuzibandakanya kumakomiti amancane ahambelana nomkhakha waloko abakukhonzile . Indlela esuselwa kulokho okungamandla iyagudluka ekuhleleni okususelwa ezinkingeni , okuyindlela egxile ezihibeni , futhi yona iyindlela egxile embonweni ngokubheka lapho umphakathi ofisa ukuba khona nokuthi uzofinyelela kanjani lapho . Uhlelo Lwezentuthuko Edidiyelwe ( IDP ) luhlonza izinjongo zikamasipala kanti namaphrojekthi azokwenziwa alungiselwa uhlelo . Esikhathini esiningi ngendlela efanayo , uhlelo lwesigceme luyovama ukuhlinzeka ngezidingo zamaphrojekthi akhethwa yiKomidi Lesigceme . Ukuvikelwa komphakathi kuletha empilweni ukusebenzisana komphakathi nokuqinisekisa izinga elisemqoka lokuphila . Kuphinde kubambe iqhaza elisemqoka ukusiza amakhaya nemindeni ilawule izingozi zempilo , nokwenza lula izinguquko zezimakethe , okufaka isandla emnothweni ovulelekile . Ikhansela Lesigceme Z libeke imihlahlandlela yokukhethwa kweKomidi Lesigceme . Umasipala ukhangise emahhovisi omkhandlu , ezikoleni , emasontweni , emakliniki endawo nezinye izindawo zomphakathi mayelana nokuthi iKomidi Lesigceme lizokwakhiwa nokuthi yini iqhaza nomsebenzi walo . Isaziso sichaze epheshananeni lolwazi ukuthi inhlangano noma iqembu ( futhi liwabekile amaqembu ) lingathumela iziphakamiso zamagama kumkhandlu wendawo abazokhethwa . Ipheshana libuye labeka usuku lokhetho , indawo nesikhathi futhi lamema abavoti ababhalisiwe ukuba beze . Emhlanganweni amagama abazokhethwa afundiwe futhi abazokhethwa baphakanyiswe ngamunye emhlanganweni futhi bacelwa ukuba bachaze ukuthi bangobani nokuthi bamele maphi amaqembu . Bekunabazokhethwa aba-28 . Amagama abazokhethwa abhalwe kwiphepha lebhalothi kwase kuthi abasemhlanganweni bacelwa ukuba bavotele aba-10 . Aba-10 bokuqala abathole amavoti amaningi benze iKomidi Lesigceme . Okwesibili , umasipala kumele anqume ngokuthi yimiphi imisebenzi okumele ukuba yelulwe noma yenziwe ngcono . Ingabe zikhona yini ezinye izindawo emphakathini ezingcole kakhulu impela nezingabhekiwe kahle ? Umphathi kamasipala uqokwa ngumkhandlu ngenkontilaka yeminyaka eyisihlanu encike ekusebenzeni . Uyinhloko yokuphathwa komkhandlu futhi ubheka ukuphathwa kwezimali , nokuqashwa nokuyalwa kwabasebenzi . Umphumela waleli zinga ukwemukelwa kwe-IDP kamasipala . Ukulandelela - iKomidi Lesigceme lingacela imibiko yansuku zonke kumaprojekthi kanye nezidingo . Ukuphathwa kwenqubo yezemfundo . Ukunciphisa amazinga abaphathi kuyokwenza ukuthi izisetshenziswa zibe khona ukusekela izikole nothisha . Umthetho osemqoka ovamile ukuthi ukungenelela , ngokuxhasa nokulungisa , kudingeka uphikisane nesilinganiso sokusebenza kwesikole . Ngaleyo ndlela , izikole ezisebenza kangcono zinganikezwa inkululeko yokuqhubeka nomsebenzi , kuphela nje uma kuzoba nendlela yokulinganisa ukukhula kokwenziwa komsebenzi . Senza izincomo ezikhethekile ezigxile ekusekelweni kangcono kwezikole , ukulethwa kwezidingo ezisemqoka zemfundo enhle nokulinganisa izinto eziyizo . Sihlongoza umkhankaso wokuthuthukisa ingqalasizinda ezikoleni ezimpofu , ikakhulukazi ezindaweni ezisemakhaya . Ekupheleni kwalo mhlangano umphakathi uzoba nombono okuxoxwe kwavunyelwana ngawo wokuthuthukisa umphakathi . OHulumeni Bendawo : UMthetho Wokuphathwa Kwezimali Zomasipala , ka-2003 ( MFMA ) uncike kuMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala ( MSA ) , ka-2000 njengoba yomibili le mithetho ikhuluma ngezinhlelo zangaphakathi kuhulumeni wasekhaya ; izinqubo zokuxhumana ; izinhlelo zokusebenza nezindlela zokuthuthukisa ukuzinikela . I-MFMA ichaza ukuthi zisebenza kanjani izinhlelo zemali yomasipala nokuthi yiliphi iqhaza lamakhansela lokwenza ukuthi lokhu kusebenze . Khombisa uzwelo nenhlonipho komunye , ngaphandle kokubheka inkolo yakhe , amagama noma indlela yokuziphatha . Kunokusemqoka okulahlekayo okumele kunakwe uma kukhishwa okumbiwa phansi okunenzuzo . INingizimu Afrika ilahlekelwa ngamasheya ezimakethe zomhlaba okufanekisa efana ne-ferrochrome . yokuvela , isigaba sokuqala sokwenza noma sokuncibilikisa sisebenzisa amandla nemali eningi , sithatha amandla nemali kweminye imikhakha . INingizimu Afrika kumele ikhethe mayelana nezindawo okuguquka ukuzisekela kuzo esigabeni sokuqala . Izindawo okumele zibhekelelwe kuqala kumele zibandakanye lapho kunomthamo ofanele , lapho inzuzo ivame ukuholela Okuhlangabezane kwezimboni . Ukuguqulwa kwazo zonke izimbiwa zezwe zibe okuhola kusemqoka ekukhuliseni umkhakha wezimboni . Luvume futhi ulwamukele ulaka lwakho . Cabanga ngalo . Ungakwali ubukhona bolaka noma wenqabe ukubhekana nalo . Uma wenza lokhu , lungavese luvele ngesikhathi esingafanele futhi luphumele kwabanye abantu olungaqondene nabo . Ukuhlaziywa kwesabiwomali esiqondene nokuphendula ngobulili kubhekiswe ekuhlaziyweni kwezindleko zikahulumeni kanye nasezimalini eziqoqwayo kubantu besifazane kanye namantombazane kuqhathaniswa nabesilisa kanye nabafana . Izabiwomali zobulili akuzona izabiwomali ezihlukile zabesifazane kuphela futhi azihlosile kuphela ukwandisa izimali ezichithwa ezinhlelweni eziqondene nabantu besifazane kuphela . Ezikwenzayo nje ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izidingo zabesifazane ziyabandakanywa futhi ziyahlinzekelwa . Lolu wuhlelo lwaseNingizimu Afrika . Luhlinzeka ngohlaka lwamasu asemqoka ngenhloso yokuhlahla indlela yokukhetha nokwenza izinto okusemqoka . Ukuphumelela kwalo kuyoncika kubo bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika abazibophezelayo kulolu hlelo , oluholwa uMongameli neKhabhinethi . IKomidi Lesigceme limela okufunwayo okuyingxubevange okuhlanganisa izikhungo zabantukazana noma zabakhokhi bentela , izinhlangano zentuthuko , izinyunyana zabasebenzi , izinhlangano zosomabhizinisi , amaqembu abantu besifazane , intsha kanye nezinhlangano ezigxile kwezenkolo . Ukuphathwa kwephrojekthi kubandakanya ukulawulwa kokusetshenziswa kohlelo , kufaka phakathi ukuhlaziya ukuthi izinto ziqhubeka kanjani nokubukeza izinhlelo ezibhekelele izinselelo noma izinguquko zesimo ezingenzeka ngokuqhubeka kokwenzeka kwezinto . EGibhithe endala , abesilisa babehlala ekhaya bathunge . Abesifazane babephatha amabhizinisi omndeni . Abesifazane babethola impahla njengefa abesilisa bengatholi lutho . Amakhasi okucatshangwayo ngephrojekthi ' wumsebenzi wephepha ' odinga ukulungiselelwa wethulwe emkhandlwini noma eminyangweni yemikhakha ngokwehlukana kwayo . Angamarekhodi alokho okuvunyelwene ngakho ukuze bonke abathintekayo bakwazi ukulandela inqubekelaphambili . Imisuka engadala ingxabano ezigcemeni zababambe iqhaza . Ukusungula umthetho omusha nohlaka lukazwelonke lwezindawo . Ukuhlanganyela nezinhlangano zendawo ezifana nezinhlangano ezingezona ezikahulumeni , izinhlangano ezesekwe phezu kwenkolo zinganikeza indawo yokudingida izindaba kanye nolwazi oluzonikezwa luphinde luthathwe emphakathini . Umsebenzi 2 Hlonza imigomo ebalulekile yokubamba iqhaza komphakathi . UMBUZO 2 Ungazixazulula kanjani izinkinga zokulethwa kwemisebenzi ? Amathuluzi enza i-LFA angasetshenziswa ukubulala noma ukuhliphiza iphrojekthi ehlongozwayo , ukuqhubeka nokuhlola ukuqondana nokwenzeka kwayo . Esimweni seKomidi Lesigceme abadlalindima bengakhuthaza inqubomgomo ebonakalayo yokufakwa kobulili kuzo zonke izinqubomgomo kanye nezinhlelo , ukuze ngaphambi kokuba izinqumo zithathwe kuhlazinywe umthelela wazo kwabesifazane nabesilisa . I-PCM izinze kumjikelezo wephrojekthi futhi iphinde ibhekelele zonke izingxenye zephrojekthi ngaso sonke isikhathi sokuqhubeka kwephrojekthi . Lokhu kusho ukuthi noma yiziphi izinguquko noma izinselelo zifakiwe esakhiweni nasohlelweni lwesinyathelo esilandelayo . Kwi-LFA kwesinye isikhathi izinkomba zibizwa ngokuthi ' yizinkomba eziqinisekiswa ngokungachemi ' . Yingenxa yokuthi noma ubani kumele akwazi ukulinganisa ' ngokungachemi ' izinkomba bese ethola umphumela ofanayo , akusho lutho ukuthi umuntu obezilinganisa ucabanga kanjani . Ubhubhane lwe-HIV / AIDS selukhombise ukukwazi kweNingizimu Afrika ukwenza amaphutha amakhulu kwezenhlalakahle nakwezombusazwe - kanjalo nokukwazi kwayo ukuwalungisa nokusebenzisa uhlelo olunzima ngempumelelo . Impumelelo yenqubo yezempilo ekulawuleni lolu bhubhane esikhathini esiyiminyaka emihlanu eyedlule iyancomeka . Kodwa-ke akukho ukweneliseka . Kunesidingo esiqhubekayo sokufundisa , ukuvimbela , ukuhlola nokwelapha . Ukwehlisa izinga labatheleleka kabusha kuyokwehlisa izidingo enqubweni yezempilo yomphakathi . Yize bengekho abasha abathelelekayo , sisazolokhu sisikhulu isibalo sabantu abaphila ne-HIV abadinga imishanguzo , okwenza ukuthi kube nenselelo eqhubekayo ezingeni lokutheleleka yisifo sofuba kanye nengozi yokuvela kwenkinga yokungezweli kwemishanguzo ye-HIV . Lolu bhubhane nomthelela walo kwinqubomgomo kahulumeni kuvama ukuthi kuhlale okungenani kuze kufike esinye isizukulwane - kokunye ezimbili . Inqubo kufanele kuvunyelwane ngayo yibo bonke abathintekayo futhi amarekhodi enqubo abhalwe ngokucacile kumele umphakathi ukwazi ukuwathola ukuze uwacwaninge . Ubulili buphenduka igama eliphethe zonke izingxenye zempilo . Umqondo wobulili obulinganayo awunqundi ukubandakanywa kwabesilisa ; kunalokho uvumela umsebenzi ongcono nozinzile phakathi kwabesilisa kanye nabesifazane , nokuzogcina ekulawulweni emiphumeleni engcono yokulondoloza . Izindlela zokulungisa okungalungile emsebenzini kumele zigxile ekuthuthukisweni kwamabhizinisi , ukutholakala kokuqeqeshwa , ukukhuphuka ngokomsebenzi nokuba nabafundisa imisebenzi emsebenzini . UMbiko Wohlelo Ngohulumeni Wendawo wuhlaka lokuqala lwenqubomgomo kazwelonke kahulumeni wendawo emva kokuphela kobandlululo . UMbiko Wohlelo Lokuzokwenziwa uveza isidingo sokuthi uhulumeni wendawo alungiselelwe abheke ngasentuthukweni . Ubeka phambili umbono weqhaza lokuthuthuka kukahulumeni wendawo . Izinhlangano ezisebenzela imiphakathini ukuthuthukisa kanye nokusimamisa abantu kumele zithathele phezulu udaba lobulili . Izishoshovu zentuthuko eziningi zibona ' abantu ' njengeqembu abahlose ukulisiza bese zingazami ukuqonda amaqiniso ahlukene ezimpilo zabesilisa kanye nabesifazane . Ngisho ezimweni lapho abesifazane uthola ukuthi bakhonjwe njengeqembu elisemqoka okumele lisizwe , uhlaziyo olufanele aluvamisile ukwenziwa ngomthelela iprojekthi noma inqubomgomo ezoba nawo ezimpilweni zabesifazane . Ngaso leso sikhathi , izinhlangano ziyahluleka ukuthola imibono kanye nezimvo zabesifazane kumaprojekthi anomthelela oqonde ngqo ezimpilweni zabo . Umhlangano wokulungiselela ukuhlela kumelele ubanjwe kusasele isonto noma amabili ngaphambi kwesonto elisemqoka lokuhlela . Abaholi kumele bahlanganiswe bathathwe ezigabeni ezehlukene zomphakathi ukulungiselela isonto lokuhlela nokukhuthaza ubunikazi bomphakathi nomsebenzi wawo ekwenziweni kwenqubo . Iqoqa elilapha ngezansi lethula izimpawu ezisemqoka zomhlangano wokulungiselela ukuhlela nenqubo yakhona . Sungula isimo sokulalela esiqhelile emisindweni lapho abantu begxilile khona kokukodwa futhi bengakwazi ukulalela ngokucophelela . Ukuphathwa kwephrojekthi kusebenzisa ithuluzi eliwusizo kwababambe iqhaza ukuthi bazuze ukuqonda okujulile kwezidingo zabo ezisemqoka nokuqonda imiphumela yenkinga . Ngokwenza isihlahla sezinkinga zonke izimbangela nemiphumela yenkinga kungabhekisiswa . Ukuchema imibono eyakhiwe noma ukuchema , okuphindwe kuchazwe njengomqondo ongemuhle , imicabango engemihle ngelungelo lomuntu noma abantu . IKomidi Lesigceme lizilandelele zombili lezi zindaba nekomidi lokuqondisa futhi emva kwezinyanga ezi-3 amalambu emgwaqeni afakiwe futhi iKomidi Lesigceme lisebenze ne-Community Policing Forum ukugada endaweni . Abantu babamba iqhaza ngokuzithathela izinyathelo zokuthola izinsiza nolwazi ngezobuchwepheshe , kodwa bese kuba yibona abalawula indlela yokusebenzisa izinsiza . Zikhona yini izindawo zamanzi ezingaba semqoka kwezobudlelwano bokuphilayo , kwezokongiwa kwemvelo noma kwezokungcebeleka , isibonelo amaxhaphozi , amachibi , izizalo zomfula , amadamu , imifula ? Kusemqoka ukukhumbula ukuthi ama-KPI abhekene namayunithi okuhambisa omasipala kanye nabasebenzi , kanye nayiphina inhlangano kamasipala nomnikezeli wensizakalo loyo umasipala anesivumelwano naye sokwethula insizakalo . I-Luckytown yidolobha elincane elise-Eastern Cape ( noma kwesinye isifundazwe ) . Engxenyeni eyodwa yaleli dolobha abantu bahlala ezindlini ezakhiwe kahle ezizeni ezinkulu . Abanye babo banamapitsi abo kanti kwezinye zalezi ziza abanikazi bazo batshale imifino nemithi yezithelo . Ngaphambi kowe-1994 le ngxenye yaleli dolobha yayihlala abantu abamhlophe kuphela , emva kwalokho kwase kuthutheleka kuyo imindeni eyingcosana eqhamuka emalokishini emikhiqizweni . Ukubumbana komphakathi kudinga ukuqinisa isu . Uma iNingizimu Afrika ikhombisa inqubekela phambili ekuqedeni ubunikazi bohlanga oluthile nokulawulwa komnotho ngaphandle kokunciphisa ubuphofu nokungalingani , inguquko iyobonakala . Ngokufanayo , uma ubuphofu nokungalingani kuncishiswa ngaphandle koguquko olubonakalayo lwendlela yobunikazi , inqubekela phambili yezwe iyoba senkingeni futhi ibe buthakathaka . Uhlelo lokubili lwamawadi kanye nokumelwa okulinganayo kusho ukuthi imiphakathi bangakhetha ngqo abameli abozoboshelelwa kubo , ukuhambisa nokulungisa izikhala zabo . Ukuqapha nokulinganisa ukusebenza kokulethwa kwezidingo yinqubo ehlola inqubekelaphambili ekunyeleleni kulezo zinjongo ezibekwe ngaphambili futhi kuyadingeka ukuba kwenziwe kulolo nakulolo phiko olukhulu lwevoti yesabelomali ngokuhambisana nesigaba sama-27(4) se-PFMA . Lokho okuqondwe ukuzuzwa ngokusebenza kwenziwa ngenhloso yemisebenzi elungele imali yayo , eyenziwa ngamakhono kanye nempumelelo jikelele yezilinganiso zokulethwa kwemisebenzi . Inqubo yokuhlola inqubekelaphambili ingasetshenziswa njengethuluzi lokuzihlola , lokubeka izinjongo , lokuqapha inqubekelaphambili kanye nokuxhumana namakhasimende angaphandle . UMSEBENZI 1 Hlonza abadlalindima abehlukahlukene kanye nemisebenzi yabo mayelana nohlelo lwemisebenzi . Ukubamba iqhaza kunika amandla uma abantu benza izinqumo ngokwabo futhi bezikhethela . Ukubamba iqhaza ngokuphelele kwabantu abahlomulayo , okuyimiphakathi ebukelwa phansi , izinhlangano zabesifazane , amaqembu entsha , izinhlangano zemiphakathi , abahlali njll . kubalulekile ekuhleleni . Ukuhlela intuthuko ngokudidiyela yindlela efaka phakathi wonke umasipala nezakhamizi ekutholeni izisombululo ezifanele ekufinyeleliseni intuthuko yesikhathi eside eyimpumelelo . I-IDP yithuluzi elibalulekile lokusebenzisa izinsizakusebenza ezikhona ukuhlangabezana nezidingo ezahlukahlukene endaweni . Isiza umasipala ukubheka izidingo zemikhakha eyehlukene - njengezempilo , amanzi , ukuphepha komphakathi , uhwebo - nokuthi ungaphendula kanjani kuzo ngendlela yokubambisana . Hlola imisebenzi yohlelo lwe-CBP ngokuyiqhathanisa nephakanyiswe ohlelweni lwe-IDP ukuthola ukuthi kukhona yini ukuphindaphindeka kwemisebenzi . Ngisho noma ngabe akukho , kungenzeka noma kube yinto efanele ukucela ngqo ukuxhaswa ngezimali . Buyekeza ozokusho kusenesikhathi - umndeni noma abangani bakho noma osebenza nabo bangabantu ongabasebenzisa ukuzilungiselela ngabo . Hlelela ukuvele kuhanjwe esigcemeni , okuhlanganisa izinto ezisemqoka zendawo . Ngesikhathi kuhanjwa , qaphelani izinto ezisemqoka nokuthi zitholakalaphi . Kuyasiza ukuthatha lolu lwazi lufakwe lulandelane lube yisithombe esigqamisa izinto zendawo noma izinto zezentuthuko kuleyo naleyo ndawo , kuhlinzekwe ngokubanzi isimo sewadi njengoba isibonelo sibonisa lapha ngezansi . Sebenzisa amaphuzu okuhlola ezemvelo ukuqinisekisa ukuthi zonke izinto zifakiwe . Indlela yokusebenza kothisha . Izihlongozo zethu ngoqeqesho , amaholo , imihlomulo , isikhathi besemsebenzini , izilinganiso zokwenziwa komsebenzi , nokusekelwa ngokuqukethwe nokwezokufundisa . Ukusebenza kahle nemibandela ekhulisa indlela enhle yokwenza umsebenzi kumele kuphinde kwenziwe , ukukwazi ukuphendula ngendlela yomsebenzi kumele kukhuliswe . Lokhu kusho ukuthi kudingeka kuqiniswe ukuthuthukiswa kwezobuchwepheshe , ukubuyekezwa kontanga , ingqalasizinda yesikole , ukuhlinzekwa kwezinto zokuxhasa abafundi nenqubo yokusekela othisha . Othisha , kuwo womabili amazinga omuntu ngomuntu nelesikole , kumele bakwazi ukuziphendulela ngokusebenza kwabafundi , ngokubhekelela indawo yokufunda . Lo mfanekiso olandelayo ukhombisa umkhakha ngamunye wemiphumela yokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ekuhlolweni kabusha kwemisebenzi nokuthi umjikelezo awukho kanjani esimeni esilandelana kahle . I-Masincedane Development Corporation yasungulwa njengenkampani engaphansi Kwesigaba sama-21 . Kwakuhloswe ngayo ukuqokelela imali nokulawulwa kokuxhaswa kanye nokusebenza kwezindlela ze-LED . Okwalandela izinkundla zokucobelelana ngolwazi , umphakathi wahlonza izindlela ezibambekayo uMasincedane okumele ukuba asebenze ngazo . Lelo nalelo lungu lomphakathi likhululekile ukubeka lezi zingxenye ezintathu ziqondane nokufiswayo okukodwa noma okungaphezu kokukodwa . Umongo Womthethosisekelo Ngumthethosivivinywa Wamalungelo . Umthethosivivinywa Wamalungelo usekela amalungelo abo bonke abahlali nezakhamizi ukuba baphathwe ngokulinganayo nangenhlonipho kungabhekwanga ubuhlanga , ubulili , ubucebi noma isikhundla . Idlanzana lamalungelo ezomnotho nenhlalakahle kufakwe ngaphakathi lomthethosivivinywa Wamalungelo , okufana nelungelo lokuhlala endaweni enempilo , ukuba nokwazi ukufinyelela izindlu ezanele , ukwazi ukufinyelela kwizinsizakalo zokunakekelwa zezempilo kanye nokudla namanzi anele . Kungumsebenzi kahulumeni wendawo kanye neminye imikhakha kahulumeni , ' ukuhlonipha , ukuvikela , ukuthuthukisa nokufeza ' lawa malungelo . I-CBP ukubambisana phakathi komphakathi , umasipala kanye namakhansela . Abagqugquzeli bohlelo lwe-CBP kumele basebenze bahlele nekhansela kuleso naleso sinyathelo senqubo . Uma iNyuvesi yaseTshwane inquma ukunikeza imifundaze lapho abafundi abasuka eMpumalanga Kapa kanye nase-Gauteng bengancintisana khona , ukungalingani ngeke kubeke ethubeni abafundi abaqhamuka eMpumalanga Kapa . Isibonelo , akubona bonke abakhuluma isiNgisi esifanayo , noma abafinyelela kuzindlela ezifanayo zokuxhumana . Yini ubambiswano ngemisebenzi kamasipala ? OHulumeni Bendawo : UMthetho Wentela Yempahla Kamasipala , ka-2004 unikeza imininingwane ngendlela yokubizwa kwentela yempahla ngomasipala bonke futhi lokhu kuthinta yonke impahla ebingangeni ngaphansi kukamasipala ngesikhathi esedlule . Kubalulekile ukuba amaKomidi Ezigceme azi ukuthi angayithola kuphi le miningwane njengoba intela yempahla kuyinkinga evame ukuphakanyiswa abahlali . Iningi lemisebenzi ehlonzwe ohlelweni lwe-CBP izokwethulwa ngamakomidi ezigceme , kodwa eminye yayo ingadinga kakhulu izinsiza zangaphandle noma kube nesidingo sokuba yenziwe ngempumelelo wumasipala . Lokhu kungabandakanya ukuthi ngubani okumele abe ngumbheki wohlelo nokuthi izinsiza zihlanganiswa kanjani ekwethulweni kwalo . Uma selwethuliwe lwaqala ukusebenza uhlelo , kuba semqoka ukuba lulandelwe , lulinganiswe bese lubuyekezwa . Izinhlelo kumele zibuyekezwe kulowo nalowo mhlangano wekomidi lesigceme kanti emhlanganweni womphakathi lubuyekezwa njalo ngenyanga kuya ezinyangeni ezimbili kanye nesigceme / nesifunda / nomasipala . Amakomidi ezigceme kumele abike ngenqubekelaphambili esiyenzekile , asho nezinkinga ezigqamile ezibe khona . Le mibiko kumele ihlanganise nezezimali inikeze imininingwane yezimali ezisetshenzisiwe . Umkhandlu kumele ukuba uzamukele lezi zabelomali ngaphambi kokuqala konyaka wezimali sebemukele , emva kokuhlela nokuxoxisana okulungile Namakomidi Ezigceme kanye namanye amaqembu okubanjiswene nawo kuleyo ndawo . Amakomidi Ezigceme abalulekile ekuhambiseni isabelomali kumphakathi kanye nempendulo yomphakathi eya kumasipala . Uma Amakomidi Esigceme angaba neqhaza ekuthathweni kwesinqumo sokuthi yimalini okumele ukuba umasipala ayichithe kanye nokuthi yimalini okumele ichithwe kumaphi amaphrojethi , lokhu kungasho ukuthi isigceme sawo singasizakala ngqo . Kulindelekile ukuthi ukukhula komnotho womhlaba eshumini leminyaka elizayo kwehle kunalokhu okwakuyikho ngesikhathi sangaphambilini . Lokhu kuyodinga ukugxila kakhulu kwinqubomgomo , kugxilwe nasekusetshenzisweni ngempumelelo kwemigomo yezezimboni nasekwenziweni ngcono kokuthuthukiswa kwamakhono . Ukuphila kahle kusemqoka empilweni enenzuzo negcwele . Umbiko ohlaziyayo ukhomba izinselelo ezihlobene ezisobala ezivezwa yinqubo yokusebenza kwezempilo engasebenzi kahle nokukhula komthwalo wezifo . Inqubo kahulumeni yokusebenza kwezempilo yaseNingizimu Afrika ephukile kumele ilungiswe . Ngesikhathi ukusetshenziswa kakhulu ukunakekela okuzimele , okukhokhelwa okungaba abasebenzisi noma umshuwalense wezempilo , kuyingxenye yesisombululo , akusikhona okungena endaweni yokuthuthukiswa kokunakekelwa kwezempilo yomphakathi . Umzamo osuka phansi uye phezulu wokuthuthukisa ukunakekela okusezingeni eliphezulu uyadingeka , ikakhulukazi ezingeni eliphansi . Aqinisekisa ukuthi lokho okukhathaza umphakathi kuyalalelwa . Umsebenzi weKomidi Lesigceme ukuqinisekisa ukuthi labo ababhekene nezinhlelo zephrojekthi babandakanya umphakathi futhi bayaqinisekisa ukuthi umphakathi ubamba iqhaza ngokugcwele kwiphrojekthi . Ukuqonda Nokuhlolisisa - inhloso yalesi sinyathelo ukwenza ithuba lazo zonke izinhlangothi lokuba ' ziziwe ' futhi zivunyelwe ukubeka udaba lwazo . Lolo nalolo hlangothi / umuntu lunethuba lokuchaza isimo salo . Emva kokuba lolo nalolo hlangothi seluchaze isimo salo umlamuli uqoqela ndawonye amaphuzu futhi aqinisekisa nezinhlangothi ukuthi ukuzwile lokho ezikushilo . Izinhlangothi ziyavumelana ngezindaba okufanele zisonjululwe futhi zenza isimo esihle sokuxazulula inkinga . Lokhu kungadinga ukuba abagqugquzeli bohlelo lwe-CBP babambe imihlangano embalwa nomasipala kusenesikhathi ukuvumelana nokuxoxa ngemininingwane engenhla . Ungobani umphakathi wethu futhi baziphilisa ngani ? ' Abagqugquzeli ' kumele bathole lolu lwazi eqenjini labo bese beluloba phansi . Iqembu kumele lichaze iqembu lalo , ngokunaka isibalo sabantu eqenjini , uma beqashiwe baqashwe ngubani , uma bengaqashiwe bangaki abangaqashiwe , isizwe iqembu elivela kuso . IMISHINI KAHULUMENI : ' ukwakha izinsizakalo zomphakathi eziqhutshwa ngabantu nezesekwe ebantwini , ezinezimpawu zokulingana , izinga elifanele , ebakazayo kanye nekhodi yezimilo eqinile , ukwenza okuhle kakhulu kwezinhlangano kanye nokwethulwa kwezinsizakalo okusezingeni eliphezulu ' . Izakhamuzi zinomsebenzi wokungabakhuthazi abaholi ukuthi bathathe izikhundla ezingabakhathalele abanye abantu , ezihambisana nokuthandwa kwabo . Ukuxoxisana komphakathi okuqinile nesiko lokwethula izikhalo ngokuthula kuyoba nomthelela ekuqondeni ngokujulile izinselelo ezibhekene nemiphakathi nokufaka ukuzibophezela phakathi kwezikhulu ezikhethiwe . Isibonelo , uma imiphumela yokufunda esikoleni ingaphansi kwalokho okulindelekile , umphakathi ungasiza ukwelapha isimo ngokuqinisa ukubuswa kwesikole , ukuqinisekisa ukuthi abafundi nothisha bafika ngesikhathi esikoleni nokuthi izinhlaka zokusekela ezivela ezikhulwini zomphakathi ziyaphumelela . Enze izimpilo zabesifazane zibe ngcono . Imisebenzi yabo yokunakekela ibanikeza umthwalo owengeziwe omkhulu . Ngokucubungula izinhlelo ezibhekene nokunakekela izingane , ukutholakala kwezikhungo zezempilo , ukuthola amanzi kanye nogesi kanye nezinto zokuthutha umphakathi ezanele , umthwalo womsebenzi wokunakekela umndeni kanye nomuzi ungancipha kancane . Umsebenzi 3 Bheka uMthethosisekelo , bese uhlonza iqhaza kanye nomsebenzi kahulumeni kazwelonke . Ukuthuthukisa ukusetshenziswa kahle kwamandla ezimayini nokuguqulwa kokumbiwa phansi ngamaphesenti ayi-15 ngonyaka wezi-2030 . Lokhu kungabandakanya ukuvalwa kwezindawo ezikhiqiza ugesi ezingasebenzi kahle . Ababambe iqhaza badwebela amazwi asemqoka kuleso naleso sitatimende , isibonelo . imali engcono engenayo - kungaba ' imali engenayo ' , kwezobugebengu kungaba ' ukuphepha nokuvikeleka ' bese ukubhala kwifliphushadi . Ukuhlela kabusha amadolobha , nezindawo zasemakhaya zaseNingizimu Afrika umsebenzi onzima futhi wesikhathi eside , odinga izinguquko ezinkulu nokufiswa umphakathi . Lokhu kuwumsebenzi odingekayo yize kunezinkinga zezindleko ngokwenhlalo , ngokwezindawo nangokwezimali ezenziwa ukwehlukana kwezindawo okukhona . Ukuphepha nokulondolozeka komphakathi kudinga ukuhlanganyela namandla okuphepha endawo / amaphoyisa futhi kweyeme emphakathini ukuthi usizane ukuxazulula izinkinga zokuphepha bese yakha ukuphepha kwamalungu omphakathi . Ukulawulwa kokusebenza kuncikene kakhulu nokulethwa kwemisebenzi , kokubili kuchazwa ngezamasu ohlelo lweqhinga le - Batho Pele olwasungulwa ngonyaka we-1997 . Empeleni , abantu abasha badinga amathuba angcono kwezemfundo nezomnotho , futhi kudingeka imizamo eqondile yokulwa nokungalingani ngokobulili . Ukuthuthukisa ukulingana ngokobulili namathuba amahle abantu abasha yizindikimba ezihlanganisiwe zalo lonke lolu hlelo . Osopolitiki baqinisekisa ukulandelwa nokusebenza kwezinhlelo futhi ukuzibophezela kwabo kusemqoka kule nqubo . Ngakho-ke ukubandakanyeka kwabo kusemqoka . UMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala ugxile ezinhlelweni zangaphakathi kanye nokuphathwa kukamasipala . Kungani kubalulekile ukuthi amaKomidi Ezigceme aqonde futhi asebenzise lolu hlelo ? YILOWO NALOWO MASIPALA KUDINGEKA NGOKOMTHETHO ENZE UHLELO LOKULAWULWA KOKUSEBENZA ( PERFORMANCE MANAGEMENT SYSTEM ) ( I-PMS ) EZOKWENZA NGCONO UKUSEBENZA KWENHLANGANO NGEKHONO NANGEMPUMELELO , UKUZIBOPHEZELELA EKUSETSHENZISWENI KWEZINSIZAKUSEBENZA FUTHI LUKHOMBISE UKUZUZA IMPUMELELO . I-PMS IYAKWAZI UKUBA YINDLELA YOKUXWAYISA NGAPHAMBILI NJENGOBA IKHOMBISA UKUNGASEBENZI KAHLE NOMA UKUSEBENZA OKUNGAPHANSI KWEZINGA , OKWENZA UKUBA KUBE KHONA UKUNGENELELA MAYELANA NOKWENZA NGCONO . Bonke omasipala kudingeka ukuba balungiselele uHlelo Lwentuthuko Edidiyelwe ( IDP ) . UHlelo Lwentuthuko Edidiyelwe luveza obala izidingongqangi zaleyo ndawo . UHlelo Lwentuthuko Edidiyelwe lubekelwe isikhathi esiyiminyaka emihlanu kanti luyabuyekezwa njalo ngonyaka . UMthetho Wohlaka Lokusebenzisana Kohulumeni , ka-2005 wenzelwe ukuthuthukisa nokugqugquzela ukuthathwa kwezinqumo ngokubambisana phakathi kwezakhiwo ezintathu zikahulumeni ukuze izinqubomgomo nemisebenzi kuzo zonke izakhiwo ikhuthaze ukuhlinzekwa ngezinsizakalo nokuthola izindlela zokuhlangabezana nezidingo zomphakathi ngendlela efanele . Imikhakha emithathu kahulumeni inesibopho soMthethosisekelo sokubambisana nokuxoxa ngezindlela zokuvumelana ngezindaba zokuphatha , zepolotiki nezezimali . Bheka ibhukwana elithi Working Together for Development . Nikeza izizathu zokuhlela imisebenzi ngendlela owenze ngayo bese ukhombisa lokhu efomini leshedula , ibhashadi noma ngokunikeza izibonelo . Ukuthuthukiswa kwezokuthuthwa kwempahla ukusuka eThekwini kuya eGauteng , kubandakanya nesikhumulo esisha semikhumbi esimbiwe endaweni yesikhumulo sezindiza esidala saseThekwini . Uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini ludinga ukubandakanywa kwabo bonke abathintekile ekuhleleni . Yize ukubandakanywa komphakathi kungeke kwenzeka ngokupheleleyo , kusemqoka ukuqinisekisa ukuthi wonke amaqembu asemqoka nalawo angaba wusizo ayabandakanywa . Ukubamba iqhaza akufanele kube yindaba yabaholi bendawo noma labo abavamise ukuhambela noma ukuqhuba imihlangano yomphakathi kuphela . Uhlelo lwe-CBP lusho ukuthi kumele kwenziwe umzamo wokufinyelela nakulabo abangakukhuthalele ukubamba iqhaza . Kudinga isikhathi , ukuzikhandla nokuzibophezela . Uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini kumele luholele ekwenzeni okubandakanya imiphakathi qobo lwayo , ibambisene nawomasipala . Umsebenzi 2Bheka uMthethosisekelo , bese uhlonza iqhaza kanye nomsebenzi kahulumeni wesifundazwe kanye nobudlelwano bakhe nohulumeni wendawo . Ukushicilelwa kanye nokusatshalaliswa kwemiphumela yocwaningo kumele ukuba kuhlelwe kahle kusukela ezingeni lokuhlela iphrojekthi . Isahluko sibheka okulindelekile kwi-PMS futhi sichaza Izinkomba Ezisemqoka Zokusebenza ( KPI ) , nokuthi zenziwa futhi zisetshenziswe kanjani nokuthi ungakuhlola futhi ukukale kanjani ukusetshenziswa kwazo . Sibuye sixoxe ngeqhaza elibalulekile elibanjwa ngumphakathi , kanjalo namaKomidi Ezigceme , ekubuyekezweni kokusebenza nenqubo yokuhlola ukusebenza . Kunezinhlobo eziningi ezahlukahlukene zokulawulwa kweprojekthi ezisetshenziswa emkhakheni wezentuthulo . Lezi zinhlobo zingahluka kulezo ezisetshenziswa ezinkampanini ezizimele . Esimweni saseNingizimu Afrika ayikho indlela eyodwa kuphela yomkhakha kahulumeni engasetshenziswa , futhi kunomehluko phakathi kwezindlela ezisetshenziswa yiminyango kahulumeni eyahlukahlukene . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kufanele azi ngokulawulwa kwempilo noma umjikelezo weprojekthi njengoba lena kuyindlela evamise ukusetshenziswa . Ukuhlukaniswa kanye namagama amabanga noma ezigaba zempilo / umjikelezo weprojekthi kungahluka kuncike enhlanganweni eseka ngemali noma umnyango kahulumeni . Khetha indlela engcono yokubanikeza ulwazi . Ungafisa ukuyibhala phansi eshadini , noma unike abasemhlanganweni amakhophi amaphuzu abalulekile . Umkhandlu wendawo ungasiza ekwenzeni amakhophi . Kulesi sahluko sibheka indlela eyejwayele ukusetshenziswa , indlela yokuxazulula inkinga . UMSEBENZI 1 Amakomidi Ezigceme angaba namthelela muni kuHlelo Lwentuthuko ? lesi SAHLUKO SIZONAMATHELA KAKHULU EKUTHENI AMAPHROJEKTHI AHLONZWA KANJANI ngaphakathi kukamasipala noma iKomidi Lesigceme . Siyoba nomphumela wokuvumelana nokuqhubeka nephrojekthi , noma kungatholakala ukuthi eqinisweni iphrojekthi ingenzeke ayikholakali futhi akumele yenziwe . Ukuhlonzwa kwephrojekhi , ucwaningo ngempumelelo yayo , ukuhlaziywa kwezinkinga nababambe iqhaza konke kuyizimpawu zalesi sigaba . Ababambiqhaza babeka imidwebo kanye namaphosta abo odongeni lwekilasi . Mema ababambiqhaza ukuba bazobuka amashadi namaphosta amanye amaqembu . Khetha umdwebo owodwa kumidwebo bese umema lelo qembu ukuba lichazele amanye amaqembu ngesikhathi amaqembu esehlangene wonke . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angasebenzisa lesi sibonelo ukusiza ukukala ukusebenza kukamasipala wawo . Ukubamba komphakathi iqhaza yingxenye ebalulekile yanoma yiyiphi intando yeningi . Lokhu kuvela kuMthethosisekelo , Isigaba 152 esithi umphakathi kufanele ubambe iqhaza ezindabeni zikahulumeni wasekhaya , esigcizelela ukuthi enye yezinhloso zikahulumeni wasekhaya " ukugqugquzela ukufakwa kwemiphakathi nezinhlangano zemiphakathi ezindabeni zikahulumeni wasekhaya " . Inqubo ye-CBP kuyo yonke indawo kamasipala kumele ukuba yenziwe ngaphambi kokwenziwa kwezinyathelo zokuqala zenqubo yokuhlela neyokubuyekeza i-IDP . UMthetho Wokuklanywa Kwemingcele Yomasipala , ka-1998 uveza izinqubo nezindlela zokwenza imingcele yomasipala . IBhodi Yokuklanywa Kwemingcele iyinhlangano ezimele ebekelwe ukwenza lo msebenzi . Uma lenza imingcele iBhodi libheka izinto eziningi kuhlanganisa nesimo sezimali sendawo , ukuhlanganisa izinhlanga ezahlukahlukene nokuhambisana nezingxenye zikamasipala uma kuthathwa izinqumo uma kuklanywa umngcele kamasipala . Kubalulekile ukuba amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme awazi umthetho ukuze akwazi ukuchaza emphakathini izinqumo okungenzeke zithathwe mayelana nomngcele kamasipala . Abantu babamba iqhaza ngokucelwa ukuba baveze eyabo imibono nangokubuzwa imibuzo . Izinkampani zangaphandle zikhomba izinkinga bese kuqala izinhlelo zokuqoqa ulwazi . Ngaleyo ndlela zilawula ukuhlaziywa kolwazi . Ukubonisana ngaleyo ndlela akusho ukungalibambi iqhaza ekuthathweni kwezinqumo , kanti izingcweti aziphoqelekile ukwamukela imibono yabantu . Ukuhlela : Abahlali , ama-NGO , ama-CBO kanye namaqembu ezepolotiki basebenza elitheni ukwakha iziphakamiso okumele zibhekwe ngumkhandlu , kanye nokugqugquzela umasipala ukuthi usebenzise amandla okusebenzisa ingqalasizinda , kanye nokweseka ukuhlanganyela nezinhlangano ezesekwa ngumphakathi ezingaba namakhono okuhambisa ukuqaliswa kwemisebenzi yokuthuthukisa . Noma yini emayelana nemali kumele ichazwe futhi yamukelwe kusabelomali . Noma yisiphi isinqumo esinomthelela kuzindleko noma emalini engenayo kumele ukuba sihambisane nesizathu salokho . Ukubophezeleka kuhamba nezinqumo ezithathiwe . Kungabe okuqukethwe imisebenzi kanye nezindlela ezisetshenzisiwe zizoba ngezifanele futhi zizohlangabezana nezidingo zabo bobabili abesilisa kanye nabesifazane , kungakhathaleki imvelaphi yobuhlanga , inkolo kanye nezomnotho wabo ? Ngabe lezi zinhlelo ziyimpumelelo ? Ekupheleni kwalo mhlangano ababambe iqhaza bazobe sebenze iqoqa lamaphrojekthi / lemisebenzi abazofisa ukuyethula yokuxhaswa ngemali wumasipala noma ngabalethi bezidingo , izinhlelo / imisebenzi ezofakwa ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Ukusukela ngo-1994 umbuso ubeke inqubomgomo nohlaka olusemthethweni oluzama ukuphakamisa ukubusa ngokubamba iqhaza . Lolu hlaka luchazwe emdwebeni ongezansi . I-PMS yenza izinkomba zokusebenza okwenza ukuba uhulumeni wendawo kanye nezakhamizi zikwazi ukulinganisa impumelelo ngokusebenzisa lezi zinkomba . Lapho ikhombisa khona ukungasebenzi kahle , yenza ukuba kube khona ukungenelela okudingekayo . Ifaka phakathi amazinga okuhlela , ukulandelela kanye nempendulo kanye nokubuyekezwa kokusebenza okwenziwa kanye ngonyaka . Enza ikhansela lawo ukuba lizibophezelele ekulwiseni inkohlakalo noma ukumoshwa kwezimali zikamasipala . Ukuba yisikhulu umcabango osuka phezulu uye phansi , ukuziphatha kanye nobudlelwano obakhelwe ekucabangeleni ukuthi ' isikhulu ' noma ' umqeqeshi ' uhlale azi kangcono kunalabo abangaphansi kwakhe . Yini ehlukile ezigamekweni ? Le ngxenye yesabelomali yiyo etshalwa ngumasipala ekuthuthukisweni kwezakhiwo ezintsha , izingqalazizinda , noma kwenye impahla yekhephithali enjengokwakhiwa kwemigwaqo nezindlu . Lawa maphrojekthi kuthiwa ngamaphrojekthi ekhephithali . Uhulumeni wendawo kumele azi ukuthi lokhu kutshalwa kwezimali kuzobiza malini ngonyaka ngamunye kanye nokuthi imali izovela kuphi . Zenze ukuthi uhulumeni , amabhizinizi nabo bonke abaholi emphakathini baphendule ngezenzo zabo . Izikhungo ezisebenza kahle nezinamakhono ezifana noMvikeli Womphakathi Nophiko Lwabaseshi Olukhethekile kudingeka zifakelwe imali nabasebenzi abenele ukuze bangagxambukeli abangaphandle . Ukuze ube ngumuntu oxhumana ngendlela efanele nabanye kufanele wazi indlela okufanele udlulise ngayo umyalezo . Ukuhlela lokho okuqondwe ukuzuzwa ngokusebenza mayelana nalezi zinjongo ngayinye ( isib. ukuhlinzeka imindeni eyi-10 000 ngokuthuthwa kwendle ehamba ngamanzi onyakeni wezimali ozayo ) . Ungaphazamisi , yekela abantu babeke izimvo zabo ngokuphelele . Indlela encike emandleni - lapha ngesikhathi elinye icala lisebenzisa isikhundla salo sangempela noma esicatshangwayo samandla ukuzama ukuphoqelela elinye ukuba lenze ngendlela ethile efunekayo . Le ndlela incike emandleni noma ukuphusha ukuthola umphumela . Isibonelo , amasekhurithi abopha abasesitelekeni abebevale umgwaqo , noma umuntu osegunyeni emsebenzini uthatha isinqumo abanye abasebenzi abangasithandisisi kodwa abakwazi ukusiphikisa ngenxa yobukhulu besikhundla somuntu othatha isinqumo . Izenzo ezivamile zendlela yamandla zingafaka iziteleka , imibhikisho , ukusebenzisa imisakazo ngendlela enekhono ukuhlasela elinye icala , yimpi . Lokhu kungaholela esimweni sokuthi omunye awine omunye ehlulwe . Yimiphi iminqamulaqulu yokwenza imisebenzi ? Umsebenzi wokuqala uhlanganisa izifiso ezisemqoka kakhulu eziyisihlanu , ukuqinisekisa ukuthi yonke imininingwane yokuhlela ibhaleke kahle . Lolu hlelo luhlongoza isu elimayelana nabasebenzi elimikhakhamithathu elibandakanya isu lokuqeqesha lesikhathi eside , imiphumela engcono evela emkhakheni wezemfundo ephakeme nesu lokwabiwa kwezisetshenziswa eziyindlala . Ukumeleleka ngokwendawo kumele kunakwe ukuqikelela ukuthi inqubo ihlanganisa imiphakathi . Imihlangano yokwethulwa kwemiphakathi nokubikelwa ngokwenzekayo ingadinga ukubanjelwa ezindaweni eziningi ukuze kufinyelelwe kubantu abaningi . Ukuhlanganisa bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika ohlelweni olufanayo ukuthola inqubekela phambili nokulingana . Ezinye izindaba zidluliselwa kumakomidi ezikhundla omkhandlu ukuze kubuye kuxoxwe ngazo futhi kwethulwe izincomo . Yenza iqoqa ngokugxila ezinhlosweni ezibizwa nge-Millennium Development Goals nasendlelni omasipala bendawo , kanye nomphakathi , okumele bathole ngayo izindlela zokusebenzela ukufeza lezi zinhloso . Ngaphansi Komthetho Wezakhiwo Zikamasipala [ Isigaba 32 ] , ikhanseli inganikeza amandla athize kumakomiti amawadi . Nanoma kubalulekile ukufaka amakomiti amawadi ezinqubweni zokuxoxisana loko kuzoba nomthelela ezinqumweni , ukuthweswa amandla kwenziwa ngokunakekelwa okukhulu . Izinqumo zekhanseli kufanele zithathwe ikhansela ekhethwe ngentando yeningi , enganamfihlo nenokuzibophezela . Amakomiti amawadi asingamalungu asemthethweni wokuthatha izivumelwano noma bangamangalelwa enkantolo ngamaphutha abo , ngokungaphathi kahle noma umkhonyovu . Yinoma yiziphi izinkinga izidalwa yisinqumo ezingalungile zizohlala zingumthwalo oyisibopho sekhanseli . Umzamo wethu wokwakha ube nzima kakhulu ngezikhathi zokukhula kancane komnotho . INingizimu Afrika angeke yakwazi ukuletha ukukhula okuya phansi okucija izinkinga zomphakathi . Ubuholi obuqinile buyadingeka ukukhuthaza umbono woMthethosisekelo . Ukubumbana komphakathi yikhona okungasiza ukuqinisa ukuqondana phakathi kokukhula , ukuthuthuka nokwakheka kwesizwe , kwenze umjikelezo omuhle . Izindlela zohlelo lwe-IDP zihlinzeka ngokubamba iqhaza njengengxenye yenqubo yokuhlela ngokusebenzisa izinhlaka ezithile . Lezi zinhlaka zihlanganisa inkundla ( iforamu ) yokumeleleka , amathimba ezinhlelo ( phrojekthi task team ) amaphrojekthi ) kanye nemicimbi yezamaqhinga . UMthetho uphinde uwubeke ngokusobala umgomo wokubonisana ezingeni lezigceme . Ukhomba isidingo sokuba umphakathi unikele ezinhlelweni , uphawule futhi nangokusebenza kukamasipala . Ucwaningo olusebenzayo lwamaqembu azilungiselela luyenziwa kubambisanwe nama-NGO kanye nama -CBO kungaveza imininingwane ebanzi ephathelene nezidingo ezithile kanye nokuyigugu . Ukuxhumana kwamazwe omhlaba esikhathini esiningi kusho ukukhula kokuhwebelana kwamazwe omhlaba nokukhula kokuthutheleka kwabantu , ngokwemali , imiqondo nangokobuchwepheshe kunqanyulwa imingcele , emashumini eminyaka esanda kwedlula . Lezi zimo sezisekele ukuthuthuka kwamazwe ampofu nahola imali ephakathi nendawo , ziwavumela ukuthi afinyelele ezimakethe , ezimpahleni , emisebenzini , emalini , kwezobuchwepheshe namakhono . Okwenzeka kwamanye amazwe sekube nomthelela ekukhuleni " kokuxhumana " , okwehlise izingqinamba zokungena kwakhulisa nokufinyelela olwazini . Eminyakeni embalwa ezayo , iNingizimu Afrika kumele yenze okuthile ngalesi simo ngokuqinisa amanani aphansi notshalomali ezimbonini zemikhiqizo yenani eliphezulu kanye nokukhulisa umthamo wemikhiqizo ehanjiswa ngaphandle . Esikhathini esithe ukuba side , iNingizimu Afrika kumele yenze okuthe xaxa ukukhulisa amanani aphansi emikhakheni engahlomula kuyo engasondeza abantu abaningi emsebenzini . Ngokuthuthukisa isisekelo samakhono nokwandisa ukubiza kahle kwemikhiqizo , umnotho ungaba ngowezimboni ezehlukene , ulungise umthelela oveza isimo esingesona samanani enyusiwe ezimpahla zemvelo erandini . Ukubamba iqhaza ekulalelweni kwesabelomali ngokumela umphakathi . Ukulalelwa kwesabelomali kuqinisekisa ukuthi izidingo ze-MFMA kuyahlangatshezwana nazo mayelana nokubamba komphakathi iqhaza kwinqubo yesabelomali . Ukulalelwa kwesabelomali sikamasipala kwenza amaKomidi Ezigceme akwazi ukubamba iqhaza ekuthuthukisweni kwesabelomali sikamasipala . Ukuthuthukisa amakhono amalungu Amakomidi Ezigceme ukuze akwazi ukusebenza njengezingcweti zentuthuko yendawo futhi akwazi ukusebenzisana nomphakathi kanye nokuwuthuthukisa . Izinqubo ze-IDP neze-CBP kanye nemiphumela okwenziwe futhi okusebenzelanayo , ziwumjikelezo futhi ziyaphindwaphindwa . ulwazi oluku-IDP ekhona kumele ukuba zisetshenziselwe inqubo ye-CBP , ngesikhathi imiphumela ye-CBP izosetshenziselwa ukubuyekeza i-IDP ngonyaka olandelayo . Ukuhlaziya ubulili kwenziwa kanti kwayinqoba inkinga . Kwahlala obala ukuthi abesifazane yibona abalimi , kodwa banegalelo elincane emizini yabo noma emphakathini . Izimali ezibolekisayo kubantu besifazane , Izinsizakalo zoxhaso kanye nemibuthano yokwenza izinqumo ngokuhlanganyela zamiswa kanti nemali yasetshenziselwa ukuguqula abalimi abahluphekayo ababengakwazi ngisho nokuziphilisa ukuba babe ngabaphumelelayo . Ezinye izindawo zokulinganisa zingaziswa , ukusebenzisana nebandla , noma imikhakha yokusebenza ngemfanelo ebekwa Yikomiti Lewadi lizibekela yona ukuqinisekisa ukuthi amalungu alo enza izibopho zawo njengoba kucatshangwe emthethweni wokubamba iqhaza komphakathi . Abantu babamba iqhaza ngokusebenzisana ekuhlaziyeni , ekwenzeni izinhlelo zokwenza nasekusungulweni noma ekuqinisweni kwezikhungo zendawo . Lolu hlelo luhlanganisa izindlela zemikhakha ehlukene zemibono eminingi , ezisebenzisa inqubo yokufunda ehlelekile nenesakhiwo . Uma amaqembu esekwazi ukuthatha izinqumo ngendawo , anqume ngendlela izinsiza ezikhona ezingasetshenziswa ngayo , asuke enelungelo lokugcina izinhlaka nemisebenzi kusesimeni esifanele . Ukuthuthukisa ukuxhumana ngokwezindawo ezingomakhelwane ukwenza ukuthi umphakathi , amabhizinisi , nohulumeni baxazulule izinkinga ngokubambisana . lesi SAHLUKO SICHAZA IQHAZA LAMAKOMIDI EZIGCEME kanye namanye amalungu omphakathi ekuhleleni okugqugquzela ukuba umphakathi usebenze . Isahluko soku-1 siqhakambisa ukuthi uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini kumele lulungiselelwe ngabantu bendawo esigcemeni sabo , lube ngolomphakathi futhi luqinisekise ukukhuthala komphakathi ekusebenzeni kwalo . Ukusebenza ngemfanelo kumuntu ngamunye , amaqembu kanye Nabahlanganyeli Bomphakathi Bangasese abasiza ukufeza izinjongo eziyisu zomnyango noma zikamasipala kumele kuhlolwe ukuqinisekisa ukwethulwa kwezinsizakalo ezisezingeni elifanele . Ukusebenza ngemfanelo komuntu ngamunye kuzokunikezwa inani ngokuhambisana nohlelo lokuphatha ukusebenza ngemfanelo olusetshenziswa ngumasipala wakhe . Ukuzihlola nokubuyekezwa ngontanga ngamathuluzi asetshenziswayo ekuhloleni umuntu ngamunye . Ukuhlelwa kwezinsizakusebenza : Ukunquma ukuthi yiziphi izinsizakusebenza ( abantu , izinto zokusebenza , impahla yokusebenza ) nokuthi kudingeka okungakanani ngakunye ukwenza imisebenzi yephrojekthi . Uhlelo lwe-CBP lusungula inqubo yokubamba iqhaza yokuthola imibono emphakathini kanye nokuhlela okususelwa ezinkingeni zezindawo kanye nendlela lolu lwazi olungahlobana ngayo nombono jikelele kamasipala wokuhlela . Isibonelo esingezansi sethula uhlelo lwesigceme olufanele uhlelo lwe-IDP . Chaza imikhakha emithathu yomasipala bese ucela ababambe iqhaza ukuthi bahlonze umkhakha ongena ngaphansi kwawo umasipala wabo . Basize uma bengenaso isiqiniseko . Ukuqashwa komphakathi kumele kwande , kugxilwe kakhulu entsheni nabesifazane . Kulindeleke ukuthi ukuqashwa komphakathi kuyohlinzeka ngemisebenzi okungesiyo eyetoho elinganiselwa ezigidini ezi-2 ngonyaka wezi-2020 . Imiphakathi , izinhlangano nabantu babamba iqhaza ngezizathu ezehlukene futhi baletha amakhono nolwazi olwehlukene , okungaba wusizo kulolu hlelo . Ithebula elisekhasini lama-21 lethula izinhlobo zokubamba iqhaza nokuthi zimeleni . Ukuxhumanisa imiphumela yohlelo lwe-CBP neyohlelo lwe-IDP kuyinqubo yemicimbi elandelanayo . Le micimbi elandelanayo eyethulwa ohlelweni lwe-CBP idinga ukuxhunyaniswa nemicimbi elandelanayo yohlelo lwe-IDP . Lokhu kusemqoka ngoba ngohlelo lwe-CBP kuzanywa ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izidingo zemiphakathi ziyahlonzwa futhi ziyafakwa ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Njengoba uhlelo lwe-IDP kuhloswe ngalo ukuveza izinto ezisemqoka zomphakathi , uma kuwukuthi le misebenzi ayihambisani , imiphakathi ingadumala ngokuhlela okulandela indlela yohlelo lwe-CBP . Umasipala angenza iqembu lentuthuko lababo okubanjiswene nabo lapho engaletha ndawonye abantu abavela kuma-CBO nama-NGO ; amabhizinisi endawo , ama-SMME , ezolimo njll . Leli qembu lizokweluleka umasipala mayelana nezindaba zentuthuko yezomnotho wendawo kanye neze-IDP . Indlela yeqembu labo okubanjiswene nabo ingengeza kwezinye izindlela zokubamba iqhaza esezivese zikhona komasipala ; iqinise umbuso wentando yeningi wokubambisana futhi yenyuse nenani labantu abanezwi futhi abangabanikazi bezinqumo zikamasipala . Ukukhuthaza ubuholi obuqinile kuwo wonke umphakathi ukuze kusetshenzwe ngokubambisana ukuxazulula izinkinga . Kuhulumeni othuthukayo , izinyunyana zabelana ngesibopho sokwenziwa komsebenzi osezingeni eliphezulu , sokuthuthukisa ukusebenza kahle kukahulumeni nokulwa nenkohlakalo nokungasebenzi kahle . Yonke imininingwane ebhalwe ngaphansi kwesihloko ' Indlela ' inanyathiselwa odongeni lubone yiwona wonke amalungu . Umgqugquzeli ufunda yonke imininingwane bese ecela eminye angayingeza eqenjni . Njengoba lo mhlangano umelwe wukuqhakambisa izimo ezifiswayo ezizoba wuhlelo lwesigceme , iqembu kumele livumelane ngokuthi kuyini okumele kuqhakanjiswe . Kudingeka kucace uma izinhlaka ezingaphandle kukahulumeni kumele zisebenzise ingxenye yohlelo . Amabhizinisi , abasebenzi nomphakathi ngamaqembu ahlukene futhi akuvamile ukuthi kukhulume ngazwi linye . Kodwa-ke imisebenzi ecacile nochungechunge lokuzibophezela , okubandakanya abalingani basemphakathini , kusemqoka ukwenza ukuthi lolu hlelo lube yimpumelelo . Ezindaweni eziningi , amabhizinisi , abasebenzi nomphakathi bangaveza ukuthi bangabamba liphi iqhaza ezintweni ezisemqoka zohlelo . Kodwa-ke ngezinye izikhathi leli qhaza kuyodingeka lenziwe libe semthethweni . Ukusebenzisana ukufeza injongo ethile ohlelweni kuyosiza ukwakha ukwethembana ngaphakathi naphakathi kwemikhakha . Ngakho-ke ukuhlela okugqugquzela umphakathi ukuba emiholweni kuwuhlobo lokuhlela , okuvula amathuba okubamba iqhaza , okuklanyelwe ukuqhubezela ukuzebenza komphakathi futhi kuxhumana nohlelo olubandakanya umasipala wonke nezakhamuzi zawo , uhlelo lwe-IDP . UMBUZO 4 Yini imikhakha ebalulekile yemiphumela ( ama-KRA ) ? Ngenxa yokuthi uhlelo zokuthathwa ngalo ukuletha izinguquko ezinqala esikhathini esicishe sibe yiminyaka engamashumi amabili , ludinga izinga lokungaguquki kwenqubomgomo enezinguquko zezinhlangothi ezimbili ebuholini bukahulumeni , amabhizinisi nabasebenzi . Amaphuzu amaningi ohlelo ayodinga imizamo yeminyaka ukuveza imiphumela . Isibonelo , ukuguqukela emnothweni onezinga eliphansi lekhabhoni kuyodinga inqubomgomo yesikhathi eside nemithetho yokuhlela indawo iyothatha amashumi eminyaka ukubhekana nokuhlukaniswa ngezindawo zokuhlala kombuso wobandlululo . Izinguquko zenqubomgomo kumele zenziwe ngokucophelela kuye ngokolwazi nobufakazi ukuze izwe lingalahlekelwa yizinhloso zalo zesikhathi eside . Ukubamba kweqembu iqhaza : Abaningi omasipala bakhula kakhulu uma abasha kubhekwa ubukhulu bezakhamizi kanye nendawo ukuvumela ukubamba iqhaza okuqondile kwabahlali abaningi kwizinqubo zokuhlela ezinzima . Ukubamba iqhaza ohlelweni lokuthuthukisa oluhlanganisayo , ngakho-ke kudinga imithetho nezinqubo ezicacile ezicacisa ukuthi ngubani okumele abambe iqhaza noma okumele kuxhunyanwe naye , maqondana nobani , ngaluphi udaba , ngokusebenzisa maphi amasu nenhlangano , anomthelela muni . Iziphakamiso nemibono kumele kubhalwe eceleni kwezinkomba kukhombise imiphumela eyayingalindelekile kwikholomu yemibono neziphakamiso . Izinga lokucabangela okuhlangatshezwane nakho kumele kuqashelwe . Ninayo imibono yokwenza kangcono ngokuzayo ? Ukubamba iqhaza kwiForamu Yohlelo Lwentuthuko Oludidiyele - ukugqugquzela ukubamba iqhaza kwiforamu ngendlela eqondile noma ngokumelwa yiKomidi Lesigceme uma ezinye izinhlaka zikamasipala wonke ezingabamba iqhaza zingekho . Ucwaningo nezentuthuko , i-Research and development ( i-R&D ) . Ukugxila okusheshayo kwi-R&D nasezingeni eliphezulu lokufundisa kuyothuthukisa izinga lemfundo ephakeme , kodwa ngaphandle kokunaka , ukunganeli kwamakhono abantu kuyophazamisa ukukhiqizwa kolwazi nokuqamba izinto ezintsha . Amayunivesithi kudingeka abe yizikhungo zokusebenza kahle ngasohlangothini lokugcina lwezobuchwepheshe . Ngokuheha abafundi abavela emazweni angaphesheya kwezilwandle , amayunivesithi angazakhela imali yentela aphinde andise inani lamakhono . Abafundi abavela phesheya kwezilwandle abathola iziqu zasemayunivesithi aseNingizimu Afrika kumele bavumeleke ukuthola imvume yeminyaka eyisikhombisa yokusebenza lapha ukubakhuthaza ukuthi bahlale basebenze lapha . Ngesikhathi iNingizimu Afrika kudingeka ichithe isikhathi esiningi kwi-R&D jikelele , isakhiwo sesikhungo kudingeka naso sithuthukise ukuxhumana phakathi kokuqamba kabusha nezidingo zebhizinisi . Uhulumeni kumele asebenzisane nomkhakha ozimele ukuphakamisa izinga le-R&D , ngezisetshenziswa ezihlosiwe ekwakheni ingqalasizinda yocwaningo oludingwa umnotho wesikhathi samanje . INingizimu Afrika inezinyunyana zabasebenzi ezisebenza kahle . Ngokomlando , izinyunyana zabasebenzi zabamba iqhaza kwezombusazwe , ukuqonda ukuthi izindaba ezimayelana namalungu azo azipheleli esangweni lasembonini . Izinyunyana zikhulisa izimfuno zamalunga azo nokukhulumela abasebenzi abangakwazi ukuzikhulumela , abafana nabasebenzi basemapulazini , abasebenzi basezindlini noma abasebenzi bamatoho . Amalungelo nemihlomulo enikezwe abasebenzi nokukhuphuka kwamazinga okuphila osekubonwe yiningi labasebenzi kusukela ngonyaka we-1994 kukhomba inzuzo enkulu yezwe . Ukwethula izinsizakalo ezibhekene nomphakathi njengoba umasipala ubhekela izidingo zomphakathi kunokuba uphoqelele imibono yawo phezu komphakathi . Uma selwenziwe uhlelo olukushoyo okudingwa wumphakathi , kumele kwenziwe uhlelo lokwenza lwemisebenzi okumele yenziwe ngokushesha ukuze umphakathi ukwazi ukuqhuba uhlelo lwawo lokuzithuthukisa . Lokhu kungabandakanya ukwabelwa kwemali esivele ikhona esetshenziswa ngokubona izidingo , okumele kwenziwe wumphakathi ukuqhuba ukuqhuba izinhlelo , kanye neminye imisebenzi yendawo njengokuhlela ifestiveli , umcimbi wokuqoqa udoti njll . Inqubo y-CBP kumele yenzeke ngaphambi kwezinyathelo zokuqala zokuhlelela uhlelo lwe-IDP nenqubo yokubuyekeza ukuze lube nomthelela ohlelweni lwe-IDP kuleyo naleyo ndawo kamasipala . Ukuhlela kufanele kube ngokuqondile kube nemininingwane kulowo nalowo masipala . Ekuboniseni ishejuli yokwethula uhlelo lwe-CBP njengengxenye yomjikelezo wokuhlela , isabelomali sigqamile . Lokhu kungenxa yokuthi isabelomali asiguquki njengoba sibekiwe onyakeni . IKHONO - kusho ukuthi izinsizakusebenza azimoshwa kumsebenzi noma kukhasimende eyodwa okudala ukulimazeka kwelinye ikhasimende . Ithimba labagqugquzeli kumele liqikelele ukuthi imininingwane emisha evelayo iyafakwa bese yenza izilungiso ukuze ulwazi olufakwayo ohlelweni kube yilolo oluqinisekisiwe wumphakathi ngokubanzi . Abantu , imiphakathi , izinhlaka namaqembu kuhlukahlukene futhi kunezimfuno nokukhetha okungefani . Lezi zimo zinomthelela emphakathini oguquguqukayo nonekhono . AmaKomidi Ezigceme adinga ukuba nesibindi futhi abe nekhono lokubhekana nemibono eyahlukahlukene ukusiza umphakathi . Kukhona ukwesweleka kwemigwaqo , amanzi kanye nokuxhunywa kukagesi kanti akukho ukuthuthwa kwendle ngamanzi . Izinqubo zokubika kudingeka zichazwe kahle kunoma yikuphi ukuphathwa kwephrojekthi . Kusemqoka ukuthi abantu bazi ukuthi kubikwa kubani nokuthi kunini lapho kufanele khona ukuthi kudluliselwe udaba kwabaphethe . Iphuzu ngalinye lalawa kumele kuxoxwe ngalo bese kunqunywa ngalo ezigabeni zokuqala zomjikelezo wephrojekthi . Amacebo kanye namaqhinga awazokunaka ukuthi abesilisa kanye nabesifazane banezidingo , izimfuno , ulwazi kanye nendlela yokuziphatha engafani kanti amaprojekthi azolahlekelwa umbono , ulwazi isipiliyoni , ukuxhumana kanye nezinsiza ezitholakala ezinhlanganweni zomphakathi zabesifazane . Njengoba iKomidi Lesigceme liphinde lisebenze njenge-ejenti evukuzayo emisebenzini yomphakathi kubalulekile ukuthi kufakwe ezobulili ezinhlelweni zokusebenza kanye nasemaqhingeni asetshenziswayo . UMthetho Wohlaka Lokusebenzisana Kukahulumeni , ka-2005 uthi izinhlaka ezintathu zikahulumeni kufanele zisebenzisane ukuze ziqinisekise ukuthuthukiswa komphakathi . Ababambiqhaza bengamaqembu angama-4 badweba ithebula elinamakholomu amabili ephepheni lephephandaba bese bebonisana ngezindlela Amakomidi Ezigceme angabandakanyeka ngazo kumazinga ahlukahlukene okwenziwa kwesabelomali , bebe befaka imibono kukholomu yesibili . INGXABANO YINTO YANSUKUZONKE . Yenzeka ngendlela esezingeni eliphansi , njengesinqumo sokuthi yini okufanele igqokwe namhlanje , ukuxabana nesihlobo , umngani noma umlingani osebenza naye kuze kube ukuxabana kwamazwe , ukungqubuzana ngezombusazwe noma impi yokubanga izinsizakusebenza , okungaholela odlameni nasekufeni kwabantu . Njengoba amaKomidi Ezigceme exhumana nabantu abanezidingo ezahlukahlukene nomasipala abanezinsizakusebenza ezingalingani , kunamathuba amaningi engxabano . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele akwazi ukubhekana nengxabano ngendlela efanele . lesi sahluko siveza izinhlobo zengxabano ezingenzeka okungafuneka amalungu eKomidi Ezigceme ukuba abhekane nazo . Sikhuluma ngamasu okuxazulula ingxabano futhi sinikeza ngamafuphi amakhono okuxazulula ingxabano . Bheka izigameko ekhasini 68 ebese usebenzisana nophathina wakho ekuvezeni indlela esetshenzisiwe engxabanweni esigamekweni ngasinye . Uhlelo lugxila ekukwazini ukusebenza okudingekayo ukuguqula umnotho nomphakathi . Ukufeza lokhu kukwazi ukusebenza angeke kuzenzakalele , futhi kwenzeka uma izwe liqhubeka ngendlela yalo eliyisebenzisayo . Ukukhula kwamazinga okuphatheka kabi nokungabekezeli kusho ukuthi isikhathi sisemqoka kakhulu : ukuhluleka ukwenza okuthile kuyokhubaza okutholakala embusweni wentando yeningi . Kahle kahle , iNingizimu Afrika kumele ithole izindlela zokunciphisa ngokushesha amazinga athusayo okungatholi imisebenzi kwabantu abasha nokuhlinzeka abantu abasha ngamathuba asemqoka . Sebenzisa isifundo sokubonakalayo ukwenza isigaba ngasinye . Banike isikhathi ukwenza lokhu ebese ukhetha elinye iqembu ukuba liveze ukuthi lingasenza kanjani isigaba ngasinye . Emva kwesigaba ngasinye , cela iqembu ngalinye ukuba libeke uvo mayelana nokuthi yikuphi okusebenze kahle ebese unikeza amasu okwenza kangcono . Ngobani Abasebenzi Bentuthuko Yomphakathi ( CDWs ) esigcemeni futhi iliphi iqhaza abangalibamba ekwesekeni iKomidi Lesigceme ? Amaphrojekthi kumele abe nokuxhumana ngqo namaphuzu asemqoka nezinhloso ezivezwe enqubeni yokuhlela . Indlela encike emalungelweni - lapha ingesikhathi icala elikwingxabano likholelwa ngukuthi elinye lamalungelo alo lephuliwe ebese liya ohlakeni oluthile ukuthola isinqumo ngokwephulwa kwelungelo . Izindlela zifaka izinkantolo , ukuqulwa nokulamula . Isibonelo , abahlali baseMoutse baphikisa isinqumo sokufakwa komunye umngcele ngokususa iMoutse eMpumalanga iyiswe eLimpopo ngokusebenzisa inkantolo . Lokhu kuholele esimweni sokuthi omunye awine omunye ehlulwe . INingizimu Afrika kudingeka izicije kwezokuziqambela izinto , iqhubeke nokufaka isandla ekuthuthukisweni kwamazwe omhlaba kwezesayensi nobuchwepheshe . Lokhu kudinga ukutshala kakhulu imali kwezocwaningo nezentuthuko , nokusebenzisa kahle izisetshenziswa ezikhona , nezikhungo ezisebenzayo ezengeziwe ezisiza ekuqambeni izinto zikhulise nokubambisana phakathi kwesayensi yomphakathi nezikhungo zobuchwepheshe kanye nezimboni ezizimele . Ukuphakama kwezindleko zamakhaya zokuxhumana nge-inthanethi yisithiyo esikhulu . Bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika kumele bakwazi ukuthola nokusebenzisa ulwazi ngempumelelo . Kuze kube manje , amalungiselelo ezikhungo okulawula indawo yemininingwane , ukuxhumana nobuchwepheshe , i-information , communications and technology ( i-ICT ) kumele kuhlelwe kangcono ukuqinisekisa ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika ayibi senkingeni ngenxa " yokwehlukaniswa ngokwezinombolo , i-digital divide " . Umgqugquzeli kufanele enze isiqiniseko sokuthi izinqumo ziyathathwa , izinhlelo ziyathuthukiswa futhi wonke umuntu uyazimisela . Umgqugquzeli omuhle uyakhathazeka ngokuzokwenziwa emhlanganweni noma embuthanweni wokucobelelana , kanye nesitayela sawo .
