Ukukhulisa imihlomulo yalokhu " kwehlukana kwezimo zomumo wabantu " izwe lidinga ukudla okunomsoco okungcono nokunakekelwa ngokwezempilo , amazinga emfundo athuthukisiwe , ukwenyuka kokuya ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme , ukungena kalula emisebenzini nokwanda kokukwazi ukuhamba ngokomsebenzi ( ukwazi ukuya lapho kutholakala khona imisebenzi ) . Onke la maphuzu kudingeka kucatshangwe ngawo ohlelweni lukazwelonke . Iyiphi indlela esetshenziswayo ? Khombisa ababambe iqhaza uhlelo lomsebenzi nelogifreyimu abayenzile ukungenisa imali yephrojekthi yengadi ( emisebenzini yesi-2.2 nowesi-3.1 ) . Isihlahla sezinkinga singaqedelwa manje ngokudweba imigqa eya phansi ukukhombisa ukuxhumana phakathi kwezimbangela ( ngaphansi kwengxenye yesihlahla ) nokuxhumana phakathi kwemiphumela ( engxenyeni engenhla ) . Imigqa evundlile kumele idwetshwe ukukhombisa lapho okunezimbangela ezihlanganisiwe , noma imiphumela ehlanganisiwe . Amaprojekthi asebenzise ukulingana kobulili futhi akhuthaza namacebo okuqasha ngokungakhiphi inyumbazane ukubandakanya amagalelo abesifazane emaKomidini Ezigceme abe yimpumelelo kakhulu futhi azinzile . Ahlonza izidingo zomphakathi , bese encoma lawo maphrojekthi angathuthukisa izimpilo zabantu kuleso sigceme . UMBUZO 1 Iyini inhloso yohlelo lokulawulwa kokusebenza ? Zisebenze nabanye emphakathini ukukhulisa intuthuko , ukuxazulula izinkinga nokuveza izinkinga zabangakwazi ukuzikhulumela nabancishwe amathuba . Umsebenzi obalulekile Wamakomiti Amawadi ukusiza amakhanseli ewadi akhethwe ngentando yeningi ukufeza imibono ukumela abantu bewadi . Ezemfundo eqhubekayo nokuqeqeshwa ( ama-FET ) . Inqubo ye-FET ayisebenzi ngempumelelo . Incane kakhulu futhi nezinga lomphumela wokusebenza libi kakhulu . Ukuthuthuka kwezinga okuqhubekayo kuyadingeka uma inqubo yokusebenza ikhula . Izinga nokuqondana kwezifundo kudingeka kubhekwe ngokushesha . Uma izinga liqala ukukhuphuka nokuqasheka kwabaneziqu kuqala kwanda , ukufuneka kwemisebenzi ehlinzekwa ama-FET kuyovele kwande . Ukwanda komkhakha ngaphandle kokugxila kakhulu ezingeni eliphezulu kuthanda ukumba eqolo futhi kwehlise izinga elihle lokuziphatha kubantu abasha , okuqhubeka nokunyundela inqubo yokusebenza . Ngonyaka wezi-2030 , umkhakha we-FET kuyomele uphathe cishe amaphesenti angama-25 abantu abaneminyaka efanele , okusho ukukhula kusuka cishe ezi-300 000 namhlanje kuya esigidini esi-1.25 ngonyaka wezi-2030 . Ukusebenzisa izimali kutshalomali eNingizimu Afrika kwehlile kusuka esilinganisweni cishe esingamaphesenti angama-30 e-GDP ekuqaleni kweminyaka ye-1980 kuya cishe kumaphesenti ayi-16 e-GDP ngasekuqaleni konyaka wezi-2000 . Ukusebenzisa izimali engqalasizindeni yomphakathi nakho kusemazingeni aphansi ngokwamazinga omlando . Empeleni , iNingizimu Afrika iphuthetlwe ukufakwa kwezimali emigwaqeni , emizileni yesitimela , emachwebeni , kwezogesi , kwezamanzi , kwezokususwa kokungcola , kwezokuthutha umphakathi nezezindlu . Ukukhula ngokushesha nangendlela efaka bonke abantu , izwe lidinga indlela esezingeni eliphezulu lokusetshenziswa kwemali . Ukwenziwa kwemali ephelele ezinzile kudinga ukuba kufike cishe kumaphesenti angama-30 e-GDP ngonyaka wezi-2030 , utshalomali lomkhakha womphakathi lufike kumaphesenti ayi-10 e-GDP , ukufinyelela embandeleni osimeme emisebenzini yokukhula neyasemakhaya . Kulo msebenzi olandelayo umphakathi uhlela izigigaba ngokulandelana kwazo ngokulandela umlando womphakathi . Ngokuhlonza ukuphindaphindeka kwezigigaba nezimo lo msebenzi kumele wenze umphakathi uqonde ngokujulileyo isimo sawo , uwenze ucabange ngempumelelo yokungenelela kwesikhathi esedlule . I-Seymour indawo yemisebenzi encane esemaphandleni engxenyeni esenyakatho nesabelo sangaphambilini i-Ciskei . Inabantu abalinganiselwa ku-3 000 . Abalinganiselwa kuma-80% balaba bantu abaqashiwe kanye izinga labantu abangafundile lilinganiselwa kuma-60% . Ukwakha uhulumeni okwazi ukusebenza nothuthukayo . Izinselelo eziningana zidinga ukubhekwa , kubandakanya ukunganeli kwamakhono , indlela enzima yokusebenzisana kukahulumeni , amazinga aphezulu enkohlakalo , ukuziphendulela okungahambi kahle , ukungabhekwa kahle kwezomthetho nomlando omude wokungasebenzisani kahle phakathi kwenhlangano nohulumeni . Lokhu kungamaphuzu anzima , adinga ukubhekwa ngokwethembeka , ukuhlela kahle nobuholi obusemqoka . Qoka amavolontiya amabili ukuba enze umdlalo wokulingisa wemizuzu emithathu bese uwanikeza imizuzu embalwa yokucabanga ngokuthi azolingisa kanjani . Ungavumeli abanye abadlali kumbe ababambe iqhaza ukuba bazibone loku kulingisa . Tshela iqembu ukuthi lizokube libukele umdlalo wokulingisa . Ukuzinikela ngesinye sezimiso ezibalulekile zokubambisana futhi amaKomidi Esigceme , njengamakhansela akhethiwe , anesibophezelo kumphakathi awusebenzelayo . Ukubheka nokuhlola amaphrojethi omphakathi nokubika njalo emphakathini mayelana nenqubekela phambili yokusebenza yindlela enhle yokulandelela . Ukwethula ulwazi ngendlela phakathi komkhandlu nomphakathi naphakathi kwabo okubanjiswene nabo kusemqoka . Ukunikezwa kolwazi olungesilo iqiniso kungaholela ekungqubuzaneni phakathi kwamaqembu . Kungagqugquzela ukusabalala kwamahemuhemu futhi kudale ukudideka phakathi kwabahlali . Lokhu kungalibazisa intuthuko noma inqubekela phambili kwi-IDP noma amanye amaphrojethi . AmaKomidi Ezigceme axhumana nokubanjiswene nabo abayizinhlobonhlobo . Laba bafaka phakathi ikhansela lesigceme , iziphathimandla zikamasipala kufaka phakathi nomphathidolobha , umphathi kamasipala , abasebenzi bakamasipala , abasebenzi abathuthukisa umphakathi , abaholi bendabuko nemiphakathi , abenziwe yinqwaba yamaqembu amele izimfuno njengezinhlangano zenkolo , abamabhizinisi , izinhlangano zentsha , izinhlangano zabesifazane , izinhlangano zabalimi namanye amaqembu ehlukene nezinhlangano . Ukuzisho imvelaphi - Imiphakathi ingehlukahluka ngokobuzwe , inkolo , indawo yokuhlala , okungadala ingxabano . Ukungena kwabantu kakhulu abavela kwelinye izwe abanolimi nesiko elehlukile noma kwesinye isifundazwe noma idolobha , kungadala ingxabano . Ukwakhiwa kwezindlu : Isicelo sokucela izimali kuBhodi Lezezindlu Kuzwelonke okwenziwe ngenhloso yokuxazulula izinkinga ezingapheli zezezindlu kule ndawo sivunyiwe . Noma kunjalo , ukubambezeleka kokudedelwa kwemali , umbango womhlaba endaweni okuzokwakhiwa kuyo kanye nokudedelwa kancane komhlaba kahulumeni kuhulumeni wendawo sekube nomthelela Isithombe ekwenziweni kwale phrojekthi . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kudingeka akhuthaze ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi kuhulumeni wendawo . Asebenza njengabaxhumanisi phakathi komphakathi kanye nomkhandlu kamasipala . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angenza izincomo ekhanseleni lesigceme nokufanele lidlulisele izincomo ezifanele kuSomlomo kamasipala mayelana nezinqubomgomo ezithinta isigceme . Ngonyaka wezi-2030 , inqubo yokusebenza kwezempilo kumele ihlinzeke ngokunakekela okusezingeni eliphezulu kubo bonke abantu , kube mahhala lapho okwenziwa khona , noma kukhokhelwe ngokuhlinzekwa ngumphakathi noma kukhokhelwe umshuwalenze ozimele . Inqubo yokusebenza kwezempilo esemqoka neyezigodi kumele itholakale kubo bonke abantu , igxile kakhulu ekuvimbeleni , ekulawulweni nasekwelashweni kwezifo , nasekufundisweni ngazo . Izibhedlela kumele zisebenze ngempumelelo nangokonga , zihlinzeke ngokwelapha okusezingeni eliphezulu esigabeni esiphakathi nesiphakeme kulabo abadinga ukwelashwa . Ochwepheshe bezempilo abaningi kumele babe khona , ikakhulukazi emiphakathini empofu . NJENGOHLELO LOKUHLOLA UMTHELELA KWABESIFAZANE NABESILISA KUNOMA YISIPHI ISINYATHELO ESIHLELIWE , KUBANDAKANYA IMITHETHO , IZINQUBOMGOMO KANYE NEZINHLELO , KUNOMA YIYIPHI INDAWO NOMA AMAZINGA . YIQHINGA LOKWENZA UKUKHATHAZEKA KANYE NESIPILIYONI SABESIFAZANE NABESILISA INGXENYE YOKUDWEBA , YOKUQALISA KANYE NOKUQAPHA NOKUHLOLWA KWEZINQUBOMGOMO KANYE NEZINHLELO KUWO WONKE AMAZINGA EZEPOLITIKI , EZOMNOTHO NAWOMPHAKATHI UKUZE ABESIFAZANE NABESILISA BAHLOMULE NGOKULINGANAYO FUTHI KUNGABHEBHEZELWA UKUNGALINGANI . INJONGO UKUFEZA UKULINGANA NGOKOBULILI . Ekusebenziseni lezi zinhlelo ezisemqoka zengqalasizinda , kusemqoka ukuqinisekisa ukuthi imiphakathi yasemakhaya ingazuza kukho kokubili ingqalasizinda enkulu neyohlaka lokusabalalisa kanye nokuthi intengo yale ngqalasizinda iyisidingo esinqala semiphakathi yasemakhaya . Abagqugquzeli kumele besekwe yizingcweti zohlelo lwe-CBP . Lezi zingcweti zizohlinzeka ngezobuchwepheshe nezokuthuthwa kwabantu futhi zizonikezwa imisebenzi yezigceme ezithile . Isayensi nobuchwepheshe kuzoqhubeka nokuguqula indlela izimpahla nemisebenzi okukhiqizwa kudayiswe ngayo . Njengezwe elinemali engenayo elingene , iNingizimu Afrika idinga ukusebenzisa ulwazi nemikhiqizo ezenzele yona ukuncintisana namanye amazwe . Ngokwayo iyodwa , izindleko ezibiza kahle angeke zenela ukusabalalisa ukuba khona kwemboni yaseNingizimu Afrika emhlabeni wonke . Lokhu kuqondiswe kukho kokubili izimboni ezintsha nemikhakha ejwayelekile , efana nezimayini . Ukuziqambela kuyadingeka ezweni elingenisa imali elingene ukuze lithuthuke . UMPHAKATHI JIKELELE YONKE INDAWO EMHLABENI WESEKA IMIBONO YAWO NGOHULUMENI NGOHLOBO NEZINGA LEZINSIZAKALO ELIZITHOLA NSUKUZONKE EZANDLENI ZABASEBENZI BAKAHULUMENI . ' UBUSO ' BUKAHULUMENI NGUBUSO NGUBUSO / NOMA IZWI LABANIKEZELI BEZINSIZAKALO ABASEMUGQENI OPHAMBILI . LOKHU YIKHO KONKE ABANTU ABAKUTHOLAYO KANTI UMA INSIZAKALO IYIMBI FUTHI INGENABUNGANE , UHULUMENI NGOKUSHESHA UTHATHWA NJENGONGAFANELE NOBUSA NGENDLELA OKUNGEYONA . UMA NGABE INSIZAKALO IYIMBI , UHULUMENI elizosekela KANTI UMA INSIZAKALO IYINHLE , UHULUMENI MUHLE , KULULA NJE KANJALO . LOKHU KUYIQINISO EMHLABENI WONKE JIKELELE FUTHI AKWEHLUKILE ENINGIZIMU AFRIKA . Imithetho Yokuhlela Nokusebenza Kukamasipala , ka-2001 ibeka uhlobo Izinhlelo Zokuhlola Ukusebenza . Njengoba amaKomidi Ezigceme ebamba iqhaza ekuhloleni ukusebenza kukamasipala , amalungu kufanele azi okuqukethwe yimithetho . Eminyakeni eyishumi nesishiyagalombili yentando yeningi , iNingizimu Afrika isalokhu iwumphakathi ongalingani kakhulu lapho abantu abaningi bephila ngaphansi kobuphofu futhi bebancane kakhulu abasebenzayo . Izinga lemfundo yeningi labafundi abamnyama liphansi . Ukuhlukana kwezindawo ngenxa yobandlululo kuyaqhubeka nokuba khona . Iningi labantu abasha babona izinto zingahambi ngendlela ebavunayo . Okwashiywa wubandlululo kuyaqhubeka nokulawula amathuba empilo yabantu abaningi . Lezi zinselelo ezinkulu kungabhekanwa nazo kuphela ngokwenza izinguquko ekusebenzeni kwezwe . Akuqikelelwe ukuthi ziyafakwa izifiso zalawo maqembu ancishwe amathuba . Ukusungula izinhlaka zendlela yokudlulisa imininingwane isuka kwenye indawo iya kwenye zikazwelonke , zesifunda nezikamasipala ukuhlinzeka ngomgogodla wokutholakala kwezindlela zokuxhumana ngezingcingo . Utshalomali oluzimele luhambe phambili kule ndawo , luhambisane nezimali zomphakathi ezidingekayo ukuhlangabezana nezinjongo zomphakathi . Kudingeka inqubomgomo , imithetho namalungiselelo ezikhungo okuphumelelayo ukufeza lokhu . Ukuguqula lo mnotho kungumsebenzi onikeza inselelo , nowesikhathi eside . Ngokufingqiwe , sihlongoza ukukhulisa umnotho wabasebenzi , umthamo womkhiqizo nengqalasizinda ukukhulisa okuthunyelwa ngaphandle , okuyokhulisa izisetshenziswa zokutshalwa kwemali nokunciphisa ukuthemba izimali ezingenayo . Utshalomali oluphezulu , olusekelwa yingqalasizinda yomphakathi engcono namakhono , kuyokwenza ukuthi umnotho ukhule ngokushesha futhi kusebenzeke kahle . Ukukhula kwamathuba emisebenzi nokukhiqiza kuyoholela ekukhuleni kwemali engenayo namazinga okuphila nokuncipha kokungalingani . Ukuguqula umnotho ube ukutshalwa kwemali nokunciphisa ukusetshenziswa kwawo kuyadingeka ekukhuleni komnotho kwesikhathi eside . Emva kokuphothulwa kwe-IDP , kumele ukuba ithunyelwe kumkhandlu kamasipala ukuze icutshungulwe bese yemukelwa . Umkhandlu kumele ukuba abheke ukuthi ingabe le-IDP iyazihlonza yini izindaba ( izinkinga ) ezithinta leyo ndawo kanye nokuthi izindlela kanye namaphrojekthi azoba negalelo elingakanani ekulungiseni izinkinga . Umkhandlu kumele ukuba uqinisekise ukuthi i-IDP iyahambisana nesidingo somthetho ngaphambi kokwemukelwa . Ukuxhumana kuyizandla ezigezanayo . Kungukugeleza nokucobelelana ngolwazi nemiqondo kusuka komunye umuntu kuya komunye . Kuyinqubo lapho umuntu , OTHUMELAYO , ethumela umyalezo oya komunye umuntu owemukela umyalezo , lowo-ke NGOMUKELAYO . Uma singaxhumani ngendlela efanele , lokhu kudala ukuxabana , ukuphikisana nokungezwani okungaqubuka . Ngoba amaKomidi Ezigceme angumgudu obalulekile wokuxhumana ezingeni lezasekhaya , kufanele aqinisekise ukuthi ulwazi alunikeza umphakathi luyiqiniso futhi luyezwakala kuwo wonke umuntu nokuthi nabo abanye abantu badlulise ulwazi oluyiqiniso kumkhandlu namakhansela . Khumbuza ababambe iqhaza ukuthi ilogifreyimu iyithebula nje okumele libasize hhayi ukubavimba . Kumele ibhekwe njengedokhumenti ephilayo eyoguqulwa iphinde ilungiswe ngokuhamba kwesikhathi . Ngendlela esebenzayo i-Batho Pele izothelela indlela umsebenzi owenziwa ngayo ngokuphoqelela Uhlelo lokuphatha Ukusebenza Ngemfanelo okubeka izinkomba zokusebenza ngemfanelo futhi ngalokho-ke zivumela uhulumeni wendawo kanye nezakhamizi ukulinganisa ukufeza maqondana nalezi zinkomba . Lapho ibonisa ukungasebenzi ngemfanelo , ihambisa ukungenela okudingekayo . Ifaka amazinga okuhlela , ukulandelela nokunikeza izimpendulo kanye nokubuyekezwa kokusebenza ngemfanelo konyaka ngonyaka . Intuthuko yaseNingizimu Afrika ikhubazwa ngokwenzeka esifundeni nasemhlabeni . Impumelelo iyoncika ekuziqondeni lezi zimo kanye nasekuthini yenzani ngazo . Ukwengeza ekucutshungulweni kwezinhlelo zezindawo ezihlala abantu , uhlelo luxoxa ngezinto ezinhlanu eziqaphelekayo : izinguquko emnothweni womhlaba , ezobuchwepheshe , okwenzeka emhlabeni wonke , ukuguquka kwesimo sezulu nokukhula komnotho wase-Afrika . UMSEBENZI 2 Yiziphi izindlela zokubandakanya abadlalindima bangaphandle . Imithetho eminingi iphasiswe yiPhalamende , emva kokhetho lwentandoyeningi luka-1994 , exhasa futhi iqinise amandla okusebenza komsipala ukuphatha izindaba zabo nokwenza imisebenzi yabo ngendlela yokubambisana nefaka abanye abantu . Ukwakha ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi . Ukubamba iqhaza kwezinhlangano zomphakathi nomphakathi jikelele kuyadingeka ukusungula imiphakathi ephephile . Izikhungo zokuphepha komphakathi kumele zibhekelelwe . Izimvula ezinamandla zibe nomphumela wokuthi inhlabathi eningi yangaphezulu ezingadini iguguleke . Amanzi aqoqelwe emathangini azosetshenziswa ezinyangeni ezizayo , kodwa kodwa umsebenzi okumele wenziwe ukuze iphrojekthi iphinde isebenze kahle . Ukukhipha umnotho ombiwa phansi ukuze kukhiqizwe izinsizakusebenza zokukhuphula amazinga okuphila , amakhono nengqalasizinda ngendlela esimeme . Okucatshangwayo kuphinde futhi kubhekane ' nobumqoka ' kwabo bonke abantu . Lokhu kusho ukuthi omunye nomunye umuntu kukhona afanele akunikele kuzo zonke izingxenye zempilo yabo . Lokhu futhi kwamukela amakomiti amawadi njengezikhungo ezihlanganisa abaholi abakhethiwe nabantu . Inqubo yendlela exubile yokuqasha abaphathi beminyango kumele yenziwe , ihlanganise womabili amaphuzu ezombusazwe nawezokuphatha . Izindaba zomphakathi ezibaluleke kakhulu . Yini iKomidi Lesigceme elingayenza ukusiza ? Ngesikhathi kwenziwa okokuqala lokhu , kungenzeka kuqukathe izinto eziningi zohlelo . . . Kodwa , uma sekuqhutshekwa nokwethulwa kwakho kulowo nalowo mhlangano wekomidi lesigceme kuzoba yinto ephathekayo uma enyusiwe umsebenzi . Ukuze iphrojekthi iphumelele kusemqoka ukuthi imisebenzi nezibopho zelungu ngalinye lethimba ichazwe ngokucophelela . Ilungu ngalinye elibandakanyeka kwiphrojekthi linesibopho sokwenza imisebenzi yalo ngendlela eqhubezela phambili izinjongo zephrojekthi nokuqinisekisa impumelelo yayo . Inani : Ukuqoka amashifu amabili yabaqaphi bendawo yokumisa izimoto / onogada bezimoto abayisihlanu . I-Batho Pele ithi iminyango yomibili ezingeni lesifundazwe nakuzwelonke kumele ibe nezinhlelo zokuphatha ukusebenza ngemfanelo okufaka ukwethulwa kwezinkomba zokwethulwa kwezinsizakalo kanye nokulinganiswa kokusebenza ngemfanelo . INingizimu Afrika kumele yenze okuthile mayelana neqiniso lokuthi izigidi zabantu abaphilayo ngokomzimba zidinga ukusebenza . Esikhathini esifishane umnotho kudingeka udale amathuba emisebenzi yabantu baseNingizimu Afrika abangasebenzi , okuholela kubo kuyintsha enamakhono aphansi , ngesikhathi bekhuphula amakhono nolwazi lomnotho ohlukile esikhathini esizayo . Ukukhuphula amazinga okusebenza kuyoba nenzuzo engaphezu kokuba nolwazi olutholakala ngokuba ngumuntu oqashiwe . Kuyobasiza abantu uma betshala imali emfundweni yezingane zabo , bathuthukise amakhaya abo futhi balawule izingozi zempilo . Ukusebenza nemfundo kuyovumela izakhamuzi ukuthi zithuthukise izimpilo zazo . Isimo siyenzeka futhi kubhekwana naso ngendlela encike kwindlela esenza ngayo izinto nesicabanga ngayo . Kungabe ukuhlolwa kwezidingo / ucwaningo oluyisisekelo lubandakanya izingxoxo nabo bobabili abesifazane kanye nabesilisa futhi kumele umphakathi ngokwehlukana kwawo ( abancane / abadala , abasemakhaya / abasemadolobheni , ngokobuhlanga ? ) Kungabe bobabili abesilisa kanye nabesifazane bazozenza izingxoxo futhi baqoqe nolwazi ? Ezokongiwa kwemvelo : Umhlaba wasendle noma wemvelo unciphile noma wandile yini ? Yini imbangela yalokho ? Zikhona yini izindawo ezahlonzelwa ukuvikelwa ? Zikhona yini izindawo ezinezimo zezejiyoloji , inhlabathi kanye nemimango ezingaba yinkinga ekwakheni , isib. izindawo ezehla kakhulu , inhlabathi egcwele amanzi kanye nedwala elingaphansi elingazinzile ? Kusemqoka ukwehlisa izindleko zokuphila emakhaya ampofu . Amanye amaphuzu ohlelo ayoba nomphumela wokukhuphula izindleko emnothweni . Empeleni ukwenza ingqalasizinda ibe yintsha emva kwamashumi eminyaka kufakwa imali ohlaziyayo kungadinga imali eningi . Ukulungisa lokhu kwenyuka , inqubomgomo kumele igxile ekukhuliseni ukubiza kahle nokufakwa kwezimali engqalasizindeni entsha ezindaweni ezinomthelela omkhulu kwabampofu , ezifana nochungechunge lwezinga lokudla , ezokuthutha umphakathi , ezemfundo , ezempilo nezokuxhumana ngocingo . Ukusebenza ngempumelelo komkhakha kahulumeni kuyoholela esimeni esiphansi sezindleko zomnotho . Ukuqinisekisa ukuthi lawo maphrojekthi ahlonziwe axhumene ngqo nalezo zindaba kanye nezinhloso okuphambili ohlwini lokubalulekile okwakuhlonziwe kumazinga adlulile . KUYISIDINGO SOMTHETHO UKUBA BONKE OMASIPALA BENZE uhlelo lokulawulwa kokusebenza ( PMS ) Inhloso ye-PMS wukuzibophezelela ekusetshenzisweni kwezinsizakusebenza zikamasipala , ukuthuthukisa amakhono kanye nokusebenza ngempumelelo kwezinhlangano kanye nokukhombisa imiphumela yempumelelo . Ukukhuthaza ukuba yizakhamuzi ezisebenzayo okuqinisa intuthuko , uhulumeni wentando yeningi nokubophezeleka . Umhlangano omkhulu neqembu elikhulu lomphakathi ngokubanzi lapho okufiswayo komsebenzi wesonto okuhlanganisa iNkombandlela , okufiswayo okuhlanganisiweyo kanye nolwazi lwalokho nalokho okufiswayo kuxoxwa khona kuvunyelwane ngokusemqoka emphakathini . Chaza ukuthi uma kwenziwa lokhu emphakathini umuntu okubhalayo angasebenzisa amaminithi kamabhalane , amarekhodi omphakathi kanye namanothi omgqugquzeli ukuthola ulwazi uma kunesidingo . Qala ngezibonelo zezimo ezaba namandla kakhulu , isibonelo , yimuphi unyaka owaba mubi kakhulu , yibaphi abantu abanganikeza izibonelo zezimo ngokwamandla azo . Indlela omasipala abaxhumana ngayo nezinhlaka zikahulumeni kazwelonke kanye nabezifundazwe . Ungowesifazane . Utshala imifino ukuze umndeni ukwazi ukudla . Umyeni wakho usebenza endaweni kanti futhi uyilungu leKomidi Lesigceme . Umndeni wakho udla ingxenye yemifino kodwa eminingi uyidayisa emakethe kanti lokhu kukunikeza imadlana ozoyisebenzisa . Ngale kwalokho awunayo imali okweyakho . Umyeni wakho akakunikezi imali , umane alethe ukudla kanye nezinye izidingo akuthatha lapho esebenza khona . Udinga ukuba nemali ekhona ukuze ukwazi ukuthengela abantwana bakho izipho ezincane , noma ukhokhele umtholampilo uma udinga ukuya khona . Umyeni wakho ufika ekhaya akutshela ukuthi umngane wakhe ekuqinisekiseni ukudayisa izitshalo zakho zemifino edolobheni elikhulu . IKhomishana Yamalungelo Abantu inamandla okucwaninga nokwethula umbiko mayelana namalungelo abantu , ukuthatha izinyathelo ukulungisa ukuhlukunyezwa kwamalungelo abantu , ukucwaninga nokufundisa mayelana namalungelo abantu . Ukuthatha indlela edidiyelayo . Ukuba nomphakathi ophephile kusho ukubhekana nezimbangela ezisemqoka zobelelesi , ezidinga izisetshenziswa zikahulumeni nezomphakathi . Ukukhulisa ukuguquguquka kwabantu nomnotho ngenxa yokuguquka kwesimo sezulu . Isigaba sama-29(b) salo Mthetho sixoxa ngenqubo okumele ilandelwe ekusunguleni uhlelo lwe-IDP , kanti siyasho futhi ukuthi umphakathi wendawo kumele kuxoxwe nawo ngezidingo zezentuthuko nezinto ezisemqoka zohlelo lwe-IDP kanye nokuthi umphakathi kumele ubambe iqhaza ekuhlanganisweni kohlelo lwe-IDP . AmaKomidi Ewadi adinga ukwakha icebo lokuqinisekisa ukuthi umphakathi uyaziswa ngezindaba zomkhandlu ukuze nomkhandlu nawo waziswe ngezindaba zomphakathi nezimpendulo zawo ezinhlelweni nasezinqumweni zomkhandlu . Izincwadi - lezi yizincwadi ezibhekiswe ekomidini noma izincwadi ezithunyelwa yikomidi . Incwadi ngayinye kufanele yaziwe yikomidi njengoba zisuke zikhishwa egameni lalo . Omunye yemisebenzi ebaluleke kakhulu kamasipala ukuthola izidingo zezakhamizi zawo kanye nokuthi ungabhekana kanjani nalezi zidingo . Bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika kumele bakhuthazwe ukufunda ulimi lwabamnyama futhi izinhlelo zikahulumeni kumele zisebenze ukwenza lokhu kwenzeke . Ukuthuthukiswa kwezimboni okufana nokwenziwa kwemikhiqizo yezolimo , ezokuvakasha , ezokudoba izinhlanzi namabhizinisi amancane lakho kungezeka khona . Yabelanani ngemiqondo nalo lonke iqembu . Ukuhlola umsebenzi weziphathimandla . Indlela yokuxazulula inkinga yithuluzi elibalulekile lokusiza amaKomidi Ezigceme . Ake sibheke isibonelo ngezansi nokuthi ingasetshenziswa kanjani esimweni sangempela . Melana / bhekana nesimo - ubhekane kanjani nengxabano ? Esimeni esihle kakhulu , ingxenye enkulu yalolu lwazi ibizobe isihlanganiswe kusenesikhathi ngabohlelo lwe-CBP abaqokelwe lo msebenzi , kodwa qinisekisa nekomidi lesigceme nekhansela uma kukhona imithombo yolwazi enokusebenziseka . Okuqondiwe ngokobungako bezwe nezilwandle okungaphansi kokuvikeleka ( esikhathini samanje cishe izigidi eziyi-7.9 zama-hectares ezwe , amakhilomitha angama-848 ogu nezi-4 172km2 zolwandle kuvikelekile ) . Umkhandlu kamasipala kufanele uhlole ukuthi ungazifeza kanjani izinhloso zawo ngendlela efanele . Wenza lokhu ngokuxhumana nemiphakathi kanye nezinhlangano zomphakathi mayelana nezinga lendlela osebenza ngayo . Khumbula : ababambe iqhaza bangaba yingxenye yamaqembu angaphezu kwelilodwa , futhi ababambe iqhaza akubona nje kuphela labo ababanga umsindo kakhulu ! Iqhaza lamaKomidi Ezigceme ukuba aphinde edlulele nasekuvumeleni kanye nasekwenzeni ngcono imizamo yomphakathi yokufeza amaphupho akumaprojekthi ozenzela wona . Amaqembu okusebenza noma amaKomidi amiswe emphakathini ukwenza izinhlelo ezithile azozuza ngalolu lwazi oluyisisekelo lokuphatha iprojekthi . Ukuqinisa ukukwazi ukuhlela kukahulumeni . Aqinisekisa ukumeleka kwalabo okubanjiswene nabo kumakomidi amaphrojekthi amancane . Ungoti wezobulili , noma umuntu onolwazi mayelana nezindaba zobulili , kumele abe yingxenye yawo wonke amaqembu alinganisayo ezinhlelo ezinkulu . Kumele kube khona umzamo owenziwayo ukuba nabo bobabili abesifazane nabesilisa bemelelekile kulawa maqembu . Izinxenye ezihlangeneyo zikahulumeni wendawo othuthukisayo ngendlela yebhajethi nendlela yomthetho kamasipala , ukuphathwa okwesekwe ngokwendawo , ukuphathwa kokusebenza kwabasebenzi bakamasipala kanye nohlelo lokuthuthukisa ukuhlanganisa ( i-IDP ) ngakunye kunikeza amathuba okubamba iqhaza komphakathi ezinqumweni zikamasipala . Ukuthola nokugcina lokhu kuzinza kudinga ukuhlanganiswa kwamaphuzu amaningana , hhayi ukuthi onke angaphansi kokulawulwa uhulumeni . Umnotho okhulayo , ukukhula kwamathuba emisebenzi nemali engenayo , ukwehla kokungalingani , ezemfundo ezithuthukayo , izimo ezikahle zamabhizinisi nokukhuphuka emsebenzini kuyoba nomthelela osemqoka ekuhlanganiseni abantu baseNingizimu Afrika . Izinhlelo ezifana nohlelo lukasenzangakhona , ukuthuthukiswa komnotho wabantu abamnyama nokuguqulwa kwezindawo kuyimpumelelo enkulu uma umnotho ukhula nesimo sezemfundo sithuthuka . Ngaphandle kwendawo enjalo , lezi zinhlelo zingakhuphula izinga lenkinga yomphakathi . Lolu hlelo lwenza izihlongozo eziningana ukuthuthukisa ukusebenza kahle kwezinhlelo , ikakhulukazi lezo ezimayelana nokwandiswa kwamathuba ezomnotho kulabo ababencishwe amathuba . Ukuthintana nemibiko - iKomidi Lesigceme lenza inkundla , isibonelo , ukuhlela umhlangano womphakathi , ukukhuluma emhlanganweni wesitokofela , ukukhuluma emhlanganweni weqembu lezemidlalo , njll . ukuletha ulwazi nemibiko emphakathini mayelana nezinqumo zomkhandlu nezindaba eziphakanyiswe ngumphakathi ebezibikwe ekhanseleni noma emkhandlwini . Akwethulwe imibono ehlukahlukene ngolwazi komasipala babo olungaba wusizo ekuhleleni . Thatha izimpendulo uzibhale kwifliphushadi ukuze bonke balubone . Indlela ye-WID ithatha abantu besifazane njengabamukeli bosizo lwentuthuko abangenaqhaza , kunokuba ngama-ejenti aneqhaza ekuguquleni kanye nasekushintsheni izimo zabo zomnotho , zenhlalonhle , zezombusazwe kanye nezamasiko . Umphumela obalulekile kwaba ukuthi ukukhathazeka kwabesifazane kwakubhekwa kodwa njengezindaba ezihlukene , kwaholela ekuncishweni kwabo amathuba ohlelweni lombuso kanye nasezinhlakeni zomphakathi . Ngokuyiqiniso , indlela ye-WID ibhekana nezindaba zabesifazane njengezingahlobene nezinkinga ezinkulu zentuthuko njengezindaba zamalungelo abantu , ukubusa ngentando yeningi , ukuvikelwa kwemvelo , ukuhlangana komhlaba , uxolo kanye nokuqeda izikhali , njll . Umphathi wezokuphathwa kwemisebenzi yomphakathi kumele abe khona , abe nomsebenzi wokulawula inqubekela phambili ngokomsebenzi wabaphathi beminyango kubandakanya ukuhola esigungwini sokuqasha , ukuhlolwa kokwenziwa komsebenzi nenqubo yokuqondiswa kwezigwegwe . Uhlu lwamaqembu amele izimfuno kufanele lusetshenziswe ukukusiza ukuwathinta uma kunemihlangano yomphakathi , noma umhlangano wezimfuno ezithile , isibonelo , ukulungiselela uvo loHlelo Lwentuthuko Oludidiyele . Izinhlelo ze-IDP zidwetshwa ngokubambisana phakathi kweminyango nawo wonke omunye umuntu olangazelela ukubona imiphumela . Izinsizakusebenza zihlukaniselwa imisebenzi esiza ukufinyelelisa imigomo yentuthuko okuvunyelenwe ngayo kamasipala . Le ndlela eyisu yenzelwe ukufinyelela emisebenzini ezosiza ekuthuthukisweni okuphelele kwendawo okuzosiza wonke umuntu . AmaKomidi Ezigceme ayimigudu yokuxhumana esemthethweni phakathi kwemiphakathi nomkhandlu . Ngabe unazo izabelomal zomndeni , kanti uma kunjalo ngabe ziquketheni ? Cela ababambiqhaza ukuba banikezele ngezibonelo zalokho abangakufaka kuzindleko kanye nasemalini engenayo kusabelomali somndeni ngesikhathi besihlelela . Qopha lezi zinto kuflipshadi ngaphansi kwamakholomu amabili , abizwa IZINDLEKO kanye ne-IMALI ENGENAYO . Izindleko zingafaka phakathi , ucingo , ugesi , imali yesikole . Imali engenayo kungafaka phakathi umholo , imalo yokuqasha ( uma kukhona abaqashe ikamelo ekhaya labo noma uma benenye indlu eqashisiwe ) , omunye umsebenzi abawenzayo ongenisa imali . Ukuthoba - kuvela egameni elithi ' thoba ' elisho ukuthulisa noma ukuxolisa . Umkhandlu ' uvuma ngomlomo nje ' kwimibono neziphakamiso zomphakathi ukuze uhlale ujabule umphakathi kodwa awenzi lutho noma ucabange nganoma yiziphi zalezi ziphakamiso noma izincomo . Iphesenti lemindeni ethola izinga lamanzi eliyisisekelo , ukuthuthwa kwendle , ugesi kanye nokuthuthwa kukadodi . Kuyasiza ukuqonda ulimi olusetshenziswa kwi-PCM , nokuthi yimaphi amagama angasetshenziswa ngezinye izindlela , njengamalungu eKomidi Lesigceme angahlangabezana nala magama kwesinye isigaba . Ulimi olusetshenziswa kule mojuli ulimi oluvama ukusetshenziswa kumqondosizinda wohulumeni bezindawo baseNingizimu Afrika . Amazinga amukelekile aphansi okuphila kumele achazwe , kubandakanya nokuthi yini edingekayo engenza abantu bakwazi ukuthuthukisa lokho abakwazi ukukwenza . Le mojuli ihlukaniswe izahluko ezine ; esokuqala isahluko esiyisingeniso semiqondo ngokuphathwa kwephrojekthi bese kuba yisahluko esisodwa sesigaba ngasinye ezigabeni ezintathu . Thatha izimpendulo emaqenjini . Uma kuwukuthi umbuzo owodwa uphendulwa ngamaqembu angaphezu kwelilodwa qikelela ukuthi wonke amaqembu ayawuphendula . Isibonelo , ungacela iqembu elilodwa ukuba liphendule umbuzo owodwa , elinye liphendule owesibili , noma uthathe izimpendulo ezimbalwa eqenjini elilodwa bese wedlulela eqenjini elilandelayo . Izinto ezizosetshenziswa - kuyasiza ukuhlela kusenesikhathi izinto ezizodingeka , inani lazo nokuthi zizosetsheziselwani . Lokhu kungahlanganisa izinto ezisemqoka ezifana namaphepha namapeni kanye namafomu , ama-laptop kanye nama-data projector . Ukuxhumana - ingxabano ingenzeka ngokuhambisana nesu elilungile elizosetshenziswa ukufinyelela emgomweni okuvunyelenwe ngawo . Isibonelo , bonke abaneqhaza bangavumelana ukuthi iziphathimandla zikahulumeni kufanele zilethe izinsizakalo ezidingekayo . Abanye abahlali bangafisa ukuthi kulethwe imali yokuqeqesha , kodwa abanye bengabona ukuthi amakhompyutha amaningi angasiza ukuxazulula inkinga yezinsizakalo ezingezi ngendlela efanele . Ukuxhumanisa uhlelo lwe-CBP nolwe-IDP kunikeza ithuba lokuqinisekisa ukuthi uhlelo lwe-IDP lususelwa endaweni futhi lwenza kube lula ukuqonda imigomo yokubamba iqhaza yoMthetho Wezinhlelo Zomasipala wezi-2000 . Yiba nezingxoxo ezingabekelwe migomo eminingi nabantu abawumthombo wolwazi ubagqugqzele ukubuza imibuzo . Sebenzisa izingxoxo ukuhlonza abantu abangenawo amandla okuzivikela . Ukuqala imikhandlu ye-AIDS endaweni kubo bonke omasipala abayisishiyagalolunye . Umkhakha ozimele uqasha cishe abasebenzi baseNingizimu Afrika abangamakota amathathu futhi utshale imali engaphezu kokubili kokuthathu nemali esebenzile ye-R&D . INingizimu Afrika idinga umkhakha ozimele osebenza kanzima otshala imali endaweni enenzuzo . Ngesikhathi inzuzo ihamba phambili ebhizinisini , izinkampani angeke zikhule ngaphandle uma zisebenza endaweni lapho amathuba emisebenzi namazinga emiholo kukhuphuka khona . Umthetho udinga amabhizinisi abhekelela ukuqasha ngokulingana , ukuthuthuka komnotho wabantu abamnyama , ukuthuthukiswa kwamakhono , okwasendaweni , ukuthuthukiswa kwamabhizinisi amancane , ukuzibophezela enhlalakahleni yomphakathi nokuningana okufunwa yindawo leyo okufana namasu okuthuthukisa ezokumbiwa phansi kwaleyo ndawo . Kulo mqondosizinda onzima , kungaba wusizo lwesikhathi eside lwawo wonke amabhizinisi ezwe akhula ngokushesha , abantu abaningi bathole imisebenzi . Leli thebula elisekhasini elingemuva kwaleli liyithemplethi engasetshenziselwa ukukhombisa izindawo zokusebenza ezibalulekile zohlelo lokusebenza . Ama-KRA aphuliwe enziwa imisebenzi enamazinga omsebenzi okuyiNANI , IZINGANHLE , ISIKHATHI kanye NEZINDLEKO okunanyathiselwe kuwo . Ama-KPI kanye nalabo abenza imisebenzi ehlukahlukene kumele nakho kukhonjiswe ukuze kube khona indlela yokuqapha inqubekelaphambili . Amaphuzu abekwe ngezansi . Ngenxa yokwehluka kwamaphrojekthi kwamanye kanye nezinselelo ezingase zivele , lesi sigaba sisemqoka . Umphumela walesi sigaba wuhlelo lomsebenzi olusemthethweni oluyohola ithimba lephrojekthi kuzo zonke izinyathelo zephrojekthi . Ukwahlukahlukana ngaphakathi enhlanganweni noma emphakathini kwamukela ukwahluka phakathi kwabesilisa , abesifazane , amasiko kanye nobuzwe ukuqinisa ukubekezelelana kokwahlukana , ukuze lokhu kwahlukahlukana kwamukele lokhu kwahlukana . Lokhu ukulwela ukuxhumana okuhambisanayo , ukuze inhlangano noma umphakathi uxhumane futhi usebenzele izinhloso zawo . Kuyomele kutholakale ozoxhasa ngemali ukuhlinzeka ngenkokhelo yabanakekeli , kanye nezinye izindleko zeloli . Umuntu ozosiza ngemali kudingeka aqoqe izimali zokukhokhela amaphasela okudla . Ishejuli iyithuluzi eliwusizo elisiza abagqugquzeli ukuhlela izinyathelo okumele zilandelwe ukufeza uhlelo lwesigceme . Ishejuli yohlelo lwe-CBP ingehluka , kuye ngomphakathi umgqugquzeli asebenza nawo . Isibonelo , endaweni eyipulazi lezentengiso kungadingeka ukuba kube kube okwenziwayo kusihlwa okubandakanya umphakathi , imihlangano yona nekomidi lesigceme yona ibanjwe emini . Emphakathini lapho iningi lezakhamuzi ziqeqeshekile khona noma lingosomabhizinisi kungaba nzima ukubandakanya umphakathi ngenxa yengcindezi yomsebenzi . Abagqugquzeli bangadinga uhlelo oluzosebenza kanye kusihlwa noma izinsuku ezimbili kusihlwa ukuqoqela ndawonye izakhamuzi bese okunye ukuhlela kwenziwa emini . Ubude besikhathi sokuhlela esibekelwe ukuhlela singancishiswa uma ukuhlaziywa kwesimo sekuphothuliwe noma uma sekuphothulwe ingxenye yakho ngoba lokho kungonga isikhathi kulolu daba . Umkhandlu kamasipala ungaphinda udlulisele kumaKomidi Ezigceme eminye imisebenzi kanye namandla . Umkhandlu kufanele wenze amalungiselelo afanele okuphatha ukuze amaKomidi Ezigceme akwazi ukwenza imisebenzi yawo ngendlela nangempumelelo . Imihlahlandlela yoKwakhiwa Nokusebenza KwamaKomidi Ezigceme Kamasipala , uMqulu Kahulumeni uNomb 27699 , ka-Juni 2005 - Imihlahlandlela ichaza ukuthi iKomidi Lesigceme lizimele , liyinhlangano enikeza izeluleko futhi kufanele lingachemi ekusebenzeni kwalo ngaphandle kokwesaba , ukukhetha noma ukubandlulula neqhaza elibalulekile elidlalwa yiKomidi Lewadi njengomhlanganisi wokuqinisekisa ukubamba komphakathi iqhaza . Okwamanje iqhaza labaholi bendabuko alikakachazwa kahle ohlelweni olusha lukahulumeni wendawo . Izinhlaka zendabuko zisabalulekile ezindaweni zasemakhaya . Isibonelo , KwaZulu-Natal iziphathimandla zezendabuko zabamba iqhaza elibalulekile ohlelweni lwamanzi nokuthuthwa kwendle olubizwa nge-Isulabasha / Mvunyane kanye nasekomidini lesifunda lokuhlela , iMaluti District Planning Committee . Yize imisebenzi yeziphathimandla zezendabuko ingakacaciswa , kumele zilibambe iqhaza ohlelweni lwe-CBP ezindaweni zasemakhaya . Yizona ezisebenzela izinguquko futhi zibalulekile njengoba kungenwa ngazo emiphakathini yazo ngoba ziyahlonishwa emiphakathini yazo futhi zinethonya ebantwini . UKWAHLUKAHLUKANA KUNJENGENGXUBE : bonke abantu abasebenzela inhlangano banjengezingcezu ezincane zengxube ; bonke bahlukile kodwa bahlangana bonke babe yinto eyodwa . Ukusebenza ngempumelelo kwendlela engaphakathi kuhulumeni yisihloko okuxoxiswana ngaso kabanzi . Izinhlaka ezahlukene zikahulumeni zihlobene , kudingeka sithole izindlela zokuqinisekisa ukuthi zisebenzisana ngempumelelo nangokubambisana . Lolu hlelo luhlongoza ukuguqula indlela isuke ekuzameni ukuthola izinhlelo zezinhlaka ezintsha , ezingasimamisi , kuyiwe ekutholeni nasekusombululeni ukungasebenzi kahle okuthile ekulawuleni nakwezamakhono . Uhulumeni kumele athuthukise ukulawula kwakhe uhlelo , kubandakanya izivumelwano zokuxolelana phakathi kwesifunda nomasipala bezindawo lapho okunokuphindaphindeka noma ukungqubuzana khona ngokwabiwa kwemisebenzi nezisetshenziswa . Izifundazwe kumele zigxile emisebenzini yazo esemqoka bese zithuthukisa amakhono azo okusekela nokubheka ukusebenza kohulumeni bezindawo . Umbuso wobandlululo washiya ifa lezezindawo elibi . Ngesikhathi imindeni eyizigidi ezilinganiselwa kwezi-3.2 isihlomulile ekwakhiweni okusha kwezindlu , [ 1 ] nemisebenzi nengqalasizinda kuhlinzekwa emiphakathini eminingi , yincane inqubekela phambili eyenzekile ekuqedeni ukungalingani okujulile kwezezindawo . Kwezinye izikhathi , inqubomgomo yangemva konyaka we-1994 iqinise ukuhlukana ngokwezindawo ngokubeka izindlu zabahola imali encane ngasekugcineni kwamadolobha . Umbuzo 2 Kungabe umbhalo weprojekthi uyazichaza yini izinjongo ezizuzekayo nezicacile eziphendula ngobulili , imiphumela kanye nezinkomba zokusebenza ezihambisana nezinjongo zentuthuko yomhlaba wonke ? Indlela yokuqala kahle wukucela omdala eqenjini ukuba asho isigameko asikhumbulayo esenzeka esenzeka kunazo zonke . Sebenzisa leso sigameko sibe ngesokuqala ohlelweni lwezigigaba . Qala ngokuloba izikhathi ngokulandelana kwazo ephepheni ulunamathisele odongeni . Kuyasiza ukucela abantu ukuba babhale izigigaba emakhadini bese bewanamathisela ephepheni lohlelo lwezigigaba elisodongeni . Uma ukubhala kuyinkinga umgqugquzeli angababhalela izigigaba ohlelweni lwezigigaba ephepheni . Lolu hlelo lwezigigaba olusephepheni kumele luhlale odongeni ukuze kwengezwe kulona nomphakathi ukwazi ukuloba kulona . Sebenzisa amanothi esifundo emakhasini ama-87- 92 bese ugcwalisa ngokwengeza olunye ulwazi . Qhakambisa umehluko phakathi komgqugquzeli wesigceme , umgqugquzeli kamasipala kanye nelungu lekomidi lesigceme , uqinisekise ukuthi ababambe iqhaza bayaliqonda iqhaza lohlelo lwe-CBP nokuxhumana kwalo namakomidi ezigceme . Le nkundla yabona ukuthi abanawo amakhono enele yase ifuna ukwelulekwa kwangaphandle , ukwesekwa kanye nezimali . Ngo-1992 , banxusa i-Corplan , okuyinhlangano yomphakathi engekho ngaphansi kukahulumeni yase-East London , ukuba iyisize ngokwenza uhlaka kanye nokusebenza kwendlela efanele ye-LED . Bakwazi ukuhekana nokwesweleka kwamakhono obungcweti nakwezokuphatha kulelo dolobha kanye nokuthola imali evela emhlabeni jikelele . Kungabe seluke lwaba khona uqeqesho lokuthi isetshenziswa kanjani imihlahlandlela ehlanganise ubulili kubona bonke abasebenzi bokuphathwa kweprojekthi ? Cela ababambe iqhaza ukuba bafunde isifundo sokubonakalayo esingezansi ebese ubuyekeza izigaba ezahlukene kwindlela yokulamula , xoxani ngokuthi kwenzekani esigabeni ngasinye nibhekise emanothini asesigabeni 5.6 . Ukwakha indawo enesimo esivumela ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi . Isibonelo , ukunikeza umphakathi amagama nemininingwane yokuxhumana ngokuphathelene nezinsizakalo ezifana nokuqoqwa kwezibi , imitholampilo kanye namagama abasebenzi okungaqondiswa kubo izikhalazo . Lokhu kudonsa ihora neqembu elixube abantu abasemqoka asebeyizakhamuzi zewadi okungenani iminyaka eyishumi . Imisebenzi yobulili yezinkoleloze izobhebhetheka kanti nomsebenzi ongalingani phakathi kwabesilisa kanye nabesifazane okungashaywa ndiva . Indikimba ebuya njalo kulolu hlelo ukuthi umgudu wokuzibophezela kudingeka uqiniswe . Umphakathi kudinga kuwucacele ukuthi ubani okumele abophezeleke ukwenza okuthile . Kumele kube nezindlela zokwenza ukuthi bonke abaholi emphakathini bakwazi ukuphendula ngokuziphatha kwabo . Ngesikhathi amaqembu ehlangene wonke cela ilungu elilodwa leqembu ngalinye ukuba liphendule umbuzo owodwa wemibuzo , uma unamaqembu angaphezu kwamathathu amanye amamqembu angongeza kuphela kulezo zindaba okungakhulunywanga ngazo ngesikhathi esidlulile . AmaKomidi Esigceme amele izimfuno namaqembu ahlukahlukene . Isibonelo , amanye amalungu angamela iqembu labakhokhintela , amanye iqembu labesifazane , amanye izinhlangano zentuthuko kanti amanye izinhlangano zamabhizinisi . Ngaso leso sikhathi amaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele asebenzisane ukuqinisekisa ukuthi imibono yomphakathi inendawo lapho ibekwa khona nokuthi imibono yawo yemukelwa ngendlela ezuzisa umphakathi . Kungenzeka kungabi lula ukuphendula zonke izidingo , kodwa ngokwamandla anawo amaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele afune indlela elungile nesiza umphakathi . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angabuye azithole esesimweni sengxabano nabanye bakahulumeni ababambe iqhaza abasebenzisana nabo , futhi ukuba nekhono elifanele lokuqeda nokwehlisa nokuxazulula ingxabano kungawasiza ekwenzeni umsebenzi wawo . Inqubomgomo esemthethweni izama ukuphakamisa imiphakathi leyo ethatha indima ngomdlandla ekuphatheni intuthuko yabo , befuna amalungelo abo kanye nokumela izibopho zabo , banikela ngosizo ezakhiweni zamaqembu okubusa kumazinga ahlukene , ikakhulukazi amazingeni ewadi kanye nomasipala . Omasipala abaningi bakhe izinqubomgomo noma izinhlaka zabo ezihamba ngomthetho ezizosetshenziswa amakomiti amawadi komasipala babo . Izinqubomgomo zikhombisa umthetho wokwakha , wokuhambisa kanye nomsebenzi wamakomiti wamawadi komasipala babo bese zibonise indlela nezinqubo ezigqamile ezizokwazi ukusiza ukuhambisa amakomiti amawadi ngempumelelo . Izinqubomgomo kufanele zixutshwe ngoba omasipala bahlukile futhi bafanele bazame ukubhala izinqubomgomo ezifanele izidingo zabo ukuze bazokwazi ukusiza imiphakathi yabo kahle ngempumelelo . UHULUMENI WENDAWO UTHATHWA NJENGOKUTHI ungumkhakha kahulumeni oseduze nabantu . Ukumbandakanya umphakathi ekuvezeni izidingo nasekwenzeni izinqubomigomo nezinhlelo yindlela esebenza kahle yokuphendula izidingo zomphakathi . Njengoba kungelula ukuba wonke umuntu azimbandakanye , amaKomidi Ezigceme enziwe njengesakhiwo sokwenza ukuxhumana . Kodwa-ke , ukuxhumana kufanele kwenzeke ngendlela ehlelekile . lesi sahluko sibheka iqhaza lamaKomidi Ezigceme ekuthathweni kwezinqumo zomkhandlu nokuthi awenza kanjani umsebenzi wawo ekuqinisekiseni ukuthi umkhandlu uzinikele ekwenzeni ekufezeni nasekuphenduleni izidingo zomphakathi . Amakhansela esigceme akhethwa ngabavoti ukuba abe semkhandlwini kamasipala ngokumelwa ngokobuningi benhlangano , amakhansela abizwa ngama-PR , noma njengamakhansela ewadi . Amakhansela esigceme kungenzeka futhi amele iqembu lepolitiki eliphikisayo noma azimele noma amele iqembu elimele izimfuno , njengenhlangano emele abakhokhi bentela . Izindlela zokuqhuba uhlelo lwe-CBP zihlinzeka amakomidi ezigceme ngenqubo ehlelekile yokuhlela nokusebenzisa lolu hlelo ukuze bakwazi ukwenza okulindeleke ukuba bakwenze . Baba nohlelo lwesigceme kanti ukusebenza kohlelo lwesigceme , ukulandelwa nokulinganiswa kwalo kwenza babambe iqhaza kulolu hlelo unyaka wonke . Ikhansela lewadi lingumgcinisihlalo Wekomiti Lewadi . lingakhetha ikhanseli emele ngokulingana noma iliphi ilungu lekomiti lewadi ukuba ibe ngumgcinisihlalo yokuhambisa umhlangano . I-Batho Pele indlela yokuziphatha ngaphakathi kwabanye abantu , ukuzilungiselela ukumemezela amalungelo abo nezidingo kanye nokuzimisela ukubasiza bafake okuthile okuyigugu ezimpilweni zabo . I-Batho Pele ukuzimisela kwabanye abantu okunkeneneza eminyakeni yonke yokuba nozwelo kuluntu . Ukuba wuhlaka olugqugquzela ukusebenza komphakathi , ikakhulukazi ngokusebenzisa uhlelo lwe-IDP nolukamasipala lokwenza isabelomali . AmaKomidi Esigceme kungenzeka angaphazamisi ukusebenza komkhandlu , lokhu kufaka phakathi ukunganiki imiyalo kwiziphathimandla umsebenzi wazo okunguthatha izinqumo zenqubomgomo yomkhandlu . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme asebenza kahle uma enikezwa amaphothifoliyo ngokwezinhlaka kanye nemikhakha okuvele babamba iqhaza kuyo . Isibonelo , ilungu elimele abalimi linganikezwa iphothifoliyo yeZolimo , noma ilungu leKomidi Lesigceme elinguthisha linganikwa iphothifoliyo yeZemfundo . Lokhu akulula ukuthi kwenzeke ezigcemeni ezihlakazeke kakhulu . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme anganikezwa amaphothifoliyo angaphezu kweyodwa . Inhloso ye-IDP kungukuqinisekisa ukuthi lezo zinsizakusebenza ezikhona kumasipala zisetshenziselwa ukwenza amaphrojekthi nezinhlelo ukuze kuhlangatshezwane nalokho okuvunyelwene ngakho kwezentuthuko okubekwe phambili ohlwini lokubalulekile . Uhlelo lwe-IDP yithuluzi elisemqoka eliqinisekisa ukuthi lawo maphrojekthi ahlonzwa nawenziwa ngumasipala ahambisana nezidingo zomphakathi . Ekulweleni ukuba bonke abantu bathole imisebenzi eqhakambisa isithunzi sabo , okusemqoka okumele kuqalwe ngakho esikhathini esifishane kumele kube wukukhulisa amathuba emisebenzi nokukhuthaza ukungena kwabantu abasha emisebenzini , ngesikhathi kubhekelelwa ukuvimbela ukukhishwa noma ukuncishiswa kwemibandela ekhona yokusebenza . Amanye amathuba emisebenzi angeke akwazi ukuvumela ngokushesha abantu ukuthi baphile impilo abayifisayo . Ukuthuthukisa impilo esimeme , kusemqoka ukuthi abantu noma imindeni , kungakhathalekile ukuthi ithola imali engakanani , bathole imisebenzi efana nezinga eliphezulu lezemfundo , ukunakekelwa ngokwezempilo noma ezokuthuthwa komphakathi . Kusemqoka futhi ukuthi umuntu olahlekelwe umsebenzi akwazi ukuthola umsebenzi ezinhlelweni zemisebenzi kahulumeni noma ezinhlelweni zemisebenzi egxile emphakathini . Ngalezi zindlela , inqubomgomo kahulumeni nokwenza komphakathi kusiza abantu ukuthola imisebenzi , kuhlinzeke ukuphila okusimeme kubasebenzi abampofu . Ukuxhumana kuyinqubo ephithene ngoba kufaka phakathi abantu abaqhamuka ezindaweni ezahlukahlukene . Ngakho-ke ikhwalithi yokuxhumana ibalulekile . Ukuxhumana kufaka phakathi izinto ezahlukahlukene . Ukuxhumana kunezinhlaka ezahlukahlukene njengokukhuluma , ukubhala , ukuxoxa nokulalela . IKomidi Lesigceme lingakhuthaza ukuthuthukiswa komnotho wendawo ngokugcina umphakathi wazi ngezinto ezintsha kanye namathuba . Lingenza amakhansela azi ngezinkinga ezitholwa ngamalungu omphakathi afuna ukuziqalela amabhizinisi amancane . Uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini lugxile embonweni nalokho okungamandla / okungamathuba esikhundleni sezinkinga . Lokhu kusho ukuthi izinhlelo zenziwe ngokususelwa ezintweni ezisemqoka umphakathi ofisa ukuba zenzeke , hhayi ezinkingeni ezisemqoka . UMbiko KaHulumeni ukhomba izinkundla okufanele zibe khona ' ukwenza kube lula ukuba amaqembu asungule futhi / noma abe negalelo ekwenziweni kwenqubomgomo , kanye nokubamba iqhaza ekulandelweni nasebuyekezweni kwayo kanye nasezinhlelweni zesabelomali esenziwa ngokubambisana , okuhloswe ngaso ukuxhumanisa izinto ezisemqoka emphakathini kanye nezinhlelo zengqalasizinda . Kulesi sigaba umlamuli uyazazisa ebese ebeka imigomo . Ukuyenza nokuhlaziya - lesi yisigaba lapho iphrojekthi eyenziwa khona , futhi sibandakanya ukuhlaziya okuqhubekayo nokuhlela okuphindwayo ukuqinisekisa impumelelo yayo . Amakhansela esigceme aba ngosihlalo bemihlangano yeKomidi Lesigceme futhi abiza imihlangano yomphakathi . Amakhansela angumxhumanisi phakathi komphakathi nomkhandlu futhi azinikele kumawadi awo . AmaKomidi Esigceme aba ngumxhumanisi phakathi komphakathi nekhansela . Ukuqinisekisa ukubamba iqhaza ngokuphelele nenqubekela phambili ekutholeni isixazululo umlamuli kufanele ahlole ukuguquka kwesimo sohlangothi ngalunye : anqume ngendlela yokubhekana nezinkinga , anqume ukuthi kufanele yini kube nemihlangano eyehlukene yezinhlangothi nomlamuli ; abheke izimfuno zezinhlangothi nokulindelekile , hhayi isimo ( lokho okusho indawo olumi kuyo ) ; aveze konke okungenzeka kukhethwe kukho akubhale phansi ; agqugquzele okufanayo nokungenzeka kushintshwane ngakho , isibonelo : mhlawumbe kwakhiwe umtholampilo wokudlulisela nezindlu zangasese kuphela erenke yamatekisi ebese kuthi kwi-IDP elandelayo kufakwe izitende zabathengisi nomtholampilo osebenza ngokuphelele : lokhu kwenziwe ngokuvumelana . Uhlelo lwesigceme luyisisekelo senqubo yohlelo lwe-CBP ekuqinisekiseni ukuthi umphakathi ubamba iqhaza ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Kusemqoka ukuqikelela ukuthi kukhishwa umbhalo osezingeni elifanele ukuze uhlelo lube negalelo ohlelweni lwe-IDP . I-CBP ikhuthazela imiphakathi ukuba ize nezixazululo ngokwayo . Ihlose ukuthuthukisa izinhlelo zokwenziwayo ezisebenza ngempela ngokubeka eminye yemisebenzi yokuhlela emahlombe ezakhamizi ngokwazo emahlombe . Kuyini okungamandla , ubuthakathaka , amathuba , nokuyizinselelo ( okuboniswe ekhasini lemininingwane yendawo ) ? Khetha abantu ukuthi badlale izindawo zamalungu ekomidi , usihlalo , unobhala . Isibonelo : Abantu abangama-54 babamba iqhaza ekuhleleni . Amaqembu ahlanganisa abantu abasebenzela abaqashi babo - abawufundele umsebenzi nabasebenzisa ikakhulukazi izandla zabo - abazisebenzayo , abangaqashiwe , abesifazane abaphila ngabodwane bebe benezingane . Ilungu lekomidi lesigceme , uNksz Mofolo nekhansela lendawo , uMnu Smith , bahambela yonke imihlangano . Abagqugquzeli kwakungoMnu Jones noNksz Mpefu . UMnu Mars woMnyango Wezokuphatha Nezomdabu wayekhona kanti nomhleli wedolobha , uMnu M Zungu , naye wayekhona . Amalogifreyimu amathebula agcwaliswa yilabo abaphethe iphrojekthi . La mathebula ethula ngokufingqiwe izinhlelo zephrojekthi . Inqubo yokugcwalisa amalogifreyimu ingabonakala inzima kodwa anikeza imininingwane esemqoka , futhi kubalulekile ukuyiqonda . Kusemqoka empumelelweni yephrojekthi . Futhi ngesikhathi esifanayo , amalogifreyimu ayosiza ukwakha ukusimama nokufunda kulabo ababandakanyeka kwiphrojekthi . Izinhlelo zokulawula - izinhlelo ezibandakanya ukuqapha kanye nokukala inqubekelaphambili ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izinhloso zeprojekthi kuyahlangatshezwana nazo , ukuhlonza ukwehluka ohlelweni ukuze kuthathwe izinyathelo zokulungisa . Kubandakanya izinyathelo zokuvimba izinkinga ezingavela , ukuqhathanisa umsebenzi owenziwayo kanye nalowo osohlelweni . Uhlaka lomthetho kamasipala luyashicilelwa ukuthola imibono yomphakathi . Ngokuqinisekisa ukuthi ababambe iqhaza enqubweni ye-CBP babammeli ezehlakalweni ze-IDP ezifanele ngezakhiwo nezinqubo okumanje zilungiselelwe endleleni ye-IDP equkethwe ngaphakathi Kwepheki Lemihlahlandlela ye-IDP ( ikakhulukazi Iforamu Yabamele be-IDP kanye Namaqembu Emisetshenzana Engamaphrojekthi ) . I-KPI ngayinye inemiklamo yokusebenza . Imithethomigomo inikeza izindlela eziningi zemiklamo yokusebenza futhi ingasiza amaKomidi Ezigceme uma ecubungula imiklamo yokusebenza ye-KPI . Indlela iveza ukubaluleka kwesabelomali esikhona . Lokhu kwenziwa ngukuthi i-PMS ayizimele yodwa . I-IDP kufanele ibe ngumhlahlandlela wokwenza ama-KPI . Uma i-KPI yenza imiklamo engeke yenzeke ngeke ikwazi ukuyifeza . Uhulumeni wendawo onentuthuko ugcizelela isidingo sokuveza obala , ukubophezeleka , ukuxoxisana , ukugqugquzela ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi kanye nokubambisana . Kusemqoka ukulubhala kahle uhlelo ukuqopha umbono womphakathi nokuqinisekisa ukuthi lokho kungasetshenziswa yiziphathimandla zezinga eliphezulu kanye nabanye abalethi bezidingo . Umasipala kufanele uxhumane nomphakathi ngaphambi kokwenza izinkomba zokusebenza futhi uvumele umphakathi ukuba uzimbandakanye kwinqubo yokubuyekeza . Iprojekthi ngayinye yehlukile futhi inezinhlobo zayo zezingqinamba kanye nezinkinga okumele kubhekanwe nazo . Ngakho-ke icebo elihlukile liyadingeka ukuvumela ukuphela kweprojekthi okuyimpumelelo . Khona manjalo ukunakwa okukhethekile kufanele kunikezelwe ukuqinisekisa ukulingana kobulili ekuhleleni iprojekthi . Anikeza umbiko novo ekusebenzeni komkhandlu ukuqinisekisa ukuhlinzekwa ngezinsizakalo . Ukuqonda umumo wendawo yesigceme , izindaba zezentuthuko esigcemeni nokuthi zihlobene yini nendawo . Imiphumela - kube yini umphumela wokwenza kwakho ? Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme angaba nephothifoliyo ethile ukuwasiza ukuthi amele umphakathi . Ngale ndlela amalungu aneqhaza elicacile okufanele alibambe esigcemeni futhi athola amava kanye nokuqonda izindaba ezimayelana namaphothifoliyo awo . Amalungu amaphothifoliyo azo zonke izigceme ( asebenza ngephothifoliyo efanayo ) ahlangana eminyangweni kamasipala efanele kanye nakumakomidi amaphothifoliyo ukudingida izindaba ezimayelana namaphothifoliyo awo . Umphakathi wase-Seymour uzibandakanye namaphrojekthi entuthuko amaningi kusukela ngonyaka we-1992 - wonke aphumelela ngamazinga angafani . Amaphrojekthi asemqoka enziwa kusukela ngonyaka we-1992 abekwe kafuphi lapha ngezansi . Noma kungewona wonke amaphrojekthi abukeka engenamphumela ngqo ekusizakaleni kwezomnotho kumele ukuba abhekwe njengalawo enza ukuba kuqashwe abantu asiza nalabo bantu ababenesifiso sokuqashwa noma sokuqala iphrojekthi yentuthuko . Khumbula ukuthi isabelomali kuyodingeka ukuthi sicishe sibe nemininingwane encike ekutheni sihlinzekelwe bani . Abanikelayo angeke badinga imininingwane elingana naleyo eyodingwa yithimba lephrojekthi . Yiqiniso : Lokhu kusho ukuthi sinamandla okuqinisekisa ( ukuba khona kolwazi , ukusebenza ngesikhathi , njll ) ; nanokuthi ziyazuzeka futhi zisebenziseka kalula . Inqubomgomo ngonyaka ka-1994 yayithi uhulumeni wayezokhokhela izindleko zezimali zezidingo ezintsha kanye nengqalasizinda , kanti izindleko zokugcinwa kwezindawo zikahle , kanye nezokusebenza kwendawo zizokhokhelwa abasebenzisi balezo zidingo . Ngonyaka ka-2001 kwavunyelwana ukuthi inani elithile lezidingo eziyisisekelo lalizohlinzekwa kuyo yonke imizi . Lokhu kwakuhlanganisa ukuthuthwa kukadoti , amanzi , imfucuza kanye nogesi . Inqubekelaphambili enhle seyenziwe ekuhlinzekeni ngamanzi kanye nogesi . UMthetho Wezinhlaka Zikamasipala , ka-1998 noMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , ka-2000 uhambisana noMthethosisekelo futhi uveza ukubaluleka kokubambisana futhi unikeza umhlahlandlela osemthethweni wokwakhiwa kwamaKomidi Ezigceme . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kufanele ayazi le Mithetho . Isibonelo , uMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , ka-2000 ubeka izindlela zokubusa njengokwenziwa koHlelo Lwentuthuko Oludidiyele ( oluchazwe ngenhla ) noHlelo Lokuhlola Ukusebenza . UMBUZO 3 Yiziphi izinqubo ezibalulekile zokuqapha nezokuhlola ezidingekayo ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukulethwa kwemisebenzi , futhi yikuphi ukusizakala okungaba khona ngenxa yokulinganisa inqubekelaphambili ? AmaKomidi Esigceme angasiza amakomidi ekuwanikeni ulwazi ngezihloko ezithile uma kunesidingo . Kunesidingo sokwenza ngcono ukusebenza ngempumelelo kwalezi zinsizakusebenza ezingenhla , ngokuqonda ngokushintshisana okukhona . Ukwengeza lapho , kugxilwa kakhulu ekusekeleni amabhizinisi amancane , ukukhuthaza uhulumeni nomkhakha ozimele ukuthenga impahla nemisebenzi emafemini amancane , nokukhulisa ukuthuthukiswa kwabaphathi nabanamakhono besifazane abamnyama . Umnotho okhula ngokushesha ohlukana ube yimikhakha emisha uyovula amathuba amafemu angawabantu abamnyama namabhizinisi amancane , ukukhuthaza umnotho wabo bonke abantu . INingizimu Afrika ayikhiqizi amagesi agcina ukushisa kuphela - kodwa iphinde ibe nobuthakathaka emiphumeleni yokuguquka kwesimo sezulu kwezempilo , ezindleleni zokuziphilisa , kwezamanzi nokudla , okunegalelo elikhulu kwabampofu , ikakhulu abesifazane nezingane . Ngesikhathi abezimboni nemindeni bezejwayeza lezi zinguquko , kumele banciphise umthelela wezenzo zabo ongemuhle endaweni . Lokhu kuyodinga izinguquko ezinkulu endleleni abantu abaphila basebenze ngayo . IMITHETHO KAHULUMENI WENDAWO ishayelwe ukusiza elakuleli ukuze likwazi ukusebenza ngendlela eyakhayo ukuletha izidingongqangi nokukuphucula impilo yezakhamuzi , ngokwenhlalo nangokomnotho . Njengoba ohulumeni bendawo kuyibona abalethela imphakathi izidingo , kusemqoka ukuqinisekisa ukuthi imiphakathi iyalibamba iqhaza futhi iyabeseka ohulumeni bezindawo . lesi sahluko sichaza izinhloso nemigomo yezinhlelo ezizinze emphakathini , i-CBP . Ababambe iqhaza benza imigqa emibili bebhekene . Omunye umugqa ubizwa ngokuthi ngu-A omunye ngu-B. cela ababambe iqhaza ukuba basebenzisane nababhekene nabo komunye umugqa . Cela bonke abasemgqeni B ukuba baphume endlini . Ukuqoqwa kolwazi olubhaliweyo emphakathini ngabagqugquzeli nabamele umphakathi . Lokhu kungadonsa izinsuku ezimbalwa noma kuthathe isikhathi eside , kodwa kumele kwenzeke engahlomula esihleliwe . ISahluko sesi-3 sisuselwa emibhalweni ezihloko zithi Community-Based Planning and the IDP , Guide 2 : Facilitators Guide for Community-Based Planning and Guide for Decision-Makers ebhalwe ngabe-AICDD and Development Works . Izinguquko zesikhathi eside zokuhwebelana nokutshalwa kwemali kwamazwe omhlaba kuwakha kabusha umnotho womhlaba futhi kuletha izinguquko kwezombusazwe emazweni ngamazwe . Okukhulu kule ntuthuko ukuvela komnotho okhula ngokushesha , ikakhulukazi eChina , India nase-Brazil . Emva cishe kwamakhulu eminyaka amathathu okwehlukana , ukungalingani phakathi kwezizwe kuyehla . Ukuthutheleka kwabantu emadolobheni nokukhula kwezimboni eChina nase-India kwenza ukuthi kuhlale kudingeka izisetshenziswa zemvelo esikhathini esiyiminyaka eyishumi noma ngaphezulu . Ukuvela kwabathengi abaningi emazweni asathuthuka kuyokhulisa amathuba awo wonke umnotho . Ukulwa nombuso wobandlululo kwaba ngokokuqala okusemqoka mayelana nokwakhiwa komphakathi wentando yeningi ongabandlululi ngokobuhlanga nangokobulili , lapho bonke abantu benamalungelo afanayo . Yize kwaba nenqubekela phambili ephumelelayo kusukela ngowe-1994 , iNingizimu Afrika isalokhu iwumphakathi ohlukene , lapho ubuhlanga kuseyiyona nto esemqoka ehlukanisayo . Ukuba nekhanda eliqinile kwabantu mayelana nobuhlanga nobuzwe kuyanda nokubandlulula kusalokhu kukhona . Uhlaka lwesikhungo sezwe nomnotho walo obanzi nesimo somphakathi kube nomthelela ekunciphiseni kancane ukubandlulula ngokobuhlanga , kodwa inqubekela phambili ayanele noma ayijulile ngokwenele . Nakuba inqubekela phambili yenzekile ukuthuthukisa izimpilo zabesifazane , ubandlululo , umqondo wokuthi abesilisa babaluleke ukudlula abesifazane , ukungatholi imfundo esezingeni eliphezulu , kusalokhu kukhona . Lolu hlelo lubhekene nala maphuzu ngokuwahlanganisa , lubheke okusemqoka kakhulu okumele kuqalwe ngakho njengemfundo noma ukuthuthukiswa kwezindawo zasemakhaya okuyoba nomthelela omkhulu kwabesifazane abampofu . Uhlelo Lwezentuthuko Kazwelonke luyoqondisa ukwabiwa kwezisetshenziswa esikhathini esiyiminyaka engamashumi amabili ezayo , kodwa angeke lwanquma isabelomali sonyaka . Indlela ekahle kakhulu yokukhiqiza izisetshenziswa ukusebenzisa uhlelo ukukhulisa ngokushesha umnotho . Uma umnotho ukhula ngaphezu kwamaphesenti ayisi-5 ngonyaka , intela kahulumeni nenzuzo yamafemu azimele iyophindaphindeka kabili esikhathini esiyiminyaka engama-20 ezayo . Ukuhlanganisa ukushabalaliswa kokungena kwezimali kube yisikhwama esisodwa sokwakhiwa kabusha kwendawo . Ukubamba kwesakhamuzi iqhaza kusiza futhi kuqinisekisa ukuthi uhulumeni unesibophezelo futhi uyakwethula lokho okuthembisile . Ukuba yizakhamizi akupheleli ekukhetheni abasebenzi bakahulumeni . Abasebenzi bakahulumeni nabo akulindelekile ukuba benze izinqumo ezingcono kakhulu bezenzela izakhamizi , uma izakhamizi zingabazisi ngezidingo zazo . Izakhamizi zazi kangcono kakhulu ukuthi yini eziyidingayo futhi kusemqoka ukuthi zibambe iqhaza ekwakheni izixazululo zalezi zidingo . Izakhamizi kumele zisebenzisane ngokuhlanganyela noHulumeni ukusiza ukuthuthuka kwazo . Lapha yilapho Amakomiti Amawadi angena khona adlale indima esemqoka yokuhambisa inqubo yokubandakanya umphakathi . Imihlahlandlela yenziwa ngoba baningi omasipala ebebedinga ulwazi oluwumhlahlandlela ngendlela yokumiswa kwamaKomidi Ezigceme . Iphakamisa izindlela omasipala abangahlangabezana ngazo nemibandela yoMthetho Wezinhlaka Zikamasipala , 1998 , kanye noMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , 2000 . Ukuzinikela okungcono kubaphathi kanye nabaholi bezinhlelo ukuze basebenze njengeqembu maqondana nocwaningo oluthuthukile kanye nokuphathwa ngempumelelo kocwaningo . Omasipala banezintshisekelo ezehlukene futhi bangazithola bencintisana bebodwa . Uhlelo lokulawulwa kokusebenza kumele ukuba lufake lezi zintshisekelo zibe ningi njengokwenzeka nokusimama kwazo . Kuzoba nezidingo ezehlukile emiphakathini esemakhaya kunalezo zomasipala basemadolobheni . Izinga lokuthola abantwana esizweni esimhlophe saseNingizimu Afrika laqala ukwehla eminyakeni ye-1950 neye-1960 , kanti izinga lokuthola abantwana kubantu abamnyama lona laqala ukwehla ekupheleni kweminyaka ye-1970 nasekuqaleni kweye-1980 . Kukho kokubili lokhu , ukukhula kokuthutheleka kwabantu emadolobheni namazinga angcono emfundo kwakuyimbangela yalokhu . Namhlanje isibalo sabantu baseNingizimu Afrika sikhula ngephesenti eli-1 ngonyaka futhi ngonyaka ngonyaka ngonyaka wezi-2030 , kuhlawumbiselwa ukuthi siyokhula ngephesenti eli-0.5 ngonyaka . Amakomidi ezigceme awuhlaka lwezokuhlela ( futhi bayizinhlaka ezithintekile ) okumele lumelwe enkundleni yohlelo lwe-IDP yokumeleleka kanye nasethimbeni lohlelo lwe-IDP elifanele . Uma uzwa ibinza lamagama Uhlelo Lokulawulwa Kokusebenza kusho ukuthini lokhu kuwe ? Ukubusa ngokwentando yeningi kudinga ukubamba iqhaza embusweni wentando yeningi ngokusebenzisa izwi labo bonke abomphakathi abambandakanyekayo kwinqubomgomo nakwizinqubo zombuso . Lokhu kudinga indlela yokuthatha izinqumo evulelekile nencike kubantu . Lokhu kuphinde futhi kudinge izakhamizi ezikwazi ukuthatha izinqumo , ezinovo kwingxoxo-mpikiswano nezingxoxo ezinomthelela ezimpilweni zazo kanye nokuqapha izinselelo emiphakathini yazo kanye namakhono nolwazi lokuthola izixazululo zalezi zinselelo . Ukubamba iqhaza yingxenye edingekayo yokubusa okuhle ngoba ivumela ukugeleza kolwazi phakathi kwezakhamizi nabaholi abakhethiwe kanye nokuzinikela . Kuphinde futhi kunikeze izwi kulezo zakhamizi ezithintwe kakhulu yinqubomgomo yomphakathi . Ukwakha ingqalasizinda yokungenisa amagesi emvelo angamanzi nokwandisa ukufuna ukuthola ukuphakelwa kwegesi yasekhaya ( kubandakanya ukuphenya ngokuba khona kwe-shale ne-methane yamalahle ) ukuhlukanisa ukuhlanganiswa kwamandla nokunciphisa ukukhiqizwa kwekhabhoni . Emaqenjini enu amancane xoxani ngezindlela lo mnyango ongasebenzisa ngayo i-Batho Pele ukuze ukwazi ukufinyelela ukwethula izinsizakalo ngendlela ecatshangwe nguhulumeni . Ungathathi macala - yeka zonke izimvo zibekwe kuqala ebese wengeza uvo lwakho . . zezinto ezikhona emphakathini zihambisana nezikhathi zonyaka , njengezifo , ukusetshenziswa kwabasebenzi , ezolimo , kanye nokudla okunomsoco . Le misebenzi emibili elandelayo iqhubezela ukuqonda ngokwenzekayo ngezikhathi zonyaka kanye nezimo zesikhathi eside . Ngokucacisa ngalezi zimo abahleli bayakwazi ukubikezela izigameko ezithile bese beqikelela ukuthi izinhlelo namasu abo kuhambisana nesimo . Isilinganiso sabantu baseNingizimu Afrika abahlala emakhaya sesehle ngamaphesenti ayi-10 kusukela ngonyaka we- 1994 . Namhlanje cishe amaphesenti angama-60 abantu bahlala emadolobheni . Njengoba kwenzeka emazweni omhlaba , ukuthutheleka kwabantu besuka emakhaya beya emadolobheni kulindeleke ukuthi kuqhubeke , kanti ngonyaka wezi-2030 cishe amaphesenti angama-70 abantu bazobe sebehlala emadolobheni . I-Gauteng namadolobha aseThekwini naseKapa ayizindawo zasemadolobheni ezikhula ngokushesha ngombono wokuhlela nokulethwa kwemisebenzi esemqoka . Chaza ukuthi isigaba sesibili sibandakanya ukuhlaziya ngokucophelela nokuhlanganiswa kolwazi oluqoqwe esigabeni soku-1 . Ama-KPI abuyekezwa ngonyaka ngumasipala njengengxenye yenqubo yokubuyekeza ukusebenza . Uma umasipala echibiyela i-IDP yawo kufanele futhi ubuyekeze nama-KPI . Uvo lomphakathi , ngamaKomidi Ezigceme , kufanele lusetshenziswe ekubuyekezweni kwama-KPI . Ngale ndlela i-PMS ibonwa ngumphakathi iyinto ekholakalayo . Ezolimo : zikhona yini izinguquko ezenzekile ezinhlotsheni zezithombo ezitshalwayo ? Yini imbangela yakho ? Zikhona yini izinguquko esibalweni sezilwane ezifuywayo ? Yini imbangela yakho ? Zikhona izinguquko ekufinyeleleni emadlelweni / ebungakweni bendawo eyidlelo ? Ngubani okwaziyo ukuyithola ? Amakomidi Ezigceme kudingeka azijwayeze amathuluzi kanye nezinhlelo ezingawasiza ukuhlukanisa ukulingana kobulili . Ukususa umqondo wezempi emaphoyiseni . Isinqumo sokususa umqondo wezempi emaphoyiseni , ukusuka emlandweni wawo wesihluku , kwakuyinhloso enkulu yezinguquko emva konyaka we-1994 . Ukubuyiswa komqondo wezempi emaphoyiseni kamuva nje akuzange kuwanikeze amaphoyisa inhlonipho noma kwenyuse amazinga okubopha . Uma kukhona okwenzekile , kube udlame olube umthelela wakho . Amaphoyisa kumele asuse umqondo wezempi alawulwe ngobuchwepheshe ekwenzeni umsebenzi wawo . Umasipala ABC ulungiselela i-IDP yawo . Ikhansela lesigceme neKomidi Lesigceme selazise umphakathi ukuthi umhlangano uzokwenziwa ngoMsombuluko ka-10 Julayi ngo-10.00 ekuseni eHholo Ledolobha ukuzoxoxa nge-IDP . Bathumela isaziso ezinsukwini ezintathu ngaphambi komhlangano . Emhlanganweni ikhansela lesigceme neKomidi Lesigceme litshela abantu abasemhlanganweni ukuthi sebethathe isinqumo ngalokho abacabanga ukuthi kuzoba kuhle emphakathini futhi ngaleyo ndlela sebeyalele umkhandlu mayelana namaphrojethi okufanele afakwe . Abanye abantu emhlanganweni baveza ukungeneliseki ngesikhathi esifushane sesaziso somhlangano nesikhathi , njengoba lesi kuyisikhathi lapho amalungu amaningi omphakathi esuke esemsebenzini . Abanye baveza ukuthi isidingo sabo akusona esokwakhiwa kwenxanxathela yezitolo , nakuba lokhu kungadala amathuba emisebenzi esikhathi esifushane njengoba kuchazwe kwi-IDP . Kodwa imitholampilo emisha ukusiza imijondolo elokhu iqhubeke njalo ikhula , njengoba umtholampilo okhona ungakwazi ukuhlangabezana nezidingo . Imithethomigomo ithi ama-KPI kufanele alinganiseke , afaneleke , abe nenjongo futhi ahlabe emhloleni . Abhekiswe ezinhlakeni zikamasipala zokuphatha nabasebenzi , konke okukamasipala nabasizi ngokuletha izinsizakalo umasipala anezivumelwano nabo . Abantu babamba iqhaza ngokubikelwa ngezinqumo esezithathiwe noma ngosekwenzekile . Kuhlanganisa izimemezelo zabaphathi noma zabaqhubi bohlelo ngaphandle kokulalela okushiwo ngabantu . Yize inqubo yokuhlela isungulwa ihlanganiswe wumasipala , uhlelo lwe-CBP lona luwukubambisana phakathi kwesigceme nomasipala . Lolu hlelo lungolwesigceme , emelwe yikomidi lesigceme . Umasipala uhlomisa amakhansela esigceme namakomidi ngamakhono okugqugquzela inqubo yokuhlela ezokwenza lelo nalelo komidi ligunyaze isikhathi salo sophatha izikhundla . Ukubona izidingo nokusemqoka emphakathini nokubonisana ngezixazululo zakho kusiza amakhansela namakomidi ezigceme ekwenzeni imisebenzi yabo . Isahluko sesi-2 sisuselwa Ohlelweni Oluzinze Emphakathini ne-IDP , Umhlahlandlela wesi-2 : Umhlahlandlela Wabagqugquzeli Bezinhlelo Ezizinze Emphakathini noMhlahlandlela Wabathathi Bezinqumo ohlanganiswe abe-AICDD neMisebenzi Yezentuthuko . UMTHETHO WEZINHLAKA ZIKAMASIPALA , ka-1998 uphoqa omasipala ukuba babuyekeze ukusebenza kukamasipala minyaka yonke . Isahluko 6 soMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , ka-2000 sinikeza uhlaka lokuhlola ukusebenza komasipala . Ukuhlola ukusebenza kufanele kube yingxenye yoHlelo Lwentuthuko Oludidiyele . Izithangami zesabelomali ziqinisekisa ukuthi izidingo ze-MFMA , ka-2003 ezimayelana nokubanjwa kweqhaza ngumphakathi kunqubo yesabelomali kuyahlangatshezwana nazo . Izithangami zesabelomali zikamasipala zenza ukuba Amakomidi Ezigceme akwazi ukubamba iqhaza ekuthuthukeni kwesabelomali sikamasipala . Kuyini ukuphathwa kweprojekthi ? Ukuhlola imibiko yokuhlinzeka ngezinsizakalo - i-MFMA ifuna ukuthi omasipala baveze imibiko mayelana nenqubekela phambili yokuhlinzekwa ngezinsizakalo ezindaweni zabo . Le mibiko isiza imiphakathi ukuhlola intuthuko . Ngesikhathi sokuxoxisana ngesabelomali , amakhansela , ngokusebenzisa amaKomidi Ezigceme , kufanele eluleke umphakathi mayelana nokuthi isinqumo esibalulekile sizowuthinta kanjani . Kuyadingeka impela kokubili ukuphatha ngokubambisana kanye nokusebenzisana kwayo yonke imikhakha . Imigomo yenzelwa ukuqinisekisa ukusebenza kwesimo esinemiqathango mayelana nokulethwa kwezingqalazizinda zikamasipala , esibeka imiqathango kuleyo ndlela yokusebenzisana . Udoti endaweni lapho ohlala khona awuqoqwa njalo . Abahlali bakule ndawo sebekhalaze iziqubu ezimbalwa kumkhandlu kamasipala , kodwa inkinga isaqhubeka . Umasipala uphinda uthi ezinye zezizathu ukuthi abahlali abayikhokheli irenti kamasipala kanye nentela , futhi lokhu kuphazamisa ukulethwa kwezidingo , ikakhulukazi njengoba ezinye izindawo edolobheni zikhokha ngendlela efanele , futhi uhulumeni ucabanga ukuthi kubalulekile ukuthi lezo zindawo zilethelwe kahle izidingo . Izindlela ezibuthaka , nezisebenza kabi zenza kube nzima ukuzibophezela , kuvama ukuthi kube nomphumela wokuthi kungabibikho muntu oziphendulelayo ngomsebenzi wakhe . Lolu hlelo luveza isibonelo sokuthi kwenzekani uma amanzi asedolobheni kutholakala ukuthi awaphuzeki . Abezindaba basola uNgqongqoshe Wezamanzi . Umphakathi usole usodolobha . Usodolobha usola ophethe ekusetshenzisweni kwamanzi . Ophethe ekusetshenzisweni kwamanzi usola unjiniyela . Unjiniyela uthi isabelomali sokubhekela ukusebenza kahle kwamanzi sancishiswa eminyakeni emithathu eyedlule manje amanzi awasaphuzeki . Ophethe kwezezimali kumasipala uthi isabelomali sancishiswa ngoba izindleko zabasebenzi bese zidlula izindleko zokunakekela amanzi . Usodolobha yena uthi umumo wamaholo kuxoxiswana ngawo ezingeni likazwelonke wuPhiko LwaseNingizimu Afrika Lohulumeni Bezindawo . Uphiko luthi omasipala bangaphuma kulezi zivumelwano uma bengeke bakwazi ukuzikhokhela , njalo njalo njalo . Abaholi bomphakathi bamele umphakathi ezindabeni eziseduze kakhulu nezinhliziyo zawo futhi kumele zithathwe njengezisemqoka . Laba baholi banesibopho sokuqinisekisa ukuthi ukugxeka nokukhononda kwenziwa ngesithunzi nangendlela ezinokuthula . Yize kwesinye isikhathi abaholi bomphakathi babhekele okuncane okufunwa umphakathi osabalele nohlukene , benza ingxenye esemqoka yomphakathi ophilayo wentando yeningi ebandakanya abantu entuthukweni yabo . Indlela encike ekuvumelaneni noma ezimfunweni - le ndlela ibheka ingxabano njengento eyimvelo ebudlelwaneni babantu . Le ndlela ayibheki ukuthi ngubani ' olungile ' nokuthi ngubani ' ongalungile ' engxabanweni , kodwa ukuthola isixazululo esizosiza wonke amacala . Le ndlela ifuna isisombululo sokuwina kwawo wonke amacala . Isebenzisa ukuxazulula inkinga nokusebenzisa inqondo futhi ibheka ukubhekana nengxabano ngendlela eholela kumphumela omuhle kubo bonke abantu . Lapho kunesidingo khona emibuzweni engenhla , buza uma zikhona izinguquko nokuthi zibe namthelela muni ezinhlotsheni zabantu ngokwehlukahlukana ( kuzohlinzeka olunye ulwazi ekwahlukanisweni kwabantu ngokwenhlalo ) . Umbono kahulumeni ngentuthuko kahulumeni wendawo ukudala omasipala abakwazi ukuphatha ezezimali ngemfanelo ukubhekana nezidingo zokuhlalisana kwabantu , zezomnotho kanye nezidingo eziyisisekelo zabantu babo ngendlela yokuhlanganyela kanye nangendlela exhasayo . Indima yokuthuthuka kahulumeni wendawo igxilisiwe yama Kumthethosisekelo kanye nasemibhalweni eminingi yezinqubomgomo nomthetho okukhulunywa ngakho kulesi sahluko . Indlela okucatshangwa ngayo ngoMnu Nkosi ileyo yokuthi abanye abantu endaweni banochuku futhi ababacabangeli abanye . Emqondweni wabahlali bendawo kukhona ukuthi uMnu Nkosi mubi futhi unochuku . Imihlangano yomphakathi - le yindawo ekusebenzelayo yokwabelana ngemicabango nolwazi . Imikhandlu ingabiza imihlangano yomphakathi mayelana nezindaba ezithile , noma ukubika mayelana nomphumela womhlangano noma umsebenzi ; ukunikeza imibiko eyejwayelekile emphakathini maqondana nemihlangano yomkhandlu nemihlangano yeKomidi Lesigceme , ngale kwalokho , ikhansela lesigceme , ngokumela iKomidi Lesigceme , lingabiza umhlangano ukubika mayelana nesihloko esithile ukuze lithole imibono yabahlali kulolo daba . Iphrojekthi yinoma yikuphi okwenziwayo ukuthuthukisa umsebenzi noma umkhiqizo esikhathini esithile esibekiwe . Kumele ifake ukubaluleka noma ilethe izinguquko ezinhle ngandlela thile . Iphrojekthi inesikhathi esinqunyiwe kunokuthi ibe yinqubo eqhubekayo noma eyisimbelambela , inesabelomali esichaziwe futhi ivama ukwenziwa isikhathi esisodwa . Ohulumeni abakwazi ukumela izidingo zazo zonke izakhamizi . Ngenkathi izakhamizi ziyovota , zivotela iqembu lezepolitiki elizikhethele lona ukumela izidingo zazo , abantu bayehluka , futhi banezidingo ezehlukile . Nanoma uhulumeni angazama kangakanani kunzima kakhulu ukwenelisa zonke izakhamizi . Ukubamba iqhaza kwezakhamizi kungasiza ukugcwalisa lesi sikhala ngoba zingahambisana nokuqalwe nguHulumeni nalokho ezikwenzayo futhi ngale ndlela zibeka izwi lazo ngaphambili . Kungalesi sizathu kwakhiwa Amakomiti Amawadi ukuze asize uhulumeni ekuqinisekiseni ukuthi izakhamizi zifaka okuthile ekuthathweni kwezinqumo ezizithintayo . UMqulu Wamalungelo ubandakanya namalungelo esimo somnotho nokuhlalisana emphakathini , njengelungelo lendawo enempilo , ukuthola izindlu ezanele , ukufinyelela emisebenzini yokunakekelwa ngokwezempilo kanye nokudla kanye namanzi anele . Ukuhambela imihlangano - yenza uhlu lwamalungu eKomidi Lesigceme unike yilelo nalelo lungu umhlangano okufanele liye kuwo . Isahluko soku-1 nesesi-4 zethula ulwazi ngezinhlobo zabagqugquzeli abathintekayo ekwenzeni uMhlahlandlela we-CBP kanye nabanye abehlukene abathintekayo okumele bathintwe . Ukuba yisakhamuzi esisebenza ngokuzimisela nokuhlangana komphakathi kuyadingeka ukuze kusimame intando yeningi nentuthuko . Uhulumeni angeke avele enzele abantu - kufanele asebenze nabantu , asebenze ngokubambisana nezinye izikhungo ukuhlinzeka ngamathuba okukhula kuyo yonke imiphakathi . Aqinisekisa imibono yomphakathi nokubuyekezwa kwendlela yokusebenza ukuze ihambisane nalokho okubhekwe ngumphakathi wendawo . Ama-KPI kumele abuyekezwe ngonyaka nonyaka ngumasipala njengengxenye yenqubo yokubuyekeza ukusebenza ngemfanelo futhi uma umasipala eguqula i-IDP yakhe kumele aphinde abuyekeze nama-KPI . Ukubika ngemibuzo yezimpendulo okuvela Kumakomiti Ewadi kumele kunakwe uma kubuyekezwa ama-KPI . Le nqubo iqinisekisa ukuboshezelwa futhi ithuthukisa ukuvumelana ngaphakathi komphakathi nomkhandlu . Iphinde futhi isebenze maqondana nokuqinisekisa ukuthi i-PMS ibonwa ngumphakathi njengefanele . Ukukhishwa komoya ongcolile , i-carbon dioxide namanye amagesi agcina ukushisa kuguqula isimo sezulu somhlaba , kulethe izindleko ezinkulu zomhlaba ezizoba nomthelela omubi kwabampofu . Ukukhuphuka kwamazinga okushisa , izimvula eziningi ezingalindelekile nezigameko ezinzima kakhulu zesimo sezulu kuyolindeleka ukuthi kwenzeke kakhulu e-Afrika , okuzohambisana nokusabalala kwezifo ezidalwa wukushisa nokudlondlobala kokulahlekelwa ( ngabantu nemali ) ngenxa yesomiso nezikhukhula . Ukuguquka kwesimo sezulu kunamandla okunciphisa ukukhiqizwa kokudla nokuba khona kwamanzi ahlanzekile / asebenzisekayo , okulandelwa wukufuduka kwabantu kanye namazinga okungqubuzana . Kusemqoka ukuqinisekisa ukuthi abantu abasemqoka abawumthombo wolwazi nabo bonke abangenawo amandla okuzivikela bayalibamba iqhaza kulolu hlelo ukuze umphakathi uzizwe ungabanikazi bohlelo futhi kuyiwona olawulayo . Bhala le mibuzo elandelayo kwifliphushadi , ababambe iqhaza bayiqedele emaqenjini abo amancane ngokusebenzisa ulwazi olusemanothini esifundo . Yomibili imikhakha kahulumeni nezimele ingabamba iqhaza elisemqoka ekwakheni ingqalasizinda , okubandakanya ingqalasizinda enkulu . Ngasekupheleni kokwehla kwesimo esibi somnotho ngonyaka wezi-2009 , umkhakha ozimele ubumanqikanqika ukutshala amazinga awo aphezulu emthamweni wezimali zomkhiqizo wawo eziwutholile . Ngesikhathi esifanayo , umkhakha kahulumeni ubusebenzisa kakhulu imali ngaphezu kokuyonga . Ngokubona lokhu , uhulumeni usememezele ukuguquka ekwakhiweni kokusetshenziswa kwezimali kuyiwa ekutshalweni kwezimali , isimo okumele senzeke ukulwa nokungabibikho kwenqubekela phambili . Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi , ukutshalwa kwezimali komkhakha kahulumeni kungasiza kutshalomali oluzimele . Umasipala wendawo Ewadini-ABC ubeke iphosta enkulu enikeza imininingwane yezinsizakalo ezinikezwayo . UMnu Jones akukudala ehlala kule ndawo kamasipala uza ehhovisi ukuzokhalaza ukuthi isitaladi ahlala kuso sinezibane ezenza ukukhanya okungenele . Utshelwa ukuthi kumele ajabulele nje ukuthi unendlu . Izinhlobo zabantu ngokwenhlalo kumele zihlonzwe esigabeni sokulungiselela ukuhlela bese ziqinisekiswa emhlanganweni wokwethula umphakathi , kodwa ezinye izinhlobo zabantu zingahlonzwa ngesikhathi sokuhlela . Funda isigameko ebese wenza umbono nomsebenzi kamasipala wakho futhi wenze umhlahlandlela wokubamba komphakathi iqhaza ukufeza umbono . Lungisa uhlelo lomhlangano ngaphambi kokuqala komhlangano . Lona ngumsebenzi kasihlalo kanye nonobhala . Ekusebenzeni nezinhlangano ezifanele zikahulumeni ukubika ngenqubekela phambili yezinhloso . I-MFMA , ka-2003 idinga ukuba omasipala bakhiphe imibiko mayelana nenqubekela phambili ekulethweni kwezidingo ezindaweni zawo . Le mibiko iyindlela imiphakathi eqapha ngayo ukuthuthuka . Izindawo zasemakhaya zinezinselelo ezithile . Ngaphezu kokukodwa kokuthathu kwabantu baseNingizimu Afrika bahlala kokwakubizwa ngokuthi " yizabelo " , futhi ingxenye enkulu yalaba bantu ayimile kahle kwezomnotho . Kudingeka inqubomgomo ukuletha la makhaya akulezi zindawo emnothweni wabo bonke abantu . Kodwa-ke kunezindawo zasemakhaya , lapho ezokuthutha zikahle futhi lapho kwenzeka khona ukuminyana kube kungekho ukulawulwa ngendlela kokusetshenizswa kwendawo nokubuswa kwendawo yasemadolobheni . Lokhu kudinga ukungenelela ngokushesha . Abantu babamba iqhaza ngokunikela ngezinsiza , isibonelo , ukusebenzela ukuthola ukudla , imali noma noma okuyinzuzo . INingizimu Afrika isibe nenqubekela phambili ebonakalayo ekuguqukeni kusuka embusweni wobandlululo kuya embusweni wentando yeningi . Le nguquko ibe nokuthula yize kunomlando wezwe wodlame nokuphucwa kwabantu izinto zabo . Ukuqeqeshwa okwanele : Ithimba labantu ababili kumele liqeqeshwe bese lisebenza ngokubambisana nekomidi lendawo lesigceme . Ngokubheka okwenzekile esikhathini esedlule kanye namakhono adingekayo uma kugqugquzelwa abantu , uhlelo lokuqeqeshwa lungadonsa izinsuku eziyi-15 . Ngokwezibalo eziqhamuka ocwaningweni , abesifazane benza umsebenzi womhlaba ongamaphesenti angama-67 , kodwa bahola amaphesenti ayi-10 emali yomhlaba eholwayo . Bhala phansi okuvunyelenwe ngakho : yenza zonke izinhlangothi zisayine ; kwethule lokhu ngqo kwiForamu Emele I-IDP . Ingqalasizinda ayibalulekile kuphela ekukhuliseni ngokushesha umnotho nokwandisa amathuba emisebenzi . Iphinde ikhuthaze ukukhula ngokuhlanganyela , ihlinzeke izakhamuzi ngezindlela zokuthuthukisa izimpilo zazo nokukhuphula izinga lemali engenayo . Ingqalasizinda isemqoka kwezentuthuko . Umthelela wokuguquka kwesimo sezulu usemhlabeni wonke futhi kumele kutholakale izisombululo zomhlaba wonke , ngokunaka kakhulu izimo zesifunda nezikazwelonke . Umsebenzi 1 Bheka uMthethosisekelo , hlonza izingxenye ezintathu ezikhuthaza ukubusa ngentando yeningi futhi uchaze ukuthi izingxenye ezintathu ezinhlonziwe zikugqugquzela kanjani ukubusa ngentando yeningi . Ukukwazi ukuphendula uma kukhona okungahambi kahle emabhizinisini kahulumeni kuthikamezekile ngenxa yenqubo yokuqasha enzima nengacacile , futhi kwesinye isikhathi kuba nokugxambukela okungadingekile kwezombusazwe . Sincoma izindlela ezicacile zokukwazi ukuphendula uma kukhona okungahambi kahle ngokuthuthukisa igunya lokufunwa umphakathi elibeka obala ukuthi amabhizinisi kahulumeni aletha kanjani lokho okufunwa umphakathi , ukuqinisekisa ukuthi inqubo yokuqasha isebenza ngendlela efanele futhi isobala , nokuthuthukisa ukulawula phakathi kweminyango yenqubomgomo nabanikazi bamasheya . Lokhu okuphoqayo okukabili yizona zinto ezidingekayo entuthukweni ephumelelayo kazwelonke . Ukuhlanganisa iNingizimu Afrika kuyikho kokubili okusemqoka enqubweni yokunciphisa ubuphofu nokungalingani futhi kungumphumela oqondile wokunciphisa ubuphofu ngempumelelo . Ukwakha umphakathi ohlangene , iNingizimu Afrika kudingeka inciphise ubuphofu nokungalingani ngokwandisa amathuba nemisebenzi ngokuhlanganisa umnotho , imfundo namakhono , nezindlela zokulungisa ezithile , ukuthuthukisa ukuhloniphana nokuhlangana ngokuziphatha ngendlela efunwa wumthethosisekelo ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika ngeyabo bonke abahlala kuyo , nokuthi bonke bayalingana ngaphambi komthetho ; nokujulisa ukubonga imisebenzi nokuzibophezela kwezakhamuzi komunye nomunye . Amashedula ezindleko avumela imibandela yokungena kwemali ukuthi ihlolwe ( kubandakanya iminikelo yababambe iqhaza abehlukene ) , nobubanzi beZivumelwano Zezimali ukuthi bunqunywe . Ukuhlaziya ubulili kuyithuluzi lokudalula umehluko phakathi kwabesifazane kanye nabesilisa mayelana nemisebenzi eqondene nabo , izimo , izidingo , ukuthola kanye nokulawula imithombo , kanye nokuthola imivuzo yentuthuko kanjalo nokuthatha izinqumo . Licwaninga ukuxhumana kwalezi zinto kanye namanye amaphuzu emkhakheni omkhulu wezenhlalo , ezomnotho , ezombusazwe kanye nezemvelo . Ukuhlaziya ubulili kuqukethe , okokuqala nje , ukuqoqa ulwazi olumayelana nokwehlukaniswa kobulili kanye nolwazi oluzwelana nobulili mayelana nomphakathi othintekayo . Ukuhlaziya ubulili kuyisinyathelo sokuqala ekuhleleni okuzwelana nobulili ukuze kugqugquzelwe ukulinganiswa kobulili . Yenza umsebenzi ongezansi nababambe iqhaza ebese ugqugquzela ingxoxo ebhekiswe emibuzweni . ANOHLELO - UHLELO LWESIGCEME - KANYE NOKUSEBENZA , UKUQAPHA NOKUHLOLA UHLELO LWESIGCEME OKWENZA UKUBA AQHUBEKE NOKUBA NEGALELO KUWO WONKE UNYAKA UKUZE ABHEKANE NOKUPHAMBILI OHLWINI LOKUBALULEKILE OKUQONDWAYO KWALOWO MPHAKATHI AQOKELWE UKUWUSEBENZELA .
