Ababambiqhaza baphendula imibuzo engezansi ngezinga abanikwe lona . Izinkomba ezisemqoka zokusebenza zisiza uhulumeni wasekhaya nabahlali ukukala umsebenzi owenziwe . Ama-KPI imigomo ekalekayo ' yokungenzeka ' umasipala ovumile ukuthi uzoyifeza ngesikhathi esifanele . Asiza ukubheka nokukala ukuthi umkhandlu nomasipala basebenze kanjani ngokuhambisana nezinhlelo ezibekwe kwi-IDP futhi ngale ndlela abahlali bayakwazi ukubophezelela umasipala . Ilogifreyimu ihlinzeka ngesisekelo okungalungiselwa kuso izivumelwano ngokucacisa kahle izinjongo ezilindelekile . Iphinde isize ukukhomba izinga lokuzibophezela kwabaphathi bephrojekthi nabanye ababambe iqhaza . Abagqugquzeli kumele bakulungele ukubhekana nombiko ngesabelomali esetshenziswa ngokwezidingo ovela emkhandlwini . Umphakathi ungadumala uma okunye kwalokho abakuthatha njengokusemqoka kungakhethelwanga ukuxhaswa ngemali . Ingabe lawa mazinga omsebenzi abekiwe ayahlangabezana yini nezindlela ze-SMART ? Yimaphi amaprojekthi elifisa ukuwaqala iKomidi Lesigceme ? Cabanga ngezinto ezifana namaprojekthi okuthuthukiswa komnotho wendawo , ukuqeqeshwa konompilo . Cabanga ngokuthi lawa maprojekthi engenziwa yini ngokubambisana nezinye izinhlangano zomphakathi ? Ngokuthamela imihlangano yomphakathi : Le mihlangano ingabizwa yikhansela lesigceme , yiKomidi Lesigceme noma ngumkhandlu . Bangadingida uHlelo Lwentuthuko Edidiyelwe ( IDP ) , isabelomali sikamasipala kanye nezinye izindaba ezifanele . UMthethosivivinywa Wemisebenzi , owenziwe Umnyango Wezemfundo Eyisisekelo neminye , kumele wenziwe waziwe , ukhuthaze bonke abantu ukuthi baphile ngokwemigomo yoMthethosisekelo . Uyindoda . Unomsebenzi endaweni ohlala kuyona . Unkosikazi wakho utshala imifino . Umngane wakho ekuqinisekiseni ukudayisa imifino edolobheni elikhulu ngemali enhle . Uyakufuna lokhu ngoba udinga imali yokuthenga isudi entsha yomhlangano ozayo womkhandlu kamasipala . Ayesabela abuye anikezele ngempendulo kusitatimendi senhlosombono , izindlela nezinhloso zentuthuko kanye nasekuhlonzeni amaphrojekthi e-IDP ukuzwe kuqinisekiswe ukuthi lokhu yilokho Ikomidi Lesigceme kanye nomphakathi abangathanda ukuba kwenzeke emphakathini wabo . Ukunikezwa kwezindlu kumele kuhlanganiswe nezicelo zokuxhaswa , ukuxoxisana okusemthethweni kanye nokunikezwa kwezindlu kwiphakheji eyodwa , ngalokhu kusizakala ikhasimende Ukufinyelela kwizinsizakalo ngokugcwele hhayi njengokuthile okuhlukanisiwe okuyizingcezu ngezingcezu . Ukuhlanganiswa komnotho wesifunda kungathuthukisa ukukhula komnotho kuwo wonke amazwe aseningizimu ne-Afrika . Isifunda sesikhule ngokushesha esikhathini esiyiminyaka eyishumi edlule , ngokusebenza kahle kakhulu kwezokumbiwa phansi , ezolimo , ezokuxhumana ngezingcingo nezokuvakasha . Ukufeza ukuhlanganiswa komnotho kudinga ukuvezwa kwamathuba abonakalayo lapho ukubambisana kungaletha khona inzuzo elinganayo nhlangothi zombili ; ukutshalwa kwezimali engqalasizindeni ; ukuqiniswa kwezindawo zokuhweba ezifundeni ; ukwehliswa kwentela ekhokhelwa impahla ; nokubhekana nezingqinamba zokungabibikho kwentela ekhokhelwa impahla , ezifana nokungasebenzi kahle kwezindawo zasemngceleni . Idayagramu elandelayo ikhombisa ukuthi isigaba ngasinye sokuphathwa kweprojekthi siholela kanjani ekuhlolweni kabusha kwezinyathelo kanye nokuthi umjikelezo awukho mncanyane ngokwemvelo . Indlela enkulu , esebenza ngempumelelo nekwazi okwenza okusha , esondelene kakhulu namafemu asebenza emikhakheni ehambisana nesu lokukhula . Cela iqembu elilodwa ukuba linike inkulumo futhi unike ithuba kwamanye amaqembu lokufaka imibono nokubeka uvo . Umbono usho ' iphupho ' lomphakathi , umphakathi ofisa ukuba lifezeke . Kudla isikhathi ngaphambi kokuba kuvunyelwane ngombono , ikakhulukazi ngoba imibono yezakhamuzi yehlukene ngenxa yomlando wezenhlalo nezomnotho kwalowo nalowo muntu . Lolu hlelo lunombono weNingizimu Afrika lapho wonke umuntu ezizwa ekhululekile kodwa ebambene nabanye ; lapho wonke umuntu enza konke ngokuzimisela okukhulu , izwe lapho ithuba litholakala hhayi ngokuzalwa , kodwa ngokwazi , ngemfundo nangokusebenza kanzima . Ukuthola umphakathi onjalo kuyodinga ukuguquka kwezomnotho nokugxila kakhulu emizamweni yokwakha ukukwazi ukusebenza kwezwe . Ukulwa nobuphofu nokunciphisa ukungalingani , umnotho kumele ukhule ngokushesha futhi ngezindlela ezihlomulisa bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika . Ingxabano - veza ingxabano osuke wabhekana nayo , emsebenzini , ekhaya , noma kwenye indawo . Lapha ngezansi kuboniswa izigameko ezinkulu neminyaka ezenzeka ngayo emphakathini waseBloemfontein eFree State njengesibonelo . Khuthaza amasu ezezindlu axubile nokuthuthuka kwasemadolobheni okuhlangene ukusiza abantu ukuthi bafinyelele ezindaweni nasezakhiweni zomphakathi , ezinkampanini zombuso kanye nasemathubeni emisebenzi namabhizinisi . lesi sahluko siqala ngokubheka incazelo yokuhlukahlukana . Siqhubeka sibheke izinto ezakha indlela enempumelelo yokuphatha ukwahlukahlukana futhi nezinye izindaba ezibalulekile ezinomthelela ekuphatheni ukwahlukahlukana . lesi sahluko siphetha ngohlu lokuhlola lokwakha uhlelo lokusebenza ngokwahlukahlukana . INingizimu Afrika ingahlomula ekukhuleni ngokushesha emazweni asathuthuka okuholela ekudingekeni kakhulu kwezimpahla zemvelo nasekukhuleni kwezimakethe zabathengi . Esikhathini esifanayo , lezi zimo ziletha inselelo kulawo mazwe anemali engenayo elingene ngenxa yokuncintisana okukhulu ekukhiqizeni nakweminye imisebenzi yolwazi oluhambisana nobuchwepheshe . Ukukhula kwezimakethe ezivelayo kuphinde kukhulise ukuncintisana kwamazwe ngamazwe , kubeke ingcindezi emiholweni yabasebenzi abangenamakhono emikhakheni yokuhweba . Isimo esibi kakhulu sogesi sangonyaka wezi-2008 nokunye okwenzeke kamuva sekuveze obala ubuthakathaka bezikhungo obumayelana nezinkampani zikahulumeni ezimayelana nohlaka lwengqalasizinda . Ukuvimbela lezi zinkinga kudinga amalungiselelo acacile esikhungo , ukuhlangana okusobala kwabanini masheya , imigudu ecacile yokuzibophezela nezindlela ezikahle zezezimali ukuqinisekisa ukusimama . Senza izincomo kuleyo naleyo yalezi zindawo . Imithetho elawula ukuqondisa ivama ukudida , ukudidanisa inqubomgomo nomthetho . Sihlongoza izindlela zokukulungisa lokhu . Ukwentuleka kwezinsizakusebenza - isibonelo , isigameko esibekwe ngenhla . Ngenxa yokungabi bikho kwamanzi anele umpompi wafakwa manje osufaka wonke umuntu enkingeni . Noma isibonelo , kunokushoda kwezindlu futhi ingxabano iyaqala mayelana nokunikezwa izindlu nendlela esetshenziswayo ekwabelweni izindlu . Isabelomali sonyaka sikamasipala sikhombisa ukuthi imali yomphakathi izosetshenziswa kanjani futhi kuziphi izinto kulowo masipala . Lokhu kuyizindleko zikamasipala . Isabelomali siphinde sicacise ukuthi imali kahulumeni wendawo izovela kuphi . Ababambe iqhaza basebenza emaqenjini afanayo nawoMsebenzi 1.1 futhi bacabanga ngesifundo sokubonakalayo bakhe nesu lokuxhumana . Ukuqhubeka nenqubekela phambili ekukhuphuleni imiholo namazinga okuphila , izinga lemikhiqizo kumele nalo likhuphuke . Izimakethe zemisebenzi zaseNingizimu Afrika zivama ukubonakala ngokuncintisana phakathi kwamafemu enza inzuzo nabasebenzi abakhokhelwa kahle . Imiphumela evela kule nqubo ebiza kahle kakhulu ishiya isikhala esincane sabantu abasha abangena bathole imisebenzi . Ukukhuluma ngamazinga aphezulu okungasebenzi , ikakhulukazi entsheni , izindlela ezingajwayelekile ziyodingeka . Ubuholi bezinyunyana busemqoka ukuqinisekisa ukuthi inzuzo yamalunga isimeme isikhathi eside . Ukuthola lokhu , izinga lemikhiqizo namathuba emisebenzi kumele kunyuke njalo . Indlela yohlelo oluzinze emphakathini idinga ukuhlelelwa ngokucophelela okukhulu ukuqinisekisa ukuthi iyaphumelela . Idinga isikhathi nokuzibophezela futhi idinga ukwesekwa yikomidi lesigceme , amakhansela nezikhulu zikamasipala . Uhlelo lwe-CBP luyithuluzi elisebenzayo ekufezeni inhloso yoMthetho wezi-2000 Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala . Uhulumeni othuthukayo kumele akwazi ukusebenza , kodwa uhulumeni okwazi ukusebenza akakwazi ukubonakala ngokuthi amenyezelwe , noma ukuthi abe semthethweni noma abonakale ukuthi ukhona ngokufunga . Kumele akhiwe , isitini nesitini , isikhungo ngesikhungo , futhi asimamiswe enziwe ngcono isikhathi ngesikhathi . Udinga ubuholi , inqubomgomo ekahle , abaphathi nabasebenzi abanamakhono , indlela ecacile yokuziphendulela , inqubo yendlela yokusebenza efanele , nokusetshenziswa kwemithetho okungaguquguquki nokusebenza ngendlela efanele . Cabanga ukuthi uxhumana kanjani nabanye . UMBUZO 2 Yingani sibalulekile ? Nikeza amaqembu imizuzu engama-30 ukwenza isabelomali sokusebenza salowo masipala . Kumele ukuba babhale izinto ezingena ngaphansi KWESABELOMALI SOKUSEBENZA kanye nalezo zinto ezingena ngaphansi kwezindleko zokusebenza . Kumele ukuba benze leli thebula elilandelayo ephepheni lefliphshadi bese eligcwalisa . Isigaba sesi-2 siphothulwa ngomhlangano omkhulu lapho umphakathi ukwazi khona ukubuyekeza , uhlolisise bese uqunisekisa ulwazi oluhlanganisiweyo . Lonke ulwazi olutholakele kulolu hlelo kumele luphinde luvezelwe umphakathi ukuze ulubone . Umphakathi kuzodingeka ukuba ubeke phezulu eqhulwini okuyisihlanu okufiswayo okumele kuhlelelwe uma engalingani inqubo . Beka leli thebula elingezansi ku-ovahedi phrojektha , noma usebenzise idatha phrojektha . Uma ungenakho lokhu kokubili , bhala leli thebula kuflipshadi . Le Nkombandlela iqukethe izigaba eziyisihlanu ezehlukene , lapho leso naleso sendlalela khona esilandelayo . Umdwebo osekhasini elilandelayo ubuyekeza lo Mhlahlandlela . UKUHLINZEKA IMIGOMO ESEMQOKA , IZINDLELA KANYE NEZINHLELO EZIDINGEKAYO UKUZE OMASIPALA BAKWAZI UKUSEBENZA NGENDLELA ENENQUBEKELAPHAMBILI UKUFUKULA IMIPHAKATHI YEZINDAWO , NGOKWENHLALO NANGOKOMNOTHO , NOKUQINISEKISA UKUTHOLAKALA KWEZIDINGONGQANGI NGENDLELA EBIZA IMALI ENOKUKHOKHWA NGABANTU BONKE . lesi sendlalelo singokufingqiwe kohlelo okusezingeni eliphezulu . Izahluko eziyi-15 zikhuluma ngokugcwele ngezindikimba ezisemqoka , zihlinzeka ngobufakazi , izincomo nokusetshenziswa okucacile kwezinhlaka . Yiluphi uhlobo lomsebenzi iningi labantu besifazane eliwenzayo ? Hlonza izinto eziningi ezijwayelekile , izinkinga ezikhona futhi uhlawumbisele neholo lalowo msebenzi nanokuthi bangaki abantu besifazane abenza lolo hlobo lomsebenzi . Ezansi kwaleli fomu kunesibonelo sokuthi ligcwaliswa kanjani . Umnyango kahulumeni ngamunye kumele ukuba wenze Uhlelo Lokuthuthukisa Ukulethwa Kwemisebenzi ( Service Delivery Improvement Plan ) ( i-SDIP ) . Ama-SDIP abalulekile kunqubo ye-IDP njengoba egxile ekwenzeni ' ukulethwa kwemisebenzi ngempumelelo nangekhono kube yinto yangempela futhi kwenze imigomo ye-Batho Pele kube ngephilayo ' . Ingxenye ye-SDIP iyingxenye Yomqulu Wokulethwa Kwemisebenzi . Ngakho-ke Amakomidi Ezigceme kumele ukuba ayiqondisise inqubo yokuthuthukiswa kwe-SDIP kanye nokulethwa kwemisebenzi , futhi aqinisekise ukuthi imiphakathi yawo ayazi ngalokhu , kanye nangemiqulu efanele yokulethwa kwemisebenzi . Amakomidi Ezigceme kumele ahlale enolwazi futhi azibandakanye mayelana nezokuthuthukiswa , ngezinjongo kanye nokusebenza kukamasipala . Ukubandakanyeka ekuhlelweni kokulethwa kwemisebenzi kubalulekile . Ukubandakanya izinkampani ezizimele ngempumelelo enkulu kuma-IDP ukuze kuthuthukiswe izindlela zokuthuthukiswa komnotho wesifunda nowendawo kanye nokwenza isisekelo sokuqoqwa kwezimali kanye nesisekelo sezinsizakusebenza somasipala . Ukuziphatha ngandlela thile noma umuntu engakhulumi kuyindlela enamandla yokudlulisela umyalezo kubantu . Izenzo ezilula ezifana nokunqekuzisa ikhanda , ukubukana emehlweni , ukusebenzisa ' ukukhuluma ' ngobuso okufanele , ' ukukhuluma ' ngomzimba , ukusebenzisa izandla kanye nokumisa umzimba ngandlela thile kungasiza ekuxhumaneni . Ngesikhathi salesi sigaba ukuhlola kumele kwenziwe mayelana namandla abantu nezinsizakusebenza ezikhona ngaphakathi emphakathini . Ngokubhekana ngqo nokuqinisa amandla emiphakathi ukuhlangabezana nezinkinga zayo , kwakheka amaphrojekthi asimamayo , namandla abantu bendawo aqiniswe . Yenza uhlu lwemibuzo ozoyibuza laba bantu emayelana nokuthuthukiswa kwesigceme . Le mibuzo kumele ukuba isetshenziselwe ukuqala ingxoxo kanye nokusiza lowo obuza imibuzo ukuze abuze konke okudingeka ukuba akubuze mayelana nezindaba . Amaprojekthi ahluleka ukwazisa izindaba ezahlukene zobulili ezinjengobubha , ingculaza negciwane layo , kanye nodlame olubhekiswe kubantu besifazane noma ukuthola kwabantu besifazane izinsizakalo eziyisisekelo , imithombo , imisebenzi noma umhlaba azoba nokuntuleka kokuqonda okunzulu kwenkinga . Amaprojekthi ayimpumelelo kudingeka aqonde ukuthi lezi zingqinamba zisuka eqoqweni elithize lobudlelwano bamandla kanye nokungalingani emphakathini okudinga kubhekanwe nakho ukuze kwethulwe inkinga . Mema iqembu elilodwa ukuba lizokwethula ithebula lalo ngesikhathi amaqembu esehlangene wonke . Emva kwalokho memela amanye amaqembu ukuba agcwalise ngokuthile noma aphawule . Umthetho ohlongozwayo umbhalo oyinqubomgomo obonisa ukuthi ungafinyelela kanjani umbono wokuthuthukisa uhulumeni wendawo ozimisele ukwenza ngcono izinga lempilo lemiphakathi yendawo kanye nokufeza izidingo zawo ngokusebenzisana nawo ukuthola izindlela ezixhasayo zokwenza lokhu . Omasipala kudingeka ukuthi balawule ukuhambisa kwabo izinto , izinqubo zokuhlela kanye nokubhajetha ngendlela ebeka izidingo ezisemqoka zomphakathi phambili . Izimiso ezinikezwe Emthethweni Ohlongozwayo zesekwa yimithetho ehlukene yasephalamende . Yimaphi amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme okufanele anikezwe umthwalo wokwenza imisebenzi ? Sibeke isikhathi kanye nendawo yokubambela unhlangano kusenesikhathi . Lona ngumsebenzi kanobhala . Ezingeni lesikhungo , ukuphathwa kwezokunakekelwa ngokwezempilo zisenkingeni . Muva nje Umnyango Wezempilo usuvule ngokusemthethweni uhlelo lokuhlaziya ikhono lokuphatha . Izinguquko ezihambisanayo kumele zibandakanye ukudluliselwa kwamandla kubasebenzi , izinhlaka zokushintshana kwabasebenzi kanye nenqubo yokuthengwa kwempahla nemisebenzi okwenziwa njalo . Lezi zifundo ezehlukene zomsebenzi obandakanyeka ekuphathweni kwephrojekthi zingahlukaniswa izigaba ezisemqoka ezinhlanu ezibhalwe ethebuleni elisekhasini elilandelayo . Veza ulaka lwakho uma kufanele , kuphephile futhi kulungile ukwenza lokho . Ungaluvezi ngaleso sikhathi uma luzokwenza inkinga ibe yimbi kakhulu kunakuqala noma ludale enye . Zama ezinye izinto eziphephile ukuxolisa ulaka lwakho . Akunasidingo ukuhlale njalo uveza ulaka lwakho noma ukuhambisana nalo ; ngesinye isikhathi imizwa idlula ngokushesha . Thuthukisa izinga lemfundo ezikoleni ezingasebenzi kahle nasemakolishi okuqhubeka nokufunda nokuqeqeshwa . Sebenzisa amanothi esifundo ( amakhasi ama-56 kuya kwangama-64 ) ngethuluzi lenu bese nilandela inqubo . Uma kunokwenzeka izimpendulo azisuselwe kokwenzekayo esigcemeni . Yiziphi izinhlangano zomphakathi noma iminyango kamasipala edinga ukumenywa ukuzokwethula ulwazi eKomidini Lesigceme noma emhlanganweni weziko ? Izinga eliphezulu lotshalomali , ngokugcwala kakhulu kotshalomali emkhakheni kahulumeni kutshalomali oluzimele . Lokhu kuyoncika ekusebenzisaneni nomkhakha ozimele , ukuqinisekiswa kwenqubomgomo nokwakhiwa kokuzethemba ekukhuleni kwesikhathi eside komnotho . Kuphinde kube yindlela yokuqonda izidingo eziyingxube zomphakathi . Esikhundleni sokuhlukanisa abantu njengaba ' ziwayo ' noma ' abahluphekayo ' lapho ukufunisela kwenziwa khona ngabantu abawumndeni owodwa , ukuhlaziya ubulili kuvumela ukubukela eduzane amaqiniso abantu ababhekene nawo . Kuhlukanisa ukuhlaziywa kwabesilisa kanye nabesifazane - izinkinga zabo , izidingo kanye nokukwazi ukufinyelela emandleni kanye nakumithombo . Ngonyaka wezi-2030 , iNingizimu Afrika kumele kube ngesinenqubo ephelele yokuvikela umphakathi , , ebandakanya izibonelelo zomphakathi ngokomnotho , ukongela umhlalaphansi okuphoqiwe , imihlomulo yengozi ( efana nemihlomulo yokungasebenzi , ukushona nokukhubazeka ) nokongela umhlalaphansi ngokuzithandela . Ukudala imisebenzi eminingi ngokuthuthukisa ezolimo , ngokuguqulwa kwezwe okuphumelelayo nokukhula kwezolimo nokukhiqizwa kwezindawo . Iphesenti lesabelomali sekhephithali sikamasipala okukhokhelwa ngaso amaphrojekthi ekhephithali ahlonzwe ngalowo nyaka othile wezezimali ngokuhambisana ne-IDP kamasipala . Umphathi wohlelo lwe-CBP ufundela ababambe iqhaza uhlelo , achaze indlela olwenziwa ngayo bese ecacisa lapho kunesidingo khona . Abamba iqhaza kumibuzo ephathelene nokwenziwa kwamaphrojethi athile azoba nemithelela kumiphakathi yawo . Ukuhambela imihlangano yomkhandlu - indlela yomkhandlu yokwenza umthetho kufanele ibe nokuzinikela , ivuleleke futhi ibe nezimpendulo kumalungu omphakathi . Umphakathi unelungelo lokuhambela imihlangano yomkhandlu . Ukwenza leli lungelo umphakathi udinga ukwazi ukuthi uzokuba kuphi futhi nini umhlangano womkhandlu . Uyadinga futhi ukwazi ukuthi umaqondana nani umhlangano womkhandlu . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angasiza umphakathi ngokuwunikeza le mininingwane . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kufanele ahambele imihlangano yomkhandlu ukuba ahlale enolwazi njengabamele umphakathi futhi akwazi ukwethula imibiko emphakathini . UKUFAKA UBULILI KUSHO UKUTHI NOMA KUNGABE YISIPHI ISINYATHELO NOMA AMAPROJEKTHI NOMA IZINHLELO ZIHLELWA NGAMAKOMIDI EZIGCEME . UMZAMO OHLANGANISIWE WENZELWE UKUTHI KUQINISEKISWE UKUTHI UBULILI BUYAFAKWA KULEZI ZINHLELO . Ukuhlelela ukuyenza - lokhu kubandakanya ukuhlela okunemininingwane eyanele yokuthi iphrojekthi kumele yenziwe kanjani . Isendlalelo soMthetho i-MSA sigcizelela ukuthi uhulumeni wendawo kumele ' acabange ngezentuthuko ' . Cela ababambe iqhaza ukuba behlukane baye emaqenjini abo amancane babheke ukuhlaziywa ngokwe-SWOT kwamaqembu ngokwenhlalo ekhasini lama-66 lamanothi esifundo . Ukukhula okusimeme kwezemisebenzi kuyodinga umnotho okhula ngokushesha nokususwa kwezingqinamba zezinhlaka , ezifana nezinga eliphansi lemfundo noma indlela yokuhlaliswa kwabantu endaweni engabandakanyi iningi labantu . Lokhu kusemqoka ekufinyeleleni emazingeni aphezulu okutshala imali nawokuqhudelana namanye amazwe , nokwandiswa kwemikhiqizo kanye nokuthunyelwa kwempahla ngaphandle . Amabhizinisi , imisebenzi , imiphakathi nohulumeni kuyodingeka basebenzisane ekukhuliseni umnotho ngokushesha . Ukusebenza kanye nempumelelo yanoma yiyiphi iprojekthi incike kuxhaso lwabantu leyo projekthi esuke iqonde ukubahlomulisa . Ngakho-ke kubalulekile ukuthi izwi labo bonke abakhathazekile lizwakale ukuqinisekisa ukuxhaswa kohlelo . Ngokucabanga ukuthi abantu besifazane bavamise ukukhishwa inyumbazane uma izinhlelo zifanekiswa noma zihlonzwa ngokuthi abanye abantu bangacabanga ukuthi yini izidingo zazo , kubalulekile ukuzwa imibono , izimvo kanye nezihlongozo zabo zifuniwe ukuze iprojekthi izothola uxhaso lomphakathi . Ukuzilungiselela kahle kungakusiza ukwehlisa ixhala lokwethula inkulumo . Khumbula : ukuthi umkhakha wendawo ngumkhakha lapho ababambi beqhaza bengalibamba khona ngendlela eyimpumelelo . Amawekhishophu abalulekile njengoba eletha ulwazi futhi aqwashise ngezindaba ezithile futhi anika ithuba lokwenza inqubomgomo nokuthatha izinqumo . Avame ukwenziwa ngamaqenjana ukuze ababambe iqhaza bezohlolisisa udaba ngendlela ejulile . Ababambe iqhaza bahlukaniswa ngamaqembu ebese bebheka izigameko ezisekhasini 68 . Xoxa ngamazinga okulawulwa kokusebenza . Landelisa lokhu ngokuxoxa ngezinqubo zokuqapha nezokuhlola . UMthetho Wezinhlelo zikaMasipala , ka-2000 kuhloswe ngawo ukuthuthukisa isikompilo lokubamba iqhaza komphakathi futhi wenza ukuba kube khona izindlela nezinqubo zokuqinisekisa lokhu . Lo mthetho ubeka indlela yokuthi ulwazi kumele ludluliswe kanjani ubuye ubeke umthetho mayelana nesaziso somphakathi kanye namayelana nokwamukelwa emihlanganweni yomphakathi kanye nokuthi umphakathi kumele ukuba waziswe kanjani . Sabalalisa imisebenzi yezenhlalakahle nezinhlelo zokuqashwa komphakathi , ukuvumela ukuthi uhulumeni asize asekele imiphakathi empofu , ikakhulukazi leyo enamazinga aphezulu obelelesi nodlame . I-Batho Pele inikeza uhlaka lokuguqula ukuhlinzekwa kwezinsizakalo zikahulumeni . I-Batho Pele , okusho ukuthi ' ukubeka abantu phambili ' yenzelwe ukwenza abasebenzi bakahulumeni ukuba babenomqondo wokuletha izinsizakalo nokulangazelela izinga eliphezulu ekwenzeni umsebenzi wabo . Inikeza ilungelo kumakhasimende lokubophezela izisebenzi zikahulumeni maqondana nendlela ezihlinzeka ngayo izinsizakalo . Ukuhlolwa kokusebenza kungakalwa ngokuthi zisetshenziswa kanjani Izimiso ze-Batho Pele uma abasebenzi bakahulumeni besebenza nomphakathi . Isikhathi - isikhathi obamba ngaso umhlangano noma umbuthano wokucobelelana kufanele sinakisiswe . Uma sekwephuze kakhulu noma sekusebusuku noma ngempelasonto lapho amalungu omphakathi kumele abhekane nezidingo zawo , noma esemsebenzini , umphumela ozowuthola kuzoba ukuphoxeka okukhulu . lesi sigaba siqopha lokho umgqugquzeli / abagqugquzeli abakwenzile ukwenza lolu hlelo nokuthi ngobani ababamba iqhaza . Kulesi sigaba umgqugquzeli / abagqugquzeli banikeza uhlu lwemihlangano ebanjiwe kanye negama / inombolo yababebambe iqhaza nabagqugquzeli . Kuyisidingo esibalulekile ukuthi Ikomidi Lesigceme lizibandakanye kwezamasu entuthuko okuyiwo enza ukuthi izinqubo zikamasipala endaweni yawo zihleleke esikhathini esiyiminyaka emihlanu . Kuyindlela eyisisekelo lapho Ikomidi Lesigceme likwazi ukukhombisa ukubaluleka kwalo . Omasipala kumele bahlelele uhlelo lwe-IDP isikhathi esihlanganisa iminyaka emihlanu . Lokhu kuhlela kanye nokusebenza kwakho kuhlelwe izigaba eziyisihlanu njengoba kubhaliwe lapha ngezansi . Kusemqoka ukuzejwayeza lezi zigaba ngenhloso yokuxhumanisa izikhathi zohlelo lwe-CBP nezohlelo lwe-IDP . Uhlelo lwe-IDP luyinqubo lapho omasipala behlelela khona uhlelo lwamaqhinga ezentuthuko lweminyaka emihlanu . Uhlelo lwe-IDP luwumphumela wenqubo yohlelo lwezentuthuko kamsipala wonke kanye nezakhamuzi zawo . Uhlelo lokusebenza ngokwehlukahlukana ludinga ulwazi oluningi kanye nezinhlelo ezicatshangwe kahle . Uhlelo kufanele luhlale lunendlela yokugqugquzela ukwahlukahlukana , ukulingana kanye nobulungiswa ngesikhathi esifanayo luxazulule inkinga yokucwasa . UMthethosisekelo WaseNingizimu Afrika nawo uyazisiza izikhungo eziqinisa intando yeningi egxile kumthethosisekelo . Lokhu kubizwa ngokuthi izikhungo ' zeSahluko 9 ' njengoba zibekwe kwiSahluko 9 soMthethosisekelo . Uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini olunempumelelo luwukubambisana phakathi kwabo bonke abathintekile . Amakomidi ezigceme awuhlaka olwamukelekile oluwumgudu izwi lomphakathi elizwakala ngawo . Abagqugquzeli bohlelo lwe-CBP kumele basebenze nabo bonke abathintekile ukwenza inqubo isebenze . Amakomidi Esigceme angazithola esesimweni lapho kufanele abhekane khona nengxabano . Cabanga ngalezi zimo ezilandelayo nokuthi iyiphi indlela esetshenzisiwe . Kulesi sahluko sizobheka kuhlaka lwezomthetho oluyisisekelo solwazi sokulethwa kwemisebenzi , indima okumele idlalwe Ngamakomidi Ezigceme kanye nezinhlelo okumele zibe khona ukuqinisekisa ukulethwa kwemisebenzi okuyimpumelelo . AmaKomidi Ezigceme agqugquzela ukubamba komphakathi iqhaza ngesikhathi kwenziwa intuthuko , ukubuyekezwa nokufezwa kwe-IDP . AmaKomidi Ezigceme ngakho kufanele azethembe , abe nolwazi nekhono ukuze akwazi ukwenza lokhu . Itafula yisifinyezo sababambe iqhaza , umsebenzi nobudlelwano babo neKomidi Lezigceme . Umehluko wobulili uchaza umehluko phakathi kwabesifazane nabesilisa okukhethwa ngokuzithandela futhi okungancikile kumagugu . Kodwa-ke , ' umehluko ' omkhulu phakathi kwabesilisa nabesifazane , ngisho lapho okubandakanya ukuzikhethela ( isib. yini ozoyigqoka ) , kodwa kugxile kakhulu ezinhlakeni zokungalingani ngokobulili , ngokujwayelekile okunomthelela ekubukeleni phansi ukuzikhethela kwabesifazane futhi kubhebhezela ukufinyelela emandleni kanye nasezinsizeni zokungalingani . Inqubo ehleleke ngokusezingeni eliphezulu eqhutshwa yinkantolo yomthetho , ijaji elingachemile noma imantshi ephoqelela isinqumo sokugcina emva kokulalela ubufakazi nokuphikisana okusemthethweni kwezinhlangothi zombili . Isinqumo sayo sizoncika emthethweni wecala , umthethomgomo nokomthetho okwenziwe ngaphambili . Iprojekthi yinoma yimuphi umsebenzi wokuthuthukisa ukwethulwa kwezidingo noma umkhiqizo ngesikhathi esinqunyiwe . Kufanele yengeze ukubaluleka noma ilethe ngandlelathile ushintsho oluhle . Iprojekthi inesikhathi esithile esikaliwe , hhayi ibe wuhlelo oluqhubekayo nje noma olungapheli , futhi inesabelomali esikaliwe futhi ngokujwayelekile ngumsebenzi owenziwa kanye . Ekuhanjisweni kwemisebenzi kamasipala emphakathini kunamaprojekthi aqhubeka njalo , njengokulungiswa komgwaqo . Ezimweni ezifana nalezo indlela echazwe lapha ngeke isebenze . Umkhandlu ungenza imigomo mayelana nokuthi isaziso somthetho kamasipala sizokwenziwa kanjani emphakathini , okungaba yiphosta noma iphephandaba nomsakazo . Amalungu omphakathi angenza imibono ebhaliwe angayedlulisela ehhovisi likamasipala . Umkhandlu kufanele unikeze ithuba amalunga omphakathi okungenzeka ukuthi awakwazi ukufunda nokubhala , noma anokunye ukukhinyabezeka okwenza kubenzima ukuba alethe izethulo zawo . UMSEBENZI OSEMQOKA WEKOMIDI LESIGCEME ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izakhamizi zesigceme ziyambandakanywa futhi ziyaziswa ngezinqumo zomkhandlu ezithinta izimpilo zazo . Amakomidi Ezigceme angamehlo nezindlebe zomphakathi nendlela ebalulekile yokugqugquzela ukuzwana phakathi komphakathi nomkhandlu . Lokhu kusho ukuthi iKomidi Lesigceme kufanele lithinte umphakathi mayelana nentuthuko nezinhlelo zemisebenzi kahulumeni . Ukuxhumana kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukuthi imibono , imiqondo nemicabango yomphakathi iyafakwa ezinqumweni ezimayelana nokulethwa kwezinsizakalo nentuthuko . Ukukhuliswa kwemisebenzi yamabhizinisi obudlelwane bamazwe ngamazwe ukusekela ukusabalala kwesabelo somhlaba wonke sezimakethe zaseNingizimu Afrika . Inselelo yokuqala yokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ukuqinisekisa ukuthi iphrojekthi ilethwa ngesikhathi leso esinqunyiwe . Eyesibili , enzima kakhulu , ukuqinisekisa ukuthi okuningi kwenziwa ngemali ebekelwe yona kanye nezinye izinsizakusebenza ezikhona ukuphumelelisa izinjongo zephrojekthi . Ukuhlela ukuthi iphrojekthi kuyomele yenziwe kanjani - lokhu kuphinde kwaziwe ngokuthi yisigaba sokwakha noma sokuhlanganisa noma yisigaba sokuhlela ukusebenza . Izimo nezidingo kungaguquka ngesikhathi abantu abasha befika endaweni , izidingo ezindala kungenzeka ukuba sekwabhekwana nazo , kanti ezintsha zisadinga ukubhekwa . Endaweni esemadolobheni amalungu amakomiti amawadi kufanele bamele amaqembu athile , isibonelo , amaqembu amakholwa , amaqembu abesifazane , amaqembu entsha , isigaba sezempilo , amaqembu ezemidlalo , abezezakhamuzi , kanye nezinhlangano zabakhokhi bentela . ZONKE IZAKHAMIZI KUMELE UKUBA ZIPHATHWE NGOBUMNENE FUTHI ZICATSHANGELWE . Impendulo : Esikhundleni sokuvula ithenda umkhandlu ukhetha ukuqasha inkontileka X uthi unegunya lokwenza lokho . Imisebenzi yezezimali eqinile ukwehlisa izindleko zabo nokuthuthukisa ukufinyelela emabhizinisini amancane nalingene . Leso naleso sigaba siqukethe imicimbi ethile lapho kungasetshenziswa khona ithuluzi noma amathuluzi ohlelo lwe-CBP . Kumele kube yinjongo yabo bonke abasebenzi bezentuthuko ( uhulumeni , umasipala noma abasebenzi bosizo lwangaphandle ) ukwakha imiphakathi uma belawula amaphrojekthi akuyo . Imiphakathi abesifazane yizinhlobo ezifanele zentuthuko , ikakhulukazi uma ibandakanyeka kumaphrojekthi ayithintayo . Uma ifunda ukuphumelela entuthukweni yomphakathi , imiphakathi iyosebenzisa izinto ezifundile kwezinye izingxenye zempilo yayo . Iyofunda ukuhlela ngendlela enempumelelo futhi namakhono obuholi ayoqina . Ukunikeza amandla - lokhu kusho ukuba nolawulo kuzinqumo kanye nasezindabeni ezithinta impilo yomuntu . Kusho ukumelwa ezinhlelweni zokuthatha izinqumo kanye nolawulo ekwabiweni kwezinsiza . Kudinga imizamo eyinhloso ethathayo ukushintsha isimo lapho abesifazane bengamelwe khona ngokwanele ekuthathweni kwezinqumo . Ukubamba iqhaza ezinhlelweni zokuhlela kanye nokuthatha izinqumo kunomhlomulo owengeziwe wokukhuphula umuzwa wokuzinikela kubunikazi bezinhloso zohlelo . UMBUZO 6 Kusetshenziswa kanjani ? Ngubani okusebenzisayo ? Lungiselela ukubhalwa kohlelo kusenesikhathi ngoba kungaba nesidingo sokuhlela ama-laptop noma amakhompyutha okubhala . Ukunciphisa ukukhiqizeka kwegesi egcina ukushisa nokuthuthukiswa kokusetshenziswa kahle kukagesi . Qinisekisa ukuthi iqembu liyawuqondisisa umehluko ngaphakathi ' kokusemqoka ' kanye ' nokufinyeleleka ' . Lawa magama angahunyushelwa olimini lwendawo . Ukuhlinzeka ngemisebenzi esemqoka evumela abantu ukuthuthukisa ukukwazi kwabo ukusebenza ukuze basebenzise amathuba asezweni , bakwazi ukubamba iqhaza emiphakathini yabo ngokukhokha nokudluliselwa kwamakhono . Kusukela ngasekupheleni kwekhulu leminyaka ye-19 , iNingizimu Afrika beyisebenzisa umcebo wayo wokumbiwa phansi ngokunakekela noma ngokungayinakekeli nhlobo imvelo . Izinguquko ziyadingeka ukuvikela imvelo ngesikhathi izwe livunyelwa ukuthi lizuze kokumbiwa phansi kwalo . Ukwengeza emnothweni osemqoka ongenakusetshenziswa kabusha wokumbiwa phansi , izisetshenziswa zemvelo zezwe zibandakanya izilwandle zalo , inhlabathi , amanzi , ukwahlukana kokuphilayo emhlabeni , ukukhanya kwelanga nogu olude . Azikho izindawo zemidlalo kusiGceme A. Lokhu kulimaza intsha ema emakhoneni emigwaqo , ngesinye isikhathi iphuze ilwe . Amasonto endawo ahlangene ukuxoxisana ngokuthi ingaxazululwa kanjani le nkinga . Aye kwiKomidi LesiGceme . Udaba luxoxwe eKomidini LesiGceme elivumile ukuthi ikhansela lesigceme lizolwethula emhlanganweni olandelayo womkhandlu nokucela umkhandlu ukubiza umhlangano nababambe iqhaza kuhlanganisa nabamabhizinisi , izinhlangano zentsha , izinhlangano zamasonto njll . IKomidi LesiGceme lisize ngokuhlangana nalabo okubanjiswene nabo ukubazisa ngenkinga nesizathu somhlangano walabo okubanjiswene nabo . Imiphakathi yamasonto ivumile ukusebenzisana ukuletha izinhlelo nemisebenzi engazimbandakanya kuyo intsha . Amakomidi Ezigceme kumele ukuba anikezwe ulwazi mayelana nokuphuma nokungena kwemali kumasipala . ' Ukuphuma nokungena kwemali ' kushiwo ukuphuma nokungena kwemali e-akhawuntini yasebhange kamasipala . Umsebenzi 3 Khetha ezimbili zezinyathelo ozihlonze Emsebenzini we- 2 . Nquma ukuthi yini ozoyenza ukusiza Ikomidi Lesigceme sakho ukuthatha lezi zinyathelo . Nokungabi nokwethemba - izakhamizi kungenzeka zingabi nokwethemba abaholi abakhethiwe , amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi kanye / noma abasebenzi bakamasipala ukuthi bangethula izinhlelo namaphrojekthi ngempumelelo . Lokhu kungaba ngumphumela wolwazi ngempilo lwesikhathi esedlule noma ukungabi nalo ulwazi . Amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi kumele athole izindlela zokugqugquzela nokwakha ukwethembana nokwethemba ukuthi ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi kunanoma yimuphi umphumela noma incazelo . Uma sibheka ngasohlangothini lwezombusazwe , intando yeningi yenze inqubekela phambili engalingani . Udlame lwakamuva eNyakatho Afrika luyisikhumbuzo esicacile sezingozi zokungabusi ngendlela nezikhungo ezibuthakathaka ezivumela abambalwa ukuthi banothe ngamandla abanye abantu . Izindawo ngokwebalazwe ezenza isigceme ziyanxuswa ukuthi zithumele abantu bazo ezibakhethile ukusebenza njengamalunga eKomidi Lesigceme . Goqa ngokuqoqela ndawonye isigaba ngasinye . Indawo yaseNingizimu Afrika ibonakala ngamazinga aphezulu obuphofu nokungasebenzi , nemisebenzi embalwa kwezolimo . Inqubo yobandlululo yaphoqelela iningi labantu abamnyama ukuthi lihlale ezabelweni zasemakhaya ezingavundile . Umphumela kwaba wumkhakha wokulima owakhelwe ezentengiso ohlukahlukene noncike kakhulu emisebenzini yasepulazini ekhokhela kancane , nemiphakathi empofu eminyene enamathuba omnotho angenele nemisebenzi kahulumeni engaphelele . Izincomo zeKhomishani ngengqalasizinda yomnotho zifaka ezezimali , ezokuhlela nokunakekela . Lokhu ngokugciniwe ngezinto ezisemqoka ezivela ngaphandle ( izinto ithimba lephrojekthi elingekwazi ukuzilawula ) ezisenethonya empumelelweni yephrojekthi . UKWAMUKELWA KWESABELOMALI KUYISIGABA ESISEMQOKA EKUTHOLENI UKUTHI IZINQUBO ZE-IDP NEZE-CBP ZINGENZEKA NINI . Izinjongo ezicaciswe kwilogifreyimu , zihlanganiswe nomsebenzi , izinsizakusebenza kanye namashedula ezindleko , kuhlinzeka imininingwane yokusekela ukuhlaziywa kwemihlomulo yezindleko . Umphakathi wakha ubunikazi bamaphrojekthi enziwayo . Lokhu kungaba nomphumela elihlangene okukhulu kakhulu okwenziwa ngumphakathi wokuthuthukisa elikhula namapaki noma izakhiwo . I-Batho Pele ihlahla inqubo kaHulumeni yokuhlela okunesu , wonke amazinga Okuhlela kokuthuthukisa Ahlanganisiwe , ukuphatha ukusebenza ngemfanelo kanye nokuphatha isibonelelo . Ngalokho isemqoka ekwakheni isimo sendawo yokusebenzela selunga ngalinye elisebenza ngezinsizalo zomphakathi . Izinjongo eziyisu zeminyango Kazwelonke kumele zehlele ezansi kwimibono nezinjongo eziyisu zayo yonke iminyango kaHulumeni yesifundazwe neyendawo . Ngokuhambisana nalokhu Imikhakha Eyimiphumela Esemqoka ( ama-KRA ) yabaphathi kumele yenze ngokufanayo . Iningi lezakhamuzi zaleli dolobha lihlala ezindlini ezimise okwebhokisi likamentshisi noma emijondolo ehlonywe emva kwezindlu . Kule ndawo izindlu eziningi azinawo ugesi noma amanzi avela kompompi . Izikole zintathu kuphela kanti imitholampilo mibili . Intuthuko ifezekile ekwenziweni kahle komsebenzi wuhulumeni , okuqaphelekayo , Uphiko Lwezemisebenzi Yokuqoqwa Kwentela LwaseNingizimu Afrika luhola imisebenzi eMnyangweni Wezasekhaya , Ezempilo Nezobulungiswa . Ukuphathwa kwemisebenzi nokuthuthukiswa kwendlela yokusebenza sekube semqoka kulezi zinguquko ; lokhu kuphumelela kumele kwenzeke nakwezinye izindawo zikahulumeni . Lokhu okwenzekile kukhombisa ukuthi yini engenzeka uma abaholi nabasebenzi bezimisele ukusebenza ngokubambisana ukuthuthukisa ukwenziwa komsebenzi . Ikomiti Lewadi ngalinye kufanele linqume ngezinhlobo zamakomiti amancane kanye namaphothifoliyo elifuna ukuba nawo ewadini . Amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi anikeza amaphothifoliyo athile . Izabelomali akumele ukuba zenziwe esithe ! Hlonza izimo ezinokuba khona okungaba wusizo ukuzilandela njengezisebenzi , ubunjalo bezifo , amazinga okondleka njll . Loba izinyanga zonyaka kwifliphushadi bese ubuza iqembu ukuthi senzeka nini isigameko nokuthi sasinamandla kangakanani . Ungakwenza lokhu kuzo zonke izimo ezihlonziwe . Xoxa neqembu ngokuzolandela leso naleso simo esihlonziwe . Lokhu kungasebenza kanjani ? Inselelo enkulu yeNingizimu Afrika ukuqeda ubuphofu nokungalingani . Ukukhuphula amazinga okuphila afike ezingeni eliphezulu elihlongozwa uhlelo kuyobandakanya ingxube yokwanda kwamathuba emisebenzi , imali eningi engenayo ngokukhula komkhiqizo , umholo womphakathi nemisebenzi yomphakathi esezingeni eliphezulu [ 1 ] . Zonke lezi zinselelo zihlobene . Isibonelo , intuthuko yezemfundo iyoholela ekwandeni kwamathuba emisebenzi nemiholo , ngesikhathi ukukhula ngokushesha komnotho kwandisa amathuba emisebenzi yabo bonke abantu , kulethe nokusetshenziswa ukuthuthukisa izinga lezemfundo . Ukusetshenziswa Kohlelo Oludidiyelwe Lwezisetshenziswa lonyaka wezi-2010 ( ukuthenga okungenani ama-20 000MW kagesi ovela kokungaphinde kwenziwe kabusha ) ukunciphisa ukukhiqizeka kwekhabhoni embonini kagesi kusuka kumakhilogremu ayi-0.9 i-kilowatt ngalinye ngehora kuye kumakhilogremu ayi-0.6 ikilowatt ngalinye ngehora . Abamele amaKomidi Ezigceme bangabamba iqhaza eNkundleni YoHlelo Lwentuthuko Edidiyelwe . Le nkundla ihlinzeka ngethuba lokuba iziphathimandla zimele okufunwa ngumphakathi . Ihlinzeka ngohlaka lwengxoxo , ukubonisana , kanye nokuthatha izinqumo ngokuhlanganyela phakathi komphakathi kanye nomasipala . Iphinde ihlinzeke ngethuba lokuhlola ukuhlela kanye nokusetshenziswa koHlelo Lwentuthuko Edidiyelwe . Umbono weKhomishani wukuthi esikhathini eside , abasebenzisi kumele bakhokhe izindleko eziningi zengqalasizinda yezomnotho , kuvikelwe amakhaya ampofu . Iqhaza likahulumeni nokusebenza ngezezimali ukuhlinzeka ngokuzibophezela okudingekayo ukuze izindleko zikhokhwe ngokuhamba kwesikhathi , ngokwenza njalo ibe lula indlela yamanani . Uhulumeni kumele abeke umthetho ofanele nezinhlaka zokubusa ukuze ingqalasizinda isebenze ngempumelelo nentela ekhokhelwa impahla ibekwe emazingeni afanele . Ngokwengqalasizinda engenisa imali , isikweletu siyakhuliswa kanti ukwakha izindawo kumele kube emaphepheni okukhokha amabhizinisi kahulumeni noma izinkampani ezizimele ezenza umsebenzi . Izibambiso kumele zisetshenziswe ngokukhetha ukwehlisa izindleko zemali nokuthola izimali zesikhathi eside . Ukuxhaswa kwamakhaya ampofu kufanele kuqonde futhi kube sobala . Ingqalasizinda yomphakathi engangenisi imali - efana nezikole noma izibhedlela - kumele ifakelwe imali evela esabelweni semali . Umphakathi kufanele ubambe iqhaza kwinqubo yokubheka , ukulinganisa nokubuyekeza ukusebenza , njengoba umasipala , ngemuva kokuxhumana nomphakathi , kufanele wenze futhi usebenzise izindlela nezinhlelo futhi uveze izinqubo zalokhu . Umasipala , uma ucabanga ukuthi ungathola uvo oluningi nokubamba iqhaza komphakathi iqhaza , ungenza iforamu yokubamba komphakathi iqhaza . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kungenzeka afakwe kule foramu . Kungumsebenzi wekhansela ukwenza iforamu yomphakathi . Yini engenzeka ngokushesha ? Lezi zinjongo zihambisana nezinhloso ezivezwe eNdleleni Entsha Yokukhula . Uma amathagethi okusebenza ngemfanelo kungafinyelelwanga kuwo , kumele kwenziwe imizamo yokusiza umuntu loyo ukuthi afeze izinjongo . Uma ukusebenza ngaphansi kwezinga elibekiwe kuqhubeka yilapho kungenziwa isenzo esithile esifana nokukhishwa ehhovisi , inqubo yokulungisa izigwegwe kanye nokusulwa kwenkontileka . Ukuze ulwazi lube wusizo kudingeka ukuba luhlaziywe ngempumelelo . Idatha kumele ukuba ichazwe ngenhloso yokwenza izinqumo . Ukuqapha inqubekelaphambili yeprojekthi kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukuthi isahambisana nesikhathi esibekiwe nokuthi izingozi ezingayivelela kanye noshintsho oselwenziwe kuyabhalwa phansi futhi kufakwe esigabeni sokusebenza esilandelayo . Amaqembu eprojekthi asebenzisa izinkomba ukuqapha inqubekelaphambili . Izinkomba ziyimiklamo ekhombisa ukuthi izinhloso zifeziwe yini . Kwesinye isikhathi amathebula okuloga abizwa ngezinkomba ' izinkomba okwaziyo ukuziqinisekisa ' . Izinkomba kufanele zihlobane , zanele , zishaye emhlolweni , zikaleke , zingabizi futhi zitholakale . Qedela ngesifundo esifushane esisethebulini ekhasini lama-90 . Leli thebula linikezela Amakomidi Ezigceme uhlu lokuhlola izinto angagxila kuzo futhi angavusa ngazo umphakathi . IKhomishani Yokulingana Ngokobulili noNgqongqoshe Wabesifazane , Izingane Nabaphila Nokukhubazeka , kumele ngokubambisana babeke indima ecacile ngokuthuthuka kwamalungelo abesifazane nokubika ngenqubekela phambili njalo ngonyaka . Kulesi sigaba umlamuli kufanele asebenzise indlela yokuxazulula inkinga . Iprojekthi ingachazwa njenganoma yiluphi uhlelo lokuthuthukisa insizakalo noma umkhiqizo esikhathini esithile esibekiwe . Kumele yongeze isigqi noma ilethe izinguquko ezinhle ngandlela thize . Iprojekthi inesikhathi sokuphila esinomkhawulo kunoba ibe wuhlelo oluqhubekayo noma olukhona ngokugcwele , inesabiwomali esichaziwe kanti futhi ivamise ukuba wuhlelo olwenzeka ngesikhathi esisodwa . Ekulethweni kwezidingo zikamasipala kunamaprojekthi aqhubekayo , anjengokulungiswa kwemigwaqo , kulezi zimo indlela yokwenza echazwe lapha angeke ibe ngefanelekile . Ukwenziwa kwamabalazwe akuphinde kuhlinzeke umphakathi ngomunye umbono ngomumo wendawo wamanje , izinto ezinomthelela ezifundeni ezehlukene , ingcebo yemvelo , ezemvelo edolobheni nokungakhethwa kukho ukuthuthukisa indawo ohlala kuyona . Ukwakha inqubo yomshuwalense kazwelonke wezempilo yinjongo esemqoka . Zine izidingo zempumelelo yawo : ukuthuthukisa izinga lokunakekelwa ngokwezempilo komphakathi , ukwehlisa izindleko zokwelashwa okuzimele , ukuqasha abanye ochwepheshe kuyo yomibili imikhakha , okahulumeni nozimele , nokwenza inqubo yendlela yemininigwane yezempilo efinyelela emphakathini nakwabahlinzeka ngemisebenzi yezempilo abazimele . Lezi zinguquko ziyothatha isikhathi , zidinga ukubambisana phakathi kwemikhakha kahulumeni nezimele , futhi zifuna izisetshenziswa ezisemqoka . Ngesikhathi behlanganiswe bonke ababambiqhaza bahlonza izinqubo ezisemqoka kuzwelonke nakuzifundazwe esezenziwe ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izinhlelo kuzwelonke nakuzifundazwe zixhumene nalokho okuphambili ohlwini lokubalulekile kumasipala . Indlela esizwa ngayo ingxabano inomthelela kwindlela esibhekana ngayo nayo . Kunezigaba eziningi ezenza isiyingi sengxabano . lesi siyingi singaba sihle noma sibe sibi . Isiyingi singumdwebo osizayo wokucabanga ngezindlela esebenza ngazo ingxabano ezimpilweni zabantu . Ababambe iqhaza bafunda leso naleso sigaba , noma kube wumgqugquzeli ochaza leso naleso sigaba , acacise lapho kunesidingo khona . Yini engangisiza ukuba ngilalele ngendlela efanele ? Amakomidi Ezigceme kumele enze umzamo eqinile ukuqinisekisa ukuthi wonke amaqembu ayabandakanywa ezinhlelweni zokuthatha izinqumo ezithinta umphakathi nokuthi ayabandakanyeka emihlanganeni yokubika nokuthi imibono yawo iyafakwa , kungaba amaqembu ebesifazane , imiphakathi yokufika , amaqembu ezenkolo njll . Lokhu kungadinga uhlelo lokusebenza olucacile olwenzelwe amaqembu ancishwe amathuba . Olunye lwalolu lwazi lungaba ngoluhlanganiswe kusenesikhathi ngabaqokelwe lowo msebenzi ohlelweni lwe-CBP . Qoqa ulwazi lomlando uluhlele lube yiqoqa . Qinisekisa nekomidi lesigceme kanye nekhansela uma kukhona imithombo yolwazi enokusebenziseka . Iqembu , liholwa ' ngabagqugquzeli ' , kumele lethule imisebenzi esemqoka nezinhlelo emphakathini walo nokuthi bangobani abethuli bezidingo . Umongameli uMbeki wagcizelela ukuthi ' umshikashika wokuqeda ubumpofu kanye nokuthuthukiswa okusezingeni eliphansi ezweni lakithi yinto esemqoka ukuze sifinyelele injongo yethu kazwelonke ukwakha umphakathi onakekelayo nosekwa ngabantu ' . Leyindlela okumele siqondisise ngayo i-Batho Pele . Kukulesi sigaba esisemqoka senguquko nokuguqulwa lapho i-Batho Pele ingaba nomthelela wangempela . Amakomiti Amawadi anikeza imibono yabo ngezindaba aziphathelene newadi kwikhanseli yewadi , noma ngekhansela yewadi , kwidolobha noma ikhanseli yendawo noma kumakomiti ekhanseli . Okungaphezulu izinkomba ezikhishwe nguNgqongqoshe emva kokuxhumana no-MEC bohulumeni basekhaya ne-SALGA . Ngesikhathi izinkulungwane zamacala ziphenywa , ambalwa aya enkantolo . Kumele kusungulwe amathimba akhethekile abashushisi nezinkantolo ezikhethekile . Intuthuko kazwelonke ayikaze ibe yinqubo elula futhi uhlelo lwezentuthuko luqhubeke njengomugqa oqondile . Kahle kahle sihlongoza uhlaka olumkhakhamningi ukuletha intuthuko enhle , enenqubekela phambili endaweni eyodwa esekela ukusebenza kwezinye izindawo . Isayensi nobuchwepheshe kungaphinde kuphoqeleke ukuxazulula ezinye zezinselelo ezinkulu kakhulu kwezemfundo nezempilo . Izingxenye eziningi zase-Afrika ezingakaze zijabulele ezokuxhumana ngocingo ezisimeme , zisizwa yindlela yokuxhumana ngempumelelo yamaselula / yomakhalekhukhwini ehlinzeka ngemisebenzi ehlukene . Amaphepha okufundisa angahanjiswa ngendlela esebenzisa ugesi ezindaweni ezisemakhaya . Isayensi iveze izinhlelo ezintsha zokulwa nezifo nokwehlisa izindleko zokuhlanza amanzi . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angathola ulwazi ngezindlela eziningi . Isibonelo , umasipala anganikeza ulwazi olumayelana nesibalo semizi esendaweni , noma Amaphoyisa AseNingizimu Afrika anganikeza ulwazi lwezibalo zobugebengu . Futhi , iKomidi Lesigceme lingenza olwalo uhlolovo ngokuvakashela imizi ukuthola ulwazi . Abasebenzi abathuthukisa umphakathi nabo bangasiza ekutholeleni amaKomidi Ezigceme ulwazi . Ukuletha ukukhula komnotho okusheshayo , ukonga okuphezulu nokusebenza okusezingeni eliphezulu . Umsebenzi ngamunye kumele ufakelwe zonke izinsizakusebenza ezidingekayo ( okungukuthi , izindleko zezezimali nezinye izinsizakusebenza ) eziyodingeka ukuyiqeda . Izinsizakusebenza ezidingekayo kumele zicaciswe kahle . Abantu babhekana nengxabano ngezindlela ezahlukene . Abanye bangabhekana nayo ngendlela efanayo njalo , kodwa abanye basebenzisa izindlela ezahlukahlukene kuhambisane nesimo saleyo ngxabano . Injongo enkulu yokuxazulula ingxabano ukulwa nengxabano ngendlela bonke abasengxabanweni abazokwazi ukuphuma ekungabonini ngaso linye bezizwa benelisekile ngesinqumo . Lokhu kubizwa ngokuthi isimo sokuwina kwabo bonke . Iphesenti lemndeni ehola ngaphansi kwama-R1 100 ngenyanga ethola izidingongqangi ngaphandle kokuzikhokhela . Kungabe iKomidi Lesigceme libambe iqhaza ekuthathweni kwezinqumo zomkhandlu ? Amaphrojekthi emiphakathi amancane afana nokwenziwa ngcono kokusebenza kwenhlangano yebhola lezinyawo noma ukwenziwa kwephrojekthi yokuzisiza yezingadi , futhi adinga imigomo yokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukufezeka kwezinhloso zawo . Esikhathini esifishane , inqubomgomo kudingeka iphendule ngokushesha nangempumelelo ukuvikela indawo yemvelo nokwenza ngcono imiphumela yokuguquka kwesimo sezulu . Esikhathini eside , ngokusebenzisana okuneqiniso , okunamasu aqinile , komhlaba wonke , iNingizimu Afrika ingaphatha ukuguquka komnotho ube nezinga eliphansi lekhabhoni ngesivivini esilingana nokuzibophezela komphakathi , ngaphandle kokulimaza imisebenzi noma ukuqhudelana okuhle . Qala ngokuxoxa ngokulindelekile nokukhalwa ngakho ngohlelo lwe- CBP , lwethule usho ukuthi lungena kanjani ohlelweni lwe-IDP lukamasipala , iqhaza lethimba labagqugquzeli nekomidi lesigceme . Khomba amaqembu ahlukene ngokwenhlalo atholakala emphakathini . Ungasebenzisa ukuklelisa ngokwempilo okufana nokwethulwe kulesi sibonelo esingezansi . Isizinda solwazi sendawo - ihhovisi likamasipala lendawo liyindawo efanelekile yokuthola ulwazi . Lokhu kungenziwa ngendlela yebhodi lezaziso . Ukuhlola : Imiphakathi noma abayimele bangathatha igunya ekuhlolweni kwalabo abangaba ngabanikezeli bezinsizakalo , ukubandakanya imiphakathi ekunikezeni izinsizakalo kanye nokuhlola abanikezeli bezinsizakalo . Thatha izimpendulo emaqenjini . Zama ukuhlonza izinyathelo abaxazululi bezinkinga abazisebenzisile . IKomidi Lesigceme lingumsizi ( omele ushintsho ) ekwenzeni ukuba umphakathi uzimbandakanye ezindabeni eziwuthintayo ngale ndlela lenze imiHlahlandlela ebekwe ku-1.1.1 ukuba ibe yiqiniso . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angasebenzisa amasu ahlukahlukene ukubhekana nezidingo zomphakathi . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angakwenza lokhu ngokweseka nokusiza umphakathi ukuba ubumbane . Kunezinto ezahlukene ezilawula ukuthi ngabe iphrojekthi iyenzeka yini , ngakho sekumele kuqhutshekwe nokuhlela ukuze isetshenzwe . Kunamathuluzi avunyiwe enziwe ukuthola ukuthi yini imigomo yephrojekthi nokuthi kuyafinyelelwa yini kuyo . Ababambe iqhaza basebenza emaqenjini abantu abane kuya kwabathathu ukuphendula imibuzo engezansi . Uma iqembu likhetha ukufundelwa umbuzo , funda umbuzo owodwa ngesikhathi , wonke amaqembu axoxe ngawo , bese uqhubekela kolandelayo . Uma usebenzisa ifliphushadi nikeza iqembu ngalinye imibuzo emibili . Khumbula ukuthi umbuzo owodwa unikezwa amaqembu angaphezu kwelilodwa . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme angadinga ukuphendula kubantu abanhlobonhlobo okungenzeka ukuba babe nezimfuno ezihlukene . Lezi zimfuno zingaphinde zehluke emibonweni yamalungu eKomidini Lesigceme . Ukusebenza kanye nokuxhumana nabantu abanezimfuno kanye nemvelaphi eyehlukene kungaholela engxabanweni . Uhlelo LukaZwelonke Lwezentuthuko luwuhlaka olusabalele lwamasu . Lubeka indlela ehlangene nephelele yokubhekana nobuphofu nokungalingani ngokubheka izinto ezihlobene eziyisithupha ezisemqoka okumele zenziwe kuqala ezifingqiwe lapha ngezansi . Umqondo ongumnyombo we-Batho Pele ngothi ' isakhamuzi njengekhasimende ' . Izimiso zenezelela umqondo walabo abathola izinsizakalo zomphakathi njengamakhasimende , hhayi izakhamizi nje . Ngakho-ke abasebenzi bomphakathi akumele bazifihle ngemuva kombuso ophethe ( i-bureaucracy ) , kodwa kumele babeke amakhasimende abo ekuqaleni . ulwazi oluqoqwe ekuhlaziyweni kwezindlela zokuziphilisa lusetshenziswa ekwenzeni i-SWOT yezinhlobo zabantu ngokwenhlalo . Imiphumela nokufiswayo kweqembu ngalinye kuzoqoqwa kwifliphushadi . Yini odinga ukuyazi ngamaKomidi Ezigceme ? Ukulinganisa kumayelana nokuphatha abantu ngendlela efanayo , kunganakiwe imiphumela . Kusho ukuphathwa ngendlela efanayo kumadili , ubuningi noma amagugu . Ukulinganisa kungaholela ekungalinganeni okukhulu emaqenjini ayencishwe amathuba wuhlelo olwahluleka ukubhekana nezimo kanye nokubona kwabo . Ukuphatha ngokulingana kukunikeza ukulingisa okufanayo ezimweni zomphakathi , iholo , kanye nezimo okusetshenzwa ngaphansi kwazo kubo kubo ekuhlukaneni nabesilisa . Okokuqala , umasipala kumele ukuba anqume mayelana nokuthi yimiphi imisebenzi ayihlinzekayo , ngobani abathola le misebenzi kanye nokuthi linjani izinganhle lale misebenzi . Isibonelo : Udodi uthuthwa kangaki ? Izibonelo zemiphumela ephendula ngobulili : ( a ) Ukwanda kwesibalo sabantu abakhishwa inyumbazane - ababuthwe ngokobulili futhi abahlala esikoleni ; ( b ) ukwanda kwamandla okuthatha izinqumo kubantu besifazane mayelana nezindleko zasekhaya ; ( c ) Ukubandakanywa ngokulinganayo kwabesifazane kanye nabesilisa ekuphathweni kwezinsiza zemvelo . Zama ukusebenzisa ukulalela okunozwelo . Isibonelo , ngesikhathi ulaka luvezwa , ungachazi , ungangeneleli , unganiki izizathu , ungehluleli noma ulinganisele . Lalelisisa ngozwelo , ngokukhombisa kumuntu ukuthi uyezwa lokho okushiwoyo nakuzwayo . Ezikhathini eziningi ulwazi lokuthi kunendawo ephephile yokukhiphela imizwa lwenza ukuthi abantu bakhiphele imizwa yabo ukuze baxazulule ngendlela ekhombisa ukuvuthwa ngesikhathi esizayo . Tshala imali kwezokuthuthwa komphakathi , okuyosiza imindeni engenisa imali encane ngokuyelekelela ngezinto zokuhamba . Buza abakhona ukuthi bayalwazi yini uhlelo lwe-IDP lukamasipala . Uma bethi bayalwazi babuze ukuthi luquketheni . Bhala izimpendulo kwifliphushadi . Uma kuwukuthi unawo amakhophi alabo ababambe iqhaza kwi-IDP kamasipala , mema ababambe iqhaza ukuthi babheke i-IDP nokuthi iwaqukethe yini amaphuzu aphakanyiswe ababambe iqhaza . Emsebenzini olandelayo kubanjwa izingxoxo nabalethi bezidingo ukuthola ukuthi abalethi bezidingo abahlonzwe emsebenzini ongenhla banalo yini ulwazi oludingekayo lokusiza ekwethulweni kohlelo , lokuhlola izinkinga ababhekene nazo , bese besetshenziswa ekuhleleni . Lokhu kuzosiza ekwakheni izinhlelo ezifanele nezinokufezeka . Khumbula ukuhlelela lezi zingxoxo kusenesikhathi . Ukuxhumana okungcono , ukuthembeka okuthe xaxa nezinga elikhudlwana lokuzithoba kulabo abasezikhundleni kungahamba ibanga elide ekwakheni umphakathi ongaxazulula izinkinga ngokubambisana nangokuthula . Amacebo amaprojekthi angeke abe yiqiniso uma abesifazane bengaxhunywanga ngokugcwele mayelana nedizayini kanye nokusetshenziswa kweprojekthi . Umsebenzi 1 Iyini injongo yezinga ekade libhekwe yiqembu lakho ? Amanzi : Amanzi abetholakala kanjani esikhathini esedlule . lesi simo siguquke kanjani eminyakeni edlule ? Yini imbangela yalokho ? Zikhona izinguquko ebangeni okumele lihanjwe ngabesifazane ukuyolanda amanzi ? Yini imbangela yalokho ? Zikhona yini izinguquko eqophelweni lamanzi ? Yini imbangela yalokho ? Ukhona yini umfula ? Akhona yini amadamu / izinhlelo zokuchelela ezakhiwe ? Lokhu kube namthelela muni ekutholakaleni kwamanzi / eqophelweni lamanzi ? Okungaphawulwa kungahlanganisa lokhu : ukungasekwa wumphakathi kanye nomasipala , abantu abezi emhlanganweni wokulungiselela ukuhlela , ukungabibikho kwezinsiza okwenza umphakathi nabagqugquzeli besigceme bangakwazi ukuqhuba uhlelo . Umholi - umgqugquzeli uqondisa futhi aphathe inqubo , anikeze uhlaka emhlanganweni noma inqubo ebese ezinikela kumphumela . Isigaba 2.3.2 soMthetho Ohlongozwayo ka-1998 sithi ukugqugquzelwa kwentando yeningi endaweni kufanele kubonakale njengento esemqoka kunayinoma yimuphi uhulumeni kamasipala . Sichaza izimiso ezimbili zokubamba iqhaza , okufaka phakathi ukuvumela izakhamizi , ngazinye noma ngokwamaqembu amele izimfuno , ukuba abe novo kwezepolitiki nokusiza amakhasimende ukuba abe nezwi kwindlela okuhlinzekwa ngayo izinsizakalo . Indawo yasekhaya yinkundla lapho izakhamizi zingabamba khona iqhaza ekuthathweni kwezinqumo ukwakha izindawo ezizizungezile ezihlala kuzo , nokusebenzisa futhi nokusabalalisa amalungelo azo okuzikhethela . Umthetho ophelele wokuxhasa ubhalwe kunale nhloso emqondweni . Lokhu kusho ukuthi amalungu amaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele agcine lokhu emqondweni uma ecabanga ngokuthi angawenza kanjani umsebenzi wawo njengemigudu yokuxhumana phakathi komkhandlu nezakhamizi emiphakathini yawo . Impumelelo yalolu hlelo incike ekubambeni iqhaza okusezingeni eliphezulu kwamalungu esigceme ekuhleleleni isigceme . Lokhu kuzokwenza kube lula ukuba umphakathi uzenzele ezawo izinhlelo esikhathini esizayo , okuzonciphisa ukwethembela kubagqugquzeli bangaphandle . Ikhansela lesigceme lingusihlalo weKomidi Lesigceme . Lingaqoka ikhansela elimele iqembu noma elinye ilungu leKomidi Lesigceme ukuthi libe ngusihlalo . Phendula le mibuzo elandelayo . Yenza ibinza lamagama elizoheha umphakathi wakho elingasetshenziswa kumaphosta , kumamemo kanye nakwezinye izinto . Ukukhohlisa - Umkhandlu wendawo noma inhlangano ' yenza sengathi ' ixhumana nomphakathi ukwenza inqubo ihambe ngokomthetho kube kungekho kuxhumana nomphakathi okuye kwaba khona . Isibonelo inhlangano noma inkampani noma ibandla lithi siye saxhumana nomphakathi futhi uyavuma kanti lokho okwenzekile ukuthi abantu baye batshelwa ukuthi isehlakalo siyenzeka . Namhlanje abasebenzi ( abaneminyaka eyi-15 kuya ema-64 ) benza amaphesenti angama-64 esibalo sabantu , kanti isilinganiso sezingane nabadala sincane . Emazweni ngamazwe , umumo wabantu ofana nalona uvama ukuhambisana nokukhula kwemali engenayo , ukukhula ngokushesha kwemikhiqizo , ukonga okuphezulu nokwenyuka kwamazinga empilo . Ngakolunye uhlangothi , kungaholela ekutheni kube nendawo ecasulayo futhi engasimeme lapho abantu abasha bangeke bawuthola khona umsebenzi , kwenze ukuthi kube nodlame , ubelelesi , ukusetshenziswa budedengu kophuzo oludakayo nezinye izinhlobo zokungaphili kahle komphakathi . Inkomba yempumelelo wukuthi izwe likwazi kangakanani ukusebenzisa intsha yalo enamakhono nenesifiso sokusebenza . Ukwenza njalo kusho ukubahlinzeka ngemfundo namakhono , nokusiza abashiye isikole ukuthi bathole imisebenzi ebakhuthazayo , abangayisebenzisa ukufeza izifiso zabo . Kungabe uzinikela kanjani umkhandlu nekhansela lesigceme ? Ukuveza izidingo - ukwenza ucwaningo nokuhlaziya izidingo ukuveza izinto ezibalulekile emphakathini mayelana nentuthuko , isabelomali nokuhlinzekwa ngezinsizakalo . ACHIEVABLE ( LIFEZEKE ) - ingabe izinga lomsebenzi liyafezeka ngabasebenzi abakhona njengamanje kumnyango futhi liyasebenza yini uma kubhekwa ukusebenza kwamanje noma okwedlule ? Kuphinde kube nemijondolo eyaqala eminyakeni emihlanu edlule . Lapha amanzi atholakala kompompi bomphakathi futhi ompompi bathathu kuphela . Iningi lezakhamuzi zakule ndawo lidayisa emigwaqeni kanti abantu abaningi basebenza emapulazini futhi baze batshelwa ukuthi sekufanele bahambe . Azikho izikole kule ndawo . Singaba khona isidingo sokuguqula lolu hlu lwamaphuzu okuhlola ukuze luhambisane nendawo lapho kusebenza khona uhlelo lwe-CBP ( isibonelo edolobheni , ezindaweni zasemakhaya , njll . ) . Izinyathelo ezilandelayo zithathwa neqembu elifanayo labantu abafinyelela kwabayi-12 . Kuqalwa ngokulungiselela ukwakha isitatimende sombono saleyo naleyo nhloso yokusebenza . Lo msebenzi uzokwenziwa emaqenjini amancane , kulelo nalelo qembu kube khona ilungu elilodwa lekomidi lesigceme nabantu abafanele abawumthombo wolwazi kanye nabalethi bezidingo . Ukusebenzisa lolu hlelo ngempumelelo , izwe lidinga ukubambisana kwawo wonke umphakathi usebenzela ukufeza inhloso eyodwa . Njengamanje , iNingizimu Afrika inamazinga aphezulu okungathembi phakathi kwabalingani abakhulu basemphakathini . Uyadingeka umjikelezo omuhle wokwakha ukwethembana nokubamba izingxoxo ukubhekana nezinselelo ezinzima kakhulu - lowo othatha umbono wesikhathi eside . Kungabe bezikhona ezinye izindlela ezahlukile ? Uma kunjalo bezehluke kanjani futhi zifezeni ? Sebenzisa Ikhasi lokuhlaziywa kwezindlela zokuziphilisa okuphothulwe emsebenzini waphambilini ukucela ababambe iqhaza ukwenza ithebula elifana naleli elilapha ngezansi . Umbono wobulili kumele ufakwe Kumagama Okubhekiswa kuwona alungiselelwe nanoma yikuphi ukulinganisa . Izinkinga ezilandelayo kumele zithintwe ekulinganiseni , kanti lapho kufanele khona , zibike ngendlela yokuphathwa ngokuhlukaniswa kobulili ukuze kufinyelelwe ekuhlolweni kwemiphumela yohlelo okuyiqiniso futhi okubanzi . Ukukhula kwesikhathi eside nokutshalwa kwemali kudinga umbono wabo bonke abantu , ukwethembana nokubambisana phakathi kwamabhizinisi , abasebenzi kanye nohulumeni . Namhlanje izinga lokuthembana liphansi , ubudlelwane babasebenzi bunengcindezi ( kwesinye isikhathi kunodlame ) . Akukholakali ukuthi umnotho uyoguquka ngendlela yezabasebenzi uma lezi zimo zikhona . Ukuthuthukisa ukukhula okusheshayo , okudala amathuba emisebenzi kusho ukubhekana nale ngcindezi ngendlela ethembekile nesobala . Uhulumeni wentando yeningi ukhethwa ngabantu ngokusebenzisa ukhetho olufaka wonke umuntu , oluzimele kanye nolungabandlululi nangokusebenzisa ibhalothi eyimfihlo . Aqinisekisa ukuthi umkhandlu uyazibophezelela ekusebenzeni kwawo okudlule . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kungenzeka angangeni ngqo emsebenzini womphathidolobha kodwa njengomuntu onesibopho esiphelele somkhandlu , amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme angaqinisekisa ukuthi umphathidolobha unolwazi lokwenzekayo maqondana nomphakathi . Zama ukuthola ukuthi ulaka lubhekiswe kuwe yini . Abantu abaningi abacasukile basuke bevese benaleyo mizwa ngaphakathi kubo ngaphambi kokuba ufike . Kungenzeka ukuthi usendaweni engalungile ngesikhathi esingalungile . Umhlangano ubizwe yikhansela lesigceme neKomidi Lesigceme ukuxoxa ngamaphrojethi ahlongoziwe okufanele afakwe kwi-IDP elungiswayo njengamanje . Amanye amalungu omphakathi afuna kwakhiwe umtholampilo lapho okunemijondolo eminingi khona , njengoba abahlali basemijondolo bengenayo imali yokuya esibhedlela noma kweminye imitholampilo ekude kunabo . Enye ingxenye yabahlali ifuna ukuba i-IDP ifake ukulungiswa kwerenki yamatekisi njengoba ingenazo izindlu zangasese noma indawo yabathengisayo . Ingxenye yesithathu ifuna kwenyuswe umsebenzi wokuthutha udoti ube yizinsuku ezimbili ngesonto edolobheni ngenxa yobuningi bukadoti emigwaqeni . Emhlanganweni imimoya iyenyuka futhi yileyo naleyo ngxenye igcizelela ukuthi iphrojethi yayo ayithathelwe phezulu . Kusemqoka ukuthi uhulumeni wentando yeningi avikele amalungelo omuntu ngamunye njengoba ethulwe ngaphakathi Komthethosisekelo . Izimiso ze-Batho Pele ziqinisekisa inqubo yokuguqula umnyango wezinsizakalo zomphakathi ukuze uphendule kuzidingo zemiphakathi bese ugcina amalungelo ayo . Ngokwenza lokhu izimiso ziqhubekisa ukusebenza kombuso wentando yeningi eNingizimu Afrika . Ukuhlela okunikeza ithuba lokubamba iqhaza nokugqugquzela umphakathi ukuba emiholweni kuhlomisa imiphakathi kuyenze isebenzisane , ibambe iqhaza ezinhlelweni ezifanele zokunciphisa ubumpofu ezindaweni zayo futhi kumele kuholele nasekuphuculeni izinhlelo nezidingo ezilethwa yiziphathimandla zendawo kanye nezinye izinkampani . Bheka ekhasini lama-33 lamanothi esifundo bese ufunda nababambe iqhaza iphuzu ngalinye . Qala ngezigaba zohlelo lwe-IDP . Sebenzisa imizuzu embalwa ufunde izigaba zohlelo lwe-IDP uchaze isidingo sokwazi uhlelo lwe-IDP njengoba umjikelezo we-CBP uxhumene nalowo we-IDP . Ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi kwenzeka emazingeni ehlukene . Uhlaka Oluhleliwe luchaza ' ilada Lokubamba Iqhaza ' elaqanjwa ngu-Sherry Arnstein ( ngo-1969 ) . Ilada libonisa ukuthi ungakhetha isinyathelo esisodwa ngesikhathi ngasinye . Iqembu lomphakathi ngokubanzi libamba umhlangano wamahora amabili , ongabanjwa kusihlwa ngoMgqibelo , noma uma leso sikhathi sibalungela ababambe iqhaza . Leli qembu libuyekeza umbono , liqhakambise izinhloso zalowo nalawo masu ezinhloso , iziphakamiso zemali esetshenziswa ngokwezidingo kanye nezethulo ezenziwa kwabohlelo lwe-IDP . Kuyasiza ukubhala lonke lolu lwazi kwifliphushadi . Uma kunokwenzeka lolu lwazi lungabhalwa ngekhompyutha kwenziwe namakhophi . Ingxenye enkulu yohlelo ikhuluma ngezinguquko ezikhungweni ezidingekayo ukubhekana nobuthakathaka emkhakheni kahulumeni , ikakhulukazi lapho izinhlangano zomphakathi zingakwazi ukuhlangabezana nokuzibophezela kwazo emiphakathini empofu . Lezi zihlongozo zimayelana nokwakha izimpawu ezidingekayo ukusekela lolu hlelo . Ukwakha ukukwazi ukusebenza kwezikhungo kuthatha isikhathi nokuzimisela . Isahluko esimayelana nokwakha uhulumeni okwazi ukusebenza nothuthukayo sihlinzeka ngezinkomba endleleni okumele ilandelwe . Izikhungo zithuthuka ngokufunda okuqhubekayo nezinyathelo zokukhuphuka ; zibhekana nenkinga enkulu , ziyixazulule bese zidlulela phambili kokulandelayo okumele kwenziwe . Lokhu kudinga ukulawula okuhle , ukuzimisela ukwenza umsebenzi osezingeni eliphezulu , ukugxila endleleni enhle yokuziphatha nokufisa ukufunda ngokwenzeka empilweni . UMBUZO 1 Siyini isabelomali ? Lezi zimpendulo zingasiza ezindaweni ezithile ngezikhathi ezithile . Kodwa ezikhathini eziningi zivimba ukulalela futhi ziphuce abanye amandla . Zichaza ukuthi : awumuhle ngokwanele , awuhlakaniphile , awunamandla ; yimi engaziyo . UMBUZO 5 Yini izinkomba ezibalulekile zokusebenza ( KPIs ) ? Kuphinde kube nemjondolo eyaqala eminyakeni emihlanu edlule . Lapha amanzi atholakala kompompi bomphakathi futhi ompompi ompompi kuphela . Iningi lezakhamuzi zakule ndawo lidayisa emigwaqeni kanti abantu abaningi basebenza emapulazini , baze batshelwa ukuthi sekufanele bahambe . Azikho izikole kule ndawo . Iqhaza leKomidi Lesigceme ukuqinisekisa ukuthi labo abanomsebenzi wokuhlela iprojekthi bayawubandakanya umphakathi nokuqinisekisa ukuthi ubamba iqhaza ngokugcwele . INingizimu Afrika idinga abaholi emphakathini wonke abasebenza ngokubambisana . Njengoba ukuguquka kusuka kuhulumeni wobandlululo kwakuyisisombululo sokunqoba kunokuba kube umzabalazo wamandla obuka eduzane , ukulwa nobuphofu nokungalingani kuyoba nenzuzo kubo bonke abantu - abamnyama nabamhlophe , abacebile nabampofu . Ngokuhlukana kwezwe kwesikhathi esidlule , kwesinye isikhathi abaholi banikezela ngezikhundla ezivuna ukusebenza kwesikhathi esincane esikhundleni sohlelo olusabalele lwesikhathi eside . Kusemqoka ukuyeka lo mkhuba , ngabaholi abazimisele futhi abakwazi ukuzibophezela ukubhekana nezinselelo zaseNingizimu Afrika . Ngaphandle kokungabaza ukulalela kungenye yezingxenye ezibalulekile zokuxhumana . Abantu badinga ukuzizwela ukuthi balalelwe futhi bayaqondisiswa . Lokhu kudinga ukulalela okunozwelo . Ukulalela okunozwelo kusho ukuthi ubona umhlaba ngeso njengoba ubonwa ngomunye umuntu . Kufaka phakathi ukulalelisisa kahle futhi uzwe imizwa equkethwe ngamazwi . Cela lelo nalelo qembu ukuba livumelane ngombono womphakathi walo . Chaza ukuthi ukuhlanganisa umbono kuyingxenye esemqoka yokwenza uhlelo lwesigceme njengoba umbono ' uyiphupho ' lomphakathi . Umbono ubheka lapho umphakathi ufisa ukuba khona esikhathini esizayo . Chaza ukuthi lo msebenzi udinga isikhathi , kanti uma kusetshenzwa nomphakathi ukwenza uhlelo lwesigceme kudingeka isikhathi esanele . Bheka izinyathelo soku-1 kuya kwesesi-3 uqhakambise ukuthi lezi zinyathelo zinikeza umgqugquzeli wohlelo lwe-CBP isithombe sokuthi ungobani umphakathi , njengoba umphakathi wakhiwe ngamaqembu ehlukahlukene ngokwenhlalo , amaqembu ngokwezomnotho , njll. , ukuvumelana ngombono kudinga isikhathi , ukubekezela kanye nokuphathwa ngokucophelela kweqembu . Ngakolunye uhlangothi , ingxabano ingakha ukuhlangana eqenjini ngokuchaza okwenza kungezwanwa nokucacisa okukholelwa kukho . Ingaba ngumsuka wenguquko futhi ingadala ukwazana kabusha ngesikhathi abantu bethola futhi befunda ukuthi yini eqale ingxabano . Amaphrojekthi ngokwemvelo yawo awalandelani kahle futhi adinga ukuhlaziywa okuqhubekayo kanye nokuphinda kuhlelwe njengoba esuke esetshenzwa nje . Amagama asetshenziswayo ekuphathweni kwephrojekthi angahlukahlukana kuye ngenhlangano eyenza iphrojekthi . Amakomidi Ezigceme amele okufunwa yimiphakathi kumaphrojekthi okungayithinta , futhi kumele ibandakanywe enqubeni kakhulu ngendlela okungenzeka ngayo . Izinqubo zokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ziwusizo kakhulu kumaphrojekthi amancane njengoba kunjalo nakwamakhulu . Ukunxusa yikhono elisemqoka lempumelelo ye-Batho Pele okumele bonke abaphathi nabasebenzi baliqondisise . Kubaphathi lokhu kusho ukuthi banikezela ubuphathimandla babo kwabanye abantu ukuze bakwazi ukwenza ngokuzimela ngaphandle komphathi , kodwa isibopho uma kuba nezinkinga sihlala njalo kungesomphathi . Isibopho sokuqinisekisa ukuthi umuntu unamakhono kanye nokuqeqeshwa okufanele kuhlala kungumsebenzi womphathi . Kumsebenzi lokhu kusho ukunikezwa amandla okwenza , ithuba lokusebenza ngokuzimela , ukwakha ukuzethemba kanye nokuthi kunethemba lokumnikeza amathuba okuthuthukisa amathuba akhe omsebenzi . Imisebenzi yezenhlalakahle yomphakathi kumele yande , kube nokuqeqeshwa nokufundiswa kwabasebenzi bezenhlalakahle nokubuyekezwa kokukhokhelwa kwezinhlangano ezingekho ngaphansi kukahulumeni . UKULANDELELA NEMPENDULO : Ukugcizelela imibiko eyenziwa njalo emva kwesikhathi esithile mayelana nemisebenzi namaphrojekthi kamasipala Kumakomidi Ezigceme kanye nasemihlanganweni yomphakathi kuzigceme zawo ukuze izakhamizi zihlale zazi mayelana nenqubekelaphambili kanye / noma nezinkinga . Iziphakamiso ezakhayo mayelana nokwenza ngcono kumele zenziwe , lapho kunokwenzeka khona , umphakathi ungabandakanywa ekuxazululeni kwenkinga . Ekucebiseni uhulumeni nabambisene nabo emphakathini ngokusebenzisa lolu hlelo . Iphesenti lesabelomali sikamasipala esisetshenziswe ohlelweni lwawo lokuthuthukisa amakhono okwenza umsebenzi . Uhulumeni uveza indlela enhle yokuziphatha komphakathi wonke . Uma inkohlakalo ibonakala yemukelekile kuhulumeni , iyokhubaza indlela umphakathi oziphethe ngayo . Lokhu kwenza ukuthi kube semqoka kakhulu ukuthi uhulumeni enze okuthile ukubhekana namazinga aphezulu enkohlakalo ezikhundleni zakhe . UMBUZO 1 Yini inhloso yesithangami sokulalelwa kwesabelomali ? Ukuqonda ubulili kanye nokusebenzisa uhlaziyo oluyisisekelo lobulili kungamathuluzi asemqoka amaKomidi Ezigceme ngokwentuthuko . Akudingeki ukuthi ube yisishoshovu sezobulili esifuna ukusebenzela ukukhululwa kanye nokulinganiswa kwabesifazane ukuze ukwazi ukusebenzisa uhlaziyo lobulili . Wonke umuntu osebenza emkhakheni wokuthuthukisa umphakathi ofuna ukwenza izimpilo zabantu zibe ngcono kumele azi ukuthi lawa mathuluzi asetshenziswa kanjani . Ngokwazi ukuthi abantu besifazane , ikakhulukazi abaneminyaka yobudala ephakathi kweyi-15 kuya kwengama-24 , banezinga eliphezulu kakhulu lengculaza kanye negciwane layo , unakekelo olukhethekile kudingeka lukhonjiswe ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izinhlelo kanye namaprojekthi ahlonzwe ngumphakathi ayakwazisa lokhu . Amakhasi okucatshangwayo ngawokuhlola , kodwa kumele ahlinzeke ngolwazi olwanele ukuze umasipala aqonde ukuthi luyini uhlelo bese uthatha isinqumo ngokuthi lufanele yini ukunikezwa ithuba . Emva kokuthola ukuthi yimiphi imisebenzi okumele yelulwe noma yenziwe ngcono kumele kusungulwe izikhathi kanye nalokho okuqondiwe okucacile , ukuze umasipala anganquma ngezindlela ezingcono kakhulu okumele azisebenzise zokufinyelela kulezo zinjongo zawo . Umasipala kumele anqume futhi nangokuthi yiziphi izinsizakusebenza - imali , okokusebenza , kanye namakhono - azokudinga ukuze ahlangabezane nezinjongo zawo . Ikomiti Lewadi lingasungula uhlolo njalo ngonyaka ukuze lukwazi ukubasiza ekwenzeni umsebenzi wabo . Lolu hlolo kufanele luqhutshwe ewadini amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi angaphansi kweso lekhanseli yewadi nosizo lokubusa ngokwesekwa ngumasipala . Izimo zemisebenzi ezilungiswa yiKhomishani zincoma ukuthi iningi lemisebenzi emisha livama ukunikwa amabhizinisi azinze endaweni , nasekukhuliseni amafemu amancane naphakathi . Ngesikhathi imisebenzi eminingi ingakhelwanga amafemu ahambisa imikhiqizo ngaphandle , imikhakha ehwebela ngaphandle ivama ukuba namandla okusimamisa umnotho wasekhaya . Ngenxa yezinga eliphansi lokonga eNingizimu Afrika nesidingo sezinga eliphezulu lokutshala imali , kusemqoka ukukhulisa okuphumela ngaphandle nokukhulisa inzuzo kuleyo mikhakha . Uhlelo lokuhweba lwaseNingizimu Afrika alugcinanga nokukodwa kwalokhu eminyakeni eyi-15 edlule . Ukuba nenqubekela phambili kuyochaza ukuqinisa ubukhona bezwe emhlabeni ekuncintisaneni okuhle , ngesikhathi kwakhiwa ingqalasizinda namakhono adingekayo . Aqinisekisa ukuthi amakhansela kamasipala ayayazi imiphakathi yawo , ayivakashela njalo emva kwezikhathi ezithile futhi alalela izinkinga kanye nezidingo zomphakathi . Lolu hlu lwamaphuzu okuhlola lapha ngezansi lungasiza ekuhleleni ingxoxo nomele umlethi wezidingo njengoba kuzoshiyelwana ngolwazi nabanye . Ukuhlonzwa kwezenzeko zangempela kuyisinyathelo esisemqoka sokuhlela . Lokhu kuhlanganisa imisebenzi lapho umphakathi ulibambe ngqo iqhaza ; noma imisebenzi engaxhaswa ngemali esetshenziswa ngumasipala ngokwezidingo ezivelayo . Bhala igama elithi ' ingxabano ' eshadini ebese ucela ababambe iqhaza ukuba bacabange igama lokuqala elifika emiqondweni yabo uma bezwa igama elithi ' ingxabano ' . Izimpendulo eziningi zizoveza ububi . Veza ukuthi ingxabano ayihlali iyimbi . Ingagqugquzela ushintsho futhi isenze sicabange ngezinto esizikhethayo nokuthi sizikhetha kanjani . Ukuthi sibhekana kanjani nengxabano yinselelo . Okhuthele noma onomqondo ovulekile - lo muntu uvulelekile emiqondweni emisha nemibono , uyalalelisisa , akehluleli , uyakwazi ukuthatha isinqumo , unesibindi futhi uyakwazi ukwehlisa imimoya yabantu . Nikeza amalungu ekomidi uhlelo lomhlangano ngaphambi kokuqala komhlangano ukuze azi ukuthi umhlangano ungani futhi azilungiselele . Kwesinye isikhathi kuyodingeka ukuthi kube khona imibiko eyisiphesheni ngephothifoliyo ethile , ngakho uma , umnikazi wephothifoliyo ekwazi lokhu , angaxhumana nomphakathi ngalolu daba futhi abike ekomidini ngendlela efanele . Omasipala abayimikhandludolobha kanye nomasipala bendawo kufanele bamise amaKomidi Ezigceme . Eyesibili , ukuqikelela ukuthi ababambe iqhaza ohlelweni lwe-CBP bamelelekile emicimbini yohlelo lwe-IDP ngokusebenzisa izinhlaka nezinhlelo ezihlinzekwa yinqubo yohlelo lwe-IDP equkethwe wuMhlahlandlela wohlelo lwe-IDP , ikakhulukazi enkundleni yokumeleleka yohlelo lwe-IDP kanye nasemathimbeni ezinhlelo . Nikeza umphakathi izimpendulo nolwazi futhi ubuze imiphakathi ngezimvo zawo mayelana nemisebenzi yelungu leKomidi LesiGceme . Lokhu kungafuna ukuba iKomidi Lewadi libize umhlangano . Ukwethula inkulumo emhlanganweni kungaba ngumsebenzi onzima , ikakhulukazi uma lokhu futhi kufuna ukuba owethula inkulumo asebenzise imishini njenge-overhead projector noma umbhobho wokukhuluma . Yonke le minyango kudingeka ukuba yenze ' izinhlelo zemikhakha ' ; izindlela zokusebenza ukuqinisekisa ukuletha izingqalazizinda zikamasipala ezifanele kanye nemisebenzi kamasipala esimeme ngaphakathi kwalowo mkhakha . Indlela ebheka zonke izinhlangothi iyadingeka ukubhekisisa ukuxhumana phakathi kwemikhakha futhi iqinisekise ukuthi le mikhakha ididiyelwe kuyo yonke inqubo yokuhlela kamasipala . Ukubuyekezwa kokusebenza ngemfanelo konyaka ngonyaka : Ikhanseli kumele ibike njalo nje Ekomitini Lewadi kanye nasemphakathini ngebhajethi yayo kanye nokubuyekezwa kokusebenza ngemfanelo , njengengxenye yemihlangano yomphakathi . Uma ngabe ikomiti yakho ayitholi umbiko wokusebenza ngemfanelo ovela kwikhansela yakho , yenza ukuthi umphathidolobha azi ukuthi Ikomiti Lewadi lilindele ukusebenza ngemfanelo kuhulumeni wendawo wombuso wentando yeningi . IBhodi Lokuklanywa Kwemingcele yinhlangano ezimele eklama imingcele yomasipala . Leli dolobha linemboni encane kakhulu ; lizungezwe wumphakathi omkhulu wabalimi . Baningi kakhulu abantu abangasebenzi kuleli dolobha , ngenxa yokuntula kwamathuba omsebenzi . Kunamapulazi amathathu kuleli dolobha . Abanikazi bawo babambisene , kanti abasebenza khona bathola ingxenye yenzuzo . Kungabe imisebenzi yohlelo ibe negalelo ekuthuthukisweni kokukwazi kwabesifazane ukuthola izinsiza ( yezemfundo , uqeqesho , izikweletu , njll ) ? Kanti abesilisa bona ? Lo mdwebo olandelayo ukhombisa izinga ngalinye lemiphumela yokuphatha iprojekthi ekuhloleni izinyathelo futhi , nokubheka ukuthi umjikelezo awugcini uyinto eqondile nje , engaguquki . Ukumela umphakathi kwiforamu yokuthintana - iKomidi Lesigceme kufanele lizazi izindaba ezintsha zomphakathi futhi kufanele liziveze lezi zindaba kumaforamu okuthintana . Umnotho wamazwe amaningi ase-Afrika usukhule ngokushesha esikhathini esiyishumi leminyaka edlule , unciphisa ngokubonakalayo ubuphofu obukhulu okokuqala cishe engxenyeni yekhulu leminyaka , futhi izwekazi libeke umbono omkhulu ezikhungweni zamazwe omhlaba . Amaqembu aphendula imibuzo , bese ebhala ekhasini lephephandaba lezo zindaba ezibalulekile eziphakanyisiwe ngesikhathi sezingxoxo zawo . Ukuthenga okungenani ama-20 kagesi ovuselelwayo ngonyaka wezi-2030 , ukungenisa ugesi ovela esifundeni , ukuyeka ukusebenzisa ama-11 ezikhungo zamandla kagesi ezisebenza ngamalahle esezindala nokutshala izimali ekusebenzeni kahle kwamandla . Yiba nozwelo kumuntu noma iqembu okhuluma nalo nesihloko okhuluma ngaso . Isibonelo , abanye abantu abakhululekile ukuxoxa ngendaba ye-HIV ne-AIDS futhi lesi sihloko kufanele siphathwe ngendlela enozwelo . Izinkomba ezigxile ebuningini zibhekiswe kwizinombolo kanye namaphesenti abantu besifazane kanye nabesilisa noma izinhlangano ezibandakanyekayo noma ezithintwe nanoma yiliphi iqembu elithile noma umsebenzi . Izinkomba ezigxile ebuningini zithathela ezinhlelweni zolwazi lobulili obuhlukanisiwe kanye namarekhodi aseke ahlolwa ngesikhathi sezinhlelo zenqubomgomo noma ukuhlela iprojekthi . Ukutholakala kolwazi oluyisisekelo olugxile ebuningini kuchaza ukuthi izinkomba zivamise ukuhlanganisa iphuzu lokumisa okuhlosiwe . Isibonelo : abesifazane bakha okungenani ama-33% amalungu ekomidi lamanzi ngokuphela koNyaka we- 2 . Ngonyaka we-2004 inhlolovo yaveza ukuthi omasipala abaningi bathola ukuthi uMthetho Wezinhlaka Zikamasipala , 1998 , kanye noMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , 2000 , ubungaluniki ulwazi olwanele mayelana nendlela yokumisa amaKomidi Ezigceme . Iqoqo lemihlahlandlela lafakwa kugazethi mhla zingama-24 kuNhlangulana 2005 ( Igazethi Kahulumeni No 27699 ) ukusiza omasipala ngolwazi oluthe xaxa mayelana nokuthi kufanele amiswe kanjani . Izihlahla zezinjongo ziyithuluzi eliwusizo elibheka izinjongo , kunokuthi libheke izinkinga ukuze kwenziwe uhlelo lwephrojekthi . Isihlahla sezinkinga siguqulwa sibe yisihlahla sezinjongo ngokuphendula imbangela ngayinye ibe yisitatimende yisitatimende esihle . Ukulawulwa kobubanzi , ishedula nokuguquka kwezindleko : Ukulawula ukuguquka kuphrojekthi yonke Okuthiwa yi-'Scope creep ' yilapho kusuke kwenziwa khona izinguquko ezincane eziba nomphumela wobubanzi obehlukile kunalobo obabucatshangiwe futhi kuvama ukuthi kwenze iphrojekthi ingaphumeleli . Kuvama ukuthi kudingeke ukuthi kuncishiswe ukwethulwa kulokho obekuhlelelwe khona . Ekupheleni kwalo mhlangano kuleso naleso Sifiso kuzoba khona ulwazi oluhlanganisiweyo oluzosetshenziswa ekuhleleni . Uhulumeni wezindawo uhlangabezana nezinselelo ezihlobene eziningana , kubandakanya amakhono angekho kahle , izindlela zokuphatha ezingasebenzi kahle , ukugxambukela kwezombusazwe okungadingekile ekuthathweni kwezinqumo zobuchwepheshe nokuphatha , nemali engalingani . IKhomishani ikholwa ukuthi ngaphakathi kwezinhlaka zomthethosisekelo maningi amathuba okwabiwa kwamandla nemisebenzi ngokulinganayo , okunokwehlukana kakhulu ekutheni kusetshenziswa kanjani okusemqoka kwezentuthuko okumele kwenziwe kuqala . Ukufeza lokhu , kudingeka amasu esikhathi eside , kubandakanya nokubhekana nezingqinamba zamakhono , ukuvumela ukuhlolwa kokusebenza ezindleleni ezimayelana nomthethosisekelo nokusebenza ngokubambisana nohulumeni kazwelonke nowesifundazwe . Namhlanje cishe bangamaphesenti ayi-17 abantu baseNingizimu Afrika abakwaziyo ukuthola i-inthanethi - inani elikhula cishe ngamaphesenti angama-20 ngonyaka . Ukusetshenziswa kwendlela yokuxhumana esebenzisa izinombolo sekuguqule umphakathi ngezindlela ezingakaqondakali kahle . Kuyacaca nokho ukuthi abantu abasha sebemukele ezokuxhumana ezintsha , futhi lokhu kukhomba amandla amakhulu okuqinisa ukubandakanywa komphakathi . Bonisa ababambe iqhaza isiyingi sengxabano , usebenzisa amanothi ezifundo akwiSahluko 5 ukubasiza . Kuleso naleso sigaba cela ababambe iqhaza ukuba bacabange ngokusekuke kwenzeka ezimpilweni zabo . UMnu Mali uvela e-Somalia futhi uhlala Ewadini-XYZ . Ufaka isikhalazo kumasipala ngokungabi khona kokwethulwa kwezinsizakalo ngokuphathelene nokususwa kwezibi . Uma eya ukuyokhalaza utshelwa ukuthi akasona isakhamuzi saseNingizimu Afrika futhi akanalo ilungelo lokukhalaza . Ekwenzeni ucwaningo ngamaphuzu asemqoka akhubaza intuthuko yesikhathi eside . Uma usuwafundile amanothi esifundo emakhasini ama-65 kuya kwangama-67 bachazele ukuthi kulo msebenzi bazosebenzisa ulwazi oluqoqwe ekuhlaziyweni ngokwe-SWOT kwezindlela zokuziphilisa zamaqembu ngokwenhlalo . Amaprojekthi azongazishayi ndiva izisusa zobusulu , kuhlanganisa nobulili kanye nokungalingani emphakathini , kanti namaphethini asesunguliwe okulinganiswa kanye nokulingana kobulili kuzohlala kuzitshiwe . Phuma uye ngaphandle ufike uchaze kwabebesemgqeni B ukuthi kufanele bacabange ngendaba abafuna ukuyitshela uphathina wabo . Kungaba yincazelo yokuthi yini abayidlile ngelantshi noma ukudla kwakusihlwa kwangayizolo . Kufanele kube yinkinga esandakwenzeka kubo emsebenzini , noma ekhaya . Isethembiso sokuveza okusesingenisweni soMthethosisekelo kumele senziswe bese sisetshenziswa ekuhlanganeni kwesikole . lesi singeniso kumele sibekwe obala kuzo zonke izindawo zokusebenza . Cishe kuzo zonke izimo zempilo , kwenziwa imizamo yokwakha umphakathi ohlangene , ukubuyisela emuva isithunzi somlando nokusabalalisa amathuba kubo bonke abantu . INingizimu Afrika isikwazile ukwakha izikhungo ezidingwa umbuso wentando yeningi noguqukayo . Umthethosisekelo ugqamisa indlela ezinze emalungelweni nokubeka emqondweni umbuso wentando yeningi onenqubekela phambili , engacwasi ngokohlanga nobulili , indlela engeyabo bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika . Ukupholisa amanxeba esikhathi esidlule nokubhekana nokungalingani okwabangelwa ukubandlululwa ngokobuhlanga okwenzeka isikhathi esingamakhulu eminyaka kungokubonwa njengokumele kwenzeke ngokomthethosisekelo . Ukufinyeleleka kwemisebenzi kusatshalalisiwe , umnotho usimamisiwe nomphakathi ongabandlululi ngokobuhlanga usuqalile ukubonakala . Izigidi zabantu ezazibandlululekile seziyakwazi ukuthola imfundo , amanzi , ugesi , ukunakekelwa ngokwezempilo , izindlu nenhlalakahle yomphakathi . Cishe bangaphezulu ngezigidi ezi-3 abantu abasebenzayo namhlanje kunangonyaka we-1994 , izinga lobuphofu lehlile nesilinganiso semali engenayo sikhulile ngempela . Ukulawulwa kokuphathwa kobungozi : Ukubhekana nezinguquko zobungozi kuyo yonke iphrojekthi . Ubungozi buyoguquka noma bubonakale ngesikhathi sezinqubo zephrojekthi . Uhlelo lokuphathwa kobungozi kuyodingeka lwenziwe ngcono njengoba lokhu kwenzeka , umphathi wephrojekthi kuyodingeka azise bonke ababandakanyekayo ngazo izinguquko . Nokufinyeleleka - ngokufanayo amanye malungu omphakathi kungenzeka angabi nazo izinto zokuhamba kanti uma indawo okuzobanjelwa kuyo umhlangano noma iseshini yokubika ingakwazi ukufinyeleleka kalula awakwazi ukuba khona ngoba ukukhokhela izithuthi kungabiza kakhulu kanti nesikhathi esithathwa yisithuthi ukufika kuleyo ndawo kungawavimbela ukuba beze . Amazinga okulungisela isabelomali abekiwe ohlelweni olubizwa ngokuthiwa umjikelezo wesabelomali . Amalungu omphakathi kanye Namakomidi Ezigceme kudingeka ukuba azi mayelana nalo mjikelezo ukuze bakwazi ukubamba iqhaza ngempumelelo . Kunezabelomali ezintathu kumkhandlu kamasipala ezisebenza ngesikhathi esisodwa : isabelomali sonyaka odlule , isabelomali sononyaka kanye nesabelomali esizayo sesikhathi esiphakathi . Lokhu kubizwa ngokuthiwa ukwenziwa kwesabelomali sonyakamningi .
