Bacele ukuba benze uhlu lwezinto ezintathu eziyintuthuko okumele ziqhakanjiswe kwifliphushadi njengoba bezokudinga emsebenzini olandelayo . Imithetho ethile isib. i-National Land Transport Transition Act iphoqa iminyango ethile ukuba ididiyele izinhlelo zayo namaphrojethi kuma-IDP , njengoba eminye imithetho yokwehlukana ingabhekisi kulolu daba ngokucacile . Awekho amaforamu amasha ohulumeni noma amaqembu asenzelwe inhloso yenqubo yokubuyekeza i-IDP . Amaforamu akhona naseshiwo ngaphezulu asetshenzisiwe . Ukwethula izinqubomgomo zezabasebenzi ezisebenzayo kanye nemihlomulo yokukhulisa imisebenzi , ikakhulukazi kubantu abasha kanye nasemikhakheni eqasha abantu abangenawo amakhono asezingeni eliphezulu . Ukufunda ukuba nozwelo akusikho nje ukufunda izimpendulo ' ezilungile ' kodwa ukufunda ukuba khona kuzo . Ukuba khona kusho ukuzinikela ngokugcwele komunye umuntu nemicabango yakhe , ubeke eceleni eyakho imicabango , indlela owenza ngayo nolwazi onalo . Ubukhona yisifundo sokuzidela ngendlela enempilo . Aqinisekisa ukuthi amalungu omphakathi ayaqonda mayelana nesabelomali sokugcina , i-SDBIP kanye nezivumelwano zokusebenza . Iqhaza leKhomishani Yamaphoyisa Omphakathi ekulweleni umthetho namazinga okuziphatha , ukuqapha inqubo yokuqasha kumele liqiniswe . Kwenzekeni ngesikhathi uzama ukususa uphathina wakho umletha lapho okhona ? Yiziphi izinguquko zezikhathi zonyaka ekusetshenzisweni kwezinsiza ( umdwebo wezikhathi zonyaka ungasiza lapha ) ? Kufikela eminyakeni ye-1970 i-Seymour kwakuyisifunda esasiphumelela kwezolimo . Umnotho wawuncike endlini yomshini wokusaha amapulangwe kanye nemboni yokwenza ugwayi enkabeni yedolobha . Ugwayi , amazambane , izithelo ezifana namawolintshi kwakulinywa ngenhloso yokuhweba ngazo kuleyo ndawo . Ungawumbandakanya kanjani umphakathi kwi-IDP ? KuneKomidi Lesigceme elikhuthele emphakathini wakho . Imihlangano ivamise ukubanjwa ngehora lesi-6 ntambama njalo phakathi nezinsuku . Ngenxa yokuthi abantu besifazane balindeleke ukuba banakekele izingane baphinde balungisele imindeni yabo ukudla ngaleso sikhathi , abantu besifazane abaningi abakwazi ukuhambela le mihlangano . Abanye abantu besifazane bakhathazwa ukuhamba ngezinyawo noma ukuyogibela amatekisi uma ekusabalalisweni emakhaya ebusuku . Abanye babo bayakhononda ngokuthi uma bekwazile ukufika emhlanganweni izindaba noma izikhalo zabo azishaywa ndiva . Khona manjalo abanye bathi babhekana nabayeni babo abanolaka nababahlukumezayo uma behambele le mihlangano esikhundleni sokuba babe semakhaya . Manje izingxoxo mayelana nokwenziwa kabusha kwelokishi phakathi kweKomidi Lesigceme kanye nohulumeni wasekhaya ziyaqhubeka . Abesifazane bashiywe ngaphandle . Bafuna ukuziqalela inhlangano yabo yabesifazane njengomphumela walokhu . Abesilisa bayawuphikisa lo mbono , bathi asikho isidingo sokuthi abesifazane bahlangane bodwa njengoba abesilisa benawo amandla okuthatha zonke izinkinga zomphakathi . Umkhandlu okhethiwe yiforamu ephelele yokuthatha izinqumo ngama-IDP . Igunya lokubamba iqhaza kombuso wentando yeningi ukwazisa , ukuxoxisana kanye nokuphawula ngalezo zinqumo , ngenkathi inqubo yokuhlela / yokwenza izinqumo iqhubeka . IMPOKOPHELO KAHULUMENI IME KANJE : UKUSUNGULA UMSEBENZI WOMPHAKATHI OGXILE KUBANTU NOKHUTHAZWA NGABANTU , ONIKEZELWA NGOKULINGANAYO , OZINGANHLE , ISIBINDI KANYE NENDLELA YOKUZIPHATHA OKUYIYO , UKUSEBENZA NGOKUNCOMEKAYO KWENHLANGANO KANYE NOKULETHWA KWEMISEBENZI EZINGANHLE . Ukusebenzisa imali eningi kutshalomali yisinyathelo sokuqala . INingizimu Afrika kumele yenze ngcono izinga lokusebenzisa kwayo imali ngokuhlela kangcono , izindlela zokuthenga ezisebenza kahle nokuncintisana okukhulu emnothweni . Kunesidingo sokusebenza kahle kuzo zonke izindawo zokutshenziswa kwemali kahulumeni ngoba okwembozile konke kungase kukhule kancane esigabeni esiphakathi . Kudingeka kunakwe kakhulu ukulawulwa komthethosivivinywa wamaholo kahulumeni , kwenziwe ukuthi izisetshenziswa zibe khona kwezinye izinto okumele zenziwe kuqala . Lokhu kuyobandakanya ukulinganisa okuyingcindezi okuqhudelanayo okufana nokwandisa inani labasebenzi , ukukhokhelwa ngokufanele kwabasebenzi abanamakhono nokuthuthukisa imihlomulo . Kungabe umkhandlu wakho unayo i-PMS ? Ngicela uchaze . Ikomiti Lewadi lingaveza ukungagculiseki ngokubhalela ehhovisi lesikhulumi sikamasipala ngokungasebenzi kahle kwekhanseli yewadi . Ikhanseli inganikeza ezinye izibopho Ekomitini Lewadi . Ikhasi lokucatshangwayo ngephrojekthi kufanele liphothulwe ngaleyo naleyo phrojekthi edinga ukwesekwa wuhulumeni , yizinhlangano ezingekho ngaphansi kukahulumeni , noma yizinkampane ezizimele . Leli khasi lokucatshangwayo likhuthaza ukwesekwa kwephrojekthi ngokuchaza izinto ezikuyo futhi liyasiza ekulandeleni inqubekelaphambili nasekwenzeni abantu baziphendulele ngezenzo zabo . Enhlanganweni ephelele hola ingxoxo maqondana ne-Batho Pele endaweni yokusebenzela . Buza imibuzo engezansi bese ubhala phansi izimpendulo ephepheni . Ngokuhambisana nesivumelwano umhlinzeki womsebenzi uvuma ukuhlinzeka umsebenzi othile kamasipala egameni likamasipala ngezikhathi , ngesabelomali kanye nalokho okuqondiwe abekelwe kona . Umhlinzeki womsebenzi uzohlinzeka ngomsebenzi kumphakathi wonkana noma engxenyeni yomphakathi . Futhi angahlinzeka ngomsebenzi wonke noma ngengxenye ethile kuphela yomsebenzi . Isibonelo , inhlangano yomphakathi ingenza isivumelwano sokuqoqa udodi ezindlini nasezitaladini , ziwubeke ezindaweni lapho amaloli omkhandlu ezowulanda khona . Ukuzibophezela ekuthengeni impahla nemisebenzi emphakathini nasemabhizinisini azimele izindlela ezikhulisa imboni yasekhaya nokudalwa kwamathuba emisebenzi . Ukuqinisa Amakomidi Ezigceme ukuze akwazi ukusebenzisana ngempumelelo enkulu ne-IDP njengohlelo olubanzi lukamasipala . Khumbula ukuthi izinqumo zeKomidi Lesigceme azilibophezeli ikhansela lesigceme . AmaKomidi Ezigceme awanawo amandla mayelana nezinqumo zomkhandlu . Ngakho-ke iKomidi Lesigceme lidinga ukwakha ubudlelwano bokubambisana nekhansela nokusebenzisa amathuba avezwe ngenhla ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izwi lomphakathi liyezwakala . UMthethosisekelo noMthetho Wezinhlaka Zikamasipala noWezinhlelo Zikamasipala ibeka uhlaka lokuthi imikhandlu yomasipala ingayiphasisa kanjani imithetho kamasipala imikhandlu . Iqhaza le-CDM maqondana nokuthathela phezulu udaba lwe-HIV / AIDS ngumasipala wendawo . Ukuthintana namaqembu emikhakha - isibonelo , inhlangano yabalimi ukuthola imibono yabo mayelana nezinhlelo zemakethe entsha . Okucatshangelwayo yilawo maphuzu angaphandle angaba nomthelela ezinhlosweni zephrojekthi . Kuyizinto esingekwazi ukuzilawula , futhi okudingeka zibhekelelwe ngoba uma zinganakwanga zingaholela ekutheni iphrojekthi ingaphumeleli . Isibonelo , uma usuku lokubeka isisekelo sesakhiwo selumisiwe bese liyana izinsukwana , lokho kubanga ukubambezeleka kwayo yonke inqubo , kodwa yinto engaphezu kwamandla ethu . Ngakho-ke , izindlela zokwenza zidinga ukuthi zibandakanye izinqubo kanye nokungenelela kuwo wonke amazinga ukuqinisekisa ushintsho oluhlelekile , olufaka konke futhi oluhambisana namaqhinga . Lokhu kufanele kubandakanye ukungenelela okuwushintsho ezingeni lomuntu , leqembu , lenhlangano noma lomphakathi . Wonke amalungu omphakathi anelungelo lokwethamela umhlangano womkhandlu okhethekile ngenhloso yokuzobuka lapho kunenkulumo mpikiswano emayelana nesabelomali nalapho isabelomali sesivotelwa . Amakomidi Ezigceme kumele akuqinisekise ukuthi umphakathi uyakhuthazelwa ukuba ubambe iqhaza ngokuwazisa ngalo mhlangano . Ukudlulela ngale kokuxoxisana nokubamba iqhaza ekwakhiweni kokubambisana okusimeme , ngokusungula uchungechunge oluqhubekayo lokusebenzisana kanye nokusebenzisana ngobuchule phakathi kwalabo abanamagalelo ahlukahlukene . Izinkomba zokusebenza ngemfanelo ezisemqoka ( ama-KPI ) ayizinjongo ezizwakalayo , nezikwazi ukulinganiswa abasebenzi abavumile ukuthi bazozifinyelela emva kwesikhathi esithile . Umsebenzi ngamunye kumele abe nekontileka yokuphatha ukusebenza ngemfanelo equkethe ama-KPI , le nkontileka ingasetshenziswa ukubabophezela ekwethulweni kwalawa ma-KPI . Ukwenziwa kwenqubomgomo eyisu ye-HIV ne-AIDS nenqubomgomo yendawo yokusebenza . Icebo lokuxhumana - Omasipala benza amacebo ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ukuxhumana kuyacatshangwa , ngesu kuhambisane nezinqubo zikamasipala . Emashumini eminyaka ezayo , njengoba iminotho evelayo ikhulisa ingxenye yayo ekuhwebeni komhlaba nakutshalomali , ukwehla kwesisindo somnotho waseMelika , Yurophu naseJaphani kuyoba nomphumela ongemuhle kwezombusazwe nezempi . Lokhu kuyoholela ekwakhekeni kabusha kwezindaba eziphathelene nokuphathwa kwamazwe ngamazwe nasemandleni okubusa ebungcwetini bokwakhiwa kwezindlu , kubonakale izikhungo ezintsha ezinomthelela . Umdwebo osekhasini elilandelayo ukhombisa ukuthi ezingeni lomuntu ngamunye , ukuphatha ukungenela kokwahlukahlukana kunomthelela kanjani endleleni esicabanga ngayo , emiqondweni yethu , ezifisweni zethu , ezidingweni zethu kanye nasekuziphatheni okusobala . Lokhu kuzophinda kuhlole ikhono lomuntu lokushintsha izinkolelo zakhe , nezinto ezingewona amaqiniso azicabanga ngabanye abantu . Ukungenelela kumele kuhlelwe ezingeni leqembu ukuze kuqedwe ukucwasa kanye nezinto ezingelona iqiniso ezicatshangwa ngabanye abantu kanye nokuhlonza izivimbo ezingatholakala emasikweni akhona , kuzinqubomgomo , ezinhlelweni kanye nasezinqubeni . Phuma uyochaza kwabaku-A ukuthi nabo kufanele bacabange ngendaba noma isehlakalo abazositshela ophathina babo . Ukuguquguquka kusemqoka ukuze kube nokubamba iqhaza komphakathi okuyimpumelelo . Imiphakathi ingaba khona kuphela kwezinye izikhathi futhi izinhlelo kuzodingeka ukuba zifaniselwe noma ziguqulwe ukuya ngezidingo zabantu abathintekayo ekwenziweni kwalesi sehlakalo , isib . Uhlelo lokuguqula ibhizinisi : ukuhlela ukukhuphula imali engenayo ngemikhiqizo namasevisi enkathini yesikhathi enqunyiwe . Abagqugquzeli kumele baqikelele ukuthi abamele amaqembu abangenawo amandla okuzivikela bayingxenye yamaqembu okusebenza futhi izwi labo liyezwakala emaqenjini . Omasipala kumele bahlele balawule ezokuphatha kwabo umsebenzi , ezokwabela izimali kanye nezokuhlela ukuze izidingo zomphakathi zibe phezulu eqhulwini . Isigaba 74a no-b soMthetho Wezinhlaka Zikamasipala , ka-1998 ubeka imisebenzi namandla amaKomidi Esigceme ukugcizelela isibopho samaKomidi Esigceme emphakathini ukuwuphathela izindaba zawo . Amakomidi Ezigceme engenza imizamo ekhethekile ukuqinisekisa ukuthi abesifazane bamelwe emihlanganweni yokubika nokuthi imibono yabo iyamukelwa futhi ifakwe ekubikeni phakathi komphakathi kanye nomkhandlu kanye nekhansela lesigceme . Indlela emayelana nezokuphatha kuphela kumele ilandelwe ukuqasha abasemazingeni aphansi , izikhulu ezisezikhundleni eziphezulu zinikwe igunya eliphelele lokuqasha abasebenzi abaseminyangweni yabo . Ubambiswano nekhansela lesigceme - amaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele akhe ubudlelwano bobambiswano nokusebenzisana nekhansela lesigceme yalo njengoba amakhansela esigceme eyingxenye yomkhandlu . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele akhe inqubo ehlelekile lapho ehlangana khona njalo nekhansela lawo lesigceme ukunikeza ulwazi kwikhansela maqondana nezinkinga zomphakathi , ngemihlangano yeKomidi Lesigceme , nangokuqinisekisa ukuthi imihlangano eyejwayelekile iyenziwa ukunikeza umphakathi ulwazi ngezinkinga zomkhandlu . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele abuye aqinisekise ukuthi ukuxhumana okwejwayelekile kuyenziwa nekhansela lesigceme yawo ukufaka uvo ekuhlolweni kokusebenza , isabelomali nezinqubo zohlelo lwentuthuko oludidiyele . Chazela ababambe iqhaza ukuthi umphakathi usuvumelene ngombono , izinhloso kumele kuvunyelwane ngazo bese kuklanywa amasu aleyo naleyo nhloso . Bheka emanothini esifundo asekhasini lama-44 nelama-45 ukuthola usizo . Omasipala bomkhakha A , ( noma omasipala abayimikhandludolobha ) : Lawa ngamadolobha amakhulu , anegunya eliphezulu kanye negunya lomthetho ezindaweni zabo . Nakuba kungekho ubudlelwano obubhekiswe ngqo kusomlomo , amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme angathintana naye ngemihlangano yomkhandlu nemicimbi . Chaza ukuthi amaqembu kumele ukuba bacabange ngalowo masipala abawazi kahle bese benza isabelomali sokusebenza ngomasipala abazisusela yena ekhanda . Ukusuka ekubonisaneni kuphela kuhlonyiswe abantu ngamakhono kusho ukubenza babe ngabanikazi bakahulumeni wendawo kanti kuqeda ukuthembela ekwenzelweni . Ukuthuthukisa amakhono alabo abanegalelo ekubanjweni kweqhaza ezinkundleni ezimele i-IDP ukuze bakwazi ukuzibandakanya ngokubonakalayo kunqubo yokuhlela nokusebenza . Izindlela zikahulumeni waseNingizimu Afrika azilula , kodwa le nselelo ayikhona ukuzithethelela ngokungalandeli indlela yokuzibophezela . Ukusungulwa Komnyango Wokuqapha Nokuhlaziya Indlela Yokwenziwa Komsebenzi yisinyathelo esihle sokuqinisa indlela yokuzibophezela . IKhomishani iphinde ibize ukusebenzisana phakathi kwabaninimasheya namabhizinisi kahulumeni nokwazisa umphakathi ngezivumelwano zokwenziwa komsebenzi nongqongqoshe beKhabhinethi . Ukugwema - ukubalekela ingxabano yindlela eyejwayelekile futhi ithemba ngukuthi uma ungayinaki ingxabano ' izohamba ' . Ukubhekana nengxabano ngendlela efanele kudinga ikhono , ulwazi nokuvuma ukuzimbandakanya . Ukuphika yindlela eyejwayelekile yokubalekela ingxabano . Nakuba singazizwa sengathi senza ngendlela efanele , ukugwema ingxabano kungenza abantu bazizwe benengcindezi , becasukile , belinyaziwe futhi bengasafuni lutho futhi kungenzeka ingxabano ibuye ivele . Lokhu kuholela kwisimo lapho wonke amacala akwingxabano ehluleka khona . Cabanga kudala kakhulu futhi ukhumbule isehlakalo ngesikhathi ubona ukwehluka kubafana uma uyintombazane , kanjalo ngokufanayo uma ungumfana , kwakusho ukuthi ulindelwe ukuthi uziphathe ngendlela ehlukile futhi wawuphathwa ngendlela ehlukile . Kufanele ugxile ekuhlukeni ekuziphatheni , hhayi kumehluko womzimba . Xoxela uphathina wakho indaba yakho . Uhulumeni wendawo kufanele athole bese athatha isinqumo sokuthi imali engenile ingasetshenziswa njani kanye nemali eholakele uma kukhokhelwa izinkonzo nemisebenzi abazimisele ukusiza umphakathi ngayo . Lokhu kunzima ukukuhlola , ngaphandle uma izabiwomali zibekelwe imisebenzi ' eqondene nabesifazane ' , ' eqondene nabesilisa ' noma ' ubulili ' . Ngesikhathi okusemqoka sekuqala ukuvela , kungasiza ukumema abalethi bezidingo abangaziletha ukuba beze osukwini olulandelayo ukuzobamba iqhaza ekuhleleni . Amaminithi omhlangano womkhandlu anikwa umphakathi . Ukwakha indawo evumela ukunikezwa kwezinsizakalo - ku-1.2 sixoxe ngeziboniso zombuso wentando yeningi kanye namalungelo abantu ayisisekelo . Amalungelo awami wodwa kodwa ahambisana nezibopho . Ukugqugquzela umphakathi ukuthi uthathe isibopho ngezehlakalo nemisebenzi ukuze amalungelo aqinisiwe ngaphakathi komthethosisekelo nangaphakathi koMthethosivivinywa Wamalungelo kumele anakekelwe futhi agqugquzelwe . Isibonelo ilungelo lokuba sendaweni yemvelo ehlanzekile lihambisana nesibopho sokuthi izakhamizi zikhokhele izilinganiso nentela ukuze izinsizakalo zinikezwe . Uhlelo kudingeka ukuba lunikeze izibopho kanye nemisetshenzana ebantwini abathile bese kubekwa nesikhathi sokwenziwa komsebenzi ngamunye . Ukubuyekezwa kwenqubo yesibonelelo nomxhaso wezezindlu ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izinto ezisetshenziswayo zihambisana nezinguquko ezinhle kwinqubomgomo yokuhlaliswa kwabantu . Ukuthuthukisa izinga lemfundo kudinga ukulawula okwenziwa kahle , nokuxhaswa okuvela kuzo zonke izinhlangothi ezithintekayo kanye nesikhathi . Ngokocwaningo lonyaka wezi-2010 lwezinguquko emikhakheni yezemfundo engama-20 emhlabeni wonke , izindlela ezikahle ziqala ukuthela izithelo emva kweminyaka ecishe ibe yisithupha emva kokuqaliswa kwezinguquko , ngenzuzo esimeme evela esikhathini eside . Okungaxhunyanwa naye kanye nemininingwane yakhe . Kungabe icebo liyisebenzisa ngokugcwele imibono yabesifazane kanye nabesilisa , amakhono kanye namandla abanawo ? Lapho izinombolo ezilinganayo zingenzeki , qinisekisa ukuthi ' kunesisindo esilinganayo ' sabo bobabili abesifazane kanye nabesilisa ( isibonelo okungenani ama-30% ) . Lo msebenzi uphothulwa yiqembu elincane elijutshelwe ukubhala uhlelo lokugcina . Uqala esontweni lokuhlela futhi kumele kuzanywe ukuba uphothulwe esontweni elilandelayo . Inkundla yokulalela komphakathi yenziwa maqondana nodaba oluthile . Isibonelo , inkundla yokulalela komphakathi ukuthi kutholakale uvo ngomthetho kamasipala ohlongozwayo . Lokhu kusho ukuthi iKomidi Lesigceme ngumgudu amakomidi angawusebenzisa ukufaka izikhalazo noma ukuphakamisa izinkinga noma ukuveza izidingo ezithile . AmaKomidi Ezigceme anesibopho emphakathini sokuthatha lezi zikhalazo aziyise kumkhandlu ngendlela efanele . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kungenzeka angaphazamisi ukusebenza komkhandlu , lokhu kufaka phakathi ukungayali iziphathimandla ngomsebenzi wazo wokuthatha izinqumo zenqubomgomo yomkhandlu . Qikelela ukuthi ababambe iqhaza bahlanganisa abalethi bezidingo abazinze emphakathini . I-GEP inezinhlelo eziningana zoKungenelela Kokusekwa Kokuhlela ukukusiza ukuba wakhe imihlahlandlela yokuphatha ibhizinisi lakho nokuba ubone ubuthaka obungase budinge ukulungiswa . Ungabeki ngaphambili ezakho izimvo . Lindela ukuzwa ukuthi bathini abanye abantu ebese ubeka uvo lwakho emva kwalokho . Omasipala banemali encane abayibekela ukweseka ukwethula ngokushesha kohlelo lwesigceme ukuze umdlandla obukhona ngesikhathi sokuhlela ungashabalali . Izinqumo ngokukhokhwa kwale mali kumele ziqhamuke emsebenzini wokuhlela , uhlelo lokukhetha kumele lungafihli lutho futhi umphakathi kumele waziswe . Umsebenzi olandelayo uchaza indlela yokwenza isabelo sale mali yezigceme . Umkhandlu kamasipala ungalihlakaza iKomidi Lesigceme uma lihluleka ukufeza izinjongo zalo . lesi sahluko sichaze izinhloso nemigomo yohlelo oluzinze emphakathini futhi besidingida le ndlela lolu hlelo olutholakala ngayo enqubenimgomo yezentuthuko kahulumeni wendawo . Uhlelo lwe-CBP luyadingeka entuthukweni yemiphakathi , ekuphuculeni izidingo , ekwenzeni kube lula ukusebenza kwezinqubomgomo ezibalulwe emithethweni kahulumeni wendawo kanye nasekwenzeni uMthethosisekelo ube yinto ephilayo ezakhamuzini . Izahluko ezintathu ezilandelayo ziqukethe amakhono angempela Emva uhlelo lwe-CBP . Ikhono lokwazi ukuxhumana lingathuthukisa indlela amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme asebenzisana ngayo namakhansela , izikhulu zikamasipala kanye nawo ewodwa . Izingxabano eziningi zingagwemeka futhi kungabhekwana nazo kalula ngokuthuthukisa indlela yokuxhumana . Ukuxazulula inkinga - lena yingxenye enzima ekulamuleni njengoba kungalesi sikhathi lapho kuvunyelwana khona ngesixazululo . Umlamuli usiza izinhlangothi ekucabangeni isixazululo esifanele , ebeka imicabango futhi ethola isivumelwano esifanele zonke izinhlangothi . Umlamuli angadinga ukusebenzisa amasu ahlukahlukene ukusiza izinhlangothi ukuba zifinyelele ekuvumelaneni ngokwamukelekile . Lokhu kungafaka ukuvumela izinhlangothi ukuba zikhokhase , ukusebenza nolunye uhlangothi , ukuzihlanganisa izinhlangothi , nokubhala isivumelwano esemukelekile kuzo zonke izinhlangothi . Ngesikhathi sesigaba sokuhlela ababambe iqhaza bayohlonzwa bese kuthi amandla abasebenzi abadingekayo afakwe ukuqinisekisa impumelelo ekusetshenzisweni kwephrojekthi . Kwezinye izikhathi ilunga lethimba lephrojekthi liyokuthola kudingeka ukuthi lenze ithimba lokusekela ukuze kufezeke imiphumela ebhekeke kubo . Isibonelo , ukuze kuhlelelwe ingqungquthela , amalungiselelo okuhamba kwabazothamela ingqungquthela kuyodingeka enziwe . Umphathi wephrojekthi angabe esenza ithimba elizosekela elizobhekana ngqo nezokuhamba . Ithimba lokusekela liyonikezwa umyalelo omfishane ocacile yithimba lephrojekthi oyobe ufaka phakathi isikhathi okumele sithathwe , imisebenzi , izibopho nesabelomali . Ezinye izimalimboleko ezitholakala ngaphandle zitholwa ezimakethe zekhephithali njengamabhange ohwebo . Omasipala abaningi abekho esimeni zokubolekwa imali , okwenza ukuba kube nzima kubo ukweboleka imali . Uhulumeni kusadingeka ukuba athole izindlela zokuqeda lezi zinkinga . Uhlaziyo lobulili luyithuluzi oluwusizo kakhulu ngoba lubulala izinkoleloze kubantu , lwembule imisebenzi evamise ukunganakwa , luyasiza ukuqinisekisa ukumeleleka okuyingxubevange ekuphathweni kwezemvelo , luphinde lusize ukuhlonza izinhlangano zasezindaweni eziseka imiphakathi . Khumbula ukuthi kusemqoka ukuxoxa nabalethi bezidingo ukuzwa imibono yabo ngezindaba ezithinta umphakathi kanye nezidingo abazilethayo ukweseka nokugcwalisa ulwazi lomphakathi . Umsebenzi wekhansela ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izidingongqangi ziyalethwa kanye nokuthi intuthuko iyakhuthazwa ezindaweni elizimele . Amakhansela , kanye nezikhulu , kufanele baqinisekise ukuthi kunemali eyanele ukuletha izidingo kanye nokukhuthaza intuthuko ehleliwe . Isidlobongela - umuntu onobudlobongela ukholelwa ukuthi ' ngilungile ' , unengqondo evalekile , akalaleli , uyabusa , uyisiqhwaga , ukhuluma kakhulu , uyesabisa , akakwazi ukulinda . Ukwenza isabelomali ngobudedengu noma ngokungaqapheli imali isetshenziswe nje noma yikanjani futhi kungangeni imali eyanele , kungashonisa umasipala . Sebenzisa umsebenzi wocingo oluphukile njengendlela ethokozisayo yokukhombisa ukuthi kulula kanjani ukuba ulwazi lungadluliseki ngendlela kanye , nomonakalo okuwenzayo lokhu njengoba kukhuthaza amahemuhemu futhi kudale nezinsolo . Imibiko yesabelomali kumele ihlinzekwe ngesikhathi esifanayo nesokuqaphela , ukubuyekeza nokuhlaziya imibiko . Ikhombisa ukuthi iphrojekthi inamathelana kanjani nesabelomali okuvunyelwene ngaso nokuthi ngabe ukhona yini umnyakazo okumele wenziwe ukubuyisela izinto endaweni yazo . Iyiphi indlela esetshenziswe ngumkhandlu , iyiphi indlela esetshenziswe ngumphakathi ? Empeleni ishedula yezinsizakusebenza yisabelomali . Ukwenza isabelomali kubalulekile ngoba kungachaza umehluko phakathi kokuphumelela nokungaphumeleli kwephrojekthi . Uma sisincane kakhulu isabelomali eminye imisebenzi angeke yenziwe . Uma izindleko ziqagelwe zaba nkulu kungaba nzima ukuthola izimali zephrojekthi . Manje sekuyisikhathi sokuhlonza izinkinga nezithiyo ezisemqoka esimeni esikhona , izimbangela zazo kudingeka ziqondwe kanye nendlela ezinomthelela ngayo kwezinye izinto . Okuhlangabezane neNingizimu Afrika mayelana nokwenzeka kwamanye amazwe kubandakanya imihlomulo ebonakalayo nobunzima obukhulayo . Inselelo ukusebenzisa amathuba akhona ngesikhathi kuvikelwa abantu baseNingizimu Afrika - ikakhulukazi abampofu - ezingozini ezimayelana nezindlela ezintsha zokuhweba nezokutshala imali . Isibonelo , iNingizimu Afrika inezinga eliphansi lokonga futhi lethembele kakhulu ezimalini zangaphandle ukukhokhela izindlela zayo zokonga imali . Ukwethembela kakhulu ezimalini ezingenayo ezivela ngaphandle kwenyusa ingozi yokungasimami komnotho wasekhaya . Ukukhula kancane emazweni asethuthukile bekuhambisana nokudingeka kakhulu kwemikhiqizo yamazwe asathuthuka , kufaka isandla ekwemukeleni ukuphinda kusimame kwempahla evela ngaphandle kwezwe . Kuze kube manje lesi simo siphinde sibe yinselelo kwabenza inqubomgomo nabakhiqizayo , ngoba izidingo zamanje zemikhiqizo evela ezimakethe ezisakhula zilinganiswa ngempahla nezinto zemvelo ezingakaguqulwa , kuneqoqo lemikhiqizo eyahlukene edingwa amazwe asethuthukile . Udaba okusaxoxiswana ngalo ukuthi ngabe iNingizimu Afrika ingabahlanganisa yini abantu abangasebenzi bakhiqizele izimakethe zangaphandle . Abanye bathi umnotho awukho kahle ezimbonini ezisebenzisa kakhulu izandla zabasebenzi ukwenza imikhiqizo okucija ngoba isakhiwo sezindleko siphezulu kakhulu , izinga lokushintshisana ngemali alizinzile , ingqalasizinda ayikho kahle nesisekelo samakhono sincane kakhulu . Yize kunjalo iNingizimu Afrika ingancintisana namanye amazwe ezigabeni eziningana uma lokhu kukhathazeka kungabhekanwa nakho - okuningi kwakho kuyalungiseka . Izinga lokushintshisana ngemali elingazinzile livimbela impumelelo . Lolu hlelo luhlongoza ukuthi ukuxazulula izinkinga zezindleko zezisetshenziswa zaleli zwe kuyoba negalelo elikhulu elisimeme ezindlekweni . Njengezwe elingenisa imali elingene , iNingizimu Afrika kumele incintisane namanye amazwe ngokwemikhiqizo nezinkampani esezizakhele igama , nangokungena ngempumelelo emigudwini yomhlaba wonke yokusabalalisa imikhiqizo . Lokhu kuyodinga ukuzibophezela okukhulu ocwaningweni nasentuthukweni nezentengiso yakho , enkundleni yokugcinwa kwempahla ngempumelelo nasebudlelwaneni obusizayo namanye amazwe kwezomnotho . Uhlelo lokuqasha abaneziqu zemfundo ephakeme nesu lohulumeni bezindawo lokuthuthukisa amakhono kumele kwenziwe ukuheha abafuna imisebenzi abasezingeni eliphezulu . Ukwenza ngendlela efanele izinhlelo ezintsha eziningana zamanzi zokuphakela amanzi ezindaweni zasemadolobheni nasezimbonini , izindlela ezintsha zokunisela emfuleni uMzimvubu nasendaweni yaseMakatini , nohlelo lukazwelonke lokongiwa kwamanzi ukuthuthukisa ukusetshenziswa kahle kwamanzi nangempumelelo . Ngonyaka we-1992 , izakhiwo zomphakathi edolobheni zasungula izinkundla zentuthuko zomphakathi wase-Seymour . Amalungu alezi zinkundla kwakuyi-SANCO ( okuyi-South African National Civics Organisation ) , i-ANC ( okufaka phakathi Umbutho Wentsha , noMbutho Wabesifazane ) kanye namaqembu othisha . Inhlosombono yale nkundla kwakungukusungula indlela ebanzi yentuthuko okwakuhloswe ngayo ukusiza zonke izakhamizi zakulelo dolobha kanye nokuqinisa umnotho wendawo . Kuzokuba nokuntuleka kwamathuba okubandakanya abesifazane kanye nobuholi besifazane . Amaqhinga awazogxila ekusimamiseni abesifazane , njengokuthuthukiswa kwezinsizakalo zenhlalakahle , izinhlelo zokuxhasa izingane , izikhungo zabesifazane , kanye nezinye izindawo eziphephile . Ukulalela ngokuzimisela kudinga umdlandla futhi kubandakanya ukulalela okunenhloso : yokuthola ulwazi , ukuxazulula izinkinga , ukwabelana okuthandwayo . Linda ukuba umuntu aqedele lokho akushoyo . Ungaphazamisi ukuze unikeze umbono wakho . Chaza ukuthi inqubo ye-CBP idinga ukuba kwenziwe uhlelo lwesigceme njengoba uhlelo lwesigceme luyithuluzi lokuqinisekisa ukuthi imibono yezakhamuzi kanye nokusemqoka kuzo kuyafakwa ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Bhala phansi amaphuzu abalulekile emakhadini amancane noma kwinothibhuku ukuze ukwazi ukulokhu ubheka kuwo . Ngale kwamaphepha ezimali abhaleke kahle , izinhlangano eziningi zaseNingizimu Afrika aziyitshali imali ngoba umnotho womhlaba uhlala ubuthakathaka . Amabhizinisi akhathazekile ngezinguquko kwinqubomgomo nasendaweni yokulawula okungase kukhuphule izindleko . Kwelinye izinga , utshalomali oluphansi luphinde lwenziwe ingqalasizinda engafanele ehlinzekwa ngamabhizinisi kahulumeni . INingizimu Afrika kudingeka iqede lokhu kukhula kancane notshalomali oluphansi . Uhulumeni uneqhaza elisemqoka okumele alibambe ekwakheni ukwethembeka nokuthemba ukukhuthaza utshalomali lwesikhathi eside . Ibhizinisi lineqhaza okumele lilibambe - uma wonke umuntu efaka imali eningi , inzuzo yezomnotho iyokhula ifike emkhakheni ozimele . lesi SAHLUKO SIBHEKA ABABAMBE IQHAZA ABAHLUKAHLUKENE nobudlelwane babo nokusebenza kwamaKomidi Ezigceme . Ibuye ibheke amasu afanele okugqugquzela angasiza amaKomidi Ezigceme ukuxhumana nalaba ababambe iqhaza . Nika lelo nalelo thimba labantu ababili ( kungaba nesidingo sokunikeza amathimba amaningi umgomo ofanayo , kuye ngesibalo sababambe iqhaza ) bese ucabanga ngokuthi bazowusebenzisa kanjani umgomo emphakathini wabo . Uma lesi sigaba sesiqediwe iphrojekthi kumele ichazwe kahle . Izindleko , imisebenzi , okusemqoka kakhulu namashedula kuyaqondakala futhi bonke ababambe iqhaza kumele baqonde ukuthi impumelelo iyolinganiswa kanjani nokuthi ubufakazi buyoqoqwa kanjani . Umsebenzi WeKhomishani Kazwelonke Yokuhlela ukubonisa uhulumeni nezwe ngezindaba ezithinta ukuthuthuka kwezwe kwesikhathi eside . Lolu hlelo olwezwe lonke , futhi zonke izigaba zomphakathi kudingeka zisebenzele ukulwenza lube yimpumelelo . Ukusebenzisa ngempumelelo lolu hlelo , iKhomishani ibona amaphuzu asemqoka empumelelo . Phindela emuva embuzweni ngamunye bese ucubungula kafushane ukuthi ngabe Ikomidi Lesigceme sakho linokungalingani yini phakathi kwamaqembu ezenkolo , amaqembu amaqembu , noma amanye amaqembu ? Ukuxhumana - umphakathi unikezwa ulwazi ngephrojekthi noma udaba bese ucelwa ukuba uphawule . Umbono unganikezwa ngokusebenzisa uhlolo olwenziwa ngumkhandlu noma enye inhlangano embandakanyekayo kwiphrojekthi noma umhlangano womphakathi isibonelo . Impendulo : Amalungu omkhandlu avala umnyango uma ebona iqulu labantu liza futhi aphuma ngomnyango ongemuva . Lokhu kuzosiza futhi Amakomiti Ewadi ukuthi enze izibopho zawo njengokuxhumanisa phakathi komphakathi nekhansela kanye nekhansela yawo yewadi uma enohlaka lokubamba iqhaza . UKUZE SIQINISEKE NGENTUTHUKO EQHUBEKAYO , kunesidingo sokubona ukubaluleka kobulili obubili njengezinto ezihambisanayo ngokwemvelo . Kubalulekile futhi ukuhlonipha ngokugcwele ukulingana kanye nokulinganiswa kwemisebenzi yomphakathi eyenziwa ngabesifazane kanye nabesilisa ezimpilweni zabo . Indlela abesilisa kanye nabesifazane ababukwa kanye nabaphathwa ngayo emphakathini ngenye yezinsika zanoma yiluphi uhlelo lwezombusazwe , ezenhlalonhle kanye nezomnotho . Ngokufanayo indlela esetshenziswa ngayo ngenye eveza kakhulu amaqiniso ngayo . lesi sahluko sihlola ubuhle bokuhlanganisa imigomo yobulili kanye nokulingana kumaprojekthi entuthuko . Isahluko siphetha ngengxoxo yezingqinamba ezibhekene neNingizimu Afrika uma umbono wobulili ungaqhutshwa ngokunomdlandla . Ukugxila kakhulu ekunakekelweni kwabakhulelwe nezingane ezisanda kuzalwa . Inqubo ehlelekile lapho owesithathu esiza ngendlela ethize ukwandisa ukuxhumana phakathi kwezinhlangothi ezimbili , ngokuvamile emhlanganweni . Lokhu kwenziwa ngokuqondisa okukhulunywa ngakho , ukuqgugquzela ukwabelana ngolwazi , nokusiza nokuqondisa inqubo ukuze umsebenzi othile ufezeke ngaphandle kobunzima . Ababambe iqhaza basebenza ngababili futhi bafunda yonke imigomo esemqoka yendlela esimeme yokuziphilisa . Isigungu esikhulu sekomidi noma ikomidi lesigungu lemeya lemukela izincomo ezivela kumakomidi ezikhundla nabaphathi bomkhandlu ezibe sezisetshenziswa ekwenzeni i-ajenda yomkhandlu . Kuyini okukhulu okwenzeka noma okuyizimo ezenzeka emphakathini wethu eminyakeni engama-30-50 edlule ( ngaphambi kokufika kwezinguquko ezinkulu ) ? Ukulawulwa kwezinga lomsebenzi : Ukuqaphela imiphumela ekhethekile yephrojekthi ukubona ukuthi iyahambisana namazinga afanele nokuhlonza nokusebenzisa izindlela zokunciphisa izimbangela zokwenziwa komsebenzi ngendlela enganelisi . Indllela ezinze esigodini yokunakekelwa ngokwezempilo okusemqoka yingxenye yesigaba esihamba phambili somshuwalense kazwelonke wezempilo . Ukuze le ndlela ibe yimpumelelo , inqubo yezempilo kudingeka ibe nabasebenzi abaningi ( kubandakanya ochwepheshe nabosizo oluphuthumayo ) , izindlela ezintsha zesigungu sokuphatha nokuqinisa izinhlaka zomthetho zokumeleleka komphakathi . IKomidi Lesigceme ngalinye kumele linqume mayelana namakomijana kanye namaphothifoliyo elifuna ukuba nawo esigcemeni salo . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme anikezwa amaphothifoliyo athile . INingizimu Afrika idinga ukusebenzisa ngempumelelo okusemqoka okumele kwenziwe kuqala kwenqubomgomo yayo yezomnotho . Ukuhluleka ukulawula , ukuba necala ekwahlukaneni , nezimvume ezingahlukaniseki kukhubaza ukusetshenziswa kwenqubomgomo ekhona . Ingxoxo nethimba lezokuhlela , ikomidi lesigceme noma namaqembu okusebenza abhunge udaba lwamakhasi okucatshangwayo ngezinhlelo ezidinga ukwesekwa kwangaphandle . Uvuma zonke - umuntu onguvuma zonke , ongakwazi ukuthatha izinqumo , ukhulumela phansi , ucabanga ukuthi ngeke akwazi ukwenza umsebenzi noma , akakwazi ukubhekana nabantu abaphambukile . Izindlela zohlelo lwe-CBP zihlinzeka omasipala ngendlela yokuqinisa ukubamba iqhaza ohlelweni lwabo lwe-IDP . Ngaleyo ndlela uhlelo lwe-CBP lusiza omasipala ekubeni babe negalelo elibonakalayo emigomweni yoMbiko Kahulumeni neyoMthetho wezi-2000 Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala . Zicinge ngokuzimisela amathuba okukhula , ukufunda , ulwazi namathuba . Ukungasimami kwenqubomgomo kuyinkinga . Ngesikhathi kunezinye izimo lapho kumele kuguquke khona inqubomgomo , uhulumeni uvama ukubukela phansi umphumela ophazamisayo wokulungiswa okukhulu kwenqubomgomo ekwenziweni komsebenzi . Ukusimama kumele kuqine futhi okwamanje ukusimama akukho . Ukuhamba kunqanyulwe indawo kwenza umphakathi uwubone ngenye indlela umumo wamanje wendawo yomphakathi . Ubambiswano ngemisebenzi kamasipala ( municipal service partnership ) ( i-MSP ) yisivumelwano phakathi kukamasipala kanye nomhlinzeki wemisebenzi . Umhlinzeki womsebenzi kungaba ngenye inhlangano kahulumeni ( njengebhodi lezamanzi noma umasipala wesifunda ) , inkampani ezimele , inhlangano engekho ngaphansi kukahulumeni ( i-NGO ) noma inhlangano yomphakathi ( i-CBO ) . Umsebenzi 1 Khetha iqembu elilodwa leqembu lezenhlalonhle emphakathini onolwazi ngalo-isibonelo , abalimi , abahlali basemjondolo , abanikazi bamabhizinisi amancane njll . UMthetho uhlinzeka ngamathuba amaningana ezakhamuzi ukubamba iqhaza kuhulumeni ngale kokhetho . Izigungu ezifana nemikhandlu ephethe izikole , amakomidi ezigceme , izinkundla zamaphoyisa omphakathi namakomidi emitholampilo kuhlinzeka izakhamuzi ngezwi nangamathuba okulungisa izikhungo eziseduze kwazo . Imiphakathi ingaphinde ibambe iqhaza ekudwebeni izinhlaka zezinhlelo zikahulumeni wezindawo . Yize ekhona la mathuba , kunokukhula kwegebe phakathi kwezakhamuzi nohulumeni . Ukubheduka kodlame kweminye imibhikisho yomphakathi kukhombisa ukucasuka , hhayi kuphela ngesikhathi esithathwayo sokulethwa kwezidingo , kodwa futhi ngokukhathazeka ukuthi imiphakathi ayilalelwa kahle . Hlukanisa ababambiqhaza ngamaqembu ayisithupha bese unika iqembu ngalinye izinga elilodwa phakathi kwamanye amazinga e-IDP ukuze baxoxisane ngalo , okufaka phakathi nezinga lokulungiselela . Ababambe iqhaza kufanele babelane neqembu lonke ngabakubonile . Amakomiti amawadi akusiwo amalungu ohulumeni wangempela anamandla . Ayikomiti labaluleki elakhiwe ngabantu abazi indawo kahle futhi bangasiza ikhansela ukubuza kahle , ukubika nokutshela abantu kanye nokuthatha isinqumo ekhanselini . Amakhansela amawadi awanalo ilungelo ngokomthetho lokuboshezelwa kwikomiti lewadi - baboshelelwe kwikhanseli , ingxenye yabo kanye nomphakathi . Ishejuli enemininingwane izodingeka , eyethula imidati yalowo nalowo mcimbi , ibonise inani lezinsuku , ( eziboniswa enyangeni yeshejuli ngokubanzi ) lowo nalowo msebenzi okumele wenziwe kulowo mcimbi , ukubaluleka kwalowo msebenzi , nokuthi lowo msebenzi kumele uwenze nobani . Usihlalo uyovula umhlangano bese elandela uhlelo lomhlangano udaba nodaba . Ukufakwa kwe-HIV ne-AIDS kwi-IDP . Imiphumela yezempilo yesikhathi eside yenziwa ngamaphuzu enzeka ngaphandle kwenqubo yokusebenza kwezempilo : indlela yokuphila , ezokudla namazinga okudla okunomsoco , ezemfundo , indlela yokuziphatha yezocansi , izingozi zomgwaqo nezinga lodlame . IKhomishani yenze izincomo kuzo zonke lezi zindawo . Okusemqoka kakhulu kubandakanya isifundo sezocansi , ukudla okunomsoco , ukuvocavoca umzimba nokuvimbela ukubhema nokusebenzisa budedengu uphuzo oludakayo . Le misebenzi yezenhlalakahle okumele ithathelwe phezulu yizo zonke izakhamizi nokuthi ithuthukiswe yimindeni nezikhungo . Ukulethwa kwezidingo kuncike ezinhlelweni kanye nakubasebenzi bakamasipala abaphumelelayo nabagculisayo . Ukulethwa kwezidingo okubuthakathaka kuvamise ukuba yingenxa yokuphathwa kabi noma ukusebenza okubi . Uhlelo lokuphathwa kokusebenza lwenza izinhloso kanye nokusoshiwe kuhlale obala yikhona iziphathimandla kanye namalungu omphakathi bezohlola kalula inqubekelaphambili futhi babone nezinkinga . Nakuba inqubo yokuhlela isungulwa futhi ihlanganiswe wumasipala , ukuze isebenze , lolu hlelo lube ngolwesigceme , emelwe yikomidi lesigceme . Omasipala bahlomisa amakomidi namakhansela esigceme ngamakhono ukuze agqugquzele inqubo yokuhlela ' ezosiza lelo nalelo komidi ekwenzeni izimemezelo sesikhathi zokuphatha izikhundla ' . Imicimbi yohlelo lwe-IDP elandelanayo iqala ngomhlangano kaZwelonke , i-National Cabinet Lekgotla kanye nowezifundazwe i-Provincial Exco Makgotla , okuyimihlangano ebanjwa ekuqaleni kwalowo nalowo nyaka . Le mihlangano yenza uhlelo lokwenza , i-Programme of Action ( PoA ) , lonyaka bese luphakamisa nezindaba zesikhathi sonyaka owodwa kuya kwemithathu . Le micimbi ilandelwa yinkulumo kaMengameli wezwe ayibhekise esizweni , yizinkulumo ezethulelwa izifundazwe ngoNdunankulu bazo kanye nenkulumo ngesabelomali . Kuthatha isikhathi esingakanani ngaphambi kokuba amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme eneliseke ngomsebenzi awo ? INingizimu Afrika iyobe ibukeka kanjani ngonyaka wezi-2030 ? Izwe selifike esigabeni sokuguquka komumo wabantu lapho amazinga okuzala ehla khona nesibalo sabantu sizinza . Lokhu kuguquka kunomthelela omkhulu esakhiweni sesibalo sabantu , izinga lokwanda kwabasebenzi , nezidingo zabantu ezifana nezemfundo nezempilo . UMkhandlu We-AIDS WaseMpumalanga Koloni ( ECAC ) uzoxhasa ukukhethwa komxhumanisi we-HIV / AIDS . Izinkomba ezigxile kwisimo uqobo zibaluleke kakhulu . Akwanele ukwazi ukuthi abesifazane bayabandakanywa emsebenzini : ikhwalithi yokubandakanywa kwabo kanye nesipiliyoni , noma Kungabe kusezingeni lemihlangano yomphakathi , emakilasini asezikoleni zamabanga aphansi noma njengabasebenzisi bezinsizakalo zomphakathi , konke kubalulekile . Abantu abaningi bacabanga ukuthi ukwahlukahlukana kusho umehluko okhona phakathi kwabantu bamasiko ahlukene . Abantu bahlobanisa ukwahlukahlukana nomehluko wobulili kanye neminyaka . Kodwa ukwahlukahlukana kubandakanya izinto eziningi ngaphandle kokwehluka phakathi kwabantu okwakhelwe esikweni , ebulilini noma eminyakeni . Abantu bahlukile ezintweni eziningi kubandakanya iminyaka , inkolo , isiko , ezemfundo , isipiliyoni , ezempilo , ukuhlala ngokwendawo , inzuzo , isimo sobuzali , isimo sesandulela ngculaza , amandla okusebenza , njalonjalo . Umkhandlu wedolobha umemezele ukuthi ufake imingcele endaweni eseduzane nendawo yokuhlala enendawo yegalofu ukuze kwakhiwe izindlu ezibiza intengo ephansi . Abahlali basendaweni yokuhlala enendawo yegalofu abajabule ngalezi zinhlelo ngoba lokhu kuzothelela amanani ezindlu zabo . Umphakathi ohlelelwa lezi zindlu ufuna lolu hlelo luqhubeke ngoba kunokuntuleka kwezindlu futhi indawo abahlala kuyo manje igcwele kakhulu . lesi sigaba sokusetshenziswa siyofaka phakathi ukubuyekeza , ukulungisa izinhlelo nokubika okuqhubekayo . Ukuthi uhlelo seluyasebenza akusho ukuthi yonke imithelela eyacatshangelwa ukuthi ingaba khona ekuqaleni komjikelezo wephrojekthi iyohlala injalo kuze kube sekugcineni kwephrojekthi . Kusemqoka ukuthi ukulungisa okuthile kwenziwe nokubikela bonke ababambe iqhaza kwenziwa njalo . ZONKE IZAKHAMIZI KUMELE ZITHOLE IMISEBENZI NGOKULINGANAYO EZINELUNGELO LOKUYITHOLA . MEASURABLE ( LILINGANISEKE ) - ingabe izinga lomsebenzi liyalinganiseka yini , futhi lingenziwa ngezindleko nangomzamo ofanelekile ? Nokwehluka - imiphakathi yehlukile futhi inezidingo , imiqondo nemicabango eyehlukile . Izindlela zokuxazulula ingxabano kumele zibe khona ukuze lokhu kwehluka kube ngokwakhaya bese kufaka inguquko nenqubekelaphambili efanele . UMbiko KaHulumeni ngoHulumeni Bendawo , we-1998 , uyinqubomgomo eyasungula isisekelo sohlelo olusha lukahulumeni wendawo . Uhlelo lwe-IDP lugcwalisela isidingo esibekiwe kuMthethosisekelo kanye nemithetho elandelayo ( njengoMthetho Ogunyazwayo Wohulumeni Bandawo , ka-1998 ) ukuze omasipala bakhe baphinde balawule ukuphatha kwabo kanye nezinqubo zokwenziwa kwezabelomali nezokuhlela ngenhloso yokubeka phambili ohlwini lokubalulekile ukulethwa kwezidingongqangi zomphakathi kanye nokubamba iqhaza komphakathi ezinhlelweni zentuthuko kuzwelonke nasezifundazweni . Imihlangano nomphakathi ngokubanzi kanye namaqenjana ahlanganisa ikomidi lesigceme lapho kubhungwa khona imethriksi yohlelo lokwenza neqoqa lezinhlelo ( okungabhalwa kwifliphushadi bese kuyananyathiselwa ukuze kubonwe ) . SINGAKWAZI KUPHELA UKUFINYELELA EZINJONGWENI ZETHU ZOKUBUSA NGEMFANELO UMA ABANTU , IMIPHAKATHI KANYE NEZIHLANGANO ZEPOLOTIKI , NALEZO EZINEMIBONO EHLUKILE , ZIKHOLELWA FUTHI ZESEKA IZIKHUNGO ZENKAMBISO YOMBUSO WENTANDO YENINGI " NGUMONGAMELI U-MBEKI ENKULUMWENI ESEMQOKA AYETHULA EMHLANGANWENI JIKELELE WONYAKA NGONYAKA WE-SADC ELECTORAL COMMISSIONS FORUM , E-DAR ES SALAAM , E-THANZANIYA , NGO-SEPTEMBA KA-1999 . Usihlalo uzoqhuba umhlangano ngokohlelo lomhlangano olubhalwe ngababambe iqhaza . Lolu lwazi lusemqoka ekukhombeni izidingo zomphakathi . Lolu lwazi luhlanganisa izibalo nemibiko , okuhlinzeka ngomlando wesigceme . Umsebenzi 4 Yikuphi osekwenziwe kuleli zinga ? Uhlelo lwe-CBP lubandakanya ukukhetha nokuqeqesha abagqugquzeli abazosebenza nemiphakathi ukubasiza nokubeseka ekubambeni iqhaza ekuhleleni emiphakathini yabo . Lokhu kubalulekile ngoba kuzokusiza ekutholeni izidingo zomphakathi . Kuqopha amaqembu ehlukehlukene emphakathini , izinhlobo zezindlela zokuziphilisa , labo abangenamandla okuzivikela emphakathini , imisebenzi esemqoka kanye nabalethi bezidingo . Imiphumela , Izinkomba Nezindlela Zokuqinisekisa ( imisebenzi , izinsizakusebenza nezindleko ) kuhlinzeka ngohlaka lokulungisa imibiko yenqubekelaphambili yephrojekthi ( ukuqhathanisa lokho okwakuhleliwe nalokho okufeziwe ) . Uhlelo lwe-CBP wuhlelo olugqugquzelwayo olwenzelwe ukuqinisekisa ukuthi imibono yomphakathi iyafakwa entuthukweni yomphakathi . Indlela esebenzayo ngebandakanya ithimba elisemqoka okungenani labagqugquzeli ababili esigcemeni ngasinye , elihambisana nekomidi lesigceme lendawo . Leli thimba kumele lihlanganise okungenani umgqugquzeli oyedwa oqhamuka esigcemeni noyedwa oqhamuka kumasipala , kanye , uma kunokwenzeka , nomunye umgqugquzeli oqhamuka kwelinye isigceme . Esimeni esihle kakhulu abagqugquzeli bakamasipala kumele bathathwe emikhakheni ehlukehlukene , ukuqinisekisa ukuthi imikhakha ehlukehlukene kamasipala iyazi ngohlelo lwe-CBP , nokubeka umuntu wohlelo lwe-CBP okungaxhunyanwa naye kulowo nalowo mnyango . Ingxoxo yekomidi lesigceme yemethriksi yohlelo lokusebenza kanye nohlelo lwaphambilini lokusebenza . Indlela YabeSifazane Entuthukweni igxile ekutheni abesifazane bengafakwa kanjani kangcono emhlabeni wabesilisa / abesilisa kanye nakwezinye izinhlelo zentuthuko ezihambelana nalokhu . Leli lisu libheka ngokuqondile umsebenzi wokukhiqiza wabesifazane uma uqhathaniswa nomsebenzi ongakhiqizi lutho , futhi unezimpawu zokuba namaphrojekthi afaka imali abesifazane ngaphandle kokubhekana nezimbangela ezihlelekile zokungalingani ngobulili . UMbiko KaHulumeni ngoHulumeni Bezindawo , we-1998 , ungumbhalo wenqubomgomo obeka isisekelo sohlelo olusha lwezentuthuko lukahulumeni wendawo . Lolu hlelo olusha olokuzibophezela ekusebenzisaneni nezakhamuzi , amaqembu nemiphakathi ukuhlinzeka ngeqophelo eliphezulu lempilo kanye nokuhlangabezana nezidingo zemiphakathi zezenhlalakahle , ezomnotho kanye nezinto ezibonakalayo . Lokhu kusho ukuthi omasipala kumele bahlele balawule ezokuphatha , kanye nezinhlelo zesabelomali nezokuhlela ngendlela ezokwenza izidingongqangi zomphakathi zibe phezulu eqhulwini . Intuthuko yamazwe ngamazwe neyezifunda inomthelela eNingizimu Afrika ngezindlela ezixakile . Umbono wethu uthi ukusimama , okwenzeka emhlabeni wonke , kungaba nomthelela omuhle entuthukweni yaseNingizimu Afrika , nakuba kunobungozi obuningana obubonakalayo . Ukuqonda nokubhekana kahle nezinselelo ezinzima ezenzeka emhlabeni wonke kuwumsebenzi wokuqala wokuhlela . Omasipala abakha uhulumeni wendawo banikezwe amandla kanye nemisebenzi ethile . Amazinga kazwelonke kanye nawesifundazwe nawo anamandla kanye nemisebenzi yawo . Ababambe iqhaza kumele banikeze izizathu zokuhlela imisebenzi ngendlela abenze ngayo ngokuthi bazibhale efomini leshedula , ibhashadi noma ngokunikeza izibonelo . Uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini lungaholela ezinguqukweni ezindleleni omasipala abaletha ngazo izidingo . Isibonelo , umasipala ungacabanga ngokusungula ukubambisana neqembu elithile lomphakathi ekuletheni isidingo esithile . Ukubandakanywa komphakathi ekulethweni kwezidingo sekuvele kuyenzeka ezindaweni ezifana neKwaZulu-Natal ne-Eastern Cape lapho umphakathi ubandakanywa ekuhlinzekweni ngamanzi , ukuthuthwa kwendle kanye nakwezokuvakasha . Esigabeni sokuqala seNkombandlela yohlelo lwe-CBP ithimba lezokuhlela liqoqa lihlaziye ulwazi okuhlanganisa nolwazi olukhona emphakathini ngokusebenzisa uchungechunge lwezingxoxo nokusebenzisa amathuluzi ahlukehlukene ohlelo lwe-CBP . Ukuhlaziya ngesineke le mininingwane kuhlinzeka ithimba lezokuhlela ngomlando ophelele nokuqonda isimo somphakathi , izinkinga , amasiko izinhlelo nokuyigugu kulowo mphakathi . Ukuhlonza izinhlangano ezehlukehlukene emphakathini bese kukleliswa ukuletha kwazo izidingo ngokubaluleka nokutholakala kwazo . Isigaba- 152 - izinhloso zikahulumeni wendawo ukugqugquzela imiphakathi kanye namaqembu omphakathi kanye nezinhlangano zomphakathi ezindabeni zikahulumeni wendawo . Cela ababambe iqhaza ukwenza lo msebenzi ongezansi . Qinisa ukusebenza kwemisebenzi ukuthuthukisa ukutholakala kwamakhono , ukuqondanisa abafuna umsebenzi nezikhala zomsebenzi , nokunciphisa ukungqubuzana . Khumbuza ababambe iqhaza ukuthi sisebenzisa lo msebenzi ukwenza ababambe iqhaza bazi ngezinselelo zokwenza uhlelo lwesigceme nokuthi asinaso isikhathi esanele sokulandela leso naleso sigaba ngokujulile , ngakho-ke sizosebenzisa kuphela imizuzu eyi-10 kuya kweyi-15 kulesi sinyathelo , kodwa amaqembu kumele aphume nombono kulesi sikhathi . Uma engakwazi ukuqedela umbono wawo kumele aqhubeke ngangokunokwenzeka . Ukuphathwa nokuthuthukiswa kukamasipala kuyinselelo futhi kubandakanya izindaba eziningana ezinzima . Njengoba lokhu kubandakanya abantu kwasekuqaleni , izidingo zabo , ukunaka kanye nezimfuno kumele kuphathwe ngendlela yokuthi inzuzo ephezulu kakhulu ifinyelele kubantu abayinani eliphezulu kakhulu . Kodwa imiphakathi yenziwe ngamaqembu ahlukile anokunaka kokuncintisana kanti futhi akusho ukuthi wonke amaqembu azokwaneliseka ngasikhathi sinye . Ukusiza abasebenzi bakamasipala kanye nabasizi abakhethiwe ekuphenduleni ngendlela enhle kwizakhamizi endaweni ezikuyo , ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi nokuzibandakanya kuyadingeka . Amakomiti Ewadi adlala indima esemqoka ekwenzeni ukuthi lokhu kuphumelele . Yini oyizwayo kuwe uma ukhuluma nomuntu omuzwayo ukuthi ukulalele ? Lona wumsebenzi wethimba nesampula lezakhamuzi ezimele umphakathi ngokubanzi obandakanya ukudweba noma ukwenza ibalazwe . Sebenzisa amahora amabili kulo msebenzi wokwenza ibalazwe . Ezingeni lezwe , ukukwazi ukusebenza okusemqoka kubandakanya umthetho nezinye izikhungo , ingqalasizinda ( ezokuxhumana ngocingo , ezamanzi , ezamandla nezokuthutha ) , indlela yezemfundo nokuqeqesha , ukuphathwa kwendawo okusimeme , indlela yokwenza izinto ezintsha nezindlela zokuthuthukisa indawo . Ukukwazi ukusebenza kwabantu kubandakanya ezemfundo , ezempilo , ezokuvikelwa nezokuphepha komphakathi . Ikhomishana Yobulili igqugquzela ukuhlonishwa kokulingana ngokobulili futhi isiza ukuvikela , ukuthuthukisa nokufinyelela ekulinganeni ngokobulili . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kufanele alazi ihhovisi lesifunda lalawa makhomishana ukuze akwazi ukutshela umphakathi ngalawa mahhovisi . Futhi kungaba usizo ebhizinisini ukuthi kunciphe izinga lokungalingani . Ukungalingani kukhulisa izindleko zokwenza ibhizinisi , kwenza isimo sezimakethe singaqondi futhi kunciphisa amathuba okukhula . Kwenza ukuthi kube nokungathembani nokuphatheka kabi . Amaholo aphezulu ezikhulu enza umehluko omncane ukwakha umphakathi wabo bonke abantu lapho bonke abantu bezizwa ukuthi bayingxenye yezithelo zentuthuko . Ngesikhathi kungeke kwenzeka ukuthi kulawulwe ngokomthetho amaholo , abaholi kudingeka baqinisekise ukuthi amabhizinisi asebenza kahle . Uhlelo lwe-CBP luyakwamukela ukuthi umphakathi unolwazi olusemqoka lokuqonda ezentuthuko yawo futhi luwugcizelela kakhulu lo mbono . Kulo msebenzi olandelayo izingxoxo nabantu abasemqoka abawumthombo wolwazi zisetshenziselwa ukuthola imibono yabo ngezixazululo ezingaba khona . Ukukwazi ukuphendula uma kuba khona okungahambi kahle kusemqoka embusweni wentando yeningi . Kunamaphutha amaningana enqubweni yokukwazi ukuziphendulela , ngesiko elivamile lokusolana . Inqubo yokukwazi ukuphendula kumele iqiniswe kusuka phezulu kuya phansi . Ekuqaleni nje , ukukwazi ukuziphendulela kwephalamende akukho esimeni esihle , ngoba iphalamende liyahluleka ukwenza umsebenzi walo osemqoka . Imiphumela yezemfundo angeke yathuthuka ngaphandle uma kuzoqinisekiswa ukukwazi ukuziphendulela kuyo yonke inqubo , kusukela emiphumeleni yabafundi kuye ekuhanjisweni kwezincwadi . Ukwanda kwamamashi okukhala ngokulethwa kwezidingo kukhomba ukuthi uhulumeni kumele enze kube lula ezakhamuzini ukusho lokho okuziphethe kabi . Uma zingena esakhiweni sikahulumeni , izakhamuzi kumele zibone ukuthi yimuphi umsebenzi ezingawulindela , nokuthi zingaya kuphi futhi ubani ezingakhuluma naye uma zinganelisekile . Imihlahlandlela YeBatho Pele izosiza amaKomidi Ezigceme ekuphenduleni amalungu omphakathi angaveza umbono wokuthi izinsizakalo azinikezwa yiziphathimandla azikho sezingeni elishiwo yimihlahlandlela YeBatho Pele . Ukuhlola Uhlelo Lokuhlola Ukusebenza - i-PMS kufanele isetshenziswe yibo bonke omasipala ukuze bakwazi ukuzibophezela ekusebenziseni izinsizakusebenza zikamasipala , ukuthuthukisa ukusebenza kahle nangendlela kombutho nokuveza ukufinyelela emiphumeleni . Umasipala kufanele enze Inkomba Yokusebenza Okusemqoka ukukala umsebenzi wawo futhi kufanele ufake nomphakathi . IKomidi Lesigceme liyithuluzi lokumbandakanya umphakathi . Ukuqonda ulwazi lwabalethi bezidingo ngenhloso yokusiza ekusetshenzisweni kwezinhlelo ezigqugquzela umphakathi ukuba usebenze , izinkinga abebhekene nazo nokubenza babe ngabanikazi bezinhlelo futhi bazibophezele kuzo . Izwe lonke laseNingizimu Afrika lihlukaniswe laba ngomasipala . Kunezinhlobo noma imikhakha emithathu ehlukahlukene yomasipala . Ukwenza ukuthi inqubekela phambili isheshe , ukugxilisa umbuso wentando yeningi nokwakha umphakathi wabo bonke abantu , iNingizimu Afrika kumele isuke enkululekweni yezombusazwe iye enkululekweni yezomnotho wabo bonke abantu . Kusemahlombe abo bonke abantu baseNingizimu Afrika ukuzakhela ikusasa , kuqalwe namhlanje . UMnu Nkosi uhlala emakhaya lapho umpompi usandakufakwa khona njengoba kungesiwo wonke amakhaya anamanzi ahambayo . Umpompi ufakwe phambi kwesango lakhe . Abantu abasebenzisa umpompi abawuvalisisi ngakho alokhu eqhubekile amanzi econsa . Lokhu kwenza ukuba indawo ibe nodaka futhi kuletha omiyane . UMnu Nkosi usekhathele ukuba nendawo enodaka esangweni lomuzi wakhe futhi unquma ukufaka ucingo abiye ukuze umpompi ube ngaphakathi kwegceke lakhe futhi avale isango . Abantu bendawo bacasukile futhi beza ukuzokhalaza . Bathi uMnu Nkosi akabacabangeli futhi uzibona ebaluleke kunabo bonke abanye abantu endaweni . UMnu Nkosi ubona sengathi abantu bakule ndawo abamcabangeli futhi bakhombisa ukungabi nandaba njengoba yena nomndeni wakhe behlushwa ngoba abawuvali umpompi . Zikhona yini izindawo zezimila ezingaba ngezibalulekile kwezokongiwa kwemvelo noma kwezokungcebeleka , isibonelo izindawo zemvelo ezinezinto ezikhethekile njengemithi emihle nenomthunzi ? Hlukanisa ababambe iqhaza babe ngamaqembu abantu aba-3 . Cela iqembu ngalinye ukuthi licabange ukuthi yini umsebenzi wokulandelayo ngakunye . Kufanele bacabange ngomasipala wabo uma bephendula imibuzo . Engxoxweni lapho ababambiqhaza behlangene xoxa ngezinjongo zokuhlela komphakathi , ube usebenzisa amanothi akho esifundo ( bheka ithebula ekhasini lama-38 ) njengomkhombandlela . Kungabe Ikomidi Lesigceme linazo izindlela zokwakha amandla abasebenzi ukwenza ukuhlaziya ubulili kwinqubomgomo , uhlelo , kanye nasemazingeni ezikhungo , kanye namandla okufanekisa kanye nokuqhubezela izinhlelo ezixhasa ukulinganiswa kobulili ? Yiziphi lezo zindlela ? Amazinga aphezulu enkohlakalo akhubaza ukukwazi ukusebenza kahle nangempumelelo kukahulumeni , kanye nokukwazi ukuletha imisebenzi ngokomyalelo wezentuthuko . Ngokocwaningo lokuba sobala kwenkohlakalo lwamazwe ngamazwe omhlaba , phakathi konyaka wezi-2001 nonyaka wezi-2010 , izinga lenkohlakalo likhuphukile . Inkohlakalo ivama ukubandakanya bobabili ababambe iqhaza kuyo yomibili imikhakha kahulumeni nezimele . Umqondo wamazinga aphezulu okungasebenzi kahle emazingeni aphezulu kahulumeni kwenza ukuthi kube nzima ukulwa nenkohlakalo . Ikomidi lesigceme nabagqugquzeli bohlelo lwe-CBP basebenzisa ukuhlaziywa kwezindlela zokuziphilisa ngokwe-SWOT kanye nolwazi oluthathwe eSigabeni soku-1 engxoxweni yamahora ayisithupha neqembu . Umsebenzi 5 Nikeza izibonelo ezithile zendlela umphakathi wakho ongazibandakanya ngayo kuleli zinga le-IDP , kanye nalezo zakhiwo ezikhona zokuthuthukiswa kokuzibandakanywa komphakathi . Ukwakhela phezu kwemininingwane eqoqwe esigabeni sokuqala , isigaba sesibili sibandakanya ukuhlaziya ngokucophelela nokuhlanganisa lolu lwazi . Esigabeni sesibili imininingwane eqoqiweyo iyahlaziywa bese kuxoxwa ngayo emaqenjini amancane . Le nqubo iqoqela ndawonye ukuhlaziywa kwezindlela zokuziphilisa zabantu abehlukehlukene ngokwenhlalo , amathuluzi ohlelo lwe-CBP ( amabalazwe , umdwebo kaVenn , indawo enqanyuliwe , ukuguquguquka kwezikhathi zonyaka nomlando wezimo zesikhathi eside ngokulandelana kwazo ) , nokutholakele ezingxoxweni nabalethi bezidingo nabantu abasemqoka abawumthombo wolwazi . Ekupheleni kwesigaba umphakathi ubuyekeza , uhlolisise bese uqinisekisa ulwazi oluhlanganisiweyo . Lokhu kuzobe sekwethulwa esigcemeni kanti izigceme zona kulindeleke ukuba zitomule imiphumela edingekayo eyisihlanu esemqoka ohlelweni lokuhlela . Isigaba 39 soMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , ka-2000 unika umphathi omkhulu wedolobha , isigungu esikhulu sekomidi noma ikomidi eliyisipesheni lamakhansela umsebenzi wokuphatha ukwenziwa kwe-PMS nokuyiletha kumkhandlu . I-PMS kufanele icacise imisebenzi neqhaza lalowo nalowo obambe iqhaza . Kungabe ukuhlaziywa kwengqikithi yeprojekthi kubandakanya ukubuyekezwa kwezinga labesifazane kwezomthetho , ezenhlalo kanye nezomnotho ? Ibhizinisi noma ' izindaba ' ezivuka emaminitini adlule - leli phuzu lifaka izindaba ezadingidwa emhlanganweni odlule amalungu ekomidi okufanele alethe umbiko ngazo . Ngokujwayelekile ungabona kalula ukuthi yiziphi ' izindaba ezivukayo ' ngokubheka izinyathelo okwakufanele bazithathe abantu . Ingabe imisebenzi ehlinzekwayo iyalinganiseka yini namazinga ? Ezemisebenzi ezikwazi ukuphendula emathubeni omnotho . Lokhu kudinga ukufunda kwesikhathi eside nokukhula ngokomsebenzi , ukusimama kwendawo yokusebenza , ukuqiniswa kwezikhungo zokuxazulula izingxabano , ukubuyekezwa kwemithetho namazinga amabhizinisi amancane nalingene , ukugxila emkhakheni wezobudlelwane basemsebenzini kahulumeni , ukuqiniswa kokufakwa kwamazinga aphansi phakathi kwabaqashi , izinhlangano zokufunelana umsebenzi , ukuqinisa ukusebenza kahle kwenqubomgomo yemisebenzi nokuqondanisa imisebenzi , nokuvumela ukufika kwabasebenzi abanamakhono . Uhlelo luklanyiwe kodwa kumele luguqulwe lube wuhlelo lokusebenza ukuze lusebenziseke . Nansi indlela yokukwenza lokhu . Ukwenza izincomo nganoma ngabe yiziphi izindaba ezithinta isigceme ekhanseleni lesigceme noma ngokusebenzisa ikhansela lesigceme kumasipala . Emzuluswaneni waphambilini wezinhlelo ze-IDP , abeluleki babamba iqhaza elikhulu - esikhathini esiningi kwakuba nemiphumela ehambisana nezinkinga . Abeluleki nabahleli bakamasipala bavamise ukuba onjiniyela noma abahleli bedolobha , ngakho-ke basuke beqeqeshelwe ukugxila ezindabeni zendawo nengqalasizinda , esikhundleni sokunaka okuletha izinguquko nokubonisana nomphakathi . Le nkinga yabonwa ngokubanzi wuMnyango Wezokuphatha Nezomdabu kanti ukuqeqeshelwa uhlelo lwe-IDP okwenziwa ngowezi-2001 kwazama ukukhulisa ukuqonda ezentuthuko kunokunaka ukuhlela izindawo . Omasipala bomkhakha B , noma omasipala bendawo : Laba omasipala babelana igunya eliphezulu kanye negunya lomthetho nomasipala bomkhakha C noma bezifunda . Bonke omasipala bendawo bangaphansi kwemingcele yomasipala bezifunda . Umthethosisekelo waseNingizimu Afrika unomthetho sivivinyo Wamalungelo Abantu onikeza isiqiniseko sokuthi uzovikela amalungelo abantu . Lawa malungelo afaka amalungelo okuba sendaweni eyimvelo ' engeke ilimaze ezempilo yabo noma ukuphila kahle ' kanye ' nokuthuthuka kwe-ikholoji okuxhaswayo nokulondekile nokusetshenziswa kwemithombo yemvelo ngenkathi kuqhutshekiswa ukuthuthuka kwezomnotho nezenhlalakahle okuvunyelwe ' . Umthetho sivivinyo Wamalungelo isigaba 24 . Amakomiti Amawadi abamba iqhaza elisemqoka njengemigudu yokunaka komphakathi okumele ube nabayimele kwi-IDP kanye nokuqinisekisa ukuthi izinhlelo zenhlalalakahle nezomnotho zewadi ziwunakekela ngokuphele ngokuphelele umphakathi . AmaKomidi Esigceme asebenzisana nomphakathi ngezindlela ezintathu , okokuqala njengabamele umphakathi , okwesibili ngokwakha ubudlelwano nomphakathi okwesithathu , ngokuzinikela . RESPONSIVE ( LIYAPHENDULA ) - ingabe izinga lomsebenzi liyaphendula yini mayelana nezidingo zezakhamizi ezisizakala ngomsebenzi ? Ukuthuthukisa ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi ngokuthuthukisa izibopho zokuba yizakhamizi kanye nokusungula okusha ukuze baphendule kwizimfuno zezakhamizi . Lokhu kungafaka ukulungiselela amaphamfulethi namapheshana olwazi ukwazisa umphakathi ngezehlakalo . Umsakazo womphakathi indlela esebenzayo yokufaka umphakathi ezindabeni . Isibonelo , amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi kungaxoxiswana nawo ngezehlakalo emphakathini , noma umsakazo womphakathi ungasetshenziswa ukwazisa kabanzi / ukusakaza isehlakalo noma ukubuza umbono ngephrojekthi ehleliwe . Sebenzisa uhlu lwamaphuzu okuhlola ingcebo engxoxweni engabekelwe migomo eminingi ukuthola izindlela zokuziphilisa zeqembu . Bhala izimpendulo . Isibonelo samaphuzu okuhlola ingcebo singakusiza kulo msebenzi ukuqinisekisa ukuthi unalo lonke ulwazi oludingayo . Lokhu kwethulwa njengengxoxo futhi kudonsa amahora amabili kuya kwamathathu . Ababambe iqhaza bavela emphakathini ngokubanzi , okuhlanganisa abamele abantu bonke ngokwehlukana kwabo ngokwenhlalo . Sebenzisa uhlelo lwe-PowerPoint uma unayo umshini obizwa nge-data projector , noma ubhale phansi leso naleso sigaba kwifliphushadi bese ubonisa abahambele izingxoxo umdwebo emanothini esifundo asekhasini lama-35 . Uhlu lwezinhlangano zomphakathi - lungisa uhlu lwezinhlangano zomphakathi , olufaka nemininingwane yokuxhumana nomuntu omele inhlangano ukuze uqinisekise ukuthi ababambe iqhaza bayaziswa ngokwenziswa ngumkhandlu . Isifiso somphakathi kwezombusazwe sisemqoka ukulwa nalesi siqalekiso . Isifiso somphakathi kwezombusazwe silinganiswa ngokuhlola ubungako bemali esetshenziswa ukulwa nenkohlakalo , izindlela zezomthetho zokulwa nenkohlakalo ezikhona ezikhungweni zokulwa nenkohlakalo , ukuzimela kweziphathimandla ezilwa nenkohlakalo ekugxambukeleni kwezombusazwe nokungaguquki okusetshenziswa ngakho umthetho . Ukuthamba emacaleni amancane , ukuqina ngokungavamile enkohlakalweni ebandakanya abaphikisana nawe kwezombusazwe , kukhombisa ukuguquguquka . Yakha indawo enoxhaso esiza abantu ukuba bathobeke futhi babhekane nezinkinga . UMthethosisekelo , ka-1996 ubeka ohulumeni bendawo njengohlaka oluseceleni lukahulumeni olubhekele ukuhlinzekwa ngezinsizakalo . Imiphakathi yethu ibandakanya izinhlobo ezahlukene zabantu abanezinkolelo zamagugu ezahlukene , izindlela zempilo , ezenkolo , izilimi , ubulili , indlela yokugqoka kanye nokubukeka ngokwesimo somzimba . Uma sibhekana nalokhu kwahlukana ngendlela efanele singasho ukuthi kwenza umhlaba ube indawo ejabulisayo futhi kuyasicebisa . Ukuphila nokwahlukahlukana kuyinselele futhi Amakomidi Ezigceme kufanele akwazi ukubhekana nalezi zinselele ngendlela eyimpumelelo . Amaqembu emiphakathini anezidingo ezahlukene , nokufinyelela okwahlukene ezinsizeni futhi nezinto ezihlukene azilindele . Njengoba Amakomidi Ezigceme enomsebenzi wokwenza isiqiniseko ukuthi izidingo zomphakathi ziyafakwa ezinhlelweni kanye nasekuhleleni kukamasipala kudingeka ukuba azi ngamaqembu ahlukene emiphakathini yawo futhi aqinisekise ukuthi amaqembu azizwa ebandakanyeka ezinhlelweni zokuthatha izinqumo . Umsebenzi 2 Yiziphi izinyathelo okumele Ikomidi Lesigceme sakho lizithathe ukwethula nanoma yikuphi ukungalingani okuhlonzile ? Zama ukuhlonza okungenani isinyathelo esisodwa mayelana nombuzo ngamunye ongenhla . Gqugquzela omunye umuntu ukuba akhulume ngokucasuka kwakhe aze azizwe engasabuswa yikho - esikhundleni salokho azizwe sekunguye okubusayo ukucasuka . Ithuluzi lelogifreyimu yidokhumenti ekhombisa izingxenye zohlelo lwephrojekthi ezisemqoka kakhulu ngokulandelana kwazo . Imininingwane yesigaba ngasinye igcwalisiwe emashedulini omsebenzi nezinsizakusebenza ( kuxoxwe ngakho esigabeni esilandelayo ) okuhambisana nelogifreyimu . Indlela esixhumana ngayo ingasibhebhethekisa noma isenze ngcono isimo . Cabanga ngabantu obaziyo abangabaxhumanisi abahle bese uhlonza lokho okubenza babe ngabaxhumanisi abahle . Izinhlelo zokuvala - ziqinisekisa ukuthi zonke izidingo zeprojekthi kuyahlangatshezwana nazo , zithole ukusayindwa okubhalwe phansi yiziphathimandla eziqondene , zenza ngokusemthethweni ukuqedelwa kweprojekthi ngokukhiqiza ulwazi kanye nokulusabalalisa , ukuqedwa kanye nokukhokhelwa kwezivumelwano zomsebenzi kubandakanya nezinkinga ebezisabalele . Uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini aluzenzakaleli . Ukuhlela akusho into eyenziwa yingcweti . Kususelwa ekuzibandakanyeni nasemigomweni yentando yeningi yezepolitiki . Ukuzibandakanya kudinga ukumenywa kwabo bonke abathintekile ukuba babambe iqhaza , okuhlanganisa uhulumeni , umphakathi , osomabhizinisi , abasebenzi kanye neminye imikhakha yezakhamuzi . Gqugquzela ukuvuleleka - ungagxeki uma abantu beveza izimvo zabo . Kungenzeka ukuthi zehlukile kwezakho . Kusemqoka ukuthatha isinqumo kusenesikhathi ngokuthi okusemqoka kulabo abancishwe amathuba kuzoqhakanjiswa yini . Isibonelo , kungavunyelwana ngokuthi eyodwa ezintweni eziyisihlanu ezifiswayo kumele iqhamuke kulaba bantu . Yini ayenzayo eyenza kube lula ukukhuluma naye ? Abamba imihlangano nemiphakathi kanye nalabo okubanjiswene nabo abathintekayo . Ukubambisana phakathi kwamazinga kahulumeni , yize ehlukile kwamanye , ayesebenzelana futhi ahlobene . Abagqugquzeli : Uhlelo lwe-CBP ludinga ithimba labagqugquzeli abazinikeleyo nabaqeqesheke kahle , abayiqonda ngokupheleleyo inqubo yohlelo lwe-CBP , abazoluqhuba kahle nangendlela esebenzayo . Cela uhlangothi ngalunye ukuba lukhethe umkhulumeli walo ebese ucela usomlomo ukuba azibike nokuthi umele bani . Omele iKomidi Lesigceme nekhansela lesigceme bayazethula bona nabalingani babo . Vumelanani ngemigomo ebalulekile nazo zonke izinhlangothi . Isibonelo : vumela uhlangothi ngalunye ukuba luchaze isicelo salo ; lukhulume nomlamuli ; kungabizwana ngamagama njll . Ukuhlanganyela nenhlangano yosomatekisi bendawo bese besiza ukwazisa ngomhlangano ngenye yezindlela lapho ukuhlanganyela kungasiza ukugqugquzela izwi lomphakathi . Amalungu Ekomidi Lesigceme angabona sengathi amalunga omkhakha othile womphakathi ' angamaqili ' ngakho-ke noma yisiphi isiphakamiso abasenza mayelana nokulethwa kwezidingo noma ngamaprojekthi kumele sishaywe indiva . Amakomidi okusiza axhumana neminyango kamasipala futhi angenziwa ngumkhandlu uma kunesidingo . Ukwakha ukukwazi ukusebenza kukahulumeni ukubamba iqhaza lezentuthuko nokuguquka . Amakomiti amawadi kujwayelekile ukuthi akhethwa emhlanganweni womphakathi ukuma unyaka owodwa noma emibili . Uma ilungu lihluleka ukuza emhlanganweni , kufanele ashintshwe . Amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi akhethwa ngokuhlukile ezindaweni zasemaphandleni nasemadolobheni . Umhlangano uyabizwa futhi ikhansela lesigceme lichaza ukuthi lokhu isiphakamiso esisaxoxwayo nokuthi kuzobanjwa umhlangano womphakathi . Futhi uchaza izizathu zokususwa okuhlongoziwe , okufaka phakathi nokuthi indawo lapho kuhlala khona abahlali basemijondolo abaningi ayikulungele ukufakwa kwezindawo zendle ngakho-ke le ndawo ngeke ikwazi ukuba ithuthukiswe njengendawo okuzohlalwa kuyo isikhathi eside . Njengamanje , iningi elikhulu labahlali baguliswa yi-flu nomkhuhlane njalo nje . Labo bahlali abane-TB ngeke bakwazi ukuba ngcono futhi nalabo abane-HIV / AIDS ngeke bakwazi ukuthola ukwelapheka ngaphandle kwezinsizakalo ezanele . Ukuguquka kwesimo sezulu sekuvele kunemithelela eNingizimu Afrika , ngokuguquguquka kwesimo sezulu nezimvula nokukhuphula kwamazinga olwandle . Uhulumeni uyobophezeleka engxenyeni enkulu yezincomo ezikulolu hlelo . Ukusebenzisa lezi zincomo , kuyodingeka aqinise ukuxhumana kokuzibophezela , ukuthuthukisa amakhono akhe , azimisele ukwenza izinqumo ezinzima nokusebenzisana nabanye emphakathini ukusombulula izinselelo . Lokhu kusho ukuxhumana nomphakathi ngokuthembeka nangokuzithoba , ube wenza izakhamuzi zizizwe ziphoqekile ukuphendula ngezenzo zazo . Abaholi , ikakhulukazi kuhulumeni , kumele babhekane nezinqumo nokushintshisana okunzima . Ubuholi obuqinile bumayelana nokwenza lezo zinqumo nokuncenga umphakathi ngempumelelo ukuthi indlela eyiyo isiqaliwe . Ukusebenza kwezezimali kumasipala . Ababambe iqhaza babheka amanothi ezifundo achaza izinhlobo zemisuka yengxabano . Omasipala bangangena emithonjeni emiphakathini . Imiphakathi inezinhlobo eziningi zamakhono nolwazi lwezempilo olunguzuzisa umasipala . Ingonga imali kamasipala njengemithombo etholakala ngokulungiselelwe . Ukwenza ngcono imikhukhu endaweni efanele . Ukubuyekezwa kokusebenza konyaka wonke - umkhandlu kumele ubike emaKomidini Ezigceme kanye nasemiphakathini ngezabelomali zawo kanye nezinjongo zokusebenza . Izinhlelo zokuqalisa - ziholela ekugunyazweni kweprojekthi yizo zonke iziphathimandla . Ukuvumelana kanye nokugunyazwa akuzodingeka kuphela ekuqaleni kweprojekthi kodwa kuzodingeka kuzo zonke izigaba ezinhlobonhlobo . Ukusekela okusabalele kuwo wonke umphakathi kuyadingeka ukuze ukusetshenziswa kohlelo kube yimpumelelo . Kuhulumeni wentando yeningi osebenza kahle lokhu kusekela angeke kwabonakala kungabalulekile . Izinkulumompikoswano ezinamandla zisemqoka ukwakha ukuvumelana nobunikazi bohlelo obusabalele . Izinkulumompikiswano ezakhayo nazo zinomthelela ekwakhiweni kwesizwe ngokuvumela iNingizimu Afrika ukuthi iqonde kangcono futhi ibe umnikazi wezinhlelo zayo ezisemqoka ezenziwa ngokubambisana . Izingxenye ezehlukene zohlelo zidinga ukuvumelana nokuzinikela kwemikhakha eyehlukene . Uma kuvela ukungavumelani , kusemqoka ukuthi izizathu zokungavumelani kuxoxiswane ngazo bese zichazwa ngokucacile , khona kuzoba khona ukuvumelana ngosekuzokwenziwa ukuze kuyiwe phambili . IKhomishani Kazwelonke Yezentuthuko ingasebenzisa amandla ayo okuhlanganisa ukuhlanganisa ababambe iqhaza nokuhola izingxoxo ukuze kuvele izisombululo . Uhlelo lwe-CBP luqhubezela luqhubezela izinhlelo zenqubomgomo kahulumeni , njenge-Letsema noVuk'uzenele , zigqugquzele imiphakathi nezakhamuzi ukuba balawule indawo yabo ngokuvolontiya . Amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi kufanele babheke ukusetshenziswa kwemali ukuze babone ukuthi umasipala wenza kanjani ukuze uphethe uhlelo . Ukuvunywa kwebhajethi omunye wemisebenzi ebalulekile esetshenzwa amakhansela . Amakhansela Ewadi kudingeka ukuba babuza amakomiti amawadi ngaphambi kokuba bavume ibhajethi . Amalungu amawadi kufanele abheke izinto eziphathelene nabantu bewadi . Imithelela evela ngaphandle kwephrojekthi ingaguquka noma nini , ngakho kusemqoka ukuthi kuhlolwe ubungozi ngaso sonke isikhathi somjikelezo wephrojekthi . UHLELO LOKULAWULA UKUSEBENZA KUKAMASIPALA LUQUKETHE UHLAKA OLUCHAZA NOLUMELE UKUTHI IMIJIKELEZO NEZINQUBO ZIKAMASIPALA OKUMAYELANA NOKUHLELA , UKUQAPHA , UKULINGANISA , UKUBUYEKEZA , UKUBIKA KANYE NOKWENZA NGCONO KUZOKWENZIWA , KUHLELWE , KULAWULWE KANJANI , OKUFAKA PHAKATHI UKUNQUMA MAYELANA NEMISEBENZI YALABO ABEHLUKAHLUKENE ABADLALA INDIMA . Ezingeni lezindawo umhlangano kahulumeni wendawo , i-Local Government Makgotla , ubanjwa ngoMashi kanti uhanjelwa ngamakomiti amakhulu omasipala nezimenenja ngenhloso yokwenza uhlelo lonyaka wezimali . Uhulumeni wendawo ubuye uqale ukwenza uhlelo lweminyaka emithathu lwe-IDP . Uhulumeni wendawo njengomsunguli : Uhulumeni wendawo angasebenzisana nezinye izinhlaka zikahulumeni ukuhlonza amandla akhona endaweni engaphesheya kwemingcele kamasipala . Lokhu kunomthelela ezinhlelweni kanye nakumacebo angakhuthaza ukukhula komnotho endaweni . Ukuhambisa ngokushesha intuthuko , iNingizimu Afrika idinga ukusekelwa kakhulu yizo zonke izakhamuzi , ubuholi kuyo yonke imikhakha ebeka phambili okufunwa yizwe ngokuhlanganyela ngaphambi kwezinjongo zesikhathi esifushane , kanye nokuthuthuka kakhulu kokusebenza kukahulumeni . Kwesinye isikhathi kungadingeka ukuguqula inqubomgomo , kodwa ezindaweni eziningi kumayelana nokuthola amalungelo asemqoka , ukusebenzisa izinhlelo zikahulumeni , ukwenza abantu baphendule ngezenzo zabo nokuthola izisombululo ezinqala zezinselelo ezinzima . Amaqembu anikezwa umsetshenzana . Amaqembu anikezwa imizuzu ecishe ibe yi-10 ukuya kweyi-15 ukuthi baxoxe ngomsetshenzana wabo bese babelana ngezimpendulo zabo ekuhlelweni . Amakomidi Ezigceme kanye nabantu ababamele banelungelo lokulindela ukulethwa kwemisebenzi . Kumele ukuba kukhunjulwe ukuthi imiphakathi nayo kumele iqinisekise izinganhle nenani lemisebenzi okuchaziwe kumazinga omsebenzi . Isibonelo , kumele ukuba azise ngendlela okuyiyo , bachaze ngesimo sabo ngokuthembeka , futhi bazibophezele ukuthi bazoziphatha ngendlela emnene nehloniphayo ngesikhathi besebenzisana nabahlinzeki bemisebenzi , njll . Amakomidi Ezigceme adlala indima ekuqinisekiseni ukuthi izidingo zemiphakathi yawo zidluliswa ngempumelelo nangokuyikho . Futhi kumele ukuba aqinisekise ukuthi amalungu omphakathi ayaziswa mayelana nolwazi , ukuthi bangaluthola kuphi futhi kanjani . Kumele agcizelela ukuba anikezwe impendulo ehlelekile ephuma kumkhandlu Nakumakomidi Ezigceme . Xoxa ngezindlela ezahlukahlukene okumele ukuba zisetshenziswe ukuqinisekisa ukufakwa phakathi , bhala uhla lwazo kufliphshadi . Ababambe iqhaza banikezwa ithuba lokwengeza olunye ulwazi olwashiyeka ngaphandle ekuhlanganisweni kokuqala kolwazi . Izinhlangano ezihlonzwe eSigabeni soku-1 ziqondaniswa nesifo esisemqoka . Umhlangano uphinde uthole ithuba lokwengeza ulwazi oluvela ezingxoxweni nabalethi bezidingo nasemisebenzini bese uhlolisisa izifiso ngokuphathelene neqoqa lohlelo lwe-IDP , Ikhasi lobunjalo bempilo yezinhlobo zabantu ngokwenhlalo kanye nekhasi lemininingwane yendawo nezemvelo . Makubhekwe amaminithi - kubhekwe ukuthi ayirekhodi eliyiqiniso lomhlangano odlule ngoba amamithini ayirekhodi elisemthethweni lemihlangano . Amakomiti Amawadi awanamandla asemthethweni ngaphandle kokufaka imibono ngqo kwikhanseli noma ngekhansela lewadi . Abanawo amandla asemthethweni okuthatha isinqumo ezibopha noma ngaba ngubani kumasipala . Ikhansela lewadi lingummeli wewadi kukhanseli futhi zonke izinqubomgomo nohlelo lwezinqumo lwenziwa yikhanseli . Umphakathi kumele ukuba unikezwe ithuba lokuphawula ngohlaka ngaphambi kokwemukelwa kwe-IDP . AmaKomidi Ezigceme aba nekhansela elimele isigceme njengosihlalo kanye namalungu omphakathi angeqile kwayi-10 . Ikhansela lesigceme lingusihlalo wekomidi . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme awaholelwa ngokusebenzela iKomidi Lesigceme . Lowo nalowo mcimbi oseNkombandleleni kumele uhlelwe ngokucophelela . Abagqugquzeli bohlelo lwe-CBP kumele bazi ukuthi yini abafuna ukuyenza ngoba lokhu kwakha ukuzethemba komphakathi uma kuqhubeka kwenzeka . ulwazi olubhaliweyo luhlanganisa ulwazi olwaqoshwa ngaphambi kwesigaba sokuhlela oluhlanganisa izibalo , imibiko , amaminithi emihlangano nama-athikhili , izincwadi zamarekhodi eziphathimandla zendawo kanye nemibiko yezibalo ngokuzalwa kwabantu . Imihlangano yomphakathi nayo inikeza ithuba lemibiko nokwabelana ulwazi kodwa-ke njengoba ivame ukuba nabantu abaningi , lincane ithuba lemininingwane nengxoxo ejulile mayelana nezinkinga . Ilungele ukwethula imibiko mayelana nokusebenza komkhandlu noma mayelana nezindaba ebezethulwe emhlanganweni odlule . Sebenzisa imibuzo ukuthola ulwazi noma ukuchaza ngqo ukuthi omunye umuntu uthini . Amakomidi Esigceme angeke wona ngokwawo aphatha amaphrojekthi amakhulu okulethwa kwemisebenzi ngaphakathi ezigcemeni zawo , lokhu kuwela ngaphansi kwemisebenzi kamasipala . Ukubamba iqhaza okuvela kulabo abathola le misebenzi kusemqoka ekuqinisekiseni impumelelo yokulethwa kwemisebenzi nokuqhubezela phambili intando yeningi . Ezindaweni lapho kunendawo enkulu khona noma isibalo esikhulu sabantu , amakomijana asungulwa kuhambisane namaphothifoliyo . Ngale ndlela amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme angajulisa ukuxhumana nemiphakathi mayelana nezindaba eziyithintayo . Angaqinisa ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi kanye neKomidi Lesigceme ezinhlelweni zokuthatha izinqumo . Ngale kwezakhiwo / amaforamu ajwayelekile okuxhumana nomphakathi njengamaKomidi Ezigceme namaForamu Amele i-IDP , omasipala bangakhetha ukuvula indlela yokuthintana nokuxhumana namakomidi endaweni abasebenzela kuyo . Bangenza amaqembu abambandakenyekayo lapho bezohlanganisa ndawonye abambandakenyekayo abavela emaqenjini amele izimfuno ahlukahlukene ngokuhambisana nendlela yamaqembu njengoba yenziwa ezindaweni zabo ezahlukahlukene . Amakomidi ezikhundla - yiba nohlu oluphelele lwamakomidi ezikhundla omkhandlu nemininingwane yokuxhumana yamalungu amakomidi ezikhundla ukuze uwanike imininingwane eyejwayelekile novo mayelana nezindaba zamakomidi awo . Cela amakhophi ale Mithetho kumasipala wakho uma uyidinga . Isiphetho - lesi isimo esibaluleke kakhulu ekulamuleni futhi umlamuli kufanele aqinisekise ukuthi isivumelwano siyabhalwa ngokwamukelwa nokusayinwa yizo zonke izinhlangothi . Ukuzibandakanya kwabahlanganyeli Kumakomiti Amakhanseli athile , ikakhulukazi uma izindaba zibhekene ngqo namakomiti anesikhathi isifushane sokuphila kuzakhiwo ezingunaphakade . Abeluleki kwezobuchwepheshe bayalibamba iqhaza futhi bangakwenza lokho njengoba behlinzeka ngamakhono nobungcweti umphakathi ongenakho . Ngakho-ke kungaba yinto esemqoka ukuletha abeluleki kwezobuchwepheshe noma abalethi bezobuchwepeshe abavela emazingeni aphezulu kahulumeni wendawo , ama-NGOs noma izinkampani ezizimele . Ukubandakanywa kwabeluleki kwezobuchwepheshe kumele kusize uhlelo ngokuletha ulwazi olufanele ohlelweni , ngaphandle kokubeka imigomo ngemiphumela . Isibonelo , ukubandakanywa kwabeluleki kwezobuchwepheshe kuyasiza uma imiphakathi ikhetha amasu nezinhlelo zokufeza izinhloso zayo , okuba wusuku lwesine kwinqubo yokuhlela . Ukudidiyela umzamo kanjalo nezinga eliphezulu lokuqondisa kubalulekile ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ukufaka kwemisebenzi yezobulili njengendlela efaka konke okuhloswe ngayo ukuguqula izinhlaka ezakha noma ezibhebhethela ukungalingani ngokobulili , kunokugxila ezixazululweni kancane kancane kancane . Ezinye izindaba ezifana nobuzwe / ubuhlanga , izinga / imvelaphi kanye neminyaka kunomthelela endleleni okuphendulwa ngayo ekuhlukaneni . Ukungalingani ngokobulili ngeke kubhekwane nakho ngendlela efanele ngaphandle uma ukungalingani okuvela kulezi zimo eziguqukayo kungalungiswa . Ukwenziwa kwezinhloso kuyisinyathelo esilandelayo ngoba kuhlahla indlela umphakathi ozofeza ngayo umbono wawo . Izinhloso kumele zibe ngeziqondile , ezinokufezeka futhi zibe ngezesikhathi esifushane ukuze abantu babone imihlomulo yazo . Isikhathi esifaneleyo esibekelwa ukufezeka kwezinhloso siba yiminyaka engaphezu kwemithathu . Amakomidi Ezigceme kumele aqinisekise ukuthi wonke amaqembu kanye nemikhakha yomphakathi iyabandakanywa ekuqinisekiseni kanye nasekuqiniseni ukubamba iqhaza komphakathi . Ingxabano ingabhekwa ngendlela engalungile futhi ingadala izimo ezilimazayo kubantu . Isibonelo , isimo sengxabano singaholela odlameni , kulimale abantu kube nengcindezi nokwesaba . Ukubamba komphakathi iqhaza kubalulekile ukuhambisana nezidingo zomthetho ezibekwe kuMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , ka-2000 noMthetho Wezinhlaka Zikamasipala , ka-1998 . AmaKomidi Esigceme asebenza njengomgudu ukuze ukuxhumana phakathi kwababambe iqhaza kwenzeke , ngakho-ke kufanele bazazi izinqubo zokuxhumana ezisebenza kahle . I-PMS kamasipala kumele ukuba ifake phakathi izindaba ezihlonzwe ngumkhandlu eziqondene ngqo nezindawo zokusebenza okubalulekile kumasipala wabo . Ama-IDP kamasipala aveza amaphrojethi okufanele enziwe ngesikhathi esibekiwe futhi anezinkomba ezicacile . Amakhansela anomsebenzi obalulekile wokubheka ukusebenza kukamasipala ngokuhambisana nalokho okubalulekile okufanele kwenziwe . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele aqinisekise ukuthi ayawazi ama-KPI nemiklamo yokusebenza ebekwe kwi-IDP kamasipala wawo ukuze bakwazi ukubheka inqubekela phambili . Isibonelo esingezansi sikhombisa ukuthi ahambisana kanjani ama-KPI nezidingo zoMthethomgomo . Lezi zinqubo zibandakanya ukuqaphela nokulinganisa inqubekelaphambili ukuqinisekisa ukuthi kuyahlangatshezwana nezinjongo zephrojekthi , ukukhomba ukwehluka ohlelweni ukuze kuthathwe isinyathelo sokulungisa . Iphinde ifake phakathi isenzo sokuvimbela okungase kube yizinkinga . Ifaka phakathi ukuqhathaniswa komsebenzi owenziwayo kanye nomsebenzi ohleliwe . Ubani okhokhela ingqalasizinda yezomnotho ? Ezinye izinhlobo zengqalasizinda zihlinzeka ngenzuzo esabalele kwezenhlalakahle nezomnotho . Kodwa-ke ukukhuphula izinga kusho ukuthi izindleko kumele zikhuphuke esikhathini esincane kuya kwesilingene ukwenza imisebenzi isebenzeke kwezezimali . Iphuzu lokuthi isiphehlo samandla kagesi esisha ( esikhiqiza ama-4 800MW kagesi ) sibiza cishe ngokuphindwe kabili kuyo yonke imali eyehlile yezikhungo zamandla kagesi ezikhona ( ezikhiqiza ama-40 000MW ) likhomba inselelo . Ngaphezu kwalokho , amazinga aphezulu okungasebenzi nokungalingani kwenza ukuthi eminye yale misebenzi abantu okuholela bangakwazi ukuyikhokhela ngaphandle uma bexhaswa . Amaphuzu aqinile omphakathi abamba iqhaza elisemqoka . Umqondo wokuthi isimo somnotho asisihle , ukungalingani ngokomlando nezindlela ezintsha zezentuthuko ezihlomulise abantu abanobudlelwane nezombusazwe kwenza ukuthi inkohlakalo iqhubekele phambili kuyo yomibili imikhakha kahulumeni nezamabhizinisi . Lokhu okwenzekayo emphakathini kumele kubhekanwe nakho njengengxenye yokulwa nenkohlakalo . Nikeza amaqembu okungenani imizuzu eyi-15 ukuba enze ucwaningo lwawo . Umhlengikazi osewathatha umhlalaphansi nomabhalane bayodingeka ukusiza kwiphrojekthi nokubhekela ukusatshalaliswa kwamaphasela okudla engeziwe emindenini empofu . Kufaneke kutholakale ukusayina uma kwemukelwa amaphasela okudla , wonke amaphepha anamagama kumele agcinelwe zonke izikhathi zokuvakasha kwabanakekeli . Isinyathelo 1 - Kuvunyelwana ngesikhathi , umjikelezo wokuhlela , iminqamulajuqu yokubika . Ababambe iqhaza bafaka amakhansela ewadi , iziphathimandla zikamasipala , abasebenzi abathuthukisa umphakathi , amalungu omphakathi kanye namaqembu amele izimfuno . Nikeza iqembu ngalinye umsebenzi owodwa kule elandelayo . Indlela encike ekwenziweni kwamaqenjana inikeza imikhakha ehlukene noma amaqembu ehlukene ithuba lokuhlangana asebenzele ukufeza inhloso eyodwa . Imikhakha ehlukene namaqembu ehlukene eza ndawonye ukuze asebenzisane maqondana nephrojethi ethile . Yimiphi imininingwane okudingeka ukuba siyichaze ukuze sikwazi ukuthola izindlela ? Amakomidi Ezigceme kufanele aphathe ukwahlukahlukana ezimweni eziningi , ukusukela ekwahlukahlukaneni phakathi kwamalungu Ekomidi Lesigceme kuye ekwahlukahlukaneni emphakathini . Le mojuli igxile ekwahlukahlukaneni emphakathini nokuthi kunomthelela kanjani entuthukweni . Bonke abahlanganyeli abasembusweni wendawo obambisene badinga ukuba nolwazi oluyisisekelo lukahulumeni wendawo , izinjongo zabo , izinhloso kanye negunya nokusebenza . Ikomiti lewadi lingasiza ukunikeza lolu lwazi emphakathini . Yini oyenzayo eyenza kube lula ukukhuluma naye ? Ukuphatha umasipala kubandakanya iziphathimandla zikamasipala . Iziphathimandla zikamasipala ezisebenza ngokuphatha zinomsebenzi wokuhambisa imisebenzi ehlinzekwa ngumasipala emphakathini . Iziphathimandla , ikakhulukazi emazingeni okuphatha aphezulu , ziqashwa ngokwamakhono kanye nolwazi ezinalo . Ukuhlaziya izindlela zokuziphilisa kuyithuluzi elisemqoka ohlelweni lwe-CBP ngoba kwakha ukuqonda izindlela abantu abehlukehlukene emphakathini ngokwenhlalo abaziphiliza ngazo , okuhlanganisa okuyingcebo yabo , izinselelo , abafisa ukuba nakho kanye namathuba abawatholayo .
