Izinselelo nabafisa ukuba nakho kuzoba yisisekelo sokuhlela . IHhovisi lentuthuko : Lokhu kwaba ngeminye yemiphumela ebalulekile yokuhlela iMasincedane Development Corporation . IMasincedane inikezela ngemisebenzi yentuthuko neyokweseka kumphakathi , okufaka phakathi ideski elincane lamabhizinisi , isikhungo sokweseka izingadi zomphakathi kanye nesikhungo sezoluleko esihlinzeka ngosizo lwezomthetho kanye nokweseka kwezenhlalakahle . Isimo sayo njengenkampani engaphansi kweSigaba sama-21 senze ukuba ikwazi ukubeka izizathu zokuba inikwe imali ngempumelelo , ukulawula izinsizakusebenza kanye nokuzama ukuthuthukisa izimo zendawo . Ukudlula lapho , ukuzinza kwayo enkabeni yedolobha kuyenze ukuba ikwazi ukuxhamana nezinkampani zentuthuko zangaphandle kanye nomphakathi wendawo . Ngebhadi , ukuncipha kokuxhaswa ngezimali kwayo kule minyaka esandakudlula kunomthelela ekusebenzeni kwayo . Akubhalwe amagama abakhona . Ukwenza inqubekela phambili ezwakalayo , esheshayo nesimeme ekunciphiseni ubuphofu nokungalingani esikhathini esiyiminyaka engamashumi amabili , iNingizimu Afrika kudingeka izilungisele ikusasa , iqale namhlanje . Lolu hlelo luveza indlela entsha yezentuthuko edinga ukubandakanya imiphakathi , intsha , abasebenzi , abangasebenzi nabamabhizinisi ababambisene nohulumeni okwazi ukwenza izinto . Injongo ukuthuthukisa ukukwazi ukusebenza kwabantu nokwezwe , ukudala amathuba abo bonke . Ngokuhlaziya , uhlelo lugcizelela isidingo sokwenza inqubekela phambili esheshayo ezintweni eziningana ukunciphisa ngempumelelo ubuphofu nokungalingani . Ukwenza izethulo - izethulo zingenziwa ngokusebenzisa ikhansela lesigceme noma zenziwe ngqo kumkhandlu mayelana nezidingo zomphakathi . Uma ukholelwa ukuthi ube nomthelela ekuqaleni kolaka , ungachazi , ungaxolisi noma uphendule kuze kufike isikhathi lapho umuntu eseqedile ukuveza ulaka lwakhe . Ngaphambi kokuba lokho kwenzeke , kungenzeka ungakwazi ukuba nengxoxo enomqondo . Ubambiswano - umphakathi kanye nomkhandlu kuyasebenzisana bese kubambisana ekunikezeni imibono maqondana nokuhlela kanye nokuthatha izinqumo . Ekugcineni umkhandlu yiwona onikeza umbono wokugcina . Hlonza umkhakha ongena ngaphansi kwawo umasipala wakho . Asungula izinkundla zokuxoxisana nomphakathi . Kubiza kangakanani ukubamba ukhetho lwesigceme ? Ukwenza amaphoyisa asebenze kahle . Indlela yokuziphatha kwamaphoyisa nendlela yokwenza kahle umsebenzi kumele kuhlotshaniswe nokukhushulwa nokuqondiswa kwezigwegwe emsebenzini . Ukuqasha kufanele kuhehe abantu abanamakhono , ochwepheshe abanamakhono ngokusebenzisa inqubo enemigudu emibili ; owodwa kube owabasezikhundleni eziphezulu nokunye kube ngowabasezikhundleni eziphansi . Izinhlelo ze-GEP zokungenelela kokwesekwa ngobuchwepheshe zizokusiza ukuba wakhe isithombe ngekusasa lebhizinisi lakho . Lokhu kubandakanya ukwenza ucwaningo oluhlelwe kahle lwalo wonke amaqiniso nemininingwane edingekayo , ukuqoqa amaphepha angokomthetho adingekayo nokuhlola izingozi ezihlobene nokuqhuba ibhizinisi lakho ngempumelelo . Banikeze imizuzu eyi-10 kuya kweyi-15 ababambiqhaza ukucubungula imibuzo . Ukukhetha okunzima kumele kwenziwe . Ukuthuthukisa ukwakhiwa kwemisebenzi eminingi nokusebenza kwezabasebenzi kumele kwenziwe ngcono . IKhomishani yenza izihlongozo okuhloswe ngazo ukusiza abantu abasebasha ukungena emisebenzini , ukwenza lula imithetho yamabhizinisi amancane , ukunciphisa ukukhathazeka nenxushunxushu , nokucacisa inqubo yokuxosha abantu emsebenzini kanye nezinqubo zokubhekana nokuziphatha kabi . Kudingeka kugxilwe kakhulu ekuqeqesheni okuqhubekayo kwabasebenzayo nokuhlinzeka ngamathuba okuthuthuka emisebenzini kwabo bonke abasebenzi . Uhulumeni wendawo kufanele wazise umphakathi ukuthi izimali zisetshenziswa kanjani . Bakwenze loku ngokuveza izincwadi ezicwaningiwe . Imicabango engelona iqiniso imicabango jikelele ngeqembu labantu noma umcimbi . Noma yisiphi isitatimende mayelana nomkhakha wabantu kunamathuba amaningi okuthi sibe ngumcabango ongeqiniso . Imicabango engeqiniso ihlale ingemihle futhi abantu abaningi bayakholelwa kweminye yale micabango engelona iqiniso . Amakhansela ngabantu abakhethwe abavoti futhi bamele laba bavoti emkhandlwini kamasipala . Bakhethwa njalo emva kweminyaka emihlanu ukuthi bahlale emkhandlwini kamasipala . Amakhaya nemiphakathi . Ukudla okunomsoco nokudla okufanele , ikakhulukazi ezinganeni ezingaphansi kweminyaka emithathu , kusemqoka ekukhuleni kahle ngokomzimba nangokomqondo . IKhomishani yenza izincomo ngokudla kwengane okunomsoco , ukusiza abazali nemindeni ukulwa nobuphofu , nokuhlinzeka ngokulungiselela okuhle ezinganeni ezincane - okubandakanya isihlongozo sokuthi ingane ngayinye kumele okungenani ithole imfundo yeminyaka emibili yangaphambi kokungena esikoleni . UMBUZO 3 Unaso yini isabelomali senyanga ? Abahlinzeki bemisebenzi basetshenziswa kumaphrojekthi athile , isib. ukwakhiwa kwemigwaqo , kanye nesidingo sokuxoxisana nabo bahlale bazi ngezidingo zomphakathi . Umsebenzi wabo kungukuhlinzeka lowo msebenzi abasayine inkontileka yokuwenza . Lo mhlangano wokulungiselela ukuhlela wethulwa njengengxoxo nabamele umphakathi , okuhlanganisa ikhansela , ikomidi lesigceme , abayizibonelo emphakathini , abaholi bendabuko kanye nabanye abathintekayo . Kulesi sigaba umlamuli uyayiphetha inqubo . Isingeniso - inhloso yalesi sinyathelo ukwakha ukwethembeka nesiqinisekiso phakathi kwezinhlangothi maqondana nenqubo . Kulesi sinyathelo zonke izinhlangothi ( kuhlanganisa nomlamuli ) ziyavumelana ngemigomo yenqubo . Isibonelo , izinhlangothi ziyavumelana ukuthi ngesikhathi olunye uhlangothi lubeka udaba lwalo , lukwenza lokhu ngaphandle kokuphazanyiswa . Umlamuli - umgqugquzeli ungumsizi futhi kungadingeka ukuba angenelele ukuqinisekisa ukuthi inqubo ifinyelelisa imiphumela edingakalayo . Umgqugquzeli ubuye abe ngumxazululi wengxabano . Isigaba -195 ( e ) - mayelana nokuyigugu okuyisisekelo nezimiso zokuphatha umphakathi zikahulumeni - Izidingo zabantu kufanele ziphendulwe futhi umphakathi kufanele ugqugquzelwe ukuba ubambe iqhaza ekwenziweni kwezinqubomgomo . Amalungu ekomidi lesigceme kanye nabagqugquzeli bohlelo lwe-CBP abaphothule amakhasi okuhlaziywa kwezindlela zokuziphilisa babamba izingxoxo zeqembu . Ukwenza isabelomali kwenza ngcono ukulethwa kwemisebenzi . Ukuhlela , ukwenza isabelomali nokuqapha kokulethwa kwemisebenzi okudidiyelwe kuqinisa ukuxhumana phakathi kwemisebenzi enikezelwa yiminyango kanye nezinsizakalo kanye nezindleko zale misebenzi . Ukulinganisa ukusebenza kuthuthukisa ukubeka izinto obala nokuzibophezela kwezokulawula kanye nokusetshenziswa kwezinsizakusebenza zomphakathi . Isigaba sesi-3 sigxile ekwenziweni kwangempela kohlelo . Ngokulandela izinyathelo ezifanele , umphakathi uthatha imininingwane ehlanganisiweyo kanye nokufiswayo okusemqoka ukuhlele kube wumbono , isitatimende sezinhloso , amasu , amaphrojekthi kanye nemisebenzi ngenhloso yokuphucula impilo yomphakathi . Sabalalisa izinhlelo zokuqashwa komphakathi zifinyelele kwababambe iqhaza abayisigidi esi-1 ngonyaka wezi-2015 banayizigidi ezi-2 ngonyaka wezi-2020 . Ngesikhathi likhula inani lemisebenzi yemikhakha esemthethweni nengekho emthethweni , izinhlelo zemisebenzi kahulumeni zingancishiswa . Umdwebo kaVenn uyithuluzi lokuhlaziya ukulethwa kwezidingo emphakathini . Umphakathi uhlonza izinhlangano , izidingo nabalethi bazo ubaklelise ngokubaluleka kwabo nokutholakala kwabo . Uphinde ube wusizo ekuqondeni izidingo zomphakathi . Ukuziphendulela : Ukukhombisa ukuthi izinsizakusebenza zisetshenziswa kahle nangokuhambisana nesihlongoso sephrojekthi nezivumelwano zokukhokha . Ikomiti Lewadi lakhiwe ngekhansela yewadi kanye nabantu abayishumi abangabavoti ewadini futhi abakhethwe umphakathi abawusebenzelayo . Amalungu ekomiti lewadi kufanele kube ngabantu abamele izinhlanga zomphakathi ezahlukene ( abesifazane , intsha , omphakathi obandlululiwe , njll ) . Ukuba amalungu amaqembu ezepolitiki athile akufanelanga ukuthi kube nomthelela ekukhethweni kwabo . Amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi kufanele babambe iqhaza ngokuthanda kwabo . Ukuhlaziya iphrojekthi - ukuqaphela nokubuyekeza ukusebenzisa izinkomba ezinqunyiwe ukusho ukuthi iphrojekthi iqhubeka kanjani , yiziphi izinselelo ezivelile nokuthi ukuyenza kungalungiswa kanjani . Indawo yokuhlala eyimijondolo iye yakhiwa eduzane nesiteshi samandla kagesi . Amalungu asemijondolo aba namakhanda abuhlungu kanye nokutheleleka kwesifuba njalo nje . Bayadikibala ukusuka ngoba baseduze nendawo abasebenza kuyo . Impendulo : Ikomidi Lesigceme lithatha udaba liluyisa enkantolo . Omele ushintsho - iKomidi Lesigceme limbandakanya umphakathi ekuthatheni isinqumo ngezinqubomigomo zikahulumeni wasekhaya nezinhlelo njengoba ukumbandakanywa komphakathi kubalulekile ekuvezeni izidingo zomphakathi kuzo zonke izigaba zenqubo yokuhlela . Hlukanisa ababambiqhaza ngamaqembu amancane bese unikeza iqembu ngalinye lo mbuzo ongezansi . Njengoba kunemibuzo emithathu kuphela , amanye amaqembu azonikezwa imibuzo efana nawamanye . Ezinye izinhlelo ezihlonzwe ohlelweni lwe-CBP kumele zenziwe izethulo engasondeza ohlelweni lwe-IDP ngoba ziqukethe ulwazi olusemqoka ngezidingo zomphakathi kanye nezixazululo ezakhayo ezigxile emphakathini , kodwa kungaba wumthwalo omkhulu ukuba zisetshenziswe ezingeni lesigceme . Leli qoqa lichaza indlela yokwenza izethulo zohlelo lwe-IDP . Ukuhlonzwa nokubekwa phambili kwezinhlelo namaphrojekthi athile kudingekile ukuphephisa imiphumela okuyohlomula kakhulu kuyo umphakathi . Yimaphi amaforamu omphakathi adinga ukumelwa kuwo iKomidi Lesigceme , njengawezinhlangano zomphakathi noma ezempilo ? Inkontileka yomsebenzi yisivumelwano phakathi kukamasipala nomhlinzeki womsebenzi ekuhlinzekeni ingxenye ethile yomsebenzi kamasipala kwesikhathi esifushane ( unyaka noma iminyaka emibili kuphela ) . Umasipala unikezela ngesabelomali bese uqapha ukusebenza komhlinzeki womsebenzi ukuze aqinisekise ukuthi umsebenzi ohlinzekwayo unezinganhle elihle futhi wenziwa ngaphakathi kwaleso sabelomali owabelwe sona . Ikomidi lesigungu esiphezulu eliphelele likhethwa ngumkhandlu nekomidi lemeya elikhethwe ngumphathidolobha omkhulu . Omabili amakomidi aholwa ngumphathidolobha . Lawa makomidi akhiwe amakhansela anezikhundla ezisemqoka . Bonke abanakekeli badinga ukuqeqeshelwa ukunakekela okuzinze emakhaya . Uma sebeqeqeshiwe bayonikwa inkokhelo kanye namaphasela okudla . Uhulumeni othuthukayo ubhekana nezimbangela zobuphofu nokungalingani . Uhulumeni othuthukayo waseNingizimu Afrika uyogxambukela ukusekela ahole intuthuko ukuze inzuzo yalokho ifinyelele kubo bonke abantu emphakathini ( ikakhulukazi abampofu ) , nokwakha ukuvumelana ukuze inzuzo kazwelonke yesikhathi eside ibe ngaphezulu kweyesikhathi esifushane , okuyinselelo eseyinkinga . Engxenyeni yokuqala yeSigaba sesi-4 se-CBP ababambe iqhaza ohlelweni lwe-CBP banikezwa imigomo esizayo ngeziphakamiso ezethulwa ohlelweni lwe-IDP kanye namakhasi okucatshangwayo ngohlelo kwezinhlelo ezidingwa ukwesekwa ngabangaphandle . Ukwakhiwa kwesabelomali semali esetshenziswa ngokwezidingo esigcemeni esizokwenza ukuba umphakathi uqhubekele phambili ngokushesha nohlelo lwawo nakho kuyabhungwa . Ingxenye yesibili yeSigaba sesi-4 igcizelela ukuthi uhlelo olunemininingwane lokwenza lubalulekile ukuze uhlelo lube yimpumelelo . Lwethula indlela amaphrojekthi okudingeka ahlahlelwe ngayo abe wuhlelo lokwenza olulandela izinyathelo ezichaza ukuthi lubhalwa kanjani uhlelo . lesi sigaba siphetha ngokwethula uhlelo oseluphothuliwe kumphathi wohlelo lwe-CBP ukuze kwamukelwe isabelo semali esisetshenziswa ngokwezidingo . Uma sekwamukelwe lokhu kumele kuhlelwe umhlangano wokubikela umphakathi nokuwutshela ngokusha okuvelile . Izinsizakusebenza zikamasipala zisetshenziselwa ukuhlanganisa izindawo ezisemakhaya kanye nezasedolobheni kanti futhi zisetshenziselwa ukulethela labo bantu abahluphekayo izidingo . Ababambiqhaza baxoxelana ngalokho abake bahlangabezana nakho mayelana nokulethwa kwemisebenzi okuhle noma okubi . Yithi umbambiqhaza oyedwa noma ababambiqhaza ababili baxoxe ngalokho abake bahlangabezana nakho bese ubabuza ukuthi yini okumele ukuba yenziwe ukuze lokho kwenziwe ngcono , uma lokho ababebhekene nakho kwakungekuhle . Sebenzisa amanothi ezifundo kwiSahluko 2 , 2.2 ukukusiza emva kokuzwa uvo lwamaqembu . Kunezinhlobo eziningi ezahlukene zokuphathwa kweprojekthi ezisetshenziswa esikhungweni sentuthuko . Lokhu kuvamise ukwehluka kuzinhlobo ezisetshenziswa emhlabeni wemisebenzi eyehlukene . Ziphinde zivame ukwehluka phakathi kwamazwe ngamazwe . Emkhakheni waseNingizimu Afrika alukho uhlobo lwesikhungo somphakathi olubekwe ngokusemthethweni kanti kuzokuba khona umehluko ngisho phakathi kwezinhlobo ezisetshenziswa iminyango kahulumeni eyehlukene . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kumele akujwayele ukuphathwa komjikelezo weprojekthi njengoba lolu kuwuhlobo oluvamise ukusetshenziswa . Ukwehlukaniswa kanye namagama ezinyathelo noma izigaba zomjikelezo weprojekthi kungahluka kwencike esikhungweni esixhasa ngezimali noma umnyango kahulumeni . Izakhamizi zineqhaza elisemqoka ekwenzeni izinqumo ezithinta izimpilo zazo kanye nasekuqinisekiseni ukuthi abaholi bazo abakhethiwe bazinikela ngemfanelo baphinde benze nomsebenzi wabo . Lokhu kuhamba kwedlulele ngale kokuvota okhethweni . Ukubamba iqhaza ngemfanelo kwezakhamizi kusho ukuthi abantu babamba iqhaza elisemqoka okhethweni . Kuyo yonke imikhakha kahulumeni izakhamizi zikahulumeni kumele ziqinisekise ukuthi zifaka imibono ethile ezingxoxweni eziphathelene nokwakhiwa kwemithetho emisha ngokuya emihlanganweni yomphakathi yokuxoxa ngokudingekayo noma ukwenza izethulo . UMBUZO 1 Yini iqhaza lakho njengelungu Lekomidi Lesigceme kunqubo yesabelomali ? Thatha izimpendulo . Emhlanganweni ovulelekile , namathisela amathebhula awo wonke amaqembu odongeni bese nikhipha amaphuzu afanayo ethebhuleni nisebenzise imibuzo yengxoxo Emsebenzini wesi-4 . Uhlelo kumele luhlanganise imininingwane ngomphakathi , imicimbi emphakathini kanye namathuluzi nezindlela ezingasetshenziswa ukukhiqiza imininingwane edingekayo . Ekhasini elilandelayo kunesibonelo sohlelo nendlela okumele lubhalwe ngayo . Lokhu kwenzelwe ukunikeza isithombe sokufanele kuqukathwe wuhlelo lwesigceme . INingizimu Afrika inamasheya amaningi emhlabeni jikelele emikhiqizweni yeplatinamu , igolide , idayimane , imanganisi , amalahle , insimbi kanye neyureniyamu . Nokho eshumini leminyaka edlule izimayini zakuleli aziphumelelanga ukuhambisana nesimo sokukhula komnotho womhlaba ekuthuthelweni ngaphandle kokumbiwa phansi ngenxa yengqalasizinda engekho esimeni esihle , obekuhambisana nokulawulwa nohlaka lwenqubomgomo okuphazamisa ukutshalwa kwezimali . INingizimu Afrika ingazuza kakhulu ekukhuleni ngamandla kwezidingo zempahla ezidingwa yi-Asia . Ukwenza njalo kusho ukuthuthukiswa kwengqalasizinda yezamanzi , ezokuthutha , nezamandla , nokuhlinzeka ngenqubomgomo engcono nenesiqinisekiso ngokulawula kubatshala izimali . Lokhu kuyosiza umkhakha wezokumbiwa phansi ukuthi usabalalise amakhono , izisetshenziswa , ukwazi indlela yokwenza nemali ekhona , nokuvumela uhulumeni ukuthi akhuphule intela , okwedlula njengoba enza manje . Ukuguqula indlela yokuhlela ukusombulula imisebenzi ehlukene ekuhleleni kukahulumeni kazwelonke , ukulawula ngokungeyikho kwezinhlelo zangaphakathi kuhulumeni , ukuhlukanisa imingcele phakathi komasipala nokungasebenzi kahle kwezinhlelo ezihlangene zezentuthuko . Umphakathi jekelele ukhuthaza intuthuko nokubumbana komphakathi . Emiphakathini eminingi empofu izinhlangano ezingekho ngaphansi kukahulumeni zezenhlalakahle nezinye izinhlangano ezizinze emphakathini ziletha izinhlelo zomphakathi ezisemqoka nokutholakala kwemisebenzi . Qala ukusebenzisa uhlelo lokudla okunomsoco kwabesifazane abakhulelwe nezingane ezincane nokusabalalisa imisebenzi yokuthuthukisa izingane ezisencane ezineminyaka engaphansi kwemihlanu . Yiziphi izinhlangano zemiphakathi noma iminyango kamasipala esifisa ukuzimema ukwenza isethulo ekomidini lesigceme noma emhlanganweni wabamele izinhlangano / izindawo ? Izinsuku umasipala azobamba imihlangano yokubonisana ngazo , ongafisa ukubamba iqhaza kuyo , njengohlelo lwe-IDP kanye nesabelomali sonyaka . Ukulethwa kwemisebenzi yezingqalazizinda okusimeme ngempumelelo kuncike ekuqondisiseni kahle igalelo nemisebenzi yalabo okubanjiswene nabo ekunikezelweni kwezingqalazizinda . Umsebenzi wokulawulwa kokusebenza kusemahlombe kamenenja kamasipala . INingizimu Afrika idinga umnotho ongowabo bonke abantu , oguqukayo oveza izithelo zokukhula ezitholwa yibo bonke abantu ngokulinganayo . Ngonyaka wezi-2030 , umnotho kumele kube ngosusondele emathubeni emisebenzi aphelele , ukuhlomisa abantu ngamakhono abawadingayo , ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ubunikazi bemikhiqizo buhlukene futhi bukhula ngokushesha , futhi uhlinzeka ngezisetshenziswa ukukhokhela ukufakwa kwemali kubantu nasempahleni . Izinsiza : Ikhophi Yohlelo Lwezentuthuko Edidiyelwe , incwadi esihloko sithi Community-Based Planning and the IDP Guide 2 ( yabe-AICDD and Development Works ) , i-PowerPoint ( ngokuzikhethela ) . Iqhaza lezinhlelo zokuqashwa komphakathi , okufana nokwandiswa kohlelo lwemisebenzi yomphakathi , kumele libhekwe kabanzi . Ngisho noma ngabe iNingizimu Afrika ithola ukukhula kwe-GDP okungaphezu kwamaphesenti ama-5 ngonyaka , namathuba emisebenzi ekhula ngokushesha eshumini leminyaka elizayo , siyobe silokhu sikhona isidingo salezo zinhlelo . Nisebenza ngababili , yenza iphosta efingqa imibhalo yenqubomgomo ehlukile kanye nokhishwa komthetho wokwakha uhlaka lokuthuthukisa uhulumeni wendawo . Ababambiqhaza baxoxa ngamafuphi lemininingwane kumawadi abo futhi bachaze ukuthi izinqubomgomo kanye nomthetho okhishiwe uzisa kanjani inhlalo yabantu . Umsuka wanoma iluphi uhlobo lwengxabano ukuveza ukuthi yini ingxabano . Ingxabano ayihlale njalo ingalungile . Empeleni ingxabano ingasiza ukuletha inguquko noma ushintsho . Igama elithi ingxabano livela olimini lwesiLathini ' conflictus ' okuchaza ' ukukhuhlanisa ' . Isibonelo , uma ukhuhlanisa umentshini uyakwazi ukuveza umlilo okufanele upheke ngawo noma ukufudumeze . Indlela esibhekana ngayo nengxabano yiyo ezochaza ukuthi ingxabano iyaqhubeka , iba yimbi kakhulu kunakuqala , izokwehla , okusho ukuthi inciphisa ingxabano . Izingxabano eziningi ngeke zixazululeke , kodwa ukuhlangabezana nezidingo zabantu abaxabene kungasiza ekulungiseni isimo . IKomidi Lesigceme lingabumba ikomijana elilodwa noma ngaphezulu futhi libandakanye umphakathi kula makomijana . Bonke okubanjiswene nabo ekomidini bayakhuthazwa ukuthi babambe iqhaza kumakomijana asondelene nemikhakha abayithandayo . Uma ufuna ukuxazulula inkinga edale ulaka lwakho , bhekana nolaka lwakho noma inkinga ecaleni . Gwema ukwenza izinqumo ezibalulekile ngesikhathi usabuswa ulaka . Umphakathi ohlala emijondolo eduze nedolobha ususiwe wayiswa endaweni okwakhiwe kuyo izindlu enga-20km ukusuka edolobheni . Esinye isizathu esizwakala emijondolo sokususwa ukuthi abanye babahlali basemijondolo banikezwe amakhaya abebewaqashisa . Abahlali abaningi bacasukile njengoba bebelokhu besohlwini lwabalinde izindlu isikhathi eside futhi bathi akukuhle labo bahlali ababelwe izindlu ukuba baziqashise ngoba lokhu kuvimbela abanye abahlali ukuthola izindlu . Ngaso leso sikhathi bathi abafuni ukusuka ngoba kukude nasedolobheni futhi abaningi babo basebenza edolobheni abanayo imali yezithuthi . Abahlali bathi ngeke basuke . Enkulumweni namaphepha usihlalo wekomidi labahlali uthe ukube bebethintiwe ngaphambi kokuthi lezi zinhlelo zenziwe bebezokwazi ukuchaza ukuthi kungani bengasukanga nokuthi isizathu sabanye babahlali , ababelwe izindlu , ukuthi baqashise ngezindlu zabo ukuthi kuyabiza kubo ukuya emsebenzini zonke izinsuku . IKhomishani igunyaza uhlelo lwamaphuzu ayisikhombisa oluvezwe yinqubo yezokusebenza komthetho , okuxoxwa ngayo kabanzi esahlukweni se-12 . Lolu hlelo lusekela inhloso kahulumeni yokugudlula kancane izisetshenziswa zikahulumeni zibe ukutshalwa kwezimali okuzoguqula isimo somnotho , kwandise amathuba kukhuluse nokukwazi ukusebenza . Ngenxa yalokho , ezinye izingxenye zesabelomali sikazwelonke kuyodingeka zikhule kancanyana . Ukugqugquzela ukubamba iqhaza kuzombandakanya abahlanganyeli abahlukile ezikhathini ezehlukile abafana namavolontiya , izinhlangano zomphakathi , izinhlangano zokuhlanganyela , amalungu omphakathi , abasebenzi bakahulumeni kanye nabantu bezepolotiki . Ulaka imizwa yomuntu yemvelo evela uma abantu bezizwa besatshiswa noma behlaselwa . Amalungu amaKomidi Ezigceme angazithola esesimweni sokubhekena neqembu labantu noma umuntu ocasukile , ikakhulukazi njengoba amaKomidi Ezugceme esebenza njengemigudu yokuxhumana phakathi kukamasipala , ikhansela lewadi nomphakathi . Abahlali bangaba nolaka futhi bacasuke mayelana nezindaba njengokungahlinzekwa ngezinsizakalo noma ngezinsizakalo ezingekho sezingeni elihle noma ukulinda emigqeni ukufaka amaklemu noma ukuthola amadokhumende . Ukuxhumana okuphumelelayo kufaka phakathi ukwazi ukubhekana nolaka nokwesatshiswa . Njengoba lokhu kuyisiphetho sale mojuli , funda amaphuzu asemqoka kulesi sahluko bese ufingqa ngokuthi ubheke imininingwane evela kuzo zonke izahluko ukuze ababambe iqhaza baqonde ngokugcwele inqubo ephelele . Bheka amanothi esifundo ukuze akusize . Ukweluleka - ukweluleka nokusiza ikhansela ukuze lazi ngezindaba zomphakathi ebese likwazi ukuzidlulisela kumkhandlu . Ukuqasha ngokulingana nezinye izindlela ezilungisiwe kumele zenziwe ziphumelele ngokugxila endaweni lapho kuthuthukiswa khona ukukwazi ukusebenza . Ukulingana kumayelana nemiphumela elinganayo . Kuqondise ikakhulukazi ebulungisweni naseqinisweni , futhi kungadinga ukuthi kubhekanwe nakho ngendlela ehlukile , noma izinyathelo ezikhethekile , zabanye abantu noma amaqembu . Ukulingana kuvuma izimo ezithile noma izinkomba zomuntu ngamunye , iqembu , ubulili ngokwesimo somzimba , ubulili , izinga , inkolo noma iminyaka . Kudinga ukuthi kuqedwe izithiyo zamthuba ezomnotho kanye nezombusazwe kanye nokufinyelela kwezemfundo kanye nezidingonqangi , njengabesilisa kanye nabesifazane bayo yonke iminyaka . Ukulingana ngobobulili kusho ukuphathwa ngendlela ngendlela kwabesifazane nabesilisa , ngokwezidingo zabo ngokwehluka kwabo . Lokhu kungabandakanya ukulinganiswa kokuphathwa okuhlikile kodwa okuthathwa njengokulinganayo ngokwamalungelo , imihlomulo , izibophezelo kanye namathuba . Acabangela phambili aphinde ahlonze imisebenzi azothanda ukuba ithunyelwe emiphakathini yawo eminyakeni embalwa . Ama-IDP kamasipala ahlonza amaphrojekthi aneminqamulajuqu ecacile kanye nezinkomba zenqubekelaphambili . Umsebenzi obalulekile wamakhansela ukuqapha ukusebenza kukamasipala ngokuhambisana nalezi zivumelwano ezibalulekile . Amalungu Ekomidi Lesigceme kumele aqinisekise ukuthi azijwayele izinkomba zokusebenza okusemqoka kanye nokuphokophokoplelwe kukho ngokusebenza okubekwe ku-IDP kamasipala wawo ukuze akwazi ukuhlola inqubekelaphambili . Uma isigceme siyindawo enkulu hlela imihlangano sibe sezindaweni ezingaphezu kweyodwa ukuze bonke bazi ukuthi kwenzekani . AMALUNGU EKOMIDI LESIGCEME ASEBENZA NGOKUBAMBISANA nekhansela kanye nomphakathi . IKomidi Lesigceme lingakhetha ukwabela izikhundla amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme . Lokhu kwenza kube lula ukusebenza nomasipala kanjalo nokumela imiphakathi ezindabeni eziyithintayo . Umsebenzi weKomidi Lesigceme uphinde ufake phakathi ukwenza nokukhulisa imizamo yomphakathi yokufeza imigomo kumaphrojekthi abafuna ukuwenza bona ngokwabo . Amaqembu emisebenzi noma amakomidi ayahlangana emphakathini ukufeza amaphrojekthi athile ayohlomula olwazini oluyisisekelo lokuphathwa kwephrojekthi . Amakomiti amawadi akhiwa ngemvume yekhanseli . Imisebenzi yamakomiti amawadi yeyeme ekudluseni okungenamfihlo izinqumo zekhanseli . Lokhu ukuxazulula inkinga ngokubambisana okuhlelekile futhi kokuzikhethela lapho izinhlangothi zihlangana , ngosizo noma ngaphandle kosizo , ukufuna isixazululo esihle nesamukelekile kuzo zonke izinhlangothi ezithintekayo nokufinyelela ezivumelwaneni noma kuxazululwe ukwehlukana kwangempela noma okucatshangwayo . Ukulandelela nokunikeza izimpendulo zemibuzo : Ukuphoqelela ukunikezwa kwemibiko yamaphrojekthi kamasipala nezinsizakalo njalo Kwikomiti Lewadi kanye nasemihlanganweni yomphakathi emawadini abo ukuze abahlali bagcine benolwazi ngenqubekela phambili kanye / noma izinkinga . Iziphakamiso ezakhayo zokwenza ngcono kumele zenziwe , futhi , lapho kuphumeleleka khona , umphakathi kungenzeka ubhaliswe ekuxazululeni inkinga . AmaKomidi Ezigceme kufanele abe nendima ebalulekile ekulawulweni kokusebenza njengoba i-PMS iyithuluzi elibalulekile lokubheka inqubekela phambili yokusebenza kukamasipala ngokuhambisana nemiklamo yokusebenza nezinkomba zokusebenza okusemqoka ozibekele zona . Lokhu kufuna ukusebenzisana okuhle nekhansela lesigceme okufuneka ukuba lixhumane namaKomidi Ezigceme kuzo zonke izigaba zokulawulwa kokusebenza . Yonke iminyango kahulumeni , kuzwelonke nasezifundazweni , kudingeka yenze ukwethulwa kwezinsizakalo kube yinto ephambili , njengoba kudingwa Ngumthetho Ohlongozwayo Wokuguqula Izinsizakalo Zomphakathi , ka-1995 . Incwadi ye- Batho Pele ifuna ukunikeza abaphathi abasebenzayo ulwazi olubavumela ukuthi bakwazi ukusebenzisa izinqubo zokwethula izinsizakalo ezisemqoka nezicacile . Uhulumeni weyeme esigabeni sikahulumeni ukwethula izinsizakalo ezidingekayo ngemfanelo nangokwethembeka . lesi ngesisodwa sezizathu zokuthi i-Batho Pele ihlale ikhona kuHulumeni , yeseka zonke izinqubo ' ukusuka Ohlelweni oluyisu , wonke amazinga Ohlelo Lokuthuthukisa Oluhlanganisiwe , Ukuphatha Ukusebenza Ngemfanelo kanye Nokuphatha Ukubonelelwa futhi kumele ibe wubufakazi obugcwele ngaso sonke isikhathi lapho umsebenzi kaHulumeni enqwamana nesakhamizi ' . Imibono akufanele ibe ngejwalekile nje , kumele ihlaziywe ngosebenzisa izinyathelo zokwenziwayo . Uma okwenziwayo kuyinto ejwayelekile nje , akukho okuzokwenzeka . lesi yisigaba sokugcina ekwenzeni uhlelo lwesigceme futhi kumele sinake isabelomali esetshenziswa ngokwezidingo edingekayo ukuqhuba uhlelo , esivela eziphathimandleni zendawo nezinhlelo okumele zethulwe ukuze zihlolwe ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Mhlawumbe uphawu olusemqoka kakhulu okumele lwaziwe mayelana nezigaba zokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ukuthi azilandeli indlela eqondile ( umugqa oqondile ) lapho isigaba esisodwa silandela esinye ngaphandle kokuphindwa kwezigaba ezenzeke ekuqaleni . Izigaba ezehlukene eziningi ziyaphindeka njengoba kusuke kuqhubeka umjikelezo wephrojekthi . Isibonelo , isigaba ngasinye kudingeka siphethwe ngaphambi kokuthi kuqale esilandelayo . Amandla esakhamuzi - abantu bayazibophezela maqondana nezenzo zabo futhi bancikanga komunye umuntu ukubenzela zona . Isibonelo umgodi endleleni uvulekile futhi uyingozi . Umphakathi uthatha isinqumo sokuhlangana bese ukhetha ikomiti elizoqondana ngqo nalolu daba emkhandlwini wedolobha . Okwamanje babeka uphawu oluxwayisa abahlali ukuthi baqaphele . Balandelela lolu daba kuze kube yilapho umkhandlu ubhekana nalo . Khuluma ngokucacile ukuze wonke umuntu ezokuzwa . Sebenzisa ulimi wonke umuntu azoluzwa kahle ngale kwalokho abantu ngeke bakhombise umdlandla kokushoyo . IKhomishana Yamalungelo Amasiko , Enkolo Nawolimi igqugquzela ukuhlonishwa kwalawa malungelo ibuye igqugquzele futhi ithuthukise ukuthula , ubungani , ubuntu , ukubekezelelana nokubumbana kwezwe . Ngokusebenzisa umdwebo osekhasini lama-35 wamanothi esifundo ( sebenzisa i-PowerPoint uma ikhona , noma usebenzise amanothi esifundo bese udweba umdwebo kwifliphushadi kuleso naleso sigaba ngesikhathi ) , chaza ukuthi umjikelezo we-CBP kumele kuxhumane nohlelo lwe-IDP . Qhakambisa ukuthi isizathu wukuthi i-CBP izama ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izidingo zomphakathi ziyakhonjwa zifakwe ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Uhlelo lwe-CBP nolwe-IDP yizinhlelo zezinto ezenziwayo ezilandelanayo futhi kumele zihlelwe ngokuqondaniswa . Lona wumsebenzi wokuzejwayeza owenziwa ngokuhamba ngezinyawo endaweni . Abagqugquzeli bahola lolu hambo kanye nabantu abayisithupha abanolwazi abavela emphakathini . Kumele kudonse isikhathi esingangehora kuya kwamabili ngoba abantu ngeke baba nesikhathi sokuthatha uhambo olude . Imininingwane mayelana nemihlangano yomkhandlu - Kungabe ngiyidlulisile imininingwane mayelana nomhlangano olandelayo womkhandlu , usuku , isikhathi nendawo nodaba okuzokhulunywa ngalo ? Kungabe ngiwadlulisele kwabanye amaminithi omhlangano womkhandlu ? UKWENZIWA KOHLELO LWEZENTUTHUKO OLUDIDIYELWE ( IDP ) ngomasipala kuyisidingo Somthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala Wohulumeni Bendawo , ka-2000 . Isahluko se-MSA , ka-2000 simemezela ukuthi'umasipala ngamunye . . . asebenzise uhlelo lwezamasu olulodwa , noludidiyelayo ngenhloso yokuthuthukiswa kukamasipala ' ( isigaba 25(1) ) . Lolu hlelo lubekelwe iminyaka emihlanu kanti luwuhlaka olubanzi lokuthuthukiswa kwaleyo ndawo . Lubuyekezwa minyaka yonke . I-IDP ihlahla indlela yohlelo lokwenza lukamasipala futhi kumele ( kungumthetho ) yenziwe ngokuxoxisana nomphakathi wendawo . Ukungalingani ngokobulili ngokujwayelekile kuvamise ukuba nomthelela ongemuhle kakhulu kwabesifazane kunabesilisa . Lokhu kuqinisekisa ukubheka ngokuphambili lokho kungalingani okuncisha abesifazane amathuba . Yonke iminyango yesifundazwe nekazwelonke kudingeka icacise iphinde ibeke amathagethi okufinyeleleka kwizinsizakalo zayo okuqhubekayo nokwenyukayo kulabo abangazange bazithole esikhathini esedlule . Aqinisekisa ukuthi amalungu Ekomidi Lezigceme ayabandakanyeka ezinkundleni zokuxoxisana . Ukusekela amabhizinisi amancane ngokulawulwa okungcono kwezinhlangano eziqondene , izikhungo zokuthuthukisa ezezimali , nezinhlelo zomphakathi nezizimele zokuxhasa amabhizinisi . I-Batho Pele icabangela ukwethulwa kwezinsizakalo kwezinsizakalo okuhlanganisa ukumenyezelwa kwezidingo zamakhasimende ngokugcwele bese kuhlanganisa ' iphakheji ephelele yonke ' yezimpendulo kanye nezixazululo . ISABELOMALI WUHLELO LWEZEZIMALI . Sibeka imisebenzi yonyaka wezezimali olandelayo ngendlela yokwethula izindleko zale misebenzi kanye nokuthi imali izovela kuphi yokukhokhela lezi zindleko . Nokwakha isiko lokuzibophezela , ukuvuleka kanye nokubeka obala endleleni yokuhanjiswa kwezomphakathi noma ekusebenziseni amandla omphakathi noma ukwenza umsebenzi womphakathi , ngokunikeza ukusebenza kwelungelo lokwenza okufanele endleleni yokuhambisa . I-Batho Pele yenzelwe ukwakha isimo sezinsizakalo zomphakathi ukuqinisekisa ukuthi okuyigugu kwe-Batho Pele kuyathathwa kudluliselwe kwizakhamuzi zezwe . Kuthatha isikhathi esingakanani ukuthi amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme asebenze kahle ezikhundleni zawo ? Izingxoxo nabalethi bezidingo abasemqoka - lokhu kufanele kwenziwe kusenesikhathi ukuqinisekisa ukuthi abantu abaningi bayalibamba iqhaza . Ukuxhumana uhlelo lapho abantu beshintshana khona ngemibono kanye nezimvo . Ukuxhumana ngempumelelo kudinga ukuba abantu bahlele kahle imicabango yabo , bethule ngokucacile lokho abakushoyo futhi balalele ngendlela enokucophelela . Ukuxhumana okungenayo impumelelo kungaholela engxabanweni . I-ajenda yomkhandlu kuxoxwa ngayo kumakhokhasi amaqembu ukumela amaqembu ehlukahlukene epolitiki ezindabeni ezikwi-ajenda ngaphambi komhlangano womkhandlu . UMthetho Wezinhlelo Zikamasipala , wezi-2000 , ubeka izinhlelo zangaphakathi zomasipala ezenza kube lula ukuba basebenzele ukufukula imiphakathi yezindawo ngokwezenhlalakahle nezomnotho ngendlela eqhubekela phambili , kanye nokuqikelela ukuthi izidingongqangi zitholakala ngemali enokukhokhwa ngabantu bonke . Ukuthola isifundo : Umbiko osemthethweni wokwenziwayo ngesikhathi somjikelezo wephrojekthi uyohlinzeka isisekelo sokunye ukubuyekezwa , kanjalo nezifundo zokuthathwa kwamaphrojekthi esikhathi esizayo . Izindlela zezinhlelo zephrojekthi kungadingeka ziguquke futhi kusemqoka ukuthi kube nenqolobane yemininingwane okuyobhekwa kuyo esikhathini esizayo . lesi sahluko sethula uhlaka lapho uhlelo oluzinze emphakathini lungasetshenziswa khona . Ababambe iqhaza bazonaka izinhloso , okulandela ukwamukela uhlelo lwe-CBP , imigomo nencazelo yenqubomgomo yalolu hlelo . lesi sahluko sinikeza ababambe iqhaza isisekelo sokusungula uhlelo lwe-CBP . Kuveza , kuqinisa futhi kufaka ukuziphatha okwenzekayo kokucabanga izinto ezingelona iqiniso ngabanye kanye nokucwasa iqembu elithile . Nicabanga ukuthi yini eyenziwe yiqembu lakho esebenze kahle ? Sekuphele izinyanga eziyisihlanu iKomidi Lesigceme lagcina ukuba nomhlangano . Ikhansela lithi libhizi futhi amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme azizwa eshiywe ngaphandle . Uqhekeko luyakheka phakathi kwamalungu eKomidi Lesigceme nekhansela . Amalungu omphakathi nawo ezwa sengathi ikhansela aliwathathi njengabalulekile njengoba lingakwazi ukuxhumana nawo noma liphendule izikhalazo zawo . Umphakathi uhlela umbhikisho oya eMkhandlwini ukuyokhalaza . Isisekelo sokusabalalisa amakhono ngemfundo engcono nokuqeqeshelwa ukusebenzisa izandla . Abagqugquzeli bakamasipala - bangaqhamuka emikhakheni ehlukene kamasipala noma ezikhulwini zikahulumeni ezingochwepheshe , eminyangweni yesifundazwe noma eyezifunda . Umsebenzi 4 Bheka uMthethosisekelo , bese uhlonza inhloso yokubusa ngokubambisana kanye nobudlelwano phakathi kohulumeni . Ukuhlanganyela nesiteshi somsakazo somphakathi wendawo kuzosiza Amakomiti Ewadi ukunikeza umphakathi ulwazi bese uthola nezimpendulo zawo . lesi sinyathelo senza isithombe somphakathi , ukuthi umphakathi uwubani , okusho amaqembu omphakathi , imithombo kanye nezinhlobo zezindlela zokuziphilisa zomphakathi , imisebenzi esemqoka yomphakathi kanye nabalethi bezidingo . lesi sigaba ohlelweni lwesigceme sehlukaniswe amagumbi amathathu . Okokuqala , wumlando womphakathi nezimo ezisemqoka ; okwesibili , ungubani umphakathi ( amaqembu ngokwenhlalo ) nokuthi uziphilisa ngani ; kanti okwesithathu yimisebenzi nezidingo . Kungani ucabanga ukuthi izabelomali zikamasipala kumele zitholakale emiphakathini ? Kunezindlela eziningi lapho isimo sengxabano singanqotshwa khona . Kulesi sahluko sibheka indlela ejwayele ukusetshenziswa , indlela yokuxazulula inkinga . Ababambe iqhaza kwiphrojekthi abehlukene kumele bahlonzwe kuhlolwe namandla abo . Lokhu kusho ukuthi ithimba lephrojekthi liyoba nomqondo wokuthi ababambe iqhaza abehlukene bethemba ukuthi yini ezophunyeleliswa yiphrojekthi , futhi yini edingwa ngobambe iqhaza ngamunye mayelana nokwenza umbiko , nokuthi yiluphi usizo noma izinsizakusebenza abanganikela ngazo kwiphrojekthi . I-Batho Pele akuyona inqubo emi yodwa nehlukile , iyisimiso futhi kufanele ibe yisimiso esihlahlayo kukho konke ukwethulwa kwezinsizakalo . Yingakho kungaba yinoma yimuphi umsebenzi , okungaba ukuphinde kwenziwe ubunjiniyela obuyingxenye yehhovisi eliphambili noma ihhovisi elisemuva noma ukuxhumana kwangaphakathi noma kwangaphandle , kumele kube nolwazi ngezimiso kanye nomoya we-Batho Pele . Amaphrojekthi angenzeka , okusho ukuthi izinjongo zingafezeka ngendlela engenzeka ngokuhambisana nesimo sendawo yokusebenza kanye nokwazi ukuzisebenzisa kwezinhlangano ezizokwenza lokhu . Ukubamba iqhaza kumakomidi nakumaforamu - imikhandlu ingenza amakomidi okweluleka namanye amakomidi namaforamu , njengeforamu yentuthuko edidiyele . AmaKomidi Ezigceme angasebenzisa lezi zakhiwo ukufaka uvo ezinqumweni ezithinta umphakathi . Imiphakathi yasemakhaya aseNingizimu Afrika kumele ibe namathuba amaningi okubamba iqhaza ngokugcwele empilweni yezomnotho , ezenhlalakahle nezombusazwe zezwe , asekelwe yizinga eliphezulu lezemfundo , ukunakekelwa ngokwezempilo , ezokuthutha neminye imisebenzi esemqoka . Ukuguqulwa ngempumelelo kwezwe , ukudalwa kwamathuba emisebenzi nokukhula kwemikhiqizo yezolimo kuyoba nomthelela ekuthuthukeni komnotho wasemakhaya wabo bonke abantu . Ukubheka : Imiphakathi ingacela umasipala ukuthi ukhethe ikomiti labamele bomphakathi ukuhlola izinqubo kanye nokweluleka umasipala ngokusemqoka ngokwengeza insizakalo nokwenza ngcono . Amalungu Ekomiti Lewadi nawo angasebenza njengamalungu ekomiti . Ukukhulisa okuya ngaphandle , kugxilwe kulezo zindawo lapho iNingizimu Afrika isivele isineminikelo nobuhle bokuqhathanisa okufana nezimayini , ezokwakha izimboni zamakhono alingene , ezolimo , ukukhiqizwa kwezolimo , ezemfundo ephakeme , ezokuvakasha nemisebenzi yamabhizinisi . Izinkomba ngokuhlosiwe okuvumela ukuqaphela , ukubuyekeza nokuhlaziya ukuthi ngabe iphrojekthi iyazifeza yini izinhloso zayo . Yizinkomba eziyokhombisa ukuthi ukuhlela kudingeka kulungiswe kanye nokuqinisekisa ukuthi ziyatholakala izifundo zokusebenza iphrojekthi esikhathini esizayo . Ukwehluka : Indlela yokubamba iqhaza komphakathi okungeniswa ngayo esikhungweni kanye nokwakhiwa kwakho kumele kunikeze ithuba elanele lokwehluka kwabantu , okusho ukuthi izindlela zokubamba iqhaza ezehlukile kanye nesiko . Ngenkathi kufanele kube khona uhlaka lokuhambisa olujwayelekile lokubamba iqhaza okungeniswe esikhungweni ezweni , lolu hlaka kumele libe banzi kakhulu ukuze kukwazi ukwenziwa izinguquko ezicacile zendawo ezizokwenziwa yizifundazwe nomasipala . Ithuluzi lelogifreyimu lihlinzeka ngamaphuzu ephrojekthi asemqoka afingqiwe ngendlela egunyaziwe . Ngakho-ke lisiza labo abasebenza ukuhlola ububanzi nokulandeleka ukuthi balandele kusukela kokunye noma ukonga okuhlongoziwe . Chaza kwabasemgqeni A abasendlini ukuthi bazolalela kophathina babo uma sebebuyele endlini . Uma bebuya kuzofuneke bakhombise ukungakwemukeli abakushoyo . Bangenza lokhu ngokuzishikashika ezihlalweni zabo , babange umsindo , babonakale bedikibele , baqhwabe iminwe , baphefumule kakhulu njll . Izinkomba neZindlela Zokuqinisekisa kuhlinzeka ngohlaka oluthe xaxa loHlelo Lokuqaphela Nokuhlaziya olungenziwa luphinde lusetshenziswe ngabaphathi bephrojekthi . Izinganhle : Kumele ukuba bahambisane namazinga kazwelonke emfundo nesipiliyoni . Ukubamba iqhaza kwabahlanganyeli kuyinselelo kumasipala , amakhansela ewadi kanye namakomiti Ewadi . Iphakethe Lamagayidi e-IDP liqhakambisa izimiso zokubamba iqhaza . Lezi zimiso zingasiza Amakomiti Ewadi ekwesekeni umasipala ukuze aphakamise indlela efanele bese eyifaka emaqenjini afanele ukuqinisekisa ukubamba iqhaza ngempumelelo . UMA SEKWENZEKILE UKUHLONZWA KOKUQALA KWEPHROJEKTHI , isigaba esilandelayo ukuhlela , ngokwemininingwane egcwele ukuthi iphrojekthi kumele isetshenzwe kanjani . Lolu hlelo kwesinye isikhathi lubizwa ngokuthi uhlaka Lokuphathwa Komjikelezo Wephrojekthi . Lwenza uhlelo lomsebenzi , olwaqala esahlukweni sesi-2 , isigaba soku-1 , kwidokhumenti esebenzayo echaza ngokugcwele ukuthi yini ngempela okumele yenziwe , yenziwe ubani , nokuthi yisiphi isikhathi esinqunyiwe kanye nesabelomali . Ithuluzi elisetshenziswa ukusiza ukucatshangwa nokwenziwa kohlaka libizwa ngokuthi yiThuluzi Lohlaka Olulandelekayo , futhi lwaziwa ngokufingqiwe ngokuthi yilogifreyimu . Ngokusebenzisa la mazwi asemqoka , ababambe iqhaza bangakha isitatimende sombono . Funda isibonelo sesitatimende sombono lapha ngezansi . Chaza ukuthi ukulandelana kwamazwi ombono kumele kuveze ukulandelana kokubaluleka kwezinto ezimele intuthuko esigcemeni . Uhlelo Oludidiyelwe Lwezisetshenziswa luletha ukushona phansi okuyimpumelelo kwamanani ekhabhoni . Izinguquko kwezezimali ezihambisanayo ziyadingeka ukusabalalisa intengo yekhabhoni ukukhuthaza ukusabalala okuhle komnotho notshalomali ebuchwephesheni obusathuthuka . Yazi umsuka wolaka lwakho . Zama ukubheka ezinye izimo obhekene nazo , njengokwesaba noma ukukhathazeka . Ukufeza isifiso sikahulumeni okwazi ukusebenza nothuthukayo , izwe kudingeka likhulise iqhaza lokubheka lePhalamende , ukusimamisa umngcele wezombusazwe nokuphatha , ukwenza imisebenzi yomphakathi isebenze ngendlela eyiyo , ukuthuthukisa amakhono nokwenza ngcono ukusebenzisana . Kuphinde kudinge indlela ekholekayo nesebenzayo ukuphatha inqubo yokusebenza ngaphakathi kukahulumeni ukuqinisekisa ukusebenzisana phakathi komsebenzi nokukwazi ukwenza umsebenzi . Ngokulinganayo , uhulumeni kudingeka azilungiselele ukuhlola , ukufunda ngokwenzekile nokusebenzisa izindlela ezahlukene zokufinyelela enhlosweni eyodwa . Amaqembu enza imisebenzi aqinisekise ukuthi ayavumelana ngezindaba ezibaluleke kakhulu , aphinde abike ngesikhathi somhlangano wokuhlangana namanye amaqembu . Nikeza iqembu ngalinye ikhasi lefliphshadi kanye nokokumaka ukuba akusebenzise ngesikhathi enza imisebenzi . Umasipala kufanele wenze ama-KPI azo zonke izindawo , abasebenzi kanye nabanikezeli bezinsizakalo . IKomidi Lesigceme akusiyona inkundla yepolitiki yokusetshenziswa ngumuntu noma elinye iqembu lepolitiki , ongenele ukhetho noma iqembu elinenkathalo . IKomidi Lesigceme linikeza inkundla yokuxoxisana okuvulelekile ukuze isixazululo , noma uhlelo lokwenza luchazelwe wonke umphakathi ozozuza kulo . Ukuncishiswa kwezindleko zesivumelwano sokulawula , ikakhulukazi emafemini amancane nalingene . Amakomidi Ezigceme adlala indima ebalulekile ekuphucukisweni nasekubuyekezweni kwe-NSDP njengoba incike kumbono ovela kuhulumeni wendawo . Ilogifreyimu ihlinzeka ngohlaka lokuhlaziya , njengoba icacisa ngokusobala ukuthi yini okwakumele ifezeke ( okuyimiphumela nenhloso ) , le mpumelelo yayizoqinisekiswa kanjani ( Izinkomba Nendlela Yokuqinisekisa ) nokuthi yikuphi okusemqoka okwakucatshangelwa . Kubalulekile ukukhumbula ukuthi amalungu omphakathi avela kumasiko , izinhlanga , izilimi noma izinkolo ezahlukahlukene , noma ubudala noma amanye amaqembu anenkathalo . Uma kuxhunyanwa kubalulekile ukuqaphela lokho okuthathwa ngokuthi indlela yokuziphatha eyamukelekile kulelo qembu . Sebenzisa ulimi olwamukelekile kwabalalele ngale kwalokho ngeke babe nomdlandla kulokho okushoyo . I-HIV / AIDS isibe nomthelela omkhulu esibalweni sabantu , ikhuphule kakhulu ukushona kwabantu kusukela ngonyaka wezi-2000 futhi yanciphisa isibalo sabesifazane abaseminyakeni yokuthola abantwana . Kunezimpawu zokuthi izwe seliqalile ukuphenduka mayelana nempumelelo yezemfundo nomkhankaso wokwelapha . Izinga lokutheleleka nge-HIV selimile kumaphesenti acishe abe yi-10 . Ukutheleleka okusha phakathi kwabantu abasha sekwehlile nesikhathi sokuphila sesiyakhuphuka . Yize kunale mihlomulo , kuyohlala njalo kunesibalo esiphezulu sezintandane ze-AIDS nezingane okudinga zixhaswe uhulumeni esikhathini eside esizayo . Izinkomba kumele zithuthukiswe ngokubambisana namaqembu azohlomula . Ukumisa izinhloso zoshintsho lwesimo uqobo kungenzeka kuphela uma ulwazi oluyisisekelo lukhona . Lokhu kudinga izinhlolovo eziyisisekelo . Esikhathini esiyiminyaka eminingana ezayo umnotho womhlaba kulindeleke ukuthi ukhule kancane . Kulezi zimo , amabhizinisi aseNingizimu Afrika kudingeka acabange ngokucophelela mayelana nokuthi yini ayikhiqizayo , eyikhiqizela bani , esebenzisani . Njengomnotho omncane ovulekile , iNingizimu Afrika ingenza imikhiqizo yezindawo . Ukufaka isilinganiso esincane sokudingeka kakhulu emhlabeni ezindaweni lapho amafemu endawo engakwazi ukuthi ancintisane khona kungaba nomthelela omkhulu . Isibonelo , iNingizimu Afrika ingaba umholi womhlaba ezimpahleni nasemisebenzini ekhiqizwe embonini yezokumbiwa phansi , lapho eyazi khona ukuthi kwenziwa kanjani . Lokhu kuyokwenza kube neqhaza elisemqoka ezimakethe zezimboni . Isigaba soku-1 siqala ngokuqoqa ulwazi olukhona ngesigceme ngenhloso yokuthola izimo zokuhlela . Lokhu kuhlanganisa lokho okusemqoka ohlelweni lwe-IDP , izindawo ezingaxhaswa ngemali wumasipala kanye nolwazi ngabanye abalethi bezidingo . Aphawule ngendlela umphakathi ubamba ngayo iqhaza kumasipala , kanye nangezakhiwo ezisungulelwe ukubamba komphakathi iqhaza . Amakomidi ezigceme asesetshenziswe ngokubanzi njengendlela yokuhlela ubudlelwano phakathi kukamasipala nomphakathi . Ekuhlanganiseni uhlelo lwe-IDP , amakomidi ezigceme abamba iqhaza elisemqoka ekulinganiseni okuvezwa wumphakathi nezidingo zawo , okungafakwa ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Kodwa angaphinde agqugquzele ukubuyekezwa wumphakathi kokusebenza kohlelo lwe-IDP kanye nokusebenza kukamasipala ngokohlelo lwe-IDP . Amandla okunxusa - Umkhandlu wendawo unezibopho sokwenza izinqumo kanye nokuxhasa amaphrojekthi ngezimali . Kodwa unganxusa ezinye zezibopho zawo kwabamele umphakathi ukuze bawusize ukufeza umsebenzi wawo . Omunye wemisebenzi ebalulekile yeKomidi LesiGceme ukuthola uvo lomphakathi mayelana ne-IDP nokuqinisekisa ukuthi umasipala unalo lolu lwazi . Lokhu kungenziwa ngokubamba imihlangano yomphakathi noma ukwenza inhlolovo umuzi ngomuzi ukuveza izinto ezihamba phambili emphakathini . lesi yisigaba esidinga okwenziwayo njengempendulo noma ukumelana nesimo . Isibonelo , ukubhekana nesimo kungafaka ukumemeza noma ukushaya noma ukukhuluma noma ukukhetha ukusuka kuleso simo . Abantu babhekana nengxabano bephushwa yindlela ababheka ngayo izinto nabakholelwa kukho . Uma kuqhathaniswa namazinga amahle kakhulu amazwe ngamazwe , ingqalasizinda ye-ICT yaseNingizimu Afrika imbi kakhulu . Ingqalasizinda yolwazi esebenza kahle ekhuthaza ukukhula komnotho nokubandakanywa kwabo bonke abantu kudinga izinhlaka zokuxhumana ngocingo eziqinile nezibiza kahle . Inzuzo yomnotho namathuba emisebenzi kudlula izindleko . UKUHLOLA KOKUQALA KWEZINQUBOMGOMO EZIKHONA KWAQINISEKISA UKUTHI ININGIZIMU AFRIKA INEZINQUBOMGOMO EZIQINISEKISA UKULETHWA KWEZINGQLAZIZINDA KANYE NEMISEBENZI ESIMEME . UKUHLINZEKWA KWEMISEBENZI YEZINGQALAZIZINDA ZIKAMASIPALA ENGASIMEME KUNGEKE KWATHIWA KWENZIWA UKWESWELEKA KOMTHETHO . UMthetho Wokwehlukaniswa Kwezimali , ka-1997 ithuluzi lwesabelomali oluchaza ngokuthi ingabelwanwa kanjani imali kazwelonke ( eqoqwe ngokwentela ) ezinhlakeni zikahulumeni ukuxhasa ukwenziwa kwezinhlelo ezahlukahlukene zikahulumeni . Wenziwa njalo ngonyaka . Ngaphezu kokuqhubezela ukubamba ngokugcwele iqhaza , lo mhlangano uhlinzeka umphakathi ngokubanzi ngethuba lokuqonda ubuhle benqubo ye-CBP . Amaqembu amancane abantu ababili kuya kwabathathu abawusizo nabayizingcweti kwezezinhloso / kwezamasu / kwezezinhlelo banikwa Ikhasi lokucatshangwayo . Uzodinga isikhathi esingangehora kuya kwamabili ngalelo nalelo khasi lokucatshangwayo . UMTHETHO WEZINHLELO ZIKAMASIPALA , ka-2000 , Izahluko 4 no-5 , zibheke ukuthi amakhansela omasipala bakhe izindlela zokuxhumana nokumbandakanya umphakathi nezinhlangano zomphakathi . Lokhu kusekelwa Uhlaka Lwenqubomgomo Kazwelonke Yokubamba Komphakathi Iqhaza , ka-2005 oluchaza ubambiswano nomphakathi ' njengenqubo evulelekile , yokuzinikela lapho abantu namaqembu emiphakathini ethile babelana khona ngemibono futhi besiza ekuthathweni kwezinqumo ' . lesi sahluko sibheka amasu okuxhumana angase asetshenziswe ukusiza amaKomidi Ezigceme ekugqugquzeleni nasekwandiseni ukubamba komphakathi iqhaza . Ezomnotho : Lezi yizinto ezisetshenziswa ngabantu ukusimamisa ukuphila kwabo , ezifana nemali , ukonga imali , izinqolobane zommbila , imfuyo , amathuluzi nezinto zokusebenza . Izindawo zasemakhaya zingaba nezigceme ezinkulu kakhulu nabantu abasabalele ezigodini kanye nasemapulazini . Kunezinhlangano ezincane kakhulu ezisebenzayo . Isigodi ngasinye noma iqembu lamapulazi lingakhetha ozolimela ukuthi asebenze eKomidini Lesigceme . Ngaphambi kokuthatha lesi sinyathelo , abagqugquzeli kumele babe nekhophi yohlelo lwe-IDP ukuze bakwazi ukubona okusemqoka ngokubanzi ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Uma kuwukuthi ababambe iqhaza banayo ikhophi yohlelo lwe-IDP , banikeze imizuzu embalwa ukuloba imininingwane evela emalungeni nokukhomba okukodwa okusemqoka okusohlelweni lwe-IDP . Chaza ukuthi lesi sigaba sohlelo lwesigceme siqopha lokho abagqugquzeli abakwenzile ukwenza uhlelo nokuthi ngobani ababamba iqhaza . Nika lelo nalelo qembu imizuzu embalwa yokuloba amagama ' abagqugquzeli ' kanye namagama namagama ababebambe iqhaza abavela emphakathini . Thola ukuthi yimiphi imisebenzi edinga izinsiza ezisemqoka zangaphandle noma imisebenzi engenziwa ezingeni likamasipala . Lokhu kumele kwethulwe ohlelweni lwe-IDP . Ohlelweni lwe-CBP kusuke kwethenjelwe ekubambeni iqhaza komphakathi ukuze kube lula ukulethela abantu izidingo . Izinga nokujula kokubamba iqhaza komphakathi kusemqoka ukuze uhlelo lwe-CBP lukwazi ukusebenza . Kudinga ukuzibophezela kwabathintekayo abazobamba iqhaza bengakhathali ukuze lolu hlelo luhlomise umphakathi ngamakhono , lubenze basukume benze okufanele bakwenze . IKomidi Lesigceme lenziwe yiKhansela Lesigceme kanye nabantu abayishumi abangabavoti esigcemeni futhi abakhethwa ngumphakathi abawusebenzelayo . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme kufanele amelwe ngokusabalele yimikhakha ehlukene yomphakathi ( abesifazane , yintsha , imiphakathi eyayincishwe amathuba , njll . ) . Ukuthi baseka liphi iqembu akufanele kube nomthelela ekukhethweni kwabo . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme abamba iqhaza ngokuzithandela ngaphandle kokukhokhelwa . Izindima zobulili wukuziphatha okufundwayo emphakathini othile , noma kwelinye iqembu lomphakathi . Zenza izenzo , imisebenzi kanye nemithwalo ethathwa njengeyabesilisa noma yabesifazane . Zithathwa njengezijwayelekile , kodwa azinjalo . Izindima zobulili zithintwa yiminyaka , izinga , ubuzwe , ubuhlanga kanye nenkolo , kanye nendawo ngokwezwe , ngokomnotho kanye nangezombusazwe . Futhi zihlale zicindezela abesifazane . Isibonelo , ubulili bomzimba bowesifazane benza kube ngumsebenzi wakhe ukuncelisa ingane ngoba umphakathi ulindelele lokho kuye . Leyo yindima yakhe yobulili . Owesilisa angawenza kalula umsebenzi wakhe kwazise akukho lutho azalwa nakho okumvimbela ukuthi ayothenga , apheke ukudla noma afunze ingane . Abesilisa abaningi abawenzi umsebenzi wasekhaya ngoba uthathwa njengemisebenzi yabantu besifazane . Abahlali besiGceme A bahlaselwe ngubugebengu obuningi . Nakuba abahlali bezibikile izigameko zobugebengu emaphoyiseni endawo isimo sisaqhubeka . Abahlali bakhalile kwilungu leKomidi Lesigceme lendawo elikuvezile lokhu emhlanganweni weKomidi Lesigceme wokugcina . IKomidi Lesigceme nekhansela lesigceme linqume ukubiza umhlangano wabahlali . Emhlanganweni iziphakamiso eziningi ziveziwe ukuzama ukuphucula isimo nokwehlisa ubugebengu . Imiqondo ephambili okuvunyelwene ngayo kube ukuya emkhandlwini wendawo ukuze kwandiswe inani lezikhanyisi endaweni njengoba ukukhanya kungekho futhi ubugebengu obuningi benzeka ebusuku , nokwakha i-Community Policing Forum ( CPF ) . Umhlangano uvumile ekwakhiweni kwekomidi lokuqondisa elincane elinamalungu amabili eKomidi Lesigceme ikhansela nabahlali ababili . Ababambiqhaza bakha amaqembu abantu aba-4 kuya kwaba-6 bese benza Umsebenzi woku-1 . Qinisekisa ukuthi iqembu ngalinye lilikhethile iqembu elinentshisekelo lenhlalonhle efanayo emphakathini . UMvikeli Womphakathi uneqhaza elibalulekile ekulweni nasekucubunguleni ukungenzi kahle ezindaweni zokusebenzela umphakathi . Ihhovisi loMvikeli Womphakathi linamandla okusesha nanoma yikuphi ukuziphatha ezindabeni zikahulumeni , noma ekuphathweni kukahulumeni kunanoma yikuliphi izinga likahulumeni okungaba ukungenzi kahle noma kuholele ekubandlululweni , ukubika ngalokho kuziphatha nokwenza izindlela zokukulungisa . UHlelo Lwezentuthuko Kazwelonke luncike ocwaningweni olunzulu , ukuxoxisana nokusebenzisana . Yize lungeluhle kakhulu futhi lungaphelele , lukhombisa izinhlelo zokuxazulula izinkinga zezwe , nokugxilisa ukusebenzisana kwabantu baseNingizimu Afrika bawo wonke amazinga empilo ukwakha ikusasa lethu . Ingqalasizinda ekahle nengabizi . Ingqalasizinda yokuthuthukisa umsebenzi womnotho olungele ukukhula nokudalwa kwemisebenzi . Indlela yokwenza iyokwenziwa ukuqinisa imisebenzi esemqoka efana nezokuthutha emabhizinisini , ezamandla , ezokuxhumana ngocingo nezamanzi , ngesikhathi kuqinisekiswa ukungabizi kakhulu nokusimama kwesikhathi eside . Ukwakha indlela yamalahle entsha yokukhulula indawo yokufakwa kwamalahle eWaterberg , ukwelula izindlela zamalahle ezikhona endaweni yamalahle ezungezile maphakathi nokuthuthukisa indlela yokuthutha amalahle aya e-RichardsBay neyokuthutha insimbi eya e-Saldanha . Amaqembu kahulumeni wendawo anomsebenzi wesigungu , owenziwa ngohlelo olukhethiwe lesigungu ( kubalwa nemeya yesigungu kanye nesigungu esiqoqiwe ) kanye nomsebenzi ophathelene nomthetho okhishiweyo ngezindlela zemikhandlu . Inqubo yesigungu sikahulumeni wendawo ayivulelwanga umphakathi , kodwa inqubo yokukhipha umthetho ivulelekile . Isifanekiso sokuthuthukisa sikahulumeni wendawo sisebenzisa ukugcizelela isidingo sokuveza obala , ukubophezeleka , ukuxhumana , ukugqugquzela ukubamba iqhaza kanye nokuhlanganyela komphakathi . Bawenze kanjani abanye lo msebenzi ? Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme adinga amakhono okuxhumana amahle ukuqinisekisa ukuthi bayawaqonda abanye nokwakha ukwethenjwa phakathi komphakathi kanye nomkhandlu . Uma ikhansela selisibukezile isabelomali esetshenziswa ngokwezidingo lavuma ukweseka uhlelo , kuhlelwa umhlangano omkhulu weqembu ukubikela umphakathi ngaphambi kokusetshenziswa kohlelo . Ukuhlela ukuthi yini iphrojekthi ethemba ukuyizuza - lokhu kwesinye isikhathi kubizwa ngokuthi ukuhlela iziphumo noma imiphumela , futhi kubandakanya wonke umsebenzi wokulungiselela nokuqinisekisa ukuthi ngakube iphrojekthi izokwenzeka yini . Kubalulekile ukushintsha imiqondo yabantu kanye nemicabango engemihle , ngokucabanga izinqubo noma imicabango engelona iqiniso ngamanye amaqembu uma sifuna ukuhlonipha ukwahlukahlukana ngokwamasiko . Imicabango ifakwa ngokusebenzisa imithelela eminingi . Cabanga ngolwazi olungezansi nokuthi iKomidi Lesigceme lingayishintsha kanjani le micabango uma lifuna ukubhekana nalezi zindaba . UNkk Smith ufake isikhalazo kwamasipala izikhathi ezimbalwa mayelana nomgodi ovulekile osesitiladini sakhe . Isibani esikhanyisa esitaladini esitaladini kakhulu futhi futhi abasebenzi abeza ekhaya bebuya emsebenzi ebumnyameni bewela kulo mgodi noma becishe bawela kuwo . Umphakathi ukhathazekile ukuthi eyodwa yezingane ingawela kulo mgodi futhi lokhu kungayibulala . Ufaka isikhalazo kwamasipala . Lolu daba luyalungiswa ngokushesha . Ukwakha imigudu esemthethweni engachemile kanye nokubambisana phakathi komphakathi nomkhandlu . Umkhandlu uthathe isinqumo sokufaka amamitha amanzi okulandela ukumoshwa kwamanzi . Inkontileka kufanele iqashwe ukwenza lo msebenzi . IKomidi Lesigceme likamasipala ABC livame ukuhambela imihlangano yomkhandlu njalo . IKomidi Lesigceme lidwebe uhlu olunamagama amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme nezinsuku okufanele ahambele ngazo imihlangano yomkhandlu . Lawa malungu athola amakhophi amaminithi futhi abelana ngolwazi namanye amalungu . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme abika njalo emphakathini . Amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme asebenzisa amamithi omkhandlu ukubheka ukuthi izinqumo ezithathiwe ziyalandelelwa . Axhumana kakhulu nekhansela lesigceme futhi aveza izinkinga zomphakathi ekhanseleni ukuze ziyiswe emkhandlwini . Umthetho kamasipala omusha omayelana nobambiswano lomphakathi nabazimele wethuliwe amalungu eKomidi Lesigceme abe esehlela umhlangano womphakathi ukuxoxisana ngalolu daba ethula umbiko emkhandlwini . Ukungena kwemali yephrojekthi ngesikhathi sephrojekthi ( okuhlelwe ngamakota ukuhambisana neminyaka yezimali ehlukene yezindawo ezihlukene okuvela kuzo imali ) . Amanothi ku-3.2.1 kuze kufike ku-3.2.5 . Ababambe iqhaza bahlukaniswa emaqenjini abantu abane . Bhala imibuzo kufliphshadi . Ababambiqhaza basebenza ngababili ( yilowo nalowo ukhuluma nohleli eduze kwakhe ) bese bebonisana ngezimpendulo ( banike imizuzu eyi-10 kuya kweyi-15 ukuze bacubungule imibuzo ) . Umphathidolobha ukhethwa ngumkhandlu ukuba abheke ukusebenza komkhandlu . Umphathidolobha wenza imisebenzi yemicimbi nemisebenzi ayinikwe ngumkhandlu . Umphathidolobha omkhulu unawo wonke amandla asezingeni eliphezulu . Chaza ukuthi isabelomali sifaka phakathi IZINDLEKO kanye NEMALI ENGENAYO . Amakomidi Ezigceme angabamba iqhaza elibaluleke kakhulu kulesi sigaba , njengoba engathanda ukwazi isimo salabo abangahlomula kwiphrojekthi nokuthi yini izidingo zabo . Bayokwazi ukusiza ukuhlola agcina ukuhlaziya ababambe iqhaza ngesikhathi somjikelezo wephrojekthi ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izidingo zababambe iqhaza kuhlangatshezwana nazo ngempumelelo . Yiziphi izinhlelo ( amaphrojekthi ) ikomidi lesigceme elifisa ukuzethula ? Cabanga ngezinto ezifana nezinhlelo zokuthuthukiswa komnotho wendawo , ukuqeqesha abanakekeli abazinze emakhaya ? Singazethula yini lezi zinhlelo nakwezinye izinhlangano zemiphakathi ? Cabanga ngemikhakha emithathu kahulumeni nokuthi izakhamizi zingalibamba kanjani iqhaza emkhakheni ngamunye . Sebenzisa indlela enokuzithoba . Gwema ukuphendula ngendlela yokucasuka . ulwazi mayelana nokulethwa kwemisebenzi kumele ukuba lunikwe abahlinzeki bemisebenzi kanye nalabo abasizakalayo ngokulethwa kwemisebenzi . Uma izinganhle lokulethwa kwemisebenzi kumele ukuba libe yimpumelelo , kudingeka ukuthi imiphakathi ifundiswe mayelana nalokho engakulindela kanye nalokho okukhona engakuthola . Ukuvumela izakhamuzi zibambe iqhaza enqubweni enombono neyokuhlela indawo . Kukhona inani labathengisi abathengisa eduzane nasesiteshini . Kuye kwaba nezikhalazo ezivela kubaninizitolo sokuthi laba bathengisi abakhokhi irenti futhi bangathengisa impahla yabo ngemali ephansi nokuthi bashiya iphevumenti ingcolile emva kokuphela kosuku uma sebeya ekhaya . Sebenzisa i-POWERPOINT A ukubeka uhlaka lwamazinga e-IDP . Noma-ke , ungathi ababambiqhaza babheke ekhasini 18 kumanothi esifundo bese bebhala izinga ngalinye kufliphshadi . Ukwesekwa kwamabhizinisi amancane : Ngonyaka we-1994 inkampani yokusiza yaseBritain yaxhasa ngezimali ukuze kusungulwe ideski ye-LED . Inhloso ye-deski le-LED ukunikezela ngoqeqesho , ukweseka amabhizinisi amancane kanye nokunikezela ngemalimboleko . Nakuba kwaba khona lokhu kungenelela , amabhizinisi amancane kule ndawo abhekana nezinga elikhulu lokwehluleka okwadalwa ukungeneli kwezimakethe zemikhiqizo kuleli dolobha , amaholo amancane eningi lezakhamizi , ukusweleka kwezithuthi abakhiqizi ukuze abakhiqizi bathengise imikhiqizo yabo kwenye indawo kanye nokwesweleka koqeqesho jikelele . Nikeza imininingwane elula futhi ehlaba emhloleni . Ingxenye yendlela yethu yokuvikela umphakathi imayelana nomholo womphakathi , obandakanya izikole zamahhala , izidingongqangi zamahhala nezokuthuthwa komphakathi ezixhasiwe . Ukwengeza ekudalweni kwamathuba emisebenzi engeziwe emkhakheni ozimele , ukusatshalaliswa okusemqoka kwezinhlelo zokuqashwa komphakathi kuyosiza ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ambalwa amakhaya aphila ngaphansi kwezinga elibekiwe lemali engenayo . Amalungu Ekomidi Lesigceme angabona sengathi amalunga omkhakha othile womphakathi ' angamaqili ' futhi ngakho-ke noma yisiphi isiphakamiso abasenza mayelana nokulethwa kwezidingo noma ngamaprojekthi kumele zishaywe indiva . SPECIFIC ( LIQONDE NGQO ) - ingabe izinga lomsebenzi likusho ngokuqonde ngqo yini lokho okumele ukuba kulinganiswe ? Ekugcineni , kubandakanya ukuphethwa kwephrojekthi , ukuhlola izinga lomkhiqizo noma umsebenzi osuphelile nokuqedela izivumelwano nesabelomali .
